# notes:                
40001001	Incwadi yokuzalwa kukaJesu Kristu , indodana kaDavide , indodana ka-Abrahama .
40001002	U-Abrahama wazala u-Isaka , u-Isaka wazala uJakobe , uJakobe wazala uJuda nabafowabo ;
40001003	uJuda wazala oFaresi noZara kuTamari , uFaresi wazala u-Esiromu , u-Esiromu wazala u-Aramu ;
40001004	u-Aramu wazala u-Aminadaba , u-Aminadaba wazala uNasoni , uNasoni wazala uSalimoni ;
40001005	uSalimoni wazala uBowasi kuRakhabi , uBowasi wazala u-Obede kuRuthe , u-Obede wazala uJesayi ;
40001006	uJesayi wazala uDavide , inkosi . UDavide wazala uSolomoni kumka-Uriya ;
40001007	uSolomoni wazala uRobowamu , uRobowamu wazala u-Abiya , u-Abiya wazala u-Asafa ;
40001008	u-Asafa wazala uJosafati , uJosafati wazala uJoramu , uJoramu wazala u-Oziya ;
40001009	u-Oziya wazala uJothamu , uJothamu wazala u-Akazi , u-Akazi wazala uHezekiya ;
40001010	uHezekiya wazala uManase , uManase wazala u-Amoni , u-Amoni wazala uJosiya ;
40001011	uJosiya wazala uJekoniya nabafowabo ngesikhathi sokuthunjelwa eBabiloni .
40001012	Kwathi emva kokuthunjelwa eBabiloni uJekoniya wazala uSalatiyeli , uSalatiyeli wazala uZorobabeli ;
40001013	uZorobabeli wazala u-Abiyudi , u-Abiyudi wazala u-Eliyakimi , u-Eliyakimi wazala u-Azori ;
40001014	u-Azori wazala uSadoki , uSadoki wazala u-Akimi , u-Akimi wazala u-Eliyudi ;
40001015	u-Eliyudi wazala u-Eleyazare , u-Eleyazare wazala uMathani , uMathani wazala uJakobe ;
40001016	uJakobe wazala uJosefa , indoda kaMariya , azalwa nguye uJesu othiwa uKristu .
40001017	Zinjalo-ke izizukulwane zonke ezisukela ku-Abrahama ziye kuDavide , ziyizizukulwane eziyishumi nane ; nezisukela kuDavide ziye ekuthunjelweni eBabiloni ziyizizukulwane eziyishumi nane ; nezisukela ekuthunjelweni eBabiloni ziye kuKristu ziyizizukulwane eziyishumi nane .
40001018	Ukuzalwa kukaJesu Kristu kwaba nje : unina uMariya esemiselwe uJosefa , bengakahlangani wafunyanwa ekhulelwe ngoMoya oNgcwele .
40001019	Kepha uJosefa indoda yakhe engumuntu olungileyo , engathandi ukumthela ihlazo , wayefuna ukumlahla ngasese .
40001020	Esazindla ngalokho , bheka , ingelosi yeNkosi yabonakala kuye ngephupho , ithi : " Josefa , ndodana kaDavide , ungesabi ukumthatha uMariya umkakho , ngokuba lokho akukhulelweyo kungoMoya oNgcwele .
40001021	Uzakuzala indodana , uyiqambe igama lokuthi uJesu , ngokuba nguye oyakusindisa abantu bakhe ezonweni zabo . "
40001022	Lokhu konke kwenzeka ukuba kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa yiNkosi ngomprofethi ukuthi :
40001023	" Bheka , intombi iyakukhulelwa , izale indodana ; bayakuyiqamba igama lokuthi u-Emanuweli , " okungukuthi ngokuhunyushwa " uNkulunkulu unathi " .
40001024	UJosefa esevukile ebuthongweni wenza njengalokho imyalile ingelosi yeNkosi , wamthatha umkakhe ;
40001025	akaze aya kuye , waze wazibula ngendodana ; wayiqamba igama lokuthi uJesu .
40002001	UJesu esezelwe eBetlehema laseJudiya emihleni kaHerode inkosi , bheka , kwafika izazi eJerusalema , zivela empumalanga , zithi :
40002002	" Uphi lowo ozelwe eyinkosi yabaJuda na ? Ngokuba sibonile inkanyezi yakhe kwelasempumalanga , size ukukhuleka kuye . "
40002003	UHerode inkosi esekuzwile lokho wakhathazeka neJerusalema lonke kanye naye .
40002004	Wabutha bonke abapristi abakhulu nababhali besizwe , wabuza kubo ukuthi uKristu uzakuzalelwaphi .
40002005	Bathi kuye : " EBetlehema laseJudiya , ngokuba kulotshiwe kanjalo ngomprofethi ukuthi :
40002006	‘ Nawe Betlehema , lizwe lakwaJuda , kawusiye omncane nakanye kubabusi bakwaJuda , ngokuba kuyakuvela kuwe umbusi oyakwalusa isizwe sami u-Israyeli . ’ "
40002007	Khona uHerode , ezibizile izazi ngasese , wabuzisisa kuzo isikhathi inkanyezi ebonakele ngaso ,
40002008	wazithuma eBetlehema , wathi : " Hambani nibuzisise ngomntwana ; kuyakuthi nxa nimfumene , ningitshele ukuba nami ngiye ngikhuleke kuye . "
40002009	Seziyizwile inkosi , zamuka ; bheka , inkanyezi ezayibona kwelasempumalanga yahamba phambi kwazo , yaze yafika yema phezu kwalapho umntwana ekhona .
40002010	Zathi ukuyibona inkanyezi , zathokoza ngokuthokoza okukhulu kakhulu .
40002011	Zase zingena endlini , zabona umntwana noMariya unina , zawa phansi , zakhuleka kuye , zavula amagugu azo , zamkhunga ngezipho : igolide namakha nenhlaka .
40002012	Kwathi ziyaliwe nguNkulunkulu ngephupho ukuba zingabuyeli kuHerode , zabuyela ezweni lakubo ngenye indlela .
40002013	Sezimukile , bheka , ingelosi yeNkosi yabonakala kuJosefa ngephupho , ithi : " Vuka uthabathe umntwana nonina , ubalekele eGibithe , uhlale khona , ngize ngikutshele ; ngokuba uHerode uzakumfuna umntwana ukuba ambhubhise . "
40002014	Wavuka-ke , wathabatha umntwana nonina ebusuku , wamuka waya eGibithe ,
40002015	wahlala khona , waze wafa uHerode , ukuze kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa yiNkosi ngomprofethi ukuthi : " Ngayibiza indodana yami iphume eGibithe . "
40002016	Khona uHerode , esebonile ukuthi izazi zimphambile , wathukuthela kakhulu , wathumela wabulala bonke abantwana besilisa baseBetlehema nasendaweni yonke yangakhona , abaminyaka mibili nangaphansi njengesikhathi abesibuzisisile kuzo izazi .
40002017	Khona kwagcwaliseka okwakhulunywa ngoJeremiya umprofethi ukuthi :
40002018	" Kwezwakala izwi eRama , ukukhala nokulila okukhulu , uRakheli ekhalela abantwana bakhe , engavumi ukududuzwa , ngokuba abasekho . "
40002019	Kepha uHerode esefile , bheka , ingelosi yeNkosi yabonakala ngephupho kuJosefa eGibithe , yathi :
40002020	" Vuka uthabathe umntwana nonina , uye ezweni lakwa-Israyeli ; ngokuba sebefile ababezingela ukuphila komntwana . "
40002021	Wasuka-ke , wathabatha umntwana nonina , wafika ezweni lakwa-Israyeli .
40002022	Kepha ezwa ukuthi sekubusa u-Arkelawu eJudiya esikhundleni sikaHerode uyise , wesaba ukuya khona ; eseyaliwe nguNkulunkulu ngephupho wamuka waya kwelaseGalile ;
40002023	wafika wakha emzini othiwa iNazaretha ukuba kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa ngabaprofethi ukuthi : " Uyakubizwa ngokuthi umNazaretha . "
40003001	Ngaleyo mihla kwavela uJohane uMbhapathizi eshumayela ehlane laseJudiya , ethi :
40003002	" Phendukani , ngokuba umbuso wezulu ususondele ! "
40003003	Ngokuba nguye akhuluma ngaye umprofethi u-Isaya , ethi : " Izwi lomemezayo ehlane , lithi : ‘ Lungisani indlela yeNkosi , nenze imikhondo yayo iqonde . ’ "
40003004	Yena uJohane wayenengubo yoboya bekamela noqhotho lwesikhumba okhalweni lwakhe ; ukudla kwakhe kwakuyizinkumbi nezinyosi zasendle .
40003005	Khona kwaphumela kuye iJerusalema , neJudiya lonke , nezwe lonke laseJordani ,
40003006	babhapathizwa nguye emfuleni iJordani bevuma izono zabo .
40003007	Kepha kwathi ebona abaningi kubaFarisi nabaSadusi beza embhapathizweni , wathi kubo : " Nzalo yezinyoka , ngubani onibonise ukubalekela intukuthelo ezayo na ?
40003008	Ngakho vezani izithelo ezifanele ukuphenduka .
40003009	Ningacabangi ukuba ningasho phakathi kwenu ukuthi : ‘ Sinobaba u-Abrahama ; ’ ngokuba ngithi kini : UNkulunkulu angamvusela u-Abrahama abantwana kulawa matshe .
40003010	Izembe selibekiwe empandeni yemithi ; ngakho yonke imithi engatheli izithelo ezinhle iyanqunywa , iphonswe emlilweni .
40003011	" Mina nginibhapathiza ngamanzi , kube ngukuphenduka ; kepha yena oza emva kwami unamandla kunami engingafanele ukuthwala izicathulo zakhe ; yena uzakunibhapathiza ngoMoya oNgcwele nangomlilo ,
40003012	ombenge yakhe yokwela isesandleni sakhe ; uzakushanelisisa isibuya sakhe , abuthele amabele enqolobaneni yakhe ; kepha amakhoba uzakuwashisa ngomlilo ongacimekiyo . "
40003013	Khona uJesu evela eGalile wafika kuJohane eJordani ukuba azobhapathizwa nguye .
40003014	Kepha uJohane wamalela wathi : " Yimi engiswela ukubhapathizwa nguwe ; wena uza kimi na ? "
40003015	UJesu waphendula , wathi kuye : " Vuma kalokhu , ngokuba kusifanele ukugcwalisa kanjalo ukulunga konke . " Khona wayesemvumela .
40003016	UJesu esebhapathiziwe wakhuphuka masinyane emanzini ; bheka , izulu lavuleka , wabona uMoya kaNkulunkulu ehla njengejuba , eza phezu kwakhe .
40003017	Bheka , kwavela izwi ezulwini , lithi : " Lo uyiNdodana yami ethandekayo engithokozile ngayo . "
40004001	Khona uJesu waholelwa nguMoya ehlane ukuba alingwe nguSathane .
40004002	Esezilile ukudla izinsuku ezingamashumi amane nobusuku obungamashumi amane , wagcina walamba .
40004003	Kwafika umlingi , wathi kuye : " Uma uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu , yisho ukuba lawa matshe abe yizinkwa . "
40004004	Kepha waphendula wathi : " Kulotshiwe ukuthi : ‘ Akusinkwa sodwa umuntu ayakuphila ngaso kodwa ngamazwi onke aphuma emlonyeni kaNkulunkulu . ’ "
40004005	Khona uSathane wamthatha , wamyisa emzini ongcwele , wammisa esiqongweni sethempeli ,
40004006	wathi kuye : " Uma uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu , ziphonse phansi ; ngokuba kulotshiwe ukuthi : ‘ Uyakuyaleza izingelosi zakhe ngawe , zikuthwale ngezandla , ungaze waqhuzuka etsheni ngonyawo lwakho . ’ "
40004007	UJesu wathi kuye : " Kulotshiwe futhi ukuthi : ‘ Ungayilingi iNkosi uNkulunkulu wakho . ’ "
40004008	USathane wabuye wamyisa entabeni ende kakhulu , wamkhombisa imibuso yonke yezwe nenkazimulo yayo ;
40004009	wathi kuye : " Konke lokhu ngizakukunika khona , uma uziwisa phansi , ukhuleke kimi . "
40004010	Khona uJesu wathi kuye : " Suka , Sathane , ngokuba kulotshiwe ukuthi : ‘ Wokhuleka eNkosini uNkulunkulu wakho , umkhonze yena yedwa . ’ "
40004011	USathane wayesemshiya ; bheka , kwafika izingelosi , zamkhonza .
40004012	Kuthe esezwile ukuthi uJohane uboshiwe , wamuka waya eGalile .
40004013	Wasuka eNazaretha , weza wahlala eKapernawume elingaselwandle emikhawulweni yakwaZabuloni neyakwaNafetali
40004014	ukuba kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa ngo-Isaya umprofethi ukuthi :
40004015	" Izwe lakwaZabuloni nezwe lakwaNafetali ngaselwandle ngaphesheya kweJordani , iGalile labezizwe ,
40004016	isizwe esasihlezi ebumnyameni sibonile ukukhanya okukhulu , nababehlezi ezweni nasethunzini lokufa kuphumele kubo ukukhanya . "
40004017	Kusukela kuleso sikhathi uJesu waqala ukushumayela nokusho ukuthi : " Phendukani , ngokuba umbuso wezulu ususondele . "
40004018	UJesu ehamba ngaselwandle lwaseGalile wabona izelamani ezimbili , uSimoni othiwa uPetru no-Andreya umfowabo , bephonsa inetha elwandle ; ngokuba babe ngabadobi .
40004019	Wayesethi kubo : " Ngilandeleni ; ngiyakunenza nibe ngabadobi babantu . "
40004020	Base bewashiya masinyane amanetha , bamlandela .
40004021	Esedlulela phambili wabona ezinye izelamani ezimbili , uJakobe kaZebedewu , noJohane umfowabo , besemkhunjini kanye noZebedewu uyise , belungisa amanetha abo ; wababiza .
40004022	Base beshiya masinyane umkhumbi noyise , bamlandela .
40004023	UJesu walihamba lonke elaseGalile efundisa emasinagogeni abo , eshumayela ivangeli lombuso , ephulukisa abantu ezifweni zonke nasebuthakathakeni bonke .
40004024	Udumo lwakhe lwezwakala ezweni lonke laseSiriya ; baletha kuye bonke abagulayo abaphethwe yizifo ngezifo nobuhlungu , nabakhwelwe ngamademoni , nabanesithuthwane , nabafe uhlangothi , wabaphulukisa .
40004025	Izixuku eziningi zamlandela zivela eGalile , naseDekapholi , naseJerusalema , naseJudiya , nangaphesheya kweJordani .
40005001	Kwathi ebona izixuku , wenyukela entabeni ; esehlezi phansi , abafundi bakhe beza kuye .
40005002	Wayesevula umlomo wakhe , wabafundisa wathi :
40005003	" Babusisiwe abampofu emoyeni , ngokuba umbuso wezulu ungowabo .
40005004	Babusisiwe abakhalayo , ngokuba bayakududuzwa .
40005005	Babusisiwe abamnene , ngokuba bayakudla ifa lomhlaba .
40005006	Babusisiwe abalambele , bomele ukulunga , ngokuba bayakusuthiswa .
40005007	Babusisiwe abanesihawu , ngokuba bayakuhawukelwa .
40005008	Babusisiwe abanenhliziyo ehlanzekileyo , ngokuba bayakubona uNkulunkulu .
40005009	Babusisiwe abalamulayo , ngokuba bayakuthiwa abantwana bakaNkulunkulu .
40005010	Babusisiwe abazingelwa ngenxa yokulunga , ngokuba umbuso wezulu ungowabo .
40005011	" Nibusisiwe , nxa benithuka , benizingela , bekhuluma konke okubi ngani , beqamba amanga ngenxa yami .
40005012	Jabulani , nithokoze , ngokuba umvuzo wenu mkhulu ezulwini ; ngokuba kanjalo babazingela abaprofethi abananduleleyo .
40005013	" Nina ningusawoti womhlaba , kepha uma usawoti edumele , ubusawoti bovuswa ngani na ? Akasasizi lutho , kuphela ukulahlwa ngaphandle , anyathelwe ngabantu .
40005014	" Nina ningukukhanya kwezwe . Umuzi owakhe entabeni ungesitheke .
40005015	Nomuntu kasokheli isibani , asibeke phansi kwesitsha , kodwa usifaka othini ; khona siyabakhanyisela bonke abasendlini .
40005016	Kanjalo makukhanye ukukhanya kwenu phambi kwabantu ukuba babone imisebenzi yenu emihle , badumise uYihlo osezulwini .
40005017	" Ningathi ngize ukuchitha umthetho nabaprofethi ; angizanga ukuchitha , ngize ukugcwalisa .
40005018	Ngokuba ngiqinisile ngithi kini : Kuze kudlule izulu nomhlaba , akusoze kwadlula gamana linye nasicashana sinye somthetho , kuze kufezeke konke .
40005019	Ngakho-ke oweqa owodwa kule miyalo emincinyane , afundise abantu kanjalo , uyakuthiwa omncinyane embusweni wezulu ; kepha oyigcinayo , ayifundise , lowo uyakuthiwa mkhulu embusweni wezulu .
40005020	Ngokuba ngithi kini : Uma ukulunga kwenu kungadluli okwababhali nokwabaFarisi , anisoze nangena embusweni wezulu .
40005021	" Nizwile kwathiwa kwabasendulo : ‘ Ungabulali ; yilowo nalowo obulalayo uyakuba necala lokwahlulelwa . ’
40005022	Kepha mina ngithi kini : Yilowo nalowo othukuthelela umfowabo uyakuba necala lokwahlulelwa ; noshoyo kumfowabo ukuthi : ‘ Silima , ’ uyakuba necala emphakathini ; noshoyo ukuthi : ‘ Siwula , ’ uyakuba necala lokulahlwa esihogweni somlilo .
40005023	" Ngakho-ke nxa uletha umnikelo wakho e-altare , ukhumbula lapho ukuthi umfowenu unamagqubu nawe ,
40005024	shiya lapho umnikelo wakho phambi kwe-altare , uhambe kuqala ubuyisane nomfowenu , andukuba uze unikele umnikelo wakho .
40005025	" Shesha uzwane nolwa nawe nisesendleleni , funa olwa nawe akunikele kumahluleli , umahluleli akunikele esikhonzini , uphonswe etilongweni .
40005026	Ngiqinisile ngithi kuwe : Kawusoze waphuma khona , uze ukhiphe ifadingi lokugcina .
40005027	" Nizwile kwathiwa : ‘ Ungaphingi . ’
40005028	Kepha mina ngithi kini : Yilowo nalowo obuka owesifazane , amkhanuke , usephingile naye enhliziyweni yakhe .
40005029	Uma iso lakho lokunene likukhubekisa , likhiphe , ulilahle ; ngokuba kungcono kuwe ukuba kubhubhe sibe sinye ezithweni zakho kunokuba wonke umzimba wakho uphonswe esihogweni .
40005030	Noma isandla sakho sokunene sikukhubekisa , sinqume , usilahle ; ngokuba kungcono kuwe ukuba kubhubhe sibe sinye ezithweni zakho kunokuba wonke umzimba wakho uphonswe esihogweni .
40005031	" Kwathiwa : ‘ Yilowo nalowo olahla umkakhe kamnike incwadi yesahlukaniso . ’
40005032	Kepha mina ngithi kini : Yilowo nalowo olahla umkakhe kungengenxa yokuphinga umenza aphinge , noganwa ngolahliweyo uyaphinga .
40005033	" Nizwile futhi kwathiwa kwabasendulo : ‘ Ungafungi amanga , kepha uqinise izifungo zakho eNkosini . ’
40005034	Kepha mina ngithi kini : Ningafungi nakanye , noma izulu , ngokuba liyisihlalo sobukhosi sikaNkulunkulu ,
40005035	noma umhlaba , ngokuba uyisenabelo sezinyawo zakhe , noma iJerusalema , ngokuba lingumuzi weNkosi enkulu .
40005036	Ungafungi nekhanda lakho , ngokuba awunakuphendula nalunye unwele lube mhlophe nokuba lube mnyama .
40005037	Kepha izwi lenu malibe ngokuthi : Yebo , yebo ; qhabo , qhabo . Okudlula lokhu kuvela kokubi .
40005038	" Nizwile kwathiwa : ‘ Iso ngeso , izinyo ngezinyo . ’
40005039	Kepha mina ngithi kini : Ningamelani nokubi , kodwa uma umuntu ekumukula esihlathini sokunene , mphendulele nesinye .
40005040	Nofuna ukukumangalela , akwamuke ingubo , mnike nejazi .
40005041	Nosuka ekucindezela ukuba uhambe imayela libe linye , hamba naye abe mabili .
40005042	Muphe ocela kuwe , ungamfulatheli ofuna ukutsheleka kuwe .
40005043	" Nizwile kwathiwa : ‘ Wothanda umakhelwane wakho , uzonde isitha sakho . ’
40005044	Kepha mina ngithi kini : Thandani izitha zenu , nibabusise abaniqalekisayo , nibaphathe kahle abanizondayo , nibakhulekele abanizingelayo
40005045	ukuba nibe ngabantwana bakaYihlo osezulwini ; ngokuba yena uphumisa ilanga lakhe phezu kwababi nabahle , anise imvula phezu kwabalungileyo nabangalungile .
40005046	Ngokuba uma nithanda abanithandayo , ninamvuzo muni na ? Abenzi njalo nabathelisi na ?
40005047	Futhi uma nibingelela abafowenu bodwa , nenza lukhulu luni na ? Abenzi njalo nabezizwe na ?
40005048	Ngakho-ke manibe ngabapheleleyo , njengokuba uYihlo wasezulwini ephelele .
40006001	" Kepha qaphelani ningenzi ukulunga kwenu phambi kwabantu ukuba nibonwe yibo , funa ningabi nawo umvuzo kuYihlo osezulwini .
40006002	" Ngakho-ke nxa wabela isipho , ungakhalisi icilongo phambi kwakho , njengalokhu kwenza abazenzisi emasinagogeni nasemigwaqweni ukuba badunyiswe ngabantu . Ngiqinisile ngithi kini : Sebewamukele umvuzo wabo .
40006003	Kepha wena , nxa wabela isipho , isandla sakho sokhohlo masingakwazi esikwenzayo esokunene ,
40006004	ukuze isipho sakho sibe sekusithekeni ; noYihlo obona ekusithekeni uzakukuvuza .
40006005	" Nalapho nikhuleka , ningabi njengabazenzisi , ngokuba bethanda ukukhuleka bemi emasinagogeni nasezinhlanganweni zezindlela ukuba babonwe ngabantu . Ngiqinisile ngithi kini : Sebewamukele umvuzo wabo .
40006006	Kepha wena , nxa ukhuleka , ngena ekamelweni lakho , uthi usuvale umnyango wakho ukhuleke kuYihlo osekusithekeni ; noYihlo obona ekusithekeni uzakukuvuza .
40006007	Kodwa nxa nikhuleka , ningathemelezi njengabezizwe , ngokuba bathi bayakuzwiwa ngokukhuluma kwabo okuningi .
40006008	Ngakho-ke maningafani nabo ; ngokuba uYihlo uyakwazi enikuswelayo ningakaceli kuye .
40006009	Ngakho-ke anokhuleka kanje , nithi : ‘ Baba wethu osezulwini , malingcweliswe igama lakho ;
40006010	mawufike umbuso wakho ; mayenziwe intando yakho emhlabeni njengasezulwini ;
40006011	usiphe namuhla isinkwa sethu semihla ngemihla ;

40026037	Wathatha uPetru namadodana amabili kaZebedewu , waqala ukuba nomunyu nosizi .
40026038	Khona wathi kubo : " Umphefumulo wami ulusizi kakhulu kuze kube sekufeni ; hlalani lapha , nilinde kanye nami . "
40026039	Waqhubeka ingcosana , wawa ngobuso bakhe , wakhuleka wathi : " Baba , uma kungenzeka , akudlule kimi lesi sitsha ; nokho kungabi njengokuba ngithanda mina , kodwa njengokuba uthanda wena . "
40026040	Wayeseza kubafundi , wabafumana belele ; wathi kuPetru : " Kanti beningelinde nami ihora libe linye na ?

40026047	Esakhuluma , bheka , kwafika uJuda , omunye wabayishumi nambili , enesixuku esikhulu sinezinkemba nezinduku , sivela kubapristi abakhulu namalunga esizwe .

40026063	Kepha uJesu wathula . Wayesethi kuye umpristi omkhulu : " Ngikufungisa uNkulunkulu ophilayo ukuba usitshele uma unguKristu , iNdodana kaNkulunkulu . "

41004001	Khona wabuye waqala ukufundisa ngaselwandle . Kwabuthana kuye isixuku esikhulu kakhulu , waze wangena emkhunjini , wahlala elwandle ; isixuku sonke sasisemhlabathini ngaselwandle .

41004014	Umhlwanyeli uhlwanyela izwi .

42024026	UKristu ubengamelwe yini ukuhlupheka ngalokho , aze angene enkazimulweni yakhe na ? "
42024027	Wayesethathela kuMose nakubaprofethi bonke , wabachasisela emibhalweni okuqondene naye .
42024028	Base besondela emzaneni ababeya kuwo yena washaya sengathi udlulela phambili .
42024029	Bamncengisisa bathi : " Hlala nathi , ngokuba sekuzakuhlwa , nemini isiyadlula . " Wangena wahlala nabo .
42024030	Kwathi esehlezi nabo ekudleni , wathabatha isinkwa , wabonga , wasihlephula , wabanika .
42024031	Amehlo abo ayesevuleka , bamazi ; wayesenyamalala kubo .
42024032	Bathi omunye komunye : " Inhliziyo yethu ibingavuthi yini phakathi kwethu , lapho ekhuluma kithi endleleni , nalapho esivulela imibhalo , na ? "
42024033	Base besuka ngasona leso sikhathi , baphindela eJerusalema , bafumana abayishumi nanye nababe nabo behlangene ndawonye ,
42024034	bethi : " Impela iNkosi ivukile , ibonakele kuSimoni . "
42024035	Base belanda nabo okwenzekileyo endleleni , nokuthi yaziwa kanjani yibo ekuhlephuleni isinkwa .
42024036	Besakhuluma lokho , yena uqobo wema phakathi kwabo , wathi kubo : " Ukuthula makube kinina . "
42024037	Kepha bashaywa luvalo , besaba bethi babona ithongo .
42024038	Wayesethi kubo : " Nikhathazekeleni na ? Kuvelelani imizindlo ezinhliziyweni zenu na ?
42024039	Bhekani izandla zami nezinyawo zami ukuthi yimina uqobo ; ngiphatheni , nibone , ngokuba ithongo alinanyama namathambo , njengokuba ningibona nginakho . "
42024040	Esekushilo lokho wababonisa izandla nezinyawo .
42024041	Kepha bengakakholwa ngenxa yentokozo bemangala , wathi kubo : " Ninakho ukudla lapha na ? "
42024042	Bamnika iqatha lenhlanzi eyosiweyo neqa lezinyosi .
42024043	Wakuthatha , wadla phambi kwabo .
42024044	Wayesethi kubo : " Yiwo lawo mazwi ami engawakhuluma kini ngisenani okuthi : ‘ Kumelwe ukugcwaliseka konke okulotshwe ngami emthethweni kaMose , nakubaprofethi nasemaHutsheni . ’ "
42024045	Khona wayesevula ingqondo yabo , ukuze baqonde imibhalo .
42024046	Wathi kubo : " Kulotshiwe kanje ukuthi uzakuhlupheka uKristu , avuke kwabafileyo ngosuku lwesithathu ,
42024047	kushunyayelwe egameni lakhe ukuphenduka , kube ngukuthethelelwa kwezono ezizweni zonke , kuqalwe eJerusalema .
42024048	Nina-ke ningofakazi balezi zinto .
42024049	Bhekani , ngiyathumela kini isithembiso sikaBaba ; kepha hlalani emzini , nize nembathiswe amandla avela phezulu . "
42024050	Wabahola , baze bafika ngaseBethaniya , waphakamisa izandla zakhe , wababusisa .
42024051	Kwathi esababusisa , wahlukana nabo , wenyuselwa ezulwini .
42024052	Bakhuleka kuye , baphindela eJerusalema benokuthokoza okukhulu .
42024053	Babekhona ethempelini njalo bemdumisa uNkulunkulu .
43001001	Ekuqaleni wayekhona uLizwi , uLizwi wayekuNkulunkulu , uLizwi wayenguNkulunkulu .
43001002	Yena lowo wayekhona ekuqaleni kuNkulunkulu .
43001003	Konke kwavela ngaye ; ngaphandle kwakhe akuvelanga lutho kukho konke okuvelileyo .
43001004	Ukuphila kwakukuye , ukuphila kwakungukukhanya kwabantu ;
43001005	ukukhanya kukhanya ebumnyameni , kepha ubumnyama abukwamukelanga .
43001006	Kwavela umuntu ethunyiwe nguNkulunkulu , igama lakhe linguJohane .
43001007	Lowo wezela ubufakazi ukuba afakaze ngokukhanya , ukuze bonke bakholwe ngaye .
43001008	Yena wayengesikho ukukhanya , kepha wayengozofakaza ngokukhanya .
43001009	Kwakungukukhanya okuqinisileyo okukhanyisa wonke umuntu , okwase kuza ezweni .
43001010	Wayekhona ezweni , izwe lavela ngaye ; kepha izwe alimazanga .
43001011	Weza kokwakhe , abakhe abamamukelanga .
43001012	Kepha bonke abamamukelayo wabapha amandla okuba babe ngabantwana bakaNkulunkulu , labo abakholwa egameni lakhe ,
43001013	abangazalwanga ngagazi , nantando yenyama , nantando yendoda , kodwa bazalwa nguNkulunkulu .
43001014	ULizwi waba yinyama , wakha phakathi kwethu , sabona inkazimulo yakhe , inkazimulo njengeyozelwe yedwa kuYise , egcwele umusa neqiniso .
43001015	UJohane wafakaza ngaye , wamemeza wathi : " Nguyena lo ebengisho ngaye ukuthi : ‘ Lowo ozayo emva kwami uvelile ngaphambi kwami , ngokuba wayekhona kuqala kunami . ’ "
43001016	Ngokuba ekugcwaleni kwakhe samukele sonke umusa phezu komusa .
43001017	Ngokuba umthetho wanikezwa ngoMose , umusa neqiniso kwavela ngoJesu Kristu .
43001018	Akakho oke wabona uNkulunkulu ; iNdodana ezelwe yodwa esesifubeni sikaYise yiyona embonakalisile .
43001019	Lokhu kungubufakazi bukaJohane mhla abaJuda bethuma abapristi namaLevi bephuma eJerusalema ukuba bambuze ukuthi : " Wena ungubani na ? "
43001020	Wavuma , kaphikanga , wavuma wathi : " Angisiye uKristu mina . "

43001024	Labo ababethunyiwe babevela kubaFarisi .
43001025	Bambuza-ke , bathi kuye : " Pho , ubhapathizelani , uma ungesiye uKristu , no-Eliya , nomProfethi , na ? "
43001026	UJohane wabaphendula wathi : " Mina ngibhapathiza ngamanzi ; umi phakathi kwenu eningamaziyo :
43001027	yena ozayo emva kwami , omchilo wesicathulo sakhe ngingafanele ukuwuthukulula . "
43001028	Lokho kwenzeka eBethabara ngaphesheya kweJordani , lapho uJohane wayebhapathiza khona .
43001029	Ngangomuso wabona uJesu eza kuye , wathi : " Bheka , iWundlu likaNkulunkulu elisusa izono zezwe .
43001030	Nguye ebengisho ngaye , ngithi : ‘ Emva kwami kuza umuntu owavela ngaphambi kwami , ngokuba wayekhona kuqala kunami . ’
43001031	Nami bengingamazi ; kodwa ukuze abonakaliswe ku-Israyeli , ngalokho ngizile ngibhapathiza ngamanzi . "
43001032	UJohane wafakaza wathi : " Ngibonile uMoya ehla ezulwini njengejuba , wahlala phezu kwakhe .
43001033	Nami bengingamazi , kodwa owangithuma ukubhapathiza ngamanzi wathi kimi : ‘ Lowo oyakubona uMoya ehla ahlale phezu kwakhe , nguyena obhapathiza ngoMoya oNgcwele . ’
43001034	Mina ngibonile , ngafakaza ukuthi : Lo uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu . "

43001039	Wathi kubo : " Wozani nibone . " Ngakho-ke beza babona lapho ehlala khona ; bahlala naye ngalolo suku ; kwakungaba yihora leshumi .
43001040	Omunye walabo ababili abamuzwa uJohane balandela uJesu wayengu-Andreya umfowabo kaSimoni Petru ;
43001041	yena wafumana kuqala umfowabo uSimoni , wathi kuye : " Simfumene uMesiya , " okungukuthi ngokuhunyushwa uKristu .

43001044	UFiliphu wayengowaseBetsayida , umuzi ka-Andreya noPetru .

43002001	Kwathi ngosuku lwesithathu kwakukhona umshado eKhana laseGalile ; wayekhona lapho unina kaJesu .
43002002	NoJesu nabafundi bakhe babemenyiwe emshadweni .

43002005	Wathi unina ezincekwini : " Nayikuphi akusho kini anokwenza . "
43002006	Kwakukhona lapho izimbiza zamatshe eziyisithupha zibekwe ngesiko lokuhlamba labaJuda , ziphethe yileso naleso izilinganiso ezimbili noma ezintathu .
43002007	UJesu wathi ezincekwini : " Gcwalisani izimbiza ngamanzi ; " zazigcwalisa-ke .
43002008	Wayesethi kuzo : " Yikhani manje , niyise kumphathi wokudla ; " zayisa-ke .
43002009	Umphathi wokudla ezwa amanzi aphenduke iwayini , engazi ukuthi livelaphi , kepha izinceku ezaziwakhile amanzi bezazi , umphathi wokudla wabiza umyeni , wathi kuye :
43002010	" Wonke umuntu ubeka iwayini elimnandi kuqala , kuthi lapha sebephuze kakhulu , akhiphe elibi kunalo ; wena ugcinile elimnandi kuze kube manje . "
43002011	Lokho ukuqala kwezibonakaliso wakwenza uJesu eKhana laseGalile ebonakalisa inkazimulo yakhe ; abafundi bakhe bakholwa nguye .
43002012	Ngasemva kwalokho wehlela eKapernawume , yena , nonina , nabafowabo , nabafundi bakhe , bahlala khona izinsuku ezingeziningi .

43002014	Wafumana ethempelini abathengisa ngezinkomo nangezimvu nangamajuba , nabahlezi beshintsha imali .
43002015	Wayesenza inkalivasi ngezintambo , waxosha bonke ethempelini , nezimvu nezinkomo , wachitha imali yabashintshayo , wagumbuqela amatafula ,

43002021	Kepha wayekhuluma ngethempeli lomzimba wakhe .
43002022	Kuthe esevukile kwabafileyo , abafundi bakhe bakhumbula ukuthi washo njalo kubo ; bakholwa ngumbhalo nezwi abelishilo uJesu .

43003001	Kwakukhona umuntu wakubaFarisi , nguNikodemu igama lakhe , isikhulu sabaJuda .
43003002	Lowo-ke weza kuye ebusuku , wathi kuye : " Rabi , siyazi ukuthi ungumfundisi ovele kuNkulunkulu , ngokuba akakho ongenza lezi zibonakaliso ozenzayo , uma uNkulunkulu engenaye . "

43003006	Lokho okuzelwe yinyama kuyinyama ; nalokho okuzelwe nguMoya kungumoya .

43003009	UNikodemu waphendula , wathi kuye : " Lokhu kungenzeka kanjani na ? "

43003011	Ngiqinisile , ngiqinisile ngithi kuwe : Sikhuluma esikwaziyo , sifakaza ngesikubonileyo ; kepha anibamukeli ubufakazi bethu .
43003012	Nxa nginitshelile okomhlaba , kanakholwa ; ningakholwa kanjani , uma nginitshela okwasezulwini na ?
43003013	Akakho owenyukele ezulwini , kuphela yena owehla ezulwini , iNdodana yomuntu .
43003014	Njengokuba uMose waphakamisa inyoka ehlane , kanjalo iNdodana yomuntu imelwe ukuphakanyiswa
43003015	ukuba yilowo nalowo okholwa yiyo abe nokuphila okuphakade .
43003016	" Ngokuba uNkulunkulu walithanda izwe kangaka , waze wanikela ngeNdodana yakhe ezelwe yodwa ukuba yilowo nalowo okholwa yiyo angabhubhi , kodwa abe nokuphila okuphakade .
43003017	Ngokuba uNkulunkulu kayithumelanga iNdodana ezweni ukuba yahlulele izwe , kodwa ukuba izwe lisindiswe ngayo .

43003019	Ukwahlulela kuyilokhu ukuba ukukhanya kufikile ezweni , kepha abantu bathanda ubumnyama kunokukhanya , ngokuba imisebenzi yabo ibimibi .

43004001	Kwathi ukuba iNkosi yazi ukuthi abaFarisi bezwile ukuba uJesu wenza abafundi , ebhapathiza abaningi kunoJohane ,

43004004	Kwakuswelekile ukuba adabule iSamariya .

43004006	Wawukhona lapho umthombo kaJakobe . Ngakho uJesu ekhathele ukuhamba wayesehlala ngasemthonjeni . Kwakungaba yihora lesithupha .

43004023	Kodwa isikhathi siyeza , sesikhona namanje , lapho abakhulekayo abaqinisileyo beyakukhuleka kuBaba ngomoya nangeqiniso ; ngokuba uBaba ufuna abakhuleka kuye abanjalo .
43004024	UNkulunkulu unguMoya ; abakhuleka kuye bafanele ukukhuleka ngomoya nangeqiniso . "

43004027	Ngaleyo nkathi bafika abafundi bakhe ; bamangala ngokuba ekhuluma nowesifazane ; nokho akubangakho owathi : " Ufunani na ? " noma : " Ukhulumelani naye na ? "

43004030	Baphuma emzini , beza kuye .

43005001	Emva kwalokho kwakukhona umkhosi wabaJuda ; uJesu wakhuphukela eJerusalema .

43005025	Ngiqinisile , ngiqinisile ngithi kini : Isikhathi siyeza , sesikhona namanje , lapho abafileyo beyakulizwa izwi leNdodana kaNkulunkulu ; abezwayo bayakuphila .

43005029	abenze ukulunga baphumele ekuvukeni kokuphila , abenze okubi ekuvukeni kokulahlwa .
43005030	Mina ngingenze lutho ngokwami ; ngahlulela njengalokho engikuzwayo ; ukwahlulela kwami kulungile , ngokuba ngingafuni eyami intando kepha intando yongithumileyo .
43005031	" Uma ngizifakazela mina , ubufakazi bami abuqinisile .

43005037	NoBaba ongithumileyo ufakazile ngami . Anizange nizwe izwi lakhe , anisibonanga isimo sakhe .

43005047	Kodwa uma ningakholwa yimibhalo yakhe , niyakukholwa kanjani ngamazwi ami na ? "
43006001	Emva kwalokho uJesu wamuka waya phesheya kolwandle lwaseGalile olungolwaseTiberiya .

43006027	Ningasebenzeli ukudla okuphelayo kepha ukudla okuhlala kuze kube ngukuphila okuphakade , eyakunipha khona iNdodana yomuntu , ngokuba uYise uNkulunkulu ubekile uphawu kuyona . "

43006045	Kulotshiwe kubaprofethi ukuthi : ‘ Bonke bayakuba ngabafundiswe nguNkulunkulu . ’ Yilowo nalowo ozwile kuBaba , wafunda , uyeza kimi .

43006048	Mina ngiyisinkwa sokuphila .
43006049	Okhokho benu badla imana ehlane , bafa .
43006050	Lesi siyisinkwa esehla ezulwini ukuba umuntu adle kuso , angafi .

43006055	Ngokuba inyama yami ingukudla isibili , negazi lami lingukuphuza isibili .

43007028	Ngakho uJesu wamemeza efundisa ethempelini , wathi : " Niyangazi , niyazi futhi ukuthi ngivelaphi ; mina-ke angizizelanga , kodwa ongithumileyo uqinisile , eningamaziyo nina .

43007030	Ngakho bafuna ukumbamba , kepha akubangakho owambeka isandla , ngokuba isikhathi sakhe sasingakafiki .

43007035	Ngakho abaJuda bakhuluma bodwa , bathi : " Uzakuya ngaphi lo lapho singayikumthola na ? Uyakuya kwabahlakazekileyo kumaGreki , afundise amaGreki , na ?

43007051	" Konje umthetho wakithi uyamlahla yini umuntu ungakamuzwa kuqala , uze wazi akwenzayo , na ? "

43007053	Base behamba , kwaba yilowo nalowo waya ekhaya .
43008001	Khona uJesu waya eNtabeni Yeminqumo .

43008015	Nina nahlulela ngokwenyama , kepha mina angahluleli muntu .

43008017	Yebo , kulotshiwe nasemthethweni wakini ukuthi ubufakazi babantu ababili bungobuqinisileyo .

43008021	Khona waphinda wathi kubo : " Ngiyamuka mina , niyakungifuna , nifele ezonweni zenu ; lapho ngiya khona mina , ningeze nina . "

43008028	Wayesethi uJesu : " Nxa seniyiphakamisile iNdodana yomuntu , khona-ke nizakwazi ukuthi nginguye nokuthi angenzi lutho ngokwami , kodwa ngikhuluma lokhu njengokuba uBaba engifundisile .

43008033	Bamphendula bathi : " Siyinzalo ka-Abrahama thina , asibonange sibe yizigqila zamuntu ; wena usho kanjani ukuthi : ‘ Nizakuba ngabakhululekileyo ’ na ? "

43009001	Wathi edlula , wabona umuntu owayeyimpumputhe kwasekuzalweni kwakhe .

43010001	" Ngiqinisile , ngiqinisile ngithi kini : Ongangeni ngesango esibayeni sezimvu , kodwa ekhwela ngenye indawo , lowo uyisela nomphangi .
43010002	Kepha ongena ngesango ungumalusi wezimvu .
43010003	Umlindisango uyamvulela lowo ; nezimvu ziyalizwa izwi lakhe ; ubiza ezakhe izimvu ngamagama , aziholele phandle .

43010012	Okhokhelwayo engesiye umalusi , izimvu zingesizo ezakhe , ebona impisi iza , ushiya izimvu , abaleke — impisi izibhozomele , izihlakaze —

43010015	njengalokhu uBaba uyangazi , nami ngiyamazi uBaba ; ngidela ukuphila kwami ngenxa yezimvu .
43010016	Nezinye izimvu nginazo ezingesizo ezalesi sibaya ; nalezo ngimelwe ukuziletha ; ziyakuzwa izwi lami , kube mhlambi munye nomalusi munye .

43010018	Akakho ongangamuka ukuphila kwami , kodwa ngikudela ngokwami ; nginamandla okukudela , nginamandla okubuye ngikuthabathe . Lo myalo ngiwamukele kuBaba . "

43010034	UJesu wabaphendula wathi : " Akulotshiwe yini emthethweni wakini ukuthi : ‘ Ngithe : Ningonkulunkulu , ’ na ?

43010039	Base befuna futhi ukumbamba , kepha waphunyuka esandleni sabo .

43011001	Kwakukhona othile ogulayo , uLazaru waseBethaniya umuzi wakubo kaMariya nodadewabo uMarta .

43016001	" Lokho ngikukhulume kini ukuba ningakhubeki .

43016020	Ngiqinisile , ngiqinisile ngithi kini : Niyakukhala nilile nina , kepha izwe liyakujabula ; niyakuba lusizi nina , kepha usizi lwenu luyakuphendulwa lube ngukuthokoza .

43019014	Kwakungolokulungisela iPhasika kungathi ihora lesithupha . Wathi kubaJuda : " Bhekani inkosi yenu . "

43019016	Wayesemnikela kubo ukuba abethelwe esiphambanweni . Bamthatha-ke uJesu , bahamba naye .
43019017	Waphuma ezithwalele isiphambano , waya endaweni ethiwa iNdawo Yekhanda , ethiwa ngesiHeberu iGolgotha .
43019018	Bambethela khona nabanye ababili kanye naye ngalapha nangalapha , uJesu ephakathi .
43019019	Kepha uPilatu waloba isaziso , wasibeka esiphambanweni . Kwakulotshiwe ukuthi : UJESU WASENAZARETHA , INKOSI YABAJUDA .
43019020	Khona abaningi babaJuda bafunda leso saziso ; ngokuba indawo leyo , lapho uJesu wabethelwa khona esiphambanweni , yayiseduze nomuzi . Kwakulotshiwe ngesiHeberu , nangesiRoma , nangesiGreki .
43019021	Base bethi abapristi abakhulu babaJuda kuPilatu : " Ungalobi ukuthi : ‘ Inkosi yabaJuda , ’ kepha ukuba yena wathi : ‘ NgiyiNkosi yabaJuda . ’ "
43019022	UPilatu waphendula wathi : " Engikulobile ngikulobile . "
43019023	Kuthe amabutho esembethele uJesu esiphambanweni , athatha izingubo zakhe , azenza izabelo ezine , kwaba yilelo nalelo butho laba nesabelo , neyembe futhi . Kepha iyembe lalingenamthungo , lalukiwe lonke kusukela phezulu .
43019024	Ngakho-ke akhuluma odwa , athi : " Asingalidabuli , kodwa asilenzele inkatho yokuthi liyakuba ngelikabani , " ukuze kugcwaliseke umbhalo othi : " Babelana izingubo zami , benzelana inkatho ngesambatho sami . " Lokho-ke akwenza amabutho .
43019025	Kepha kwakumi ngasesiphambanweni sikaJesu unina kanye nodadewabo kanina , uMariya umkaKleyophase , noMariya Magdalena .
43019026	Kuthe uJesu ebona unina nomfundi amthandayo bemi ngakhona , wathi kunina : " Mame , bheka indodana yakho . "
43019027	Wayesethi kumfundi : " Bheka unyoko . " Kusukela kuleso sikhathi umfundi lowo wamyisa kwakhe .
43019028	Emva kwalokho uJesu , ekwazi ukuthi konke sekuphelelisiwe ukuba umbhalo ugcwaliseke , wathi : " Ngomile . "
43019029	Kwakubekiwe khona isitsha sigcwele uviniga ; khona bachoma ilula ligcwele uviniga othini lwehisopi , baliyisa emlonyeni wakhe .
43019030	Kwathi ukuba uJesu ewamukele uviniga , wathi : " Kufeziwe ; " wagebisa ikhanda , wafa .
43019031	Khona abaJuda , ngokuba kwakungolokulungisela , ukuze izidumbu zingahlali esiphambanweni ngesabatha , ngokuba lolo suku lwesabatha lwalulukhulu , banxusa uPilatu ukuba yaphulwe imilenze yabo , basuswe .
43019032	Ayeseza-ke amabutho , ayaphula imilenze yowokuqala neyomunye owayebethelwe naye .
43019033	Esefika kuJesu , ebona ukuthi usefile , kawayaphulanga imilenze yakhe ;
43019034	kodwa elinye lamabutho lamgwaza ohlangothini ngomkhonto , kwaphuma masinyane igazi namanzi .
43019035	Obonileyo ufakazile , ubufakazi bakhe buqinisile ; yena-ke uyazi ukuthi ukhuluma iqiniso , ukuze nikholwe nani .
43019036	Ngokuba lokho kwenzeka ukuba kugcwaliseke umbhalo othi : " Akuyikwaphulwa thambo lakhe . "
43019037	Futhi omunye umbhalo uthi : " Bayakumbheka abamgwazileyo . "
43019038	Emva kwalokho uJosefa wase-Arimatheya , engumfundi kaJesu kepha ekufihla ngokwesaba abaJuda , wacela kuPilatu ukuba asuse isidumbu sikaJesu ; uPilatu wavuma-ke . Wayesefika , wasisusa isidumbu sikaJesu .
43019039	Kweza noNikodemu owafika kuye kuqala ebusuku , waletha ixube lenhlaka nomhlaba kungathi amalitra ayikhulu .
43019040	Ngakho base besithatha isidumbu sikaJesu , basisonga ngezindwangu zelineni kanye namakha njengesiko labaJuda lokumbela .
43019041	Khona ngakuleyo ndawo , lapho wayebethelwe khona esiphambanweni , kwakukhona insimu , nasensimini kukhona ithuna elisha okwakungazange kubekwe muntu kulo .
43019042	Bambeka lapho-ke uJesu ngenxa yolokulungisela lwabaJuda , ngokuba ithuna laliseduze .
43020001	Kwathi ngosuku lokuqala lweviki uMariya Magdalena wafika ethuneni ekuseni kusemnyama , wabona itshe lisusiwe ethuneni .
43020002	Khona wayesegijima waya kuSimoni Petru nakulowo mfundi omunye uJesu amthandayo , wathi kubo : " Bayisusile iNkosi ethuneni , asazi lapha beyibeke khona . "
43020003	Ngakho wayesephuma uPetru nomunye umfundi , beza ethuneni .
43020004	Bagijima bobabili kanyekanye ; kepha umfundi omunye wagijima kakhulu kunoPetru , wafika kuqala ethuneni ;
43020005	elunguza wabona izindwangu zelineni zikhona , kepha akangenanga .
43020006	Khona wafika noSimoni Petru emlandela , wangena ethuneni , wabona izindwangu zelineni zikhona ,
43020007	neduku ebelisekhanda lakhe libekiwe lingekho ezindwangwini zelineni , kepha lisongwe lilodwa kwenye indawo .
43020008	Khona wayesengena nomfundi omunye ofike kuqala ethuneni , wabona , wakholwa ;
43020009	ngokuba bebengakawuqondi umbhalo wokuthi ubefanele ukuvuka kwabafileyo .
43020010	Base bemuka abafundi , baphindela kubo .
43020011	Kepha uMariya wema ethuneni ngaphandle ekhala ; esakhala walunguza ethuneni ;
43020012	wabona izingelosi ezimbili zembethe okumhlophe , zihlezi , enye ngasekhanda nenye ngasezinyaweni , lapho isidumbu sikaJesu besilele khona .
43020013	Zona-ke zathi kuye : " Mame , ukhalelani na ? " Wathi kuzo : " Bayithathile iNkosi yami , futhi angazi ukuthi bayibekephi . "
43020014	Eseshilo lokho waphenduka , wabona uJesu emi , kepha wayengazi ukuthi nguJesu .
43020015	UJesu wathi kuye : " Mame , ukhalelani na ? Ufuna bani na ? " Kepha yena ethi ngumphathi wensimu wathi kuye : " Nkosi , uma umsusile , ngitshele ukuthi umbekephi , ngiye ngiyakumthatha mina . "
43020016	UJesu wathi kuye : " Mariya ! " Waphenduka , wathi kuye ngesiHeberu : " Rabuni , " okungukuthi : " Mfundisi . "
43020017	UJesu wathi kuye : " Ungangithinti , ngokuba angikenyukeli kuBaba . Kepha yana kubazalwane bami , ubatshele ukuthi ngenyukela kuBaba noYihlo , kuNkulunkulu wami noNkulunkulu wenu . "
43020018	UMariya Magdalena weza wabikela abafundi ukuthi : " Ngiyibonile iNkosi , " nokuthi : " Ishilo lokho kimi . "
43020019	Kwathi-ke kusihlwa ngalolo suku , olokuqala lweviki , iminyango ivaliwe lapho abafundi bekhona ngokwesaba abaJuda , uJesu wafika wema phakathi kwabo , wathi kubo : " Ukuthula makube kinina . "
43020020	Eseshilo lokho wabakhombisa izandla nohlangothi lwakhe . Base bethokoza abafundi beyibona iNkosi .
43020021	Khona uJesu wabuye wathi kubo : " Ukuthula makube kinina . Njengokuba uBaba engithume mina , nami ngiyanithuma nina . "
43020022	Kwathi ukuba asho njalo , wabaphephetha , wathi kubo : " Yamukelani uMoya oNgcwele .
43020023	Enibathethelela izono zabo bathethelelwe ; nenibabamba ngazo babanjiwe . "
43020024	Kepha uTomase , omunye kwabayishumi nambili , othiwa uDidimu , wayengekho kubo mhla efika uJesu .
43020025	Ngakho-ke abanye abafundi bathi kuye : " Siyibonile iNkosi . " Kepha wathi kubo : " Uma ngingaboni ezandleni zayo inxeba lezipikili , ngifake umunwe wami enxebeni lezipikili , ngifake isandla sami ohlangothini lwayo , angisoze ngakholwa . "
43020026	Emva kwezinsuku eziyisishiyagalombili abafundi bakhe babesendlini futhi , uTomase enabo . UJesu wafika iminyango ivaliwe , wema phakathi kwabo , wathi : " Ukuthula makube kinina . "
43020027	Wayesethi kuTomase : " Zisa lapha umunwe wakho , ubone izandla zami ; zisa isandla sakho , usifake ohlangothini lwami ; ungabi ngongakholwayo kodwa okholwayo . "
43020028	UTomase waphendula , wathi kuye : " Nkosi yami , Nkulunkulu wami ! "
43020029	UJesu wathi kuye : " Ngokuba ungibonile , ukholiwe na ? Babusisiwe abakholwa bengabonanga . "
43020030	Izibonakaliso ezinye eziningi uJesu wazenza phambi kwabafundi bakhe , ezingalotshiwe kule ncwadi .
43020031	Kodwa lezi zilotshiwe ukuba nikholwe ukuthi uJesu unguKristu , iNdodana kaNkulunkulu , nokuba nikholwe , nibe nokuphila egameni lakhe .
43021001	Emva kwalokho uJesu wabuye wazibonakalisa kubafundi ngaselwandle lwaseTiberiya ; wazibonakalisa kanje :
43021002	kwakukhona ndawonye oSimoni Petru , noTomase othiwa uDidimu , noNathanayeli waseKhana laseGalile , nabakaZebedewu , nabanye ababili kubafundi bakhe .
43021003	USimoni Petru wathi kubo : " Ngiya kodoba . " Bathi kuye : " Nathi sihamba nawe . " Base bephuma , bangena emkhunjini ; kepha ngalobo busuku ababambanga lutho .
43021004	Kuthe sekusa , uJesu wayemi ogwini . Kepha abafundi babengazi ukuthi nguJesu .
43021005	UJesu wathi-ke kubo : " Bantwana , aninakho ukudla na ? " Bamphendula bathi : " Qha . "
43021006	Wayesethi kubo : " Phonsani inetha ngakwesokunene somkhumbi , nizakuthola . " Base bephonsa , ababe besaba namandla ukulidonsa ngenxa yobuningi bezinhlanzi .
43021007	Khona lowo mfundi uJesu amthandayo wathi kuPetru : " YiNkosi . " USimoni Petru , ekuzwa ukuthi yiNkosi , wagqoka , ngokuba wayehamba ze , waziphonsa elwandle .
43021008	Kepha abanye abafundi beza ngesikebhe , ngokuba bebengekude nenhlabathi kepha kungathi izingalo ezingamakhulu amabili , bedonsa inetha linezinhlanzi .
43021009	Kuthe sebephumele emhlabathini , babona umlilo wamalahle , nezinhlanzi zibekwe kuwo , nesinkwa .
43021010	UJesu wathi kubo : " Lethani izinhlanzi kwenizibambe manje . "
43021011	Wasuka uSimoni Petru , walihudulela emhlabathini inetha . Ligcwele izinhlanzi ezinkulu , ziyikhulu namashumi ayisihlanu nantathu ; noma zingako , inetha alidabukanga .
43021012	UJesu wathi kubo : " Wozani nidle . " Kepha akwabakho kubafundi owaba nesibindi sokumbuza ngokuthi : " Ungubani wena na ? " Bazi ukuthi yiyo iNkosi .
43021013	UJesu weza , wathabatha isinkwa , wabapha , nezinhlanzi futhi .
43021014	Lokho sekungokwesithathu uJesu ebonakaliswa kubafundi , esevukile kwabafileyo .
43021015	Khona sebedlile uJesu wathi kuSimoni Petru : " Simoni kaJona , uyangithanda kunalaba na ? " Wathi kuye : " Yebo , Nkosi , uyazi wena ukuthi ngiyakuthanda . " Wathi kuye : " Yipha amawundlu ami . "
43021016	Wabuye wathi kuye ngokwesibili : " Simoni kaJona , uyangithanda na ? " Wathi kuye : " Yebo , Nkosi , uyazi wena ukuthi ngiyakuthanda . " Wathi kuye : " Yalusa izimvu zami . "
43021017	Wathi kuye ngokwesithathu : " Simoni kaJona , uyangithanda na ? " UPetru wadabuka ngokuba wathi kuye ngokwesithathu : " Uyangithanda na ? " Wathi kuye : " Nkosi , wazi konke wena , uyazi ukuthi ngiyakuthanda . " UJesu wathi kuye : " Yipha izimvu zami .
43021018	Ngiqinisile , ngiqinisile ngithi kuwe : Usemusha wawugqoka , uhambe lapho uthanda khona ; kepha nxa usumdala , uyakwelula izandla zakho , omunye akugqokise , akuyise lapho ungathandi khona .
43021019	Kepha wakusho lokho ekhomba ukufa azakumdumisa uNkulunkulu ngakho . " Eseshilo lokho wathi : " Ngilandele . "
43021020	UPetru ephenduka wabona umfundi uJesu amthandayo elandela , oyena futhi wayencike esifubeni sakhe ekudleni , nowathi : " Nkosi , ngubani ozakukukhaphela na ? "
43021021	Kuthe uPetru embona lowo , wathi kuJesu : " Nkosi , kepha lona , pho ? "
43021022	UJesu wathi kuye : " Uma ngithanda ukuba ahlale ngize ngifike , kuyini kuwe na ? Wena landela mina . "
43021023	Ngakho-ke leli zwi laphumela kubazalwane lokuthi lowo mfundi akayikufa . Kanti uJesu akashongo ukuthi akayikufa kodwa ukuthi : " Uma ngithanda ukuba ahlale ngize ngifike , kuyini kuwe na ? "
43021024	Nguye lo mfundi ofakaza ngalezi zinto nokulobile lokhu ; siyazi ukuthi ubufakazi bakhe buqinisile .
43021025	Kukhona nezinye izinto eziningi azenza uJesu ; uma zilotshiwe zona ngazinye , ngithi nezwe lonke lingezanele izincwadi ezingalotshwa .
44001001	Incwadi yokuqala ngayiloba , Theyofilu , ngakho konke uJesu aqala ukukwenza nokukufundisa ,
44001002	kwaze kwaba lusuku akhushulwa ngalo , esebayalile ngoMoya oNgcwele abaphostoli ayebakhethile ;
44001003	waziveza kubo ephilile emva kokuhlupheka kwakhe ngobufakazi obuningi , wabonwa yibo izinsuku ezingamashumi amane ekhuluma ngezombuso kaNkulunkulu ;
44001004	kwathi ehlangene nabo , wabayala ngokuthi : " Ningamuki eJerusalema , kodwa nihlalele isithembiso sikaYise enasizwa ngami .
44001005	Ngokuba uJohane wayebhapathiza ngamanzi , kepha nina nizakubhapathizwa ngoMoya oNgcwele kungakadluli izinsuku eziningi . "
44001006	Khona labo ababebuthene bambuza bathi : " Nkosi , usawubuyisela umbuso ku-Israyeli ngalesi sikhathi na ? "
44001007	Wathi kubo : " Akusikho okwenu ukwazi izikhathi noma imizuzu uBaba akumisele ngamandla akhe ;
44001008	kodwa nizakwamukeliswa amandla , uMoya oNgcwele esefikile phezu kwenu , nibe ngofakazi bami eJerusalema , naseJudiya lonke , naseSamariya kuze kube sekugcineni komhlaba . "
44001009	Kwathi eseshilo lokho , wakhushulwa bebuka ; ifu lamsusa emehlweni abo .
44001010	Bathi besagqolozela ezulwini emuka , bheka , amadoda amabili ayemi kubo , embethe izingubo ezimhlophe ,
44001011	athi : " Madoda aseGalile , nimeleni nibheka ezulwini na ? UJesu lo , osuswe kini enyuselwa ezulwini , uyakuza kanjalo , njengalokho nimbonile eya ezulwini . "
44001012	Khona babuyela eJerusalema bevela entabeni ethiwa eyemiNqumo eseduze neJerusalema , ibanga lohambo lwesabatha .
44001013	Kwathi sebengenile , benyukela ekamelweni eliphezulu , lapho bebehlala khona : oPetru , noJohane , noJakobe , no-Andreya , noFiliphu , noTomase , noBartolomewu , noMathewu , noJakobe ka-Alfewu , noSimoni umZelothe , noJuda kaJakobe .
44001014	Bonke laba baqinisela nganhliziyonye ekukhulekeni kanye nabesifazane , noMariya unina kaJesu , nabafowabo .
44001015	Ngaleyo mihla uPetru wasukuma phakathi kwabazalwane , isixuku sabantu esasikhona ndawonye kwakungathi ikhulu namashumi amabili , wathi :
44001016	" Madoda , bazalwane , kwakumelwe ukuba kugcwaliseke umbhalo uMoya oNgcwele awukhulumayo ngaphambili ngomlomo kaDavide ngoJuda owayengumholi kulabo ababamba uJesu ,
44001017	ngokuba wayebalwe kanye nathi , wathola isabelo kule nkonzo . "
44001018	Lowo-ke wazuza insimu ngomvuzo wokungalungi , wawa ngekhanda , waqhuma phakathi , nezibilini zakhe zonke zachitheka ;
44001019	kwaziwa yibo bonke abakhileyo eJerusalema , yaze yaqanjwa leyo nsimu ngolimi lwakubo ngokuthi i-Akeldama , okungukuthi iNsimu Yegazi .
44001020	Ngokuba kulotshiwe eNcwadini yamaHubo ukuthi : ‘ Umuzi wakhe mawube yihlane , kungabikho ohlala kuwo , ’ nokuthi : ‘ Isikhundla sakhe asithathwe ngomunye . ’
44001021	" Ngakho kulawo madoda ayehamba nathi isikhathi sonke , lapho iNkosi uJesu ingena , iphuma phakathi kwethu ,
44001022	kuqalela embhapathizweni kaJohane kwaze kwaba lusuku akhushulwa ngalo kithi , kumelwe ukuba enye kuwo ibe ngufakazi kanye nathi ngokuvuka kwakhe . "
44001023	Base bemisa ababili , uJosefa othiwa uBarsaba , othiwa futhi uJustu , kanye noMathiya .
44001024	Base bekhuleka bethi : " Wena Nkosi , owazi izinhliziyo zabantu bonke , ake ukhombe omunye kulaba ababili omkhethileyo
44001025	ukuba athathe isikhundla sale nkonzo nobuphostoli aphambuka kuso uJuda ukuya endaweni yakhe . "
44001026	Base bebenzela inkatho ; yadla uMathiya ; wabalwa kanye nabaphostoli abayishumi nanye .
44002001	Kwathi sekufikile usuku lwePhentekoste , bonke babebuthene ndawonye .
44002002	Ngokungazelelwe kwavela ezulwini inhlokomo kwangathi eyokuvunguza komoya onamandla ; yona yagcwalisa indlu yonke ababehlezi kuyo .
44002003	Kwase kubonakala kubo izilimi ezahlukeneyo kungathi ezomlilo ; zahlala phezu kwalowo nalowo kubo .
44002004	Base begcwala bonke uMoya oNgcwele , baqala ukukhuluma ngezinye izilimi , njengalokho uMoya wabapha ukuphumisela .
44002005	Kepha kwakukhona abaJuda abakhile eJerusalema , amadoda akholwayo , evela ezizweni zonke eziphansi kwezulu ;
44002006	kwathi kuzwakele lowo mdumo , uquqaba lwabuthana , lwaphithiza , ngokuba kwaba yilowo nalowo wabezwa bekhuluma ngolimi lwakubo .
44002007	Bethuka , bamangala bathi : " Bheka , bonke laba abakhulumayo abasibo abaseGalile na ?
44002008	Yini , pho , ukuba sonke ngabanye sizwe ngolimi lwakithi esazalwa nalo na ?
44002009	AmaParte , namaMede , nama-Elamithi , nabakhile eMesopotamiya , naseJudiya , naseKhaphadosiya , nasePontu , nase-Asiya ,
44002010	naseFrigiya , nasePhamfiliya , naseGibithe , nasezweni laseLibiya ngaseKhurene , nezihambi zaseRoma ,
44002011	nabaJuda namaproselite , abaseKrethe nabase-Arabiya , siyabezwa bekhuluma ngezilimi zakithi ngemisebenzi emikhulu kaNkulunkulu . "
44002012	Bonke bamangala , basambatheka , bathi omunye komunye : " Kuthini lokhu na ? "
44002013	Kepha abanye bebabhuqa bathi : " Bagcwele iwayini elimnandi . "
44002014	Wayesesukuma uPetru nabayishumi nanye , waphakamisa izwi lakhe , waphumisela wathi kubo : " Madoda akwaJuda nani nonke enakhileyo eJerusalema , makwazeke lokhu kini , nibeke indlebe emazwini ami .
44002015	Ngokuba laba kabadakiwe njengokucabanga kwenu , lokhu kuseyihora lesithathu lemini ;
44002016	kodwa lokhu kuyikho okwakhulunywa ngomprofethi uJoweli ukuthi :
44002017	‘ Kuyakuthi ezinsukwini zokuphela , kusho uNkulunkulu , ngiyakuthulula uMoya wami phezu kwayo yonke inyama ; amadodana enu namadodakazi enu ayakuprofetha , izinsizwa zenu zibone imibono , abadala benu baphuphe amaphupho ;
44002018	yebo , naphezu kwezinceku zami nezincekukazi zami ngiyakuthulula uMoya wami ngaleyo mihla , ziyakuprofetha .
44002019	Ngiyakuveza izimangaliso ezulwini phezulu nezibonakaliso emhlabeni phansi , igazi , nomlilo , nokuthunqa komusi .
44002020	Ilanga liyakuphenduka ubumnyama , inyanga ibe yigazi , lungakafiki usuku olukhulu noluqhamileyo lweNkosi .
44002021	Kuyakuthi yilowo nalowo obiza igama leNkosi uyakusindiswa . ’
44002022	" Madoda akwa-Israyeli , zwanini lawa mazwi : UJesu waseNazaretha , indoda efakazelwe nguNkulunkulu phambi kwenu ngemisebenzi yamandla nangezimangaliso nangezibonakaliso uNkulunkulu azenza ngaye phakathi kwenu , njengalokhu nazi nina uqobo lwenu ,
44002023	yena lo , esenikelwe ngesu elimisiweyo nangokwaziphambili kukaNkulunkulu , nambethela ngezandla zabangenamthetho , nambulala ;
44002024	lowo uNkulunkulu wamvusa ethukulula iminjunju yokufa , lokhu kwakungenakwenzeka ukuba abanjwe yikho .
44002025	Ngokuba uDavide uthi ngaye : ‘ Ngayibona iNkosi phambi kwami njalo , ngokuba ingakwesokunene sami , ukuze nginganyakaziswa .
44002026	Ngalokho inhliziyo yami iyajabula , nolimi lwami luyethaba ; ngisho nenyama yami iyakuhlala ngokwethemba .
44002027	Ngokuba awuyikushiya umphefumulo wami eHayidese , futhi awuyikuvuma oNgcwele wakho abone ukubola .
44002028	Wangazisa izindlela zokuphila ; uyakungigcwalisa ngokujabula ebusweni bakho . ’
44002029	" Madoda , bazalwane , ake ngikhulume kini ngokusobala ngokhokho uDavide ukuthi wafa , nokuthi wembelwa , nokuthi ithuna lakhe lisekhona kithi nanamuhla .
44002030	Ngakho lokhu engumprofethi , ekwazi ukuthi uNkulunkulu wayefungile kuye ngesifungo ukuthi enzalweni yokhalo lwakhe uyakubeka omunye esihlalweni sakhe sobukhosi ,
44002031	ebona kuse phambili , wakhuluma ngokuvuka kukaKristu ukuthi akashiywanga eHayidese , nenyama yakhe ayibonanga ukubola .

44002041	Ngakho abalamukeleyo izwi lakhe babhapathizwa , kwenezelwa ngalowo muhla abantu kungathi izinkulungwane ezintathu .

44003001	UPetru noJohane bakhuphukela ethempelini ngehora lokukhuleka , elesishiyagalolunye .

44003003	Kwathi ukuba abone oPetru noJohane bezakungena ethempelini , wacela ukwabelwa isipho .

44007014	UJosefa wayesethumela wabiza uJakobe uyise nabakubo bonke , abantu abangamashumi ayisikhombisa nanhlanu .
44007015	UJakobe wehlela eGibithe ; wafa yena nawobaba .
44007016	Bayiswa eSikemi , babekwa ethuneni alithenga u-Abrahama ngenani lesiliva kumadodana kaHamori eSikemi .
44007017	" Kepha sesisondele isikhathi sesithembiso uNkulunkulu asisho ku-Abrahama , banda abantu , baba baningi eGibithe ,
44007018	kwaze kwavela enye inkosi eGibithe ebingamazi uJosefa .
44007019	Yona yasiphatha ngobuqili isizwe sakithi , yabahlupha obaba ngokubalahlisa izingane zabo zingaphili .
44007020	" Ngaleso sikhathi kwazalwa uMose , waba muhle kuNkulunkulu ; wondliwa izinyanga ezintathu endlini kayise ;
44007021	eselahliwe , indodakazi kaFaro yamthola , yazondlela yena ukuba abe yindodana yayo .
44007022	UMose wafundiswa ukuhlakanipha konke kwabaseGibithe ; waba namandla ngamazwi nangemisebenzi yakhe .
44007023	" Kuthe eseneminyaka engamashumi amane ezelwe , kwafika enhliziyweni yakhe ukuba abamele abafowabo , abantwana bakwa-Israyeli .
44007024	Wabona umuntu ephathwa kabi , wamvikela , wamphindisela ohlushwayo , wambulala owaseGibithe .
44007025	Ubethemba ukuthi abafowabo bayakuqonda ukuthi uNkulunkulu ubanika ukusindiswa ngesandla sakhe ; kepha abakuqondanga .
44007026	Nangangomuso wafika kubo belwa , wazama ukubalamula , babuyisane , wathi : ‘ Madoda , ningabazalwane ; niphathanelani kabi na ? ’
44007027	" Kepha lowo owayemona umakhelwane wakhe wamhlohloloza wathi : ‘ Ubekwe ngubani ube ngumbusi nomahluleli phezu kwethu na ?
44007028	Usufuna ukungibulala nami , njengalokho ubulele owaseGibithe izolo na ? ’
44007029	Khona uMose wabaleka ngenxa yalelo zwi , waba ngumfokazi ezweni lakwaMidiyani , lapho azala khona amadodana amabili .
44007030	" Kwathi sekuphelele iminyaka engamashumi amane , kwabonakala kuye ehlane lentaba yaseSinayi ingelosi iselangabini lomlilo esihlahleni .
44007031	UMose ekubona wamangala ngalowo mbono ; esasondela ukuba abhekisise , kwafika izwi leNkosi , lathi :
44007032	‘ NginguNkulunkulu wawoyihlo , uNkulunkulu ka-Abrahama noka-Isaka nokaJakobe . ’ UMose wathuthumela , akaba nasibindi sokubhekisisa .
44007033	" INkosi yayisithi kuye : ‘ Khumula izicathulo ezinyaweni zakho , ngokuba indawo omi kuyo ingumhlabathi ongcwele .
44007034	Ngikubonile nokukubona ukuhlushwa kwesizwe sami esiseGibithe , ngizwile ukububula kwaso ; sengehlile ukuba ngibakhiphe . Woza kalokhu , ngizakukuthumela eGibithe . ’
44007035	" UMose lowo abamalayo bethi : ‘ Ubekwe ngubani ube ngumbusi nomahluleli na ? ’ nguyena amthumayo uNkulunkulu ngesandla sengelosi eyabonakala kuye esihlahleni , abe ngumbusi nomhlengi .
44007036	Yena lowo wabakhipha enza izimangaliso nezibonakaliso ezweni laseGibithe , naseLwandle Olubomvu , nasehlane iminyaka engamashumi amane .
44007037	" Nguye uMose lowo owathi kubantwana bakwa-Israyeli : ‘ UNkulunkulu uyakunivusela umprofethi kubafowenu onjengami . ’
44007038	Nguye lowo owayesebandleni ehlane kanye nengelosi eyakhuluma naye entabeni yaseSinayi kanye nawobaba , nowamukela amazwi okuphila , ukuze aninike wona .
44007039	" Kepha obaba abavumanga ukumlalela , kodwa bamhlohloloza , babuyela emuva eGibithe ngezinhliziyo zabo ,
44007040	bathi ku-Aroni : ‘ Senzele onkulunkulu abazakuhamba phambi kwethu ; ngokuba uMose lowo owasikhipha ezweni laseGibithe , asazi ukuba wehlelwe yini . ’
44007041	Benza ithole ngaleyo mihla , baletha umhlatshelo esithombeni , bajabula ngemisebenzi yezandla zabo .
44007042	Kepha uNkulunkulu wabafulathela , wabadedela ukuba bakhonze ibandla lezulu , njengokuba kulotshiwe encwadini yabaprofethi ukuthi : ‘ Naningilethela iminikelo nemihlatshelo iminyaka engamashumi amane ehlane nina ndlu ka-Israyeli na ?
44007043	Qha , nathatha itende likaMoloki nenkanyezi kankulunkulu uRemfani , imifanekiso enayenza ukuba nikhuleke kuyo . Ngiyakunimukisela ngaphambili kweBabiloni . ’
44007044	" Kwakukhona itende lobufakazi kobaba ehlane njengalokho akuyalayo yena owakhuluma noMose ukuba alenze ngomfanekiso abewubonile ;
44007045	obaba benoJoshuwa balamukela , balingenisa ezweni lezizwe azixoshayo uNkulunkulu ebusweni bawobaba , kwaze kwaba semihleni kaDavide
44007046	owathola umusa ebusweni bukaNkulunkulu , wacela ukufunela uNkulunkulu kaJakobe idokodo .
44007047	Kepha nguSolomoni owamakhela indlu .
44007048	" Kodwa oPhezukonke akahlali ezindlini ezenziwe ngezandla njengokusho komprofethi ukuthi :
44007049	‘ Izulu liyisihlalo sami sobukhosi , nomhlaba uyisenabelo sezinyawo zami ; ngenjani indlu eniyakungakhela yona , ’ isho iNkosi , ‘ noma yiyiphi indawo yami yokuphumula na ?
44007050	Isandla sami asikwenzanga konke lokho na ? ’
44007051	" Nina bantamo zilukhuni , abangasokile ezinhliziyweni nasezindlebeni , nimelana njalo noMoya oNgcwele ; njengoyihlo ninjalo nani .
44007052	Ngumuphi kubaprofethi oyihlo abangamzingelanga na ? Bababulala ababememezela ngaphambili ukuza koLungileyo , eseningabakhapheli nababulali bakhe ,
44007053	nina enamukela umthetho ngokuyala kwezingelosi , kepha aniwugcinanga . "
44007054	Kwathi bekuzwa lokho , bahlabeka ezinhliziyweni , bamgugudela amazinyo .
44007055	Kepha yena egcwele uMoya oNgcwele wagqolozela ezulwini , wabona inkazimulo kaNkulunkulu , noJesu emi ngakwesokunene sikaNkulunkulu ,
44007056	wathi : " Bheka , ngibona izulu livuliwe , neNdodana yomuntu imi ngakwesokunene sikaNkulunkulu . "
44007057	Base bekhamuluka ngezwi elikhulu , bavala izindlebe , batheleka kuye kanyekanye ,
44007058	bamkhiphela ngaphandle komuzi , bamkhanda ngamatshe . Ofakazi babeka izingubo zabo ngasezinyaweni zensizwa egama layo linguSawulu .
44007059	UStefanu bamkhanda ngamatshe ekhuleka ethi : " Nkosi Jesu , yamukela umoya wami . "
44007060	Wayeseguqa phansi , wamemeza ngezwi elikhulu , wathi : " Nkosi , ungababaleli lesi sono . " Eseshilo lokho walala ubuthongo .
44008001	Kepha uSawulu wayevumelene nabo ngokubulawa kwakhe . Ngalolo suku kwavela ukuzingelwa okukhulu kwebandla laseJerusalema ; bahlakazeka bonke emazweni aseJudiya naseSamariya ; kwasala abaphostoli bodwa .
44008002	Amadoda akholwayo ammbela uStefanu , amkhalela isililo esikhulu .
44008003	Kepha uSawulu walichitha ibandla , engena ezindlini ngezindlu , ehudula abesilisa nabesifazane , wabafaka etilongweni .
44008004	Abahlakazekileyo base behamba , beshumayela izwi levangeli .
44008005	UFiliphu wehlela emzini waseSamariya , wabashumayeza uKristu .
44008006	Izixuku zalalela nganhliziyonye okwakhulunywa nguFiliphu , zizwa , zibona izibonakaliso azenzayo .
44008007	Ngokuba kwaphuma omoya abangcolileyo kwabaningi abakhwelwa yibo , bememeza ngezwi elikhulu ; nabaningi abafe uhlangothi nabayizinyonga baphulukiswa ;
44008008	kwaba khona ukuthokoza okukhulu kulowo muzi .
44008009	Kepha kwakukhona indoda ethile , nguSimoni igama layo , eyayikade yenza imilingo kulowo muzi , isimangalisa isizwe saseSamariya , izishaya umuntu omkhulu ;
44008010	banamathela kuye bonke kusukela kwabancinyane kuze kube kwabakhulu , bethi : " Lo ungamandla kaNkulunkulu abizwa ngokuthi Makhulu ; "

44008012	Kepha bathi ukuba bakholwe nguFiliphu eshumayela ivangeli ngombuso kaNkulunkulu nangegama likaJesu Kristu , babhapathizwa abesilisa nabesifazane .
44008013	Naye uSimoni wakholwa ; wathi esebhapathiziwe , wanamathela kuFiliphu , wamangala ebona izibonakaliso nemisebenzi emikhulu yamandla eyenziwayo .
44008014	Kwathi ukuba abaphostoli baseJerusalema bezwe ukuthi iSamariya lilamukele izwi likaNkulunkulu , bathumela kubo oPetru noJohane ;
44008015	sebehlele khona babakhulekela ukuba bamukele uMoya oNgcwele ,

44008017	Khona babeka izandla phezu kwabo ; base bamukela-ke uMoya oNgcwele .

44008020	Kepha uPetru wathi kuye : " Isiliva lakho malibhubhe kanye nawe , ngokuba uthi isipho sikaNkulunkulu singathengwa ngemali .
44008021	Awunasabelo nalifa kuleli zwi , ngokuba inhliziyo yakho ayilungile phambi kukaNkulunkulu .
44008022	Ngakho-ke phenduka kulobu bubi bakho , unxuse eNkosini , ingabe ungathethelelwa yini isizindlo senhliziyo yakho ,
44008023	ngokuba ngiyabona ukuthi usenyongweni ebabayo nasekuboshweni kokubi . "
44008024	USimoni wayesephendula ethi : " Nginxuseleni nina eNkosini , ukuze kungehleli lutho kimi lwalokho enikushiloyo . "
44008025	Kuthe sebefakazile , belikhulumile izwi leNkosi , babuyela eJerusalema , bashumayela ivangeli emizaneni eminingi yabaseSamariya .
44008026	Kepha ingelosi yeNkosi yakhuluma kuFiliphu , yathi : " Suka uye ngaseningizimu endleleni ephuma eJerusalema ehlela eGaza ; yona iyihlane . "
44008027	Wayesesuka wahamba . Bheka , nansi indoda yase-Etiyopiya , umthenwa , isikhulu sikaKhandakhe inkosikazi yase-Etiyopiya , ebiphezu kwengcebo yayo yonke , ebifikile eJerusalema izakukhuleka ;
44008028	ibisibuya , ihlezi enqoleni yayo , ifunda umprofethi u-Isaya .
44008029	UMoya wathi kuFiliphu : " Sondela , unamathele kuleyo nqola . "
44008030	UFiliphu wayesegijimela kuyo , wayizwa ifunda umprofethi u-Isaya , wathi : " Uyakuqonda kambe lokhu okufundayo na ? "
44008031	Yona yathi : " Ngingakwazi kanjani , uma kungekho ongiholayo na ? " Yamnxusa uFiliphu ukuba akhwele ahlale nayo .
44008032	Kepha isahlukwana sombhalo ebisifunda yilesi esithi : " Wayiswa ekuhlatshweni njengemvu ; njengewundlu elithule phambi komgundi walo kanjalo kawuvulanga umlomo wakhe .
44008033	Ekuthobeleni kwakhe ukwahlulelwa kwakhe kwasuswa . Ngubani ongalanda ngesizukulwane sakhe na ? Ngokuba ukuphila kwakhe kuyasuswa emhlabeni . "
44008034	Kepha umthenwa wathatha wathi kuFiliphu : " Ngiyacela , umprofethi ukhuluma lokho ngobani na ? Uzisho yena noma omunye na ? "
44008035	UFiliphu wavula umlomo wakhe , eqala kulowo mbhalo washumayela ivangeli ngoJesu .
44008036	Kwathi besahamba endleleni , bafika emanzini . Umthenwa wathi : " Bheka , nanka amanzi ; kwalani ukuba ngibhapathizwe na ? "

44008038	Wayala ukuba inqola ime . Behlela emanzini bobabili , uFiliphu nomthenwa ; wambhapathiza .

44008040	Kepha uFiliphu wafunyanwa e-Azotu , wahamba eshumayela ivangeli kuyo yonke imizi , waze wafika eKesariya .
44009001	Kepha uSawulu esafutha ngokusongela nokubulala abafundi beNkosi , waya kumpristi omkhulu ,

44009011	INkosi yayisithi kuye : " Suka uye esitaladini esithiwa Siqondile , ufune endlini kaJuda umuntu ogama lakhe linguSawulu waseTarsu ; ngokuba bheka , uyakhuleka ;

44009016	ngokuba mina ngizakumbonisa konke amelwe ukuhlushwa ngakho ngenxa yegama lami . "
44009017	Khona wahamba u-Ananiya , wangena endlini , wabeka izandla phezu kwakhe , wathi : " Sawulu umzalwane , iNkosi uJesu eyabonakala kuwe endleleni oze ngayo , ingithumile ukuba ubuye ubone , ugcwaliswe ngoMoya oNgcwele . "
44009018	Kwawa masinyane emehlweni akhe kwangathi inkwethu , wabona , wasukuma , wabhapathizwa ;

44009021	Kepha bamangala bonke abezwayo , bathi : " Lo asiye yini owachitha eJerusalema abakhuleka kulelo gama , nalapha uze ngalokhu ukuba abaqhube beboshiwe kubapristi abakhulu na ? "
44009022	Kodwa uSawulu wakhula kakhulu emandleni , wahlula abaJuda abakhileyo eDamaseku eqinisa ukuthi lowo unguKristu .
44009023	Sekudlule izinsuku eziningi , abaJuda benza icebo lokuba bambulale .

44009031	Njalo-ke ibandla laba nokuthula kulo lonke laseJudiya , naseGalile , naseSamariya , lakheka , lihamba ekwesabeni iNkosi , landa ngenduduzo kaMoya oNgcwele .
44009032	Kwathi uPetru ehambela izindawo zonke , wehlela nakwabangcwele abakhe eLida .

44009036	EJopha kwakukhona umfundikazi othile ogama lakhe linguThabitha , okungukuthi uDorka ngokuhunyushwa ; yena wayenemisebenzi eminingi emihle nokwabela abampofu izipho .

44009039	Wayesesuka uPetru , wahamba nabo . Esefikile , bamyisa ekamelweni eliphezulu ; abafelokazi bonke beza kuye bekhala , bembonisa izambatho nezingubo abezenzile uDorka esenabo .

44009041	Yena wambamba ngesandla , wamsukumisa . Wayesebiza abangcwele nabafelokazi , wambeka phambi kwabo ephilile .
44009042	Kwezwakala lokho kulo lonke iJopha ; abaningi bakholwa yiNkosi .
44009043	Wayesehlala izinsuku eziningi eJopha kwaSimoni umshuki .
44010001	Kwakukhona eKesariya indoda ethile egama layo linguKorneliyu , eyinduna yekhulu yebutho elithiwa elase-Italiya ;
44010002	wayengumuntu okholwayo nowesaba uNkulunkulu kanye nendlu yakhe yonke , abela abantu abampofu izipho eziningi , ekhuleka kuNkulunkulu njalonjalo .

44010006	yena ungenisile kwaSimoni othile , umshuki , ondlu yakhe ingaselwandle . "

44010022	Bathi : " UKorneliyu induna yekhulu , indoda elungileyo nemesabayo uNkulunkulu , efakazelwa kahle esizweni sonke sabaJuda , uyaliwe yingelosi engcwele ukuba akubizele endlini yakhe , ezwe amazwi kuwe . "
44010023	Wayesebabiza , wabangenisa . Ngangomuso wasuka wahamba nabo , abathile babazalwane baseJopha bamphelekezela .
44010024	Ngangomuso bangena eKesariya . UKorneliyu wayebalindele esebizile izihlobo nabangane bakhe abakhulu .

44010048	Wayeseyala ukuba babhapathizwe egameni leNkosi . Base bemncenga ukuba ahlale izinsuku ezithile .

44013052	Abafundi bagcwala intokozo noMoya oNgcwele .
44014001	Kwathi e-Ikoniyu bangena kanyekanye esinagogeni labaJuda , bakhuluma kwaze kwakholwa isixuku esikhulu sabaJuda namaGreki .

44014003	Nokho bahlala isikhathi eside , befundisa ngesibindi ngeNkosi eyafakazela izwi lomusa wayo , ibanika ukuba kwenziwe izibonakaliso nezimangaliso ngezandla zabo .

44014009	Yona yamuzwa uPawulu ekhuluma . Yena eyigqolozela wabona ukuthi inokukholwa kokuba iphiliswe ,
44014010	wathi ngezwi elikhulu : " Sukuma , ume ngezinyawo zakho . " Yayisigxuma , yahamba .

44018016	Wayesebaxosha esihlalweni sokwahlulela .

44018018	Kepha uPawulu esehlale khona izinsuku eziningi , wavalelisa kubazalwane , wamuka ngomkhumbi , waya eSiriya kanye noPrisila no-Akwila , esegundile ikhanda lakhe eKenikreya ; ngokuba wayezibophe ngesifungo .
44018019	Wehlela e-Efesu , wabashiya khona ; kepha yena wangena esinagogeni , washumayela kubaJuda .
44018020	Kwathi bemncenga ukuba ahlale khona isikhathi esidana , akaze avuma ,
44018021	kepha wavalelisa wathi : " Ngizakubuyela futhi kini , uma uNkulunkulu evuma ; " wayesesuka e-Efesu ngomkhumbi ;

44018023	Esehlale khona isikhathi esithile wamuka wadabula izwe laseGalathiya nelaseFrigiya ngokulandelana , eqinisa bonke abafundi .
44018024	UmJuda othile ogama lakhe lingu-Apholo , wase-Aleksandriya ngokuzalwa , indoda efundileyo nenamandla emibhalweni , wehlela e-Efesu .
44018025	Yena wayefundisiwe indlela yeNkosi ; evutha emoyeni wakhuluma , wafundisa ngesineke izindaba eziqondene noJesu , azi ukubhapathiza kukaJohane kuphela ;
44018026	yena waqala ukushumayela ngesibindi esinagogeni . Kwathi ukuba bamuzwe o-Akwila noPrisila , bamthatha bamchasisela indlela kaNkulunkulu ngesineke esikhulu .
44018027	Esethanda ukudlulela e-Akhaya , abazalwane balobela abafundi bebayala ukuba bamamukele ; esefikile wabasiza kakhulu abakholwayo ngomusa ,
44018028	ngokuba waphikisa abaJuda ngamandla phambi kwabantu , ekhomba ngemibhalo ukuthi uJesu unguKristu .
44019001	Kwathi u-Apholo eseKorinte , uPawulu wafika e-Efesu esedabulile amazwe angasenhla , wafumana abafundi abathile ,
44019002	wathi : " Namamukela yini uMoya oNgcwele mhla nikholwayo na ? " Bathi kuye : " Qhabo , asizwanga nokuzwa ukuba kukhona uMoya oNgcwele . "
44019003	Wathi : " Pho , nabhapathizelwa kukuphi na ? " Base bethi : " Kukho ukubhapathiza kukaJohane . "
44019004	UPawulu wayesethi : " UJohane wabhapathiza umbhapathizo wokuphenduka , ethi kubantu mabakholwe nguyena obezakuza emva kwakhe , kungukuthi uJesu . "
44019005	Bathi ukuzwa lokho , babhapathizwa egameni leNkosi uJesu .
44019006	Kwathi uPawulu esebekile izandla phezu kwabo , uMoya oNgcwele wehlela phezu kwabo ; base bekhuluma ngezilimi , baprofetha .

44019008	Wayesengena esinagogeni , wakhuluma ngesibindi izinyanga zaba ntathu , eshumayela ebafundisa ngombuso kaNkulunkulu .
44019009	Kepha lapho abathile bezenza lukhuni bengalaleli , bekhuluma kabi ngaleyo Ndlela phambi kwabantu , wasuka kubo , waqembula abafundi , washumayela imihla ngemihla esikoleni sikaTiranu .
44019010	Lokho kwenzeka iminyaka emibili , baze balizwa izwi leNkosi bonke abakhileyo e-Asiya , abaJuda namaGreki .
44019011	UNkulunkulu wenza imisebenzi yamandla engavamile ngezandla zikaPawulu ,
44019012	baze bathatha amaduku nezindwangu emzimbeni wakhe , bazibeka phezu kwabagulayo ; zase zisuka kubo izifo , nomoya ababi baphuma .

44019014	USkeva othile , umJuda , umpristi omkhulu , wayenamadodana ayisikhombisa ayekwenza lokho .

44019016	Lowo muntu onomoya omubi wabadumela , wahlula ababili , wabanqoba , baze baphunyuka kuleyo ndlu behambaze , belimele .

44019020	Kanjalo izwi landa ngamandla eNkosi , lanqoba .
44019021	Kwathi ukuba sezenzekile lezo zinto , uPawulu wazimisela emoyeni ukuya eJerusalema esedabulile iMakedoniya ne-Akhaya , wathi : " Emva kokufika kwami khona ngimelwe ukubona neRoma . "

44019024	Ngokuba umuntu othile ogama lakhe linguDemetriyu , umkhandi wesiliva owenza amathempelana esiliva kaDiyana , wazuzisa abakhandi besiliva inzuzo engencane ,

44019029	Umuzi wonke wagcwala isiphithiphithi , batheleka nganhliziyonye esigcawini sokubukela , babamba oGayu no-Aristarku , abaseMakedoniya , ababehamba noPawulu .
44019030	Kepha uPawulu esefuna ukungena phakathi kwabantu , abafundi abamvumelanga .
44019031	Nabanye bababusi base-Asiya , bengabahlobo bakhe , bathumela kuye , bamncenga ukuba angaze angena esigcawini sokubukela .

44026030	Inkosi yayisisukuma nombusi noBernike kanye nababehlezi nabo ;
