44026032	Kepha u-Agripha wathi kuFestu : " Lo muntu ngabe ekhululiwe , uma ebengalidluliselanga kuKesari . "
44027001	Kwathi sekunqunyiwe ukuba siye e-Italiya ngomkhumbi , banikela uPawulu nezinye iziboshwa ezithile enduneni yekhulu , igama layo linguJuliyu , eyebutho likaKesari .
44027002	Sangena emkhunjini wase-Adramitiyu obusuzakuya ezindaweni zangase-Asiya , u-Aristarku umMakedoniya waseThesalonika enathi .
44027003	Ngangomuso safika eSidoni ; uJuliyu wamphatha kahle uPawulu , wamvumela ukuba aye kubahlobo bakhe , ahlunyelelwe .
44027004	Sasuka lapho , sagudla ngenzansi kweKhupro , ngokuba imimoya yayiphambene nathi .
44027005	Sesidabulile ulwandle olungaseKhilikhiya nePhamfiliya safika eMira laseLikhiya .
44027006	Lapho-ke induna yafumana umkhumbi wase-Aleksandriya oqonde e-Italiya , yasingenisa kuwo .
44027007	Sesihambe kancane izinsuku eziningi saze safika kalukhuni ngaseKinidu , umoya ungasivumeli , sagudla iKrethe maqondana neSalimone ,
44027008	sagudla lona kalukhuni , safika endaweni ethile ethiwa Matheku Mahle ; eduze nayo kukhona umuzi waseLaseya .
44027009	Kwathi sekudlulile isikhathi eside , sekuyingozi ukuhamba ngomkhumbi , ngokuba isikhathi seNzilo sase sidlulile , uPawulu wabaluleka ,
44027010	wathi kubo : " Madoda , ngiyabona ukuthi lolu hambo luzakuba nengozi nokuchithakala okukhulu , kungabi ngokwempahla nokomkhumbi kuphela kepha nokokuphila kwethu . "
44027011	Kepha induna yekhulu yethemba umshayeli womkhumbi nomniniwo kakhulu kunalokho okwakhulunywa nguPawulu .
44027012	Njengokuba itheku lalingalungile ukuhlala khona ebusika , iningi labo laluleka ukuba kusukwe khona , mhlawumbe kwenzeke ukuba bafinyelele eFeniksi , itheku laseKrethe elibheke entshonalanga yaseningizimu nasentshonalanga yasenyakatho , bahlale khona ebusika .
44027013	Kuthe iningizimu isaphephetha kahle , bacabanga ukuthi sebetholile ababekuqondile , bakhuphula ihange , bagudla iKrethe .
44027014	Kepha emva kwesikhathi esingeside kwavuka kwehla kulo umoya oyisivunguvungu othiwa i-Ewurakiloni ;
44027015	kodwa umkhumbi usududulwa ungasenakubhekana nomoya , sayeka saqhutshwa nje .
44027016	Kwathi sigudla ngenzansi kwesiqhingana esithiwa iKlawuda , sabamba isikebhe kalukhuni ;
44027017	sebe sikhuphulile basebenzisa izinto zokusiza , bawuzongolozela umkhumbi ngezintambo ; kuthe besaba ukuthi bazakukhahleleka eSirti , behlisa izindwangu zomkhumbi , baqhutshwa kanjalo .
44027018	Kuthe ukuba sibhengulwe kakhulu yisiphepho , ngangomuso bachitha umthwalo ;
44027019	kwathi ngolwesithathu balahla izimpahla zomkhumbi ngezandla zabo .
44027020	Khona-ke ilanga nezinkanyezi zingasabonakali izinsuku eziningi , nesiphepho esingesincane siqinisa njalo , lase liphela ithemba lonke lokuba singasindiswa .
44027021	Sekuyisikhathi eside bengasadli lutho , uPawulu wasukuma phakathi kwabo , wathi : " Madoda , ngabe nalalela mina , kanamuka eKrethe , naphepha kule ngozi nakulokhu kuchithakala .
44027022	Kepha manje senginiluleka ukuba nime isibindi , ngokuba akuyikufa muntu kini , umkhumbi kuphela .
44027023	Ngokuba ngalobu busuku bekumi ngakimi ingelosi kaNkulunkulu engingowakhe nengimkhonzayo ,
44027024	yathi : ‘ Ungesabi , Pawulu ; umelwe ukuma phambi kukaKesari ; bheka , uNkulunkulu ukuphile bonke abahamba nawe emkhunjini . ’
44027025	Ngalokho yimani isibindi , madoda ; ngokuba ngiyakholwa nguNkulunkulu ukuthi kuzakuba njengalokho kukhulunyiwe kimi .
44027026	Kepha simelwe ukukhahleleka esiqhingini esithile . "
44027027	Kwathi ukuba kufike ubusuku beshumi nane sisazulazuliswa elwandle lwase-Adriya phakathi kobusuku , abomkhumbi bacabanga ukuthi bayasondela ezweni elithile .
44027028	Base bephonsa intambo yokulinganisa , bafumana kungamafatome angamashumi amabili ; sebeqhubekile kancane bayiphonsa futhi , bafumana kungamafatome ayishumi nanhlanu ;
44027029	besaba ukuthi mhlawumbe singashayeka ezindaweni ezinamadwala , baphonsa amahange amane ngasemuva , bafisa ukuba kuse .
44027030	Abomkhumbi sebefuna ukubaleka emkhunjini , behlisela isikebhe elwandle ngokungathi bazakuphonsa amahange enhlokweni yomkhumbi ,
44027031	uPawulu wathi enduneni yekhulu nasemabuthweni : " Uma laba bengahlali emkhunjini , ningesindiswe nina . "
44027032	Khona amabutho anquma amagoda esikebhe , asidedela sawa .
44027033	Kwathi sekuzakusa , uPawulu wabancenga bonke ukuba badle , wathi : " Namuhla kulusuku lweshumi nane nilindile , nihlezi nizila , ningadli lutho .
44027034	Ngalokho ngiyanincenga ukuba nidle , ngokuba lokhu kungokokusinda kwenu ; akuyikulahleka unwele lwekhanda nakoyedwa phakathi kwenu . "
44027035	Eseshilo lokho wathatha isinkwa , wabonga uNkulunkulu phambi kwabo bonke , wasihlephula , waqala ukudla .
44027036	Base bema isibindi bonke , badla nabo .
44027037	Thina sonke esasisemkhunjini besingabantu abangamakhulu amabili namashumi ayisikhombisa nesithupha .
44027038	Sebesuthi ukudla benza lula umkhumbi belahla ukolweni elwandle .
44027039	Sekusile , abalazanga izwe , kepha babona itheku elithile elinesihlabathi abanquma ukuba baqhubele kulo umkhumbi , uma kungenzeka .
44027040	Banquma amahange bawashiya elwandle , bathukulula futhi izintambo zamaphini okuqondisa , baphakamisela emoyeni indwangu ephambili , baqonda ogwini .
44027041	Batheleka endaweni enolwandle nxazombili , baqhubela umkhumbi kuyo , inhloko yomkhumbi yagxumekeka , yema ingenakunyakaziswa , kepha ingasemuva laphulwa ngamandla amaza .
44027042	Kepha amabutho ayehlosa ukubulala iziboshwa , funa ezinye zibaleke ngokuhlamba ;
44027043	kepha induna yekhulu ithanda ukusindisa uPawulu yawavimbela enhlosweni yawo , yayala ukuba labo abakwazi ukuhlamba baziphonse kuqala emanzini , bafike emhlabathini ,
44027044	nabaseleyo bafike , abanye ngamapulangwe , abanye ngezinye izinto zomkhumbi . Kanjalo-ke kwenzeka ukuba bonke baphumele emhlabathini besindile .
44028001	Kwathi sesisindile khona , sezwa ukuthi isiqhingi sithiwa iMelitha .
44028002	Abantu bakhona basiphatha ngobubele obungavamile , ngokuba babebasa umlilo , basamukela sonke ngenxa yemvula eyayisina nangenxa yamakhaza .
44028003	Kepha uPawulu ecakashile ixha lezinsaba , elibeka emlilweni , kwaphuma inyoka ngenxa yokushisa , yanamathela esandleni sakhe .
44028004	Abantu bakhona sebebona isilwane silenga esandleni sakhe , bakhuluma bodwa , bathi : " Ngempela lo muntu ungumbulali othi noma esindile elwandle ukuLunga akuvumi ukuba aphile . "
44028005	Kodwa yena wasinikinela isilwane emlilweni , akaze alimala .
44028006	Kepha babheka ukuthi usezakuvuvuka , nokuba awe phansi masinyane , afe . Kepha sebebheka isikhathi eside , bebona ukuthi akafikelwa ngozi , baphenduka bathi ungunkulunkulu .
44028007	Kwakukhona kuleyo ndawo izwe lesikhulu sesiqhingi , igama laso linguPhubiliyu ; yena wasamukela , wasiphatha kahle izinsuku ezintathu .
44028008	Kepha uyise kaPhubiliyu wayelele phansi ephethwe ngumkhuhlane nembo ; uPawulu wangena kuye , wakhuleka , wabeka izandla phezu kwakhe , wamphilisa .
44028009	Kwathi lokho sekwenzekile , beza nabanye abasesiqhingini abanezifo , baphulukiswa ,
44028010	basitusa ngokutusa okuningi ; kwathi mhla simuka ngomkhumbi , basinika esikudingayo .
44028011	Emva kwezinyanga ezintathu sase simuka ngomkhumbi wase-Aleksandriya owawudlulisa ubusika esiqhingini , uphawu lwawo lungolwamaWele .
44028012	Sangena eSirakhuse , sahlala izinsuku ezintathu ;
44028013	sasuka lapho , sagwegwesa , safika eRegiyu . Sekudlule usuku lwaba lunye , kwavuka iningizimu , safika ePhutheyoli ngosuku lwesibili .
44028014	Safumana khona abazalwane , sancengwa ukuba sihlale nabo izinsuku eziyisikhombisa ; kanjalo safika eRoma .
44028015	Abazalwame sebezwile ngathi basuka khona , beza ukusihlangabeza baze bafika e-Aphiyo Foru naseTresi Thaberne ; uPawulu ebabona wabonga uNkulunkulu , wema isibindi .
44028016	Sesifikile eRoma , uPawulu wavunyelwa ukuhlala yedwa enebutho elimlindayo .
44028017	Kwathi emva kwezinsuku ezintathu wabizela ndawonye kuye abakhulu babaJuda ; sebebuthene , wathi kubo : " Madoda , bazalwame , noma mina ngingenzanga lutho oluphambene nesizwe namasiko awobaba , nokho ngasuswa eJerusalema ngiyisiboshwa , nganikelwa ezandleni zamaRoma ;
44028018	wona esengihlolile afuna ukungikhulula , ngokuba kungekho cala kimi lokuba ngife ;
44028019	kepha abaJuda bekuphikisa , ngacindezelwa ukuba ngilidlulisele kuKesari , kungesikho ukuthi ngisimangalela isizwe sakithi ngalutho .
44028020	Ngakho ngaleso sizathu nginibizele lapha ukuba nginibone , ngikhulume nani ; ngokuba ngenxa yethemba lika-Israyeli ngiboshiwe ngaleli ketanga . "
44028021	Base bethi kuye : " Thina asamukelanga ncwadi ngawe evela eJudiya , akufikanga namuntu wabazalwane ukubika nokukhuluma utho olubi ngawe .
44028022	Kepha sithi kufanele sizwe kuwe okucabangayo , ngokuba siyazi ngaleli hlelo ukuthi liyaphikiswa ezindaweni zonke . "
44028023	Khona sebemmisele usuku beza kuye endlini yakhe bebaningi , wabachasisela efakaza ngombuso kaNkulunkulu , wabaqondisa ngoJesu ethathela emthethweni kaMose nakubaprofethi , kusukela ekuseni kwaze kwahlwa .
44028024	Abanye baneliswa ngokwakhulunywayo , abanye abakholwanga ;
44028025	kwathi ukuba bangezwani bodwa , bamuka , uPawulu esekhuluma izwi labalinye lokuthi : " Wakhuluma kahle uMoya oNgcwele ngo-Isaya umprofethi koyihlo
44028026	ngokuthi : ‘ Hamba uye kulesi sizwe , uthi : " Ngokuzwa niyakuzwa , ningaze naqonda , nangokubona niyakubona , ningaze nabonisisa ,
44028027	ngokuba inhliziyo yalesi sizwe seyaba buthuntu ; bezwa kanzima ngezindlebe , amehlo abo bawacimezile , funa mhlawumbe babone ngamehlo , bezwe ngezindlebe , baqonde ngenhliziyo , baphenduke , ngibaphilise . " ‘
44028028	" Ngakho-ke makwazeke kini ukuthi le nsindiso kaNkulunkulu ithunyelwe kwabezizwe ; bona-ke bayakuzwa . "
44028029	Kwathi eseshilo lokho , abaJuda baphuma benokuphikisana okukhulu phakathi kwabo .
44028030	Kepha uPawulu wahlala iminyaka emibili egcwele endlini yakhe ayiqashileyo , wamukela bonke abeza kuye ,
44028031	washumayela umbuso kaNkulunkulu , wafundisa ngaso sonke isibindi izindaba zeNkosi uJesu Kristu , enganqatshelwa muntu . ”
45001001	UPawulu , inceku kaKristu Jesu , umphostoli obiziweyo nowahlukaniselwe ivangeli likaNkulunkulu ,
45001002	alethembisa ngaphambili ngabaprofethi bakhe emibhalweni engcwele
45001003	mayelana neNdodana yakhe eyavela enzalweni kaDavide ngokwenyama ,
45001004	eyabonakaliswa ngamandla ukuthi iyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu ngokoMoya wobungcwele ngokuvuka kwabafileyo , uJesu Kristu iNkosi yethu
45001005	esamukela ngaye umusa nobuphostoli kube ngukulalela kokukholwa ezizweni zonke ngenxa yegama lakhe ,
45001006	enikuzo nani eningababiziweyo bakaJesu Kristu ,
45001007	kubo bonke abathandiweyo bakaNkulunkulu abaseRoma , ababiziweyo , abangcwele : Makube kini umusa nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba wethu naseNkosini uJesu Kristu .
45001008	Kuqala-ke ngibonga uNkulunkulu wami ngoJesu Kristu ngani nonke , ngokuba ukukholwa kwenu kunconywa ezweni lonke .
45001009	Ngokuba uNkulunkulu , engimkhonza emoyeni wami ngevangeli leNdodana yakhe , ungufakazi wami wokuthi ngokungaphezi ngiyanikhumbula
45001010	njalo emikhulekweni yami , nginxusa ukuba , uma kungenzeka ngentando kaNkulunkulu , ngiphumelele ukufika kini .
45001011	Ngokuba ngilangazelela ukunibona ukuze nginabele isipho esithile somusa sokomoya ukuba niqiniswe ,
45001012	okungukuthi siduduzane kanye nani phakathi kwenu ngokukholwa kwethu okwenu nokwami .
45001013	Angithandi , bazalwane , ukuba ningazi ukuthi ngazimisela kaningi ukuza kini , kepha ngathiyeka kuze kube manje ukuba nakini ngibe nezithelo njengakwezinye izizwe .
45001014	Nginecala kumaGreki nakwabezizwe , kwabahlakaniphileyo nakwabangaqondiyo ;
45001015	kanjalo mina ngokwami nginesifiso sokushumayela ivangeli nakinina baseRoma .
45001016	Ngokuba anginamahloni ngevangeli ; ngokuba lingamandla kaNkulunkulu , kube yinsindiso kulowo nalowo okholwayo , kumJuda kuqala , nakumGreki .
45001017	Ngokuba ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu kwambulwa kulo , kuvela ekukholweni , kuyisa ekukholweni , njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi : " Olungileyo uzakuphila ngokukholwa . "
45001018	Ngokuba intukuthelo kaNkulunkulu yambulwa ivela ezulwini phezu kwakho konke ukungamesabi uNkulunkulu nokungalungi kwabantu abathiya iqiniso ngokungalungi ,
45001019	ngokuba lokho okwazekayo ngoNkulunkulu kusobala phakathi kwabo ; ngokuba uNkulunkulu ukubonakalisile kubo .
45001020	Ngokuba okungabonwayo kwakhe , kuthi amandla akhe aphakade nobuNkulunkulu bakhe kubonakala kwasekudalweni kwezwe , ngokuba kuqondakala ngezenzo zakhe , ukuze bangabi nakuzilandulela ,
45001021	ngokuba kuthe bemazi uNkulunkulu , kabamdumisanga , kabambonganga njengoNkulunkulu , kodwa balutheka ekuzindleni kwabo ; inhliziyo yabo engaqondiyo yaba mnyama .
45001022	Bezisho ukuthi bahlakaniphile baba yiziwula ,
45001023	nenkazimulo kaNkulunkulu ongabhubhiyo bayiguqula ifane nomfanekiso womuntu obhubhayo , owezinyoni , nowezilwane ezinezinyawo ezine nezinwabuzelayo .
45001024	Ngalokho uNkulunkulu wabanikela ezinkanukweni zezinhliziyo zabo kukho ukungcola , bahlazisane imizimba yabo ,
45001025	baguqule iqiniso likaNkulunkulu , balenza amanga ; bahlonipha , bakhonza okudaliweyo kunoMdali ongobongekayo kuze kube phakade . Amen .
45001026	Ngenxa yalokho uNkulunkulu wabanikela ekuhuhekeni okuyihlazo ; ngokuba abesifazane babo baguqula ukwenza okwemvelo kwaba ngokuphambene nemvelo ;
45001027	ngokunjalo nabesilisa bayeka ukwenza kwemvelo kowesifazane , basha ngokukhanukelana , abesilisa benza okuyichilo kwabesilisa , bezitholela umvuzo ofanele ukuduka kwabo .
45001028	Nanjengalokho bengakunakanga ukumazi uNkulunkulu , uNkulunkulu wabanikela engqondweni yokunganaki ukwenza okungafanele ,
45001029	begcwele konke ukungalungi , nokonakala , nesangabe , nobubi ; begcwele umhawu , nokubulala , nokuphikisana , nenkohliso , nobuqili , nokuhleba ;
45001030	beyizinyevuzi , nabazonda uNkulunkulu , nezidlova , nabazidlayo , nabazigabisayo , nabaqambi bokubi , nabangalaleli abazali ,
45001031	nabangenangqondo , nabangathembekile , nabangenaluthando , nabangenasihawu ,
45001032	abathi besazi isimiso sokulunga sikaNkulunkulu sokuthi abenza okunjalo bafanele ukufa , abenzi lokho kuphela , kodwa babuye bavumelana nabakwenzayo .
45002001	Ngakho awunakuzilandulela wena muntu , noma ungubani owahlulelayo , ngokuba ngalokho owahlulela ngakho omunye uyazilahla wena , ngokuba wena owahlulelayo uyakwenza khona lokho nawe .
45002002	Siyazi ukuthi ukwahlulela kukaNkulunkulu ngokweqiniso kubehlela abenza okunjalo .
45002003	Ucabanga lokho yini wena muntu owahlulela abenza okunjalo , ubukwenza nawe , ukuthi uyakubalekela ukwahlulela kukaNkulunkulu na ?
45002004	Kumbe uyayidelela yini ingcebo yobumnene , neyokubekezela , neyenyewe yakhe , ungazi ukuthi ubumnene bukaNkulunkulu bukuyisa ekuphendukeni na ?
45002005	Kepha ngobulukhuni bakho nangenhliziyo engaphendukiyo uzibekelela ulaka ngosuku lolaka nolokwambulwa kokwahlulela okulungileyo kukaNkulunkulu
45002006	oyakuvuza yilowo nalowo ngokwemisebenzi yakhe :
45002007	labo abafuna ngokukhuthazela ekwenzeni okuhle inkazimulo nodumo nokungabhubhi bothola ukuphila okuphakade ;
45002008	kepha labo abanombango bengalaleli iqiniso , belalela ukungalungi , bothola ulaka nentukuthelo .
45002009	Usizi nokubandezeka kuyakwehlela imiphefumulo yabantu bonke abenza okubi , umJuda kuqala , nomGreki futhi ;
45002010	kepha inkazimulo nodumo nokuthula kubo bonke abenza okuhle , kumJuda kuqala , nakumGreki futhi .
45002011	Ngokuba akukho ukukhetha umuntu kuNkulunkulu .
45002012	Ngokuba bonke abonileyo bengenamthetho bayakubhubha bengenamthetho ; kepha bonke abonileyo benomthetho bayakwahlulelwa ngomthetho ;
45002013	ngokuba akusibo abezwayo umthetho abangabalungile phambi kukaNkulunkulu , kepha abenzayo umthetho yibona abayakulungisiswa .
45002014	Ngokuba nxa abezizwe abangenawo umthetho ngokwemvelo benza okomthetho , laba , bengenawo umthetho , bangumthetho wabo ngokwabo ,
45002015	babonakalisa ukuthi umsebenzi womthetho ulotshiwe ezinhliziyweni zabo , nonembeza wabo uyafakaza naye , imicabango yabo imangalelana noma ivunana ,
45002016	ngosuku uNkulunkulu ayakwahlulela ngalo okufihliweyo kwabantu ngokwevangeli lami ngoKristu Jesu .
45002017	Kepha uma uthiwa ungumJuda , wethemba umthetho , uzibonga ngoNkulunkulu ,
45002018	wazi intando yakhe , ukhetha okungcono , ungofundisiwe emithethweni ,
45002019	uzethembile wena ukuthi ungumholi wezimpumputhe , ungukukhanya kwabasebumnyameni ,
45002020	umyali weziwula nomfundisi wezingane , unakho ukuma kokwazi nokweqiniso emthethweni ,
45002021	wena-ke ofundisa omunye , awuzifundisi wena na ? Wena oshumayela ukuthi akungebiwa , uyeba na ?
45002022	Wena othi akungaphingwa , uyaphinga na ? Wena owenyanya isithombe , uphanga ithempeli na ?
45002023	Wena ozibonga ngomthetho , udumaza uNkulunkulu ngokweqa umthetho na ?
45002024	Ngokuba igama likaNkulunkulu liyahlanjalazwa phakathi kwabezizwe ngenxa yenu , njengalokho kulotshiwe .
45002025	Ngokuba ukusoka kuyasiza kambe , uma ugcina umthetho ; kepha uma ungumeqi womthetho , ukusoka kwakho kuphenduka ukungasoki .
45002026	Ngakho-ke uma ongasokile egcina izimiso zomthetho , ukungasoki kwakhe akuyikubalwa ukuthi kungukusoka na ?
45002027	Khona ongasokile ngokwemvelo , egcina umthetho , uzakwahlulela wena othi unombhalo nokusoka , weqe umthetho .
45002028	Ngokuba umJuda kakusiye onguye ngokubonwayo , nokusoka akusikho okubonwa enyameni ;
45002029	kodwa umJuda yilowo onguye ngaphakathi , nokusoka kungokwenhliziyo , ngomoya kungengegama , okutuswa kwakhe kungaveli kubantu kepha kuNkulunkulu .
45003001	Ngalokho kuyini umJuda adlula abanye ngakho na ? Kukho , ukusoka kunokusiza kuni na ?
45003002	Kukhulu ngezindlela zonke . Kuqala ngokuba baphathisiwe amazwi kaNkulunkulu .
45003003	Kunjani pho ? Uma abanye bengakholwanga , ukungakholwa kwabo kuyakwenza ize ukukholeka kukaNkulunkulu na ?
45003004	Qha nakanye ; kepha makube ngukuthi : UNkulunkulu uqinisile , wonke umuntu ungumqambimanga , njengokuba kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Ukuze uthiwe ungolungileyo emazwini akho , unqobe ekwahlulelweni kwakho . "
45003005	Kepha uma ukungalungi kwethu kubonakalisa ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu , siyakuthini na ? Imbala uNkulunkulu ungongalungile yini owehlisa ulaka na ? Ngikhulumisa okomuntu .
45003006	Qha nakanye , ngokuba uNkulunkulu uyakulahlulela kanjani izwe , pho , na ?
45003007	Kepha uma iqiniso likaNkulunkulu lavama ngamanga ami , kube yinkazimulo yakhe , ngisahlulelelwani futhi mina njengesoni na ?
45003008	Kungabi ngukuthi , njengalokhu sihlanjalazwayo nanjengalokhu abanye bathi siyasho ukuthi asenze okubi , ukuze kuvele okuhle na ? Ukulahlwa kwabo kubafanele .
45003009	Kunjani kanti ? Siyabadlula na ? Qha nakanye , ngokuba bese sibamangalele abaJuda namaGreki ngokuthi bonke baphansi kwesono ,
45003010	njengokuba kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Akakho olungileyo , akakho noyedwa ;
45003011	akakho oqondayo , akakho ofuna uNkulunkulu ;
45003012	bonke baphambukile , baphenduke imbuqa bonkana ; akakho owenza okuhle , akakho noyedwa .
45003013	Umphimbo wabo uyiliba elivulekileyo , ngezilimi zabo bayakhohlisa , isihlungu sezinyoka siphansi kwezindebe zabo ;
45003014	umlomo wabo ugcwele ukuthuka nokubaba ;
45003015	izinyawo zabo zishesha ukuchitha igazi ,
45003016	incithakalo nosizi kusezindleleni zabo ,
45003017	indlela yokuthula abayazi .
45003018	Ukwesaba uNkulunkulu akukho phambi kwamehlo abo . "
45003019	Kepha siyazi ukuthi lokhu okushoyo umthetho ukukhuluma kubo abasemthethweni ukuba yonke imilomo ivinjwe , izwe lonke libe necala kuNkulunkulu ,
45003020	ngokuba ngemisebenzi yomthetho akukho nyama eyakulungisiswa phambi kwakhe ; ngokuba ngomthetho kukhona ukwazi isono .
45003021	Kepha manje kubonakalisiwe ukulunga okuvela kuNkulunkulu ngaphandle komthetho , kufakazelwa ngumthetho nabaprofethi ,
45003022	ngisho ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu ngokukholwa nguJesu Kristu kubo bonke abakholwayo ; ngokuba akukho mahluko ;
45003023	ngokuba bonke bonile , basilalelwe inkazimulo kaNkulunkulu ;
45003024	balungisisiwe ngesihle ngomusa wakhe ngokuhlengwa okukuKristu Jesu ,
45003025	ammisileyo uNkulunkulu abe yinhlawulo ngokukholwa egazini lakhe , kubonakaliswe ukulunga kwakhe ngokuyekelwa kwezono ezenziwe ngaphambili
45003026	ekubekezeleni kukaNkulunkulu , ukuba kubonakaliswe ukulunga kwakhe esikhathini samanje , ukuze yena abe ngolungileyo , abe ngumlungisisi walowo okholwa nguJesu .
45003027	Ngakho kuphi ukuzibonga na ? Kuvalelwe phandle . Ngamthetho muni na ? Ngowemisebenzi na ? Qhabo , kodwa ngomthetho wokukholwa .
45003028	Ngakho-ke sithi umuntu ulungisiswa ngokukholwa ngaphandle kwemisebenzi yomthetho .
45003029	Kumbe uNkulunkulu ungowabaJuda kuphela na ? Kasiye nowabezizwe na ? Yebo , nowabezizwe ,
45003030	uma impela uNkulunkulu emunye oyakulungisisa abasokileyo ngokukholwa nabangasokile ngokukholwa .
45003031	Ngakho-ke umthetho siwenza ize ngenxa yokukholwa na ? Qha nakanye , kodwa siyawuqinisa umthetho .
45004001	Ngakho-ke siyakuthi uzuzeni u-Abrahama , ukhokho wethu , ngokwenyama na ?
45004002	Ngokuba uma u-Abrahama walungisiswa ngemisebenzi , unakho ukuzibonga ; kodwa phambi kukaNkulunkulu qha .
45004003	Ngokuba umbhalo uthini na ? Uthi : " Kepha u-Abrahama wakholwa nguNkulunkulu , kwambalelwa ukuthi kungukulunga . "
45004004	Kepha kosebenzayo umvuzo awubalelwa ngokomusa kodwa ngokwemfanelo ;
45004005	kepha kongasebenziyo , kodwa ekholwa nguye olungisisa ongamesabi uNkulunkulu , ukukholwa kwakhe kubalelwa yena ukuthi kungukulunga ,
45004006	njengalokhu noDavide esho ngokubusiswa komuntu uNkulunkulu ambalela ukulunga ngaphandle kwemisebenzi , ethi :
45004007	" Babusisiwe abathethelelwe izeqo zabo , nabazono zabo zisitshekelwe ;
45004008	ubusisiwe umuntu iNkosi engayikumbalela isono . U-Abrahama wamukeliswa isithembiso ngokukholwa . "
45004009	Ngakho-ke lokhu kubusiswa kuqondene nabasokile noma nabangasokile na ? Ngokuba sithi : Ukukholwa kwabalelwa u-Abrahama ukuthi kungukulunga .
45004010	Pho , kwabalelwa kanjani na ? Esesokile yini noma engakasoki na ? Akubanga esesokile , kodwa engakasoki .
45004011	Wasamukela isibonakaliso sokusoka , sibe luphawu lokulunga kokukholwa ayenakho engakasoki , ukuba abe nguyise wabo bonke abakholwayo bengasokile , ukuze ukulunga kubalelwe kubona ,
45004012	futhi abe nguyise wabasokileyo , kungabi ngowabasokileyo kuphela , kepha nowabo abahamba emkhondweni wokukholwa ubaba u-Abrahama ayenakho engakasoki .
45004013	Ngokuba isithembiso sokuthi uyakuba yindlalifa yezwe asinikwanga u-Abrahama nenzalo yakhe ngawo umthetho kodwa ngokulunga kokukholwa .
45004014	Ngokuba uma izindlalifa ziyizo ngawo umthetho , ukukholwa kwenziwe ize , nesithembiso asiselutho ;
45004015	ngokuba umthetho ubanga intukuthelo , kepha lapho kungekho khona umthetho , akukho nakweqa .
45004016	Ngalokho kuya ngokukholwa ukuba kube ngokomusa , ukuze isithembiso siqiniseke enzalweni yonke , kungabi kweyomthetho yodwa kodwa nakuleyo engeyokukholwa kuka-Abrahama ongubaba wethu sonke ,
45004017	njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi : " Ngikumisile ube nguyise wezizwe eziningi " phambi kwalowo Nkulunkulu akholwa nguye , yena ophilisa abafileyo nobiza okungekho ngokungathi kukhona ,
45004018	owathi kungekho themba wakholwa ngethemba , ukuze abe nguyise wezizwe eziningi , njengalokho okwashiwo ukuthi : " Yoba njalo inzalo yakho ; "
45004019	engabanga buthakathaka ekukholweni wabona umzimba wakhe obusufa , eneminyaka engaba ngeyikhulu , nesizalo sikaSara sifile ;
45004020	akangabazanga ngesithembiso sikaNkulunkulu ngokungakholwa , kodwa waqina ekukholweni , enika uNkulunkulu udumo ,
45004021	eqinisekile ukuthi lokho akwethembisile unamandla nokukwenza .
45004022	Ngalokho-ke kwabalelwa yena ukuthi kungukulunga .
45004023	Kepha akulotshwanga ngenxa yakhe yedwa ukuthi kwabalelwa yena ,
45004024	kodwa nangenxa yethu esiyakubalelwa khona , thina esikholwa nguye owavusa uJesu iNkosi yethu kwabafileyo ,
45004025	owanikelwa ngenxa yeziphambeko zethu , wavuswa ngenxa yokulungisiswa kwethu .
45005001	Ngakho lokhu sesilungisisiwe ngokukholwa , sinokuthula kuNkulunkulu ngeNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu ,
45005002	okungaye sinokungena ngokukholwa kulo musa esimi kuwo , siyazibonga ekwethembeni inkazimulo kaNkulunkulu .
45005003	Kepha akusikho lokho kuphela , kodwa sizibonga nangezinhlupheko ngokwazi ukuthi ukuhlupheka kuveza ukukhuthazela ,
45005004	ukukhuthazela kuveza ukuqiniseka , ukuqiniseka kuveza ithemba ;
45005005	ithemba alijabhisi , ngokuba uthando lukaNkulunkulu lutheliwe ezinhliziyweni zethu ngoMoya oNgcwele esimuphiweyo .
45005006	Ngokuba sisebuthakathaka , uKristu wafela abangamesabi uNkulunkulu ngesikhathi esifaneleyo ;
45005007	ngokuba cishe kungenzeki ukuba umuntu afele olungileyo , kodwa mhlawumbe kungase kube khona ongaba nesibindi sokufela omuhle ;
45005008	kepha uNkulunkulu uyabonakalisa ukusithanda kwakhe ngalokhu ukuthi , siseyizoni , uKristu wasifela .
45005009	Ngakho kakhulu sesilungisisiwe ngegazi lakhe , siyakusindiswa ngaye olakeni .
45005010	Ngokuba uma sathola ukubuyisana noNkulunkulu ngokufa kweNdodana yakhe sise yizitha , ikakhulu siyakusindiswa ngokuphila kwayo sesitholile ukubuyisana ;
45005011	kepha akusikho lokho kuphela , kodwa sizibonga futhi ngoNkulunkulu ngeNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu , esesamukelisiwe ngaye ukubuyisana .
45005012	Ngakho-ke njengalokho isono sangena ezweni ngamuntu munye , nangesono kwangena ukufa , ngokunjalo ukufa kwafikela abantu bonke , lokhu bonke bonile ;
45005013	ngokuba isono sasikhona ezweni kungakabikho umthetho , kepha isono asibalelwa ungekho umthetho ;
45005014	nokho ukufa kwabusa kusukela ku-Adamu kwaze kwaba kuMose , naphezu kwabangonanga ngendlela yeseqo sika-Adamu oyisifanekiso sakhe obeyakuza .
45005015	Kepha isipho somusa asinjengesiphambeko ; ngokuba uma ngesiphambeko samuntu munye abaningi bafa , ikakhulu kwavama kwabaningi umusa nesipho sikaNkulunkulu ngomusa wamuntu munye , uJesu Kristu .
45005016	Isipho asinjengokona kwalowo emunye , ngokuba uma ukwahlulela kwaba ngoyedwa kube ngukulahlwa , isipho somusa sona-ke saba ngeziphambeko eziningi kube ngukulungisiswa .
45005017	Ngokuba uma ngesiphambeko samuntu munye ukufa kwabusa ngalowo emunye , ikakhulu abamukela ukuvama komusa nokuvama kwesipho sokulunga bayakubusa ekuphileni ngalowo emunye , uJesu Kristu .
45005018	Ngalokho-ke njengokuba ngasiphambeko sinye kwaba khona ukulahlwa kubantu bonke , kanjalo ngasenzo sinye sokulunga kwaba khona ukulungisiswa kukho ukuphila kubantu bonke ;
45005019	ngokuba njengalokho ngokungalaleli kwamuntu munye abaningi benziwa izoni , kanjalo ngokulalela kwamuntu munye abaningi bayakwenziwa abalungileyo .
45005020	Kepha umthetho wangena ukuba isiphambeko sande ; kodwa lapho kwavama khona isono , umusa wavama kakhulukazi ,
45005021	ukuze njengalokho isono sabusa ngokufa , nomusa ubuse kanjalo ngokulunga , kube ngukuphila okuphakade ngoJesu Kristu iNkosi yethu . imkhonze ekulungeni
45006001	Ngakho siyakuthini na ? Sihlale esonweni , ukuze kuvame umusa na ?
45006002	Qha nakanye . Thina esafa maqondana nesono singabuye sihambe kanjani kuso na ?
45006003	Kumbe anazi yini ukuthi sonke esabhapathizelwa kuKristu Jesu , sabhapathizelwa kukho ukufa kwakhe na ?
45006004	Ngakho sembelwa naye ngokubhapathizelwa kukho ukufa ukuba njengalokho uKristu wavuswa kwabafileyo ngenkazimulo kaYise , kanjalo nathi sihambe ekuphileni okusha .
45006005	Ngokuba uma sihlanganisiwe kanye naye ngokufa okufananayo , siyakuba njalo nangokuvuka ,
45006006	sazi lokhu ukuthi umuntu wethu omdala wabethelwa kanye naye esiphambanweni , ukuze umzimba wesono wenziwe ize , singabe sisakhonza isono ,
45006007	ngokuba ofileyo ukhululiwe esonweni .
45006008	Kepha uma safa kanye noKristu , siyakholwa ukuthi siyakuphila futhi kanye naye ,
45006009	sazi ukuthi uKristu esevusiwe kwabafileyo akasafi , ukufa akusabusi phezu kwakhe .
45006010	Ngokuba ukufa , afa ngakho , wakufa kanye nje ngenxa yesono ; kepha ukuphila akuphilayo ukuphilela uNkulunkulu .
45006011	Kanjalo nani manizisho ukuthi ningabafileyo maqondana nesono , kodwa niphilele uNkulunkulu kuKristu Jesu .
45006012	Ngakho makungabusi isono emzimbeni wenu ofayo , nize nilalele izinkanuko zawo ;
45006013	futhi ninganikeli izitho zenu esonweni , zibe yizikhali zokungalungi , kodwa zinikeleni nina kuNkulunkulu njengabaphilayo bevukile kwabafileyo nezitho zenu kuNkulunkulu , zibe yizikhali zokulunga ,
45006014	ngokuba isono asiyikubusa phezu kwenu ; ngokuba aniphansi komthetho , kepha niphansi komusa .
45006015	Kunjani , pho , na ? Siyakona ngokuba singephansi komthetho kodwa phansi komusa na ? Qha nakanye .
45006016	Anazi yini ukuthi lowo enizinikela kuye ukuba nibe yizinceku zokumlalela , niyizinceku zakhe enimlalelayo , noma ezesono kube ngukufa noma ezokulalela kube ngukulunga , na ?
45006017	Kepha makabongwe uNkulunkulu ukuthi nina enaniyizinceku zesono senilalela ngenhliziyo indlela yesifundiso enanikelwa kuyo
45006018	nokuthi , senikhululiwe esonweni , naba yizinceku zokulunga .
45006019	Ngikhulumisa okomuntu ngenxa yobuthakathaka benyama yenu . Ngokuba njengalokho nanikela izitho zenu zibe yizinceku zamanyala nezokungalungi kwaba ngukungalungi , kanjalo nikelani manje izitho zenu zibe yizinceku zokulunga kube ngukungcweliswa .
45006020	Ngokuba lapho nise yizinceku zesono , nanikhululekile maqondana nokulunga .
45006021	Ngaleso sikhathi naninezithelo zini na ? Eseninezinhloni ngakho manje ; ngokuba ukugcina kwalokho kungukufa .
45006022	Kepha manje , senikhululiwe esonweni naba ngabakhonza uNkulunkulu , ninazo izithelo zenu kube ngukungcweliswa nasekugcineni ukuphila okuphakade .
45006023	Ngokuba inkokhelo yesono ingukufa , kepha isipho somusa sikaNkulunkulu singukuphila okuphakade kuKristu Jesu iNkosi yethu .
45007001	Kanti anazi yini , bazalwane , ngokuba ngikhuluma kwabawazi umthetho , ukuthi umthetho uyabusa phezu komuntu ngesikhathi sonke esekhona na ?
45007002	Ngokuba owesifazane oganileyo uboshelwe ngomthetho endodeni isekhona ; kepha nxa indoda isifile , ukhululiwe emthethweni wendoda .
45007003	Ngalokho-ke lapho indoda isekhona , uyakuthiwa isiphingi , uma eba ngowenye indoda ; kepha nxa indoda isifile , ukhululekile emthethweni , angebe yisiphingi , uma eba ngowenye indoda .
45007004	Kanjalo nani bazalwane bami , nani naba ngabafileyo maqondana nomthetho ngomzimba kaKristu ukuba nibe ngabomunye , lowo owavuswa kwabafileyo , ukuze sithelele uNkulunkulu izithelo .
45007005	Ngokuba kwathi sisenyameni , ukuhuheka kwezono okwavela ngomthetho kwasebenza ezithweni zethu ukuthelela ukufa izithelo ;
45007006	kepha kalokhu sikhululiwe emthethweni , sifile maqondana nalokho esasibanjwa yikho ukuba sikhonze emoyeni omusha , kungesegameni elidala .
45007007	Ngakho siyakuthini na ? Umthetho uyisono na ? Qha nakanye ; kepha bengingasazanga isono , uma bekungengomthetho ; ngokuba ukufisa bengingakwazanga , uma umthetho ubungashongo ukuthi : " Ungafisi ; "
45007008	kepha isono sathola ithuba ngomyalo , sasebenza kimi ukufisa konke ; ngokuba ngaphandle komthetho isono sifile .
45007009	Mina-ke ngake ngahamba ngaphandle komthetho ; kepha kwathi ukuba kufike umyalo , savuka isono ,
45007010	ngafa mina ; umyalo obungowokuphila wona wafunyanwa ungowokufa kimi ,
45007011	ngokuba isono , sithola ithuba ngomyalo , sangikhohlisa , sangibulala ngawo .
45007012	Ngakho-ke umthetho ungcwele , nomyalo ungcwele , ulungile , muhle .
45007013	Pho , okuhle kwaba ngukufa kimi na ? Qha nakanye ; kepha isono , ukuba sibonakale ukuthi siyisono , sangibangela ukufa ngakho okuhle , ukuze isono ngawo umyalo sibe ngesonayo kakhulu .
45007014	Ngokuba siyazi ukuthi umthetho ungowomoya ; kepha mina ngingowenyama , othengisiwe phansi kwesono .
45007015	Ngokuba engikwenzayo angikuqondi ; ngokuba engikwenzayo akusikho lokho engikuthandayo ; kodwa lokho engikuzondayo , yikho engikwenzayo .
45007016	Kepha uma ngenza lokho engingakuthandiyo , ngiyawuvumela umthetho ukuthi muhle .
45007017	Kodwa kalokhu akuseyimi engikwenzayo , kodwa yisono esihlala kimi .
45007018	Ngokuba ngiyazi ukuthi kimi , kungukuthi enyameni yami , akuhlali okuhle ; ngokuba intando ikhona kimi , kodwa ukwenza okuhle akukho ,
45007019	ngokuba okuhle engikuthandayo angikwenzi , kodwa okubi engingakuthandiyo lokho ngiyakwenza .
45007020	Uma-ke ngenza lokho engingakuthandiyo akuseyimi engenza lokho , kodwa yisono esihlala kimi .
45007021	Ngalokho ngifumana kimina engithanda ukwenza okuhle umthetho wokuthi kukhona okubi kimi ,
45007022	ngokuba ngiwenamela umthetho kaNkulunkulu ngokomuntu ongaphakathi ,
45007023	kepha ngibona omunye umthetho ezithweni zami olwayo nomthetho wengqondo yami , ungithumbela emthethweni wesono osezithweni zami .
45007024	Wo ! mina muntu wosizi , ngubani oyakungikhulula kulo mzimba wokufa na ?
45007025	Makabongwe uNkulunkulu ngoJesu Kristu iNkosi yethu . Ngalokho-ke mina ngokwami ngikhonza umthetho kaNkulunkulu ngengqondo kepha umthetho wesono ngenyama .
45008001	Kanjalo akusekho ukulahlwa kwabakuKristu Jesu .
45008002	Ngokuba umthetho kaMoya wokuphila okuKristu Jesu ungikhululile emthethweni wesono nowokufa .
45008003	Ngokuba lokho okwehlula umthetho , ngokuba ungenamandla ngenxa yenyama , wakwenza uNkulunkulu ngokuthuma iNdodana yakhe ifana nenyama yesono , nangenxa yesono walahla isono enyameni ,
45008004	ukuze umyalo womthetho ugcwaliseke kithina esingahambi ngokwenyama kepha ngokukaMoya .
45008005	Ngokuba abokwenyama banaka okwenyama , kepha abakaMoya banaka okukaMoya .
45008006	Ngokuba ukunaka kwenyama kungukufa , kepha ukunaka kukaMoya kungukuphila nokuthula .
45008007	Ngokuba ukunaka kwenyama kungubutha kuNkulunkulu ; ngokuba akuwuthobeli umthetho kaNkulunkulu , yebo , futhi kungekwenze ;
45008008	abasenyameni abanakumthokozisa uNkulunkulu .
45008009	Kepha nina anisenyameni , kodwa nikuye uMoya , uma uMoya kaNkulunkulu ehlala kini . Kepha uma umuntu engenaye uMoya kaKristu , lowo kasiye owakhe .
45008010	Uma uKristu ekini , umzimba ufile ngenxa yesono , kepha umoya ungukuphila ngenxa yokulunga .
45008011	Uma-ke uMoya walowo owavusa uJesu kwabafileyo ehlala kini , yena owavusa uKristu Jesu kwabafileyo uyakuphilisa nemizimba yenu efayo ngaye uMoya wakhe ohlala kini .
45008012	Ngalokho-ke , bazalwane , asinacala kuyo inyama lokuba sihambe ngokwenyama .
45008013	Ngokuba uma nihamba ngokwenyama , nizakufa ; kepha uma nibulala imisebenzi yomzimba ngoMoya , nizakuphila .
45008014	Ngokuba bonke abaholwa nguMoya kaNkulunkulu , labo bangabantwana bakaNkulunkulu .
45008015	Ngokuba anamukeliswanga umoya wobugqila ukuba nibuye nesabe , kepha namukeliswa umoya wobuntwana esimemeza ngaye sithi : " Aba , Baba ! "
45008016	Yena lowo Moya ufakaza kanye nomoya wethu ukuthi singabantwana bakaNkulunkulu .
45008017	Uma-ke singabantwana , siyizindlalifa futhi , izindlalifa zikaNkulunkulu , izindlalifa kanye noKristu , uma phela sihlupheka kanye naye , ukuze siphiwe inkazimulo futhi kanye naye .
45008018	Ngokuba ngithi izinhlupheko zesikhathi samanje azinakulinganiswa nenkazimulo eyakwambulwa kithina .
45008019	Ngokuba ukulangazela kokudaliweyo kulindele ukwambulwa kwabantwana bakaNkulunkulu .
45008020	Ngokuba okudaliweyo kwabekwa phansi kobuze , kungengentando yakho kodwa ngaye owakubekayo ,
45008021	ethembeni lokuthi nakho okudaliweyo kuyakukhululwa ebugqileni bokubhubha , kube ngukukhululeka kwenkazimulo yabantwana bakaNkulunkulu .
45008022	Ngokuba siyazi ukuthi konke okudaliweyo kuyabubula kanyekanye kunezinseka kuze kube manje ;
45008023	akusikho lokho kuphela , kepha nathi uqobo lwethu esinolibo lukaMoya siyabubula phakathi kwethu , silindele isimo sobuntwana , ukukhululwa komzimba wethu .
45008024	Ngokuba ethembeni sisindisiwe ; kepha ithemba elibonwayo alisilo ithemba ; ngokuba lokhu umuntu akubonayo usakwethembelani na ?
45008025	Kodwa uma sithemba lokho esingakuboniyo , siyakulindela ngokubekezela .
45008026	Ngokunjalo noMoya uyasisiza ebuthakathakeni bethu ; ngokuba asikwazi esingakucela ngokufaneleyo , kodwa uMoya uqobo usikhulumela ngokububula okungenakuphinyiselwa ;
45008027	kepha yena ohlola izinhliziyo uyakwazi okuqondwa nguMoya , ngokuba ukhulumela abangcwele ngokwentando kaNkulunkulu .
45008028	Siyazi ukuthi kwabamthandayo uNkulunkulu konke kusebenzelana kube ngokuhle , kulabo ababiziweyo ngecebo lakhe .
45008029	Ngokuba labo ayebazi ngaphambili wabamisa ngaphambili , bafane nesimo seNdodana yakhe , ukuze yona ibe yizibulo phakathi kwabazalwane abaningi ;
45008030	labo abamisile ngaphambili ubabizile futhi ; labo ababizile ubalungisisile futhi ; labo abalungisisileyo ubaphile nenkazimulo futhi .
45008031	Sesiyakuthini ngalokho na ? Uma uNkulunkulu emi ngakithi , ngubani ongamelana nathi na ?
45008032	Yena ongayigodlanga eyakhe iNdodana , kepha wayinikela ngenxa yethu sonke , kungaba kanjani ukuba angasiphi konke kanye nayo na ?
45008033	Ngubani ozakumangalela abakhethiweyo bakaNkulunkulu na ? UNkulunkulu ungolungisisayo ;
45008034	ngubani olahlayo na ? UKristu Jesu owafayo , yebo impela , owavuswa kwabafileyo , ongakwesokunene sikaNkulunkulu , nguyena osinxuselayo .
45008035	Ngubani ozakusahlukanisa nothando lukaKristu na ? Noma ukuhlupheka , noma ukubandezeka , noma ukuzingelwa , noma indlala , noma ukuhamba ze , noma ingozi , noma inkemba , na ?
45008036	Kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Ngenxa yakho sibulawa usuku lonke , sithiwa izimvu zokuhlatshwa . "
45008037	Kepha kukho konke lokho siyanqoba nokunqoba ngowasithandayo .
45008038	Ngiyakholwa ukuthi nakufa , nakuphila , nazingelosi , nababusi , nakho okukhona , nakho okuzayo , namandla ,
45008039	nakuphakama , nakujula , nanto enye edaliweyo akuyikuba namandla okusahlukanisa nothando lukaNkulunkulu olukuKristu Jesu iNkosi yethu .
45009001	Ngikhuluma iqiniso ngikuKristu , angiqambi amanga , unembeza wami ufakazelana nami eMoyeni oNgcwele
45009002	ukuthi nginokudabuka okukhulu nobuhlungu obungapheliyo enhliziyweni yami .
45009003	Ngokuba ngingafisa ukuba mina uqobo ngibe ngoqalekisiweyo kuKristu ngenxa yabazalwane bami abangabakithi ngokwenyama ;
45009004	bona bangabakwa-Israyeli , okungesabo isimo sobuntwana nenkazimulo , nezivumelwano , nokumiswa komthetho , nenkonzo , nezithembiso ,
45009005	abangababo okhokho avela kubo uKristu ngokwenyama , yena onguNkulunkulu ophezu kwakho konke , obongekayo kuze kube phakade . Amen .
45009006	Akusikho okungathi izwi likaNkulunkulu liphuthile . Ngokuba asibo bonke abavela ku-Israyeli abangabakwa-Israyeli ;
45009007	nakuba beyinzalo ka-Abrahama , bonke abasibo abantwana , kodwa kuthiwa : " Ngo-Isaka iyakubizwa inzalo yakho . "
45009008	Lokhu kungukuthi akusibo abantwana benyama abangabantwana bakaNkulunkulu labo , kodwa abantwana besithembiso bathiwa inzalo .
45009009	Ngokuba lingelesithembiso leli zwi lokuthi : " Ngalesi sikhathi ngizakufika ; khona uSara uzakuba nendodana . "
45009010	Akuyilokhu kuphela , kodwa kwaba njalo nakuRebeka ekhulelisiwe ngoyedwa , u-Isaka , ukhokho wethu ;

45009014	Ngakho siyakuthini na ? Kukhona yini ukungalungi kuNkulunkulu na ? Qha nakanye .

45009016	Ngakho-ke akuyi ngentando nangokuzikhathaza komuntu , kodwa kuya ngokuhawukela kukaNkulunkulu .
45009017	Ngokuba umbhalo uthi kuFaro : " Ngakuphakhamisela khona lokhu ukuba ngibonakalise amandla ami kuwe nokuba igama lami lishunyayelwe emhlabeni wonke . "
45009018	Ngakho uhawukela lowo athanda ukumhawukela , umenza lukhuni lowo athanda ukumenza lukhuni .
45009019	Usuzakuthi kimi : " Usasolelani yena na ? Ngokuba ngubani ongamelana nentando yakhe na ? "
45009020	O , wena muntu ! Ungubani-ke wena ophikisana noNkulunkulu na ? Okubunjiweyo kungasho yini kowakubumbayo ukuthi : " Wangenzelani ngaba njena na ? "
45009021	Nokuba akanamandla yini umbumbi ebumbeni ukwenza ngesigaxa sisinye isitsha esinye esihloniphekayo nesinye esingahloniphekiyo na ?
45009022	Uma , pho , uNkulunkulu , ethanda ukubonakalisa ulaka nokuveza amandla akhe , wathwala ngokubekezela okukhulu izitsha zolaka ezilungiselwe ukubhujiswa
45009023	ukuba abonakalise ingcebo yenkazimulo yakhe ezitsheni zomusa ayezilungisele inkazimulo ngaphambili ,
45009024	thina asibizayo nathi , kungesikho kubaJuda kuphela kodwa nakwabezizwe ?
45009025	Njengalokhu esho nakuHoseya ukuthi : " Ngiyakubiza abangesiso isizwe sami ngokuthi isizwe sami , nongathandiwe ngokuthi uthandiwe ;
45009026	nasendaweni lapha kwathiwa kubo : ‘ Anisibo abantu bami , ’ lapho bayakubizwa ngokuthi : ‘ Abantwana bakaNkulunkulu ophilayo . ’ "
45009027	U-Isaya umemeza ngo-Israyeli , uthi : " Nokuba umumo wabantwana bakwa-Israyeli ungangesihlabathi solwandle , yinsali eyakusindiswa ,

45009030	Ngakho siyakuthini na ? Ukuthi abezizwe abangafunisisanga ukulunga batholile ukulunga , ukulunga kambe okungokukholwa ;
45009031	kepha u-Israyeli , elandela umthetho wokulunga , kafinyelelanga emthethweni .

45010001	Bazalwane , ukulangazela kwenhliziyo yami nokunxusa kwami kuNkulunkulu ngabo kungukuba basindiswe .
45010002	Ngokuba ngiyabafakazela ukuthi bashisekela uNkulunkulu kodwa kungengokuqonda ;
45010003	ngokuba bengakwazi ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu , befuna ukumisa okwabo , abakuthobelanga ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu .
45010004	Ngokuba isiphetho somthetho nguKristu , kube ngukulunga kubo bonke abakholwayo .
45010005	Ngokuba uMose uloba ukuthi umuntu owenza ukulunga okuvela emthethweni uyakuphila ngakho .
45010006	Kepha ukulunga okuvela ngokukholwa kusho kuthi : " Ungasho enhliziyweni yakho ukuthi : ‘ Ngubani ozakwenyukela ezulwini na ? ‘ okungukuthi ukwehlisa uKristu ,
45010007	nokuba : ‘ Ngubani ozakwehlela kwalasha na ? ’ " okungukuthi ukukhuphula uKristu kwabafileyo .
45010008	Kepha kuthini na ? Izwi liseduze nawe , emlonyeni wakho nasenhliziyweni yakho , okungukuthi izwi lokukholwa esilishumayelayo .
45010009	Ngokuba uma uvuma ngomlomo wakho ukuthi uJesu uyiNkosi , ukholwa enhliziyweni yakho ukuthi uNkulunkulu wamvusa kwabafileyo , uyakusindiswa ;
45010010	ngokuba umuntu ukholwa ngenhliziyo kube ngukulunga , ngomlomo uyavuma kube ngukusindiswa .
45010011	Ngokuba umbhalo uthi : " Lowo okholwayo akayikujabhiswa . "

45010013	ngokuba " bonke abayakukhuleka egameni leNkosi bayakusindiswa . "
45010014	Kepha bayakukhuleka kanjani kuye abangakholwanga nguye na ? Bayakukholwa kanjani abangezwanga ngaye na ? Bayakuzwa kanjani , kungekho oshumayelayo na ?
45010015	Bayakushumayela kanjani , uma bengathunywa na ? Njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi : " Yeka , zinhle izinyawo zabashumayela izindaba ezinhle . "
45010016	Kodwa abalilalelanga bonke ivangeli . Ngokuba u-Isaya uthi : " Nkosi , ngubani owakholwa ngesikuzwileyo na ? "

45010018	Kepha ngithi : Abezwanga yini na ? Yebo , impela : " Izwi labo liphumele emhlabeni wonke , nokusho kwabo kuye nasemikhawulweni yelakhiweyo . "
45010019	Kepha ngithi : U-Israyeli wayengaqondi na ? Kuqala , uMose uthi : " Mina ngiyakunivusela umhawu ngabangesiso isizwe , nginithukuthelise ngesizwe esingenangqondo . "
45010020	Kepha u-Isaya unesibindi sokuthi : " Ngafunyanwa yilabo abangangifunanga , ngabonakala kulabo abangangibuzanga . "
45010021	Kodwa ngo-Israyeli uthi : " Usuku lonke ngelulela izandla zami kuso isizwe esingalaleliyo nesiphikayo . "
45011001	Ngalokho ngithi : UNkulunkulu usilahlile isizwe sakhe na ? Qha nakanye , ngokuba nami ngingumIsrayeli , wenzalo ka-Abrahama , wesizwe sakwaBenjamini .
45011002	UNkulunkulu akasilahlanga isizwe sakhe ayesazi ngaphambili . Kumbe anazi yini ukuthi umbhalo uthini ngo-Eliya ukuba umangalela u-Israyeli kuNkulunkulu ngokuthi :
45011003	" Nkosi , bababulele abaprofethi bakho , badilizile ama-altare akho , mina ngisele ngedwa , sebefuna ukungibulala nami , " na ?
45011004	Kepha impendulo kaNkulunkulu ithini kuye na ? Ithi : " Ngizishiyele amadoda ayizinkulungwane eziyisikhombisa angaguqanga ngamadolo kuBali . "
45011005	Kanjalo kukhona nangalesi sikhathi samanje insali ngokokukhetha komusa ;
45011006	kepha uma kuya ngomusa , akusayi ngemisebenzi ; uma kungenjalo , umusa awuseyiwo umusa .
45011007	Kunjani , pho ? Lokho u-Israyeli akufunayo akakufumananga , kepha abakhethiweyo bakufumana , abanye benziwa baba lukhuni ,
45011008	njengalokho kulotshiwe ukuthi : " UNkulunkulu wabanika umoya wobuthongo , amehlo okungaboni , nezindlebe zokungezwa , kuze kube lusuku lwanamuhla . "
45011009	NoDavide uthi : " Itafula labo malibe yisihibe nogibe , nesikhubekiso nempindiselo kubo ,
45011010	kufiphazwe amehlo abo ukuba angaboni , ugobe umhlane wabo njalo . "
45011011	Ngakho ngithi : Bakhubeka ukuba bawe na ? Qha nakanye ; kepha ngesiphambeko sabo insindiso ifikile kwabezizwe ukubavusela umhawu .
45011012	Kepha uma isiphambeko sabo siyingcebo yezwe , nokuncipha kwabo kuyingcebo yabezizwe , pho , kakhulu kangakanani ukuphelela kwabo .
45011013	Ngikhuluma kini nina bezizwe . Njengokuba mina ngingumphostoli wabezizwe , ngidumisa ukukhonza kwami
45011014	ukuba mhlawumbe ngingabavusela umhawu abenyama yami , ngisindise abanye kubo .
45011015	Ngokuba uma ukulahlwa kwabo kungukubuyiswa kwezwe , ukwamukelwa kwabo kungaba yini , uma kungesikho ukuphila kwabafileyo na ?
45011016	Uma ulibo lungcwele , nenhlama injalo ; uma impande ingcwele , namagatsha anjalo .
45011017	Kepha uma kwaphulwa amanye amagatsha , wena-ke ongumnqumo wasendle wafakelwa phakathi kwawo , wahlanganyela nawo impande yamafutha yomnqumo ,
45011018	ungazigabisi phezu kwamagatsha ; kepha uma uzigabisa , akusuwe othwele impande , kepha yimpande ethwele wena .
45011019	Uzakuthi-ke wena : " Amagatsha aphulwa ukuba mina ngifakelwe . "
45011020	Kulungile ; aphulwa ngokungakholwa , wena-ke umi ngokukholwa . Ungazikhukhumezi , kepha yesaba ;
45011021	ngokuba uma uNkulunkulu engayekanga amagatsha emvelo , nawe angeze akuyeka .
45011022	Bheka-ke ububele nobukhali bukaNkulunkulu ; ubukhali kulabo abawayo kepha kuwe ububele bukaNkulunkulu , uma uhlala ebubeleni ; uma kungenjalo , uzakunqunywa nawe .
45011023	Nalabo uma bengahlali ekungakholweni , bayakufakelwa , ngokuba uNkulunkulu unamandla okubafakela futhi .
45011024	Ngokuba uma wena wanqunywa emnqumweni ongowasendle ngemvelo , wafakelwa emnqumweni omuhle ngokuphambene nemvelo , ikakhulu labo abangabemvelo bayakufakelwa emnqumweni wakubo .
45011025	Ngokuba angithandi , bazalwane , ukuba ningayazi le mfihlakalo , funa nizishaye abahlakaniphileyo , ukuthi inxenye ka-Israyeli yehlelwe ngubulukhuni , kuze kungene abezizwe ngokupheleleyo ;
45011026	kanjalo u-Israyeli wonke uyakusindiswa , njengalokho kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Kuyakuvela eSiyoni uMhlangulisi , asuse ukungalungi kuJakobe .
45011027	Yilesi isivumelwano sami nabo , lapho ngisusa izono zabo . "
45011028	Ngokwevangeli bayizitha ngenxa yenu , kepha ngokukhethwa bangabathandiweyo ngenxa yawokhokho ,
45011029	ngokuba izipho zomusa nokubiza kukaNkulunkulu akaguquki kukho .
45011030	Ngokuba njengalokho nina kade ningamlaleli uNkulunkulu , kepha manje nihawukelwe ngenxa yokungalaleli kwabo ,
45011031	kanjalo nalaba kalokhu abalalelanga , ukuze ngomusa enenzelwe wona nabo bahawukelwe manje .
45011032	Ngokuba uNkulunkulu ubavalele bonke ekungalalelini ukuze abahawukele bonke .
45011033	Yeka ukujula kwengcebo , nokuhlakanipha , nokwazi kukaNkulunkulu ! Yeka izahlulelo zakhe ezingaphenyekiyo , nezindlela zakhe ezingaqondakaliyo !
45011034	Ngokuba " ngubani owawazi umqondo weNkosi na ? Nokuba ngubani owaba ngumeluleki wayo na ? "
45011035	Noma " ngubani owaqala ukuyipha ukuba kubuyiselwe kuye na ? "
45011036	Ngokuba konke kuvela kuye , kukhona ngaye , kuya kuye ; makube kuye inkazimulo kuze kube phakade . Amen .
45012001	Ngakho ngiyanincenga , bazalwane , ngobubele bukaNkulunkulu ukuba ninikele imizimba yenu ibe ngumnikelo ophilileyo , ongcwele , othandeka kuNkulunkulu , kube ngukukhonza kwenu kokuqonda ;
45012002	ningalingisi leli zwe , kodwa niguqulwe isimo ngokwenziwa ibe ntsha ingqondo yenu , ukuze nibe nokuhlolisisa okuyintando kaNkulunkulu , okuhle , nokuthandekayo , nokupheleleyo .
45012003	Ngokuba ngomusa engiwuphiweyo ngisho kulowo nalowo phakathi kwenu ukuthi angacabangi athi mkhulu kunalokho afanele ukukucabanga , kodwa acabange kube ngokuqonda , njengalokho uNkulunkulu abele lowo nalowo isilinganiso sokukholwa .
45012004	Ngokuba njengalokhu sinezitho eziningi emzimbeni munye , kepha izitho zonke azinamsebenzi munye ,
45012005	kanjalo thina esibaningi simzimba munye kuKristu , kepha ngabanye siyizitho , omunye esomunye .
45012006	Sinezipho zomusa ezahlukileyo ngokomusa esiwuphiweyo ; uma singesokuprofetha , asiprofethe ngesilinganiso sokukholwa ;
45012007	uma singesokukhonza , kube senkonzweni ; ofundisayo , kube sekufundiseni ,
45012008	oyalayo , ekuyaleni ; owabayo , enze ngobuqotho ; oholayo , ngenkuthalo ; ohawukelayo , ngentokozo .
45012009	Uthando malungabi nakuzenzisa ; nenyanye okubi , nibambelele kokuhle ;
45012010	thandanani ngenhliziyo ngothando lobuzalwane ; ekwazisaneni nandulelane ;
45012011	ekukhuthaleni ningenqeni , nivuthe emoyeni , nikhonze iNkosi ;
45012012	ethembeni nithokoze ; osizini nibekezele ; ekukhulekeni niqinisele njalo ;
45012013	hlanganyelani nabangcwele ekusweleni kwabo , nikhuthalele ukungenisa izihambi .
45012014	Babusiseni abanizingelayo ; busisani , ningaqalekisi .
45012015	Thokozani nabathokozayo , nikhale nabakhalayo .
45012016	Manibe nhliziyonye ; ningazindli okuphakemeyo , kodwa yaneliswani ngokuphansi . Ningazishayi abahlakaniphileyo .
45012017	Ningaphindiseli muntu okubi ngokubi ; nakani okuhle phambi kwabantu bonke ;
45012018	uma kungenzeka , ngokwenu hlalisanani ngokuthula nabantu bonke ;
45012019	ningaziphindiseli nina bathandwa , kodwa dedelani ulaka , ngokuba kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Ngokwami ukuphindisela , ngiyakubuyisela mina , " isho iNkosi .
45012020	Kepha : " Uma isitha sakho silambile , siphe sidle ; uma somile , siphuzise , ngokuba ngokwenza lokho uyakube ufumbela amalahle avuthayo ekhanda laso . "
45012021	Unganqotshwa ngokubi , kodwa nqoba okubi ngokuhle .
45013001	Akube yilowo nalowo azithobe phansi kwamandla ombuso , ngokuba akukho mandla ombuso angaveli kuNkulunkulu ; lawa akhona amiswe nguNkulunkulu .
45013002	Ngakho-ke omelana namandla ombuso umelana nesimiso sikaNkulunkulu ; kepha abamelana nakho bayakwamukeliswa ukulahlwa .
45013003	Ngokuba ababusi abesabeki kwabenza okuhle , kodwa kwabenza okubi . Kepha uyathanda yini ukungesabi amandla ombuso na ? Yenza okuhle , uyakubongwa yiwo ;
45013004	ngokuba uyisikhonzi sikaNkulunkulu , kube kuhle kuwe . Kepha uma wenza okubi , yesaba ; ngokuba awuyiphatheli ize inkemba ; ngokuba uyisikhonzi sikaNkulunkulu , umphindiseli wokwehlisela ulaka kowenza okubi .
45013005	Ngalokho kuswelekile ukuwuthobela , kungabi kuphela ngenxa yolaka kodwa nangenxa kanembeza .
45013006	Ngokuba ngenxa yalokho nikhipha intela ; ngokuba bayizikhonzi zikaNkulunkulu ezikhuthalela khona lokho .
45013007	Nikani bonke okubafaneleyo : intela kofanele intela , inkokhiso kofanele inkokhiso , ukwesaba kofanele ukwesatshwa , udumo kofanele udumo .
45013008	Ningabi nacala lani nakubani , kuphela elokuthandana ; ngokuba othanda omunye uwugcwalisile umthetho .
45013009	Ngokuba lokhu ukuthi : " Ungaphingi , ungabulali , ungebi , ungafisi , " noma ukhona omunye umyalelo , kuyahlanganiswa kuleli zwi elithi : " Wothanda umakhelwane wakho njengalokhu uzithanda wena . "
45013010	Uthando alwenzi okubi kumakhelwane ; ngakho-ke uthando lungukugcwaliseka komthetho .
45013011	Yenzani lokhu , njengokuba nazi isikhathi ukuthi sekuyihora lokuba nivuke ebuthongweni ; ngokuba manje insindiso isisondele kithi kunaleso sikhathi esaqala ukukholwa ngaso .
45013012	Ubusuku sebuyaphela , imini isisondele . Ngakho-ke asilahle imisebenzi yobumnyama , sihlome izikhali zokukhanya .
45013013	Asihambe ngokufaneleyo njengasemini , kungabi ngokuminza nokudakwa , kungabi ngobufebe namanyala , kungabi ngokuxabana nomhawu ;
45013014	kodwa yembathani iNkosi uJesu Kristu , ninganakekeli inyama kuvuswe izinkanuko .
45014001	Kepha obuthakathaka ekukholweni mamukeleni , kungabi ngokwahlulela ngezizindlo .
45014002	Omunye ukholwa ukuthi angadla konke , kepha obuthakathaka udla imifino .
45014003	Odlayo angamdeleli ongadliyo , ongadliyo angamahluleli odlayo , ngokuba uNkulunkulu umamukele .
45014004	Ungubani wena owahlulela inceku yomunye na ? Kusenkosini yayo ukuma noma ukuwa kwayo ; kepha iyakumiswa , ngokuba iNkosi inamandla okuyimisa .
45014005	Omunye wazisa olunye usuku kunolunye , omunye wazisa izinsuku zonke ; yilowo nalowo akaqiniseke enhliziyweni yakhe .
45014006	Ohlonipha usuku uluhloniphela iNkosi ; nodlayo udlela iNkosi , ngokuba ubonga uNkulunkulu ; nongadliyo , akadli ngenxa yeNkosi , ubonga uNkulunkulu .
45014007	Ngokuba akakho phakathi kwethu oziphilela yena , akakho nozifela yena ;
45014008	ngokuba uma siphila , siphilela iNkosi ; uma sifa , sifela iNkosi . Ngakho-ke noma siphila noma sifa , singabeNkosi .
45014009	Ngokuba ngenxa yalokho uKristu wafa , wabuye waphila ukuba abe yiNkosi yabafileyo neyabaphilayo .
45014010	Kepha wena umahlulelelani umzalwane wakho na ? Futhi umdelelelani umzalwane wakho na ? Ngokuba sonke siyakumiswa phambi kwesihlalo sokwahlulela sikaNkulunkulu .
45014011	Ngokuba kulotshiwe ukuthi : " ‘ Kuphila kwami , ’ isho iNkosi , ‘ kimina ayakuguqa amadolo onke , nezilimi zonke ziyakudumisa uNkulunkulu . ’ "
45014012	Ngalokho-ke yilowo nalowo phakathi kwethu uyakuziphendulela kuNkulunkulu .
45014013	Ngakho masingabe sisahlulelana ; kepha okungcono yahlulelani lokho kokuthi makungabekelwa umzalwane into yokumqhuzula nokuba isikhubekiso .
45014014	Ngiyazi , nganelisiwe eNkosini uJesu , ukuthi akukho lutho oluyichilo ngokwalo ; kepha kuye othi lubi , kuyena lubi .
45014015	Ngokuba uma umzalwane wakho edabukiswa ngenxa yokudla , awusahambi ngothando . Ungambhubhisi ngokudla kwakho lowo amfelayo uKristu .
45014016	Ngalokho okuhle kwenu makungahlanjalazwa .
45014017	Ngokuba umbuso kaNkulunkulu awusikho ukudla nokuphuza kepha ungukulunga , nokuthula , nokuthokoza eMoyeni oNgcwele ,
45014018	ngokuba okhonza uKristu kulokhu uthandekile kuNkulunkulu , ukholekile kubantu .
45014019	Ngalokho-ke asijonge okokuthula nokokwakhana .
45014020	Ungawuchithi umsebenzi kaNkulunkulu ngenxa yokudla . Konke kuhlanzekile , kepha kubi kulowo muntu okudla ekhubeka .
45014021	Kuhle ukungayidli inyama nokungaliphuzi iwayini noma okunye umzalwane wakho aqhuzuka ngakho .
45014022	Ukukholwa onakho , yiba nakho ngokwakho phambi kukaNkulunkulu . Ubusisiwe ongazahluleli ngalokho akukhethayo ;
45014023	kepha ongabazayo , nxa edla , ulahliwe , ngokuba kungengokukholwa ; konke okungaveli ekukholweni kuyisono .
45015001	Kepha thina esinamandla sifanele ukuthwala ubuthakathaka babangenamandla singazithokozisi thina .
45015002	Yilowo nalowo kithi makathokozise umakhelwane , kube kuhle , aze akheke ,
45015003	ngokuba noKristu akazithokozisanga yena , kepha kunjengokuba kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Ukuthuka kwabakuthukayo kwehlela phezu kwami . "
45015004	Ngokuba konke okwalotshwa ngaphambili kwalotshelwa ukufundiswa kwethu , ukuze ngokubekezela nangenduduzo yemibhalo sibe nethemba .
45015005	Kepha uNkulunkulu wokubekezela nowenduduzo makaniphe nibe nokuqonda kunye phakathi kwenu ngokukaKristu Jesu ,
45015006	ukuze nganhliziyonye nidumise ngamlomo munye uNkulunkulu uYise weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu .
45015007	Ngalokho yamukelanani , njengalokho noKristu wasamukela , ukuze kudunyiswe uNkulunkulu .
45015008	Ngokuba ngithi uKristu waba yisikhonzi sabasokileyo ngenxa yeqiniso likaNkulunkulu , ukuze aqinise izithembiso ezaphiwa okhokho ,
45015009	abezizwe bamdumise uNkulunkulu ngenxa yesihawu sakhe , njengalokho kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Ngalokho ngiyakukudumisa phakathi kwabezizwe , ngihubele igama lakho ; "
45015010	abuye athi : " Jabulani nina bezizwe kanye nesizwe sakhe , "
45015011	nokuthi : " Dumisani iNkosi nina nonke bezizwe , niyibabaze , nina bantu bonke . "
45015012	Futhi u-Isaya uthi : " Kuyakuba khona impande kaJesayi , yena oyakuvuka abuse abezizwe ; abezizwe bayakwethembela kuye . "
45015013	UNkulunkulu wethemba makanigcwalise ngenjabulo yonke nangokuthula konke ekukholweni , ukuze nivame ethembeni ngamandla kaMoya oNgcwele .
45015014	Kepha nami ngokwami nganelisiwe ngani bazalwane bami ukuthi nanigcwele ukuva , nigcwalisiwe ngokwazi konke , ninamandla futhi okuyalana .
45015015	Kepha nginilobele kokunye ngesibindi njengonikhumbuzayo futhi ngenxa yomusa engiwuphiwe nguNkulunkulu
45015016	wokuba ngibe yisikhonzi sikaKristu Jesu kwabezizwe , ngikhonze ivangeli likaNkulunkulu njengompristi , ukuze abezizwe babe ngumnikelo owamukeleka kahle , ungcwelisiwe ngoMoya oNgcwele .
45015017	Ngalokho nginokuzibonga kuKristu Jesu maqondana nokukaNkulunkulu ,
45015018	ngokuba angiyikuba nasibindi sokukhuluma lutho ngaphandle kwezinto uKristu azisebenza ngami , kube ngukulalela kwabezizwe , ngezwi nangesenzo ,
45015019	ngamandla ezibonakaliso nezimangaliso , ngamandla kaMoya oNgcwele , njengokuba ngasuka eJerusalema , ngazungeza ngaze ngafika e-Iliriku , ngishumayela ivangeli likaKristu ngokupheleleyo .
45015020	Kanjalo ngangihlose ukushumayela ivangeli kungabi lapho uKristu waziwa khona , ukuze ngingakhi phezu kwesisekelo somunye ,
45015021	kodwa njengalokho kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Abangabikelwanga ngaye bayakubona , nabangezwanga bayakuqonda . "
45015022	Ngenxa yalokho ngathiyeka kaningi ukuza kini ;
45015023	kepha manje , lokhu ngingasenandawo kulawa mazwe , futhi sekuyiminyaka eminingi ngilangazelela ukuza kini ,
45015024	ngiyakuza nxa ngiya eSpaniya ; ngokuba ngiyethemba ukuthi ekudluleni kwami ngizakunibona , ngikhashwe yinina , nxa ngiya khona , uma sengike nganeliswa yinina ;
45015025	kepha manje ngisaya eJerusalema ngiyokhonza abangcwele .
45015026	Ngokuba kwaba kuhle kwabaseMakedoniya nabase-Akhaya ukwenzela abampofu kwabangcwele baseJerusalema umnikelo othile .
45015027	Kwaba kuhle , ngokuba nembala banecala kubo ; ngokuba uma abezizwe behlanganyela nabo ezintweni zabo zokomoya , banecala futhi lokubakhonza ngezokwenyama .
45015028	Ngakho nxa sengikufezile lokho , ngabeka leso sithelo esandleni sabo , ngizakuhamba , ngidlule ngakini , ngiye eSpaniya ;
45015029	kepha ngiyazi ukuthi nxa ngifika kini , ngizakuza nokugcwala kwesibusiso sikaKristu .
45015030	Ngiyanincenga , bazalwane , ngenxa yeNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu nangenxa yothando lukaMoya ukuba nilwe kanye nami ekungikhulekeleni kuNkulunkulu ,

45015033	UNkulunkulu wokuthula makabe nani nonke . Amen .
45016001	Ngiyamncoma kini uFebe , udadewethu oyisikhonzi sebandla laseKenikreya ,
45016002	ukuze nimamukele eNkosini njengokufanele abangcwele , nimsize noma kuyiphi into angase ayidinge kini , ngokuba yena ube ngumsizi wabaningi , nowami uqobo .
45016003	Khonzani koPriska no-Akwila , izisebenzi ezikanye nami kuKristu Jesu ,
45016004	abadela ukuphila kwabo ngenxa yokuphila kwami , engibabongayo , kungeyimi ngedwa , kodwa namabandla onke abezizwe .
45016005	Khonzani nasebandleni elisendlini yabo . Khonzani ku-Ephenetu , isithandwa sami , ongulibo lwase-Asiya kuKristu .
45016006	Khonzani kuMariya owanisebenzela kakhulu .
45016007	Khonzani ko-Anidroniku noJuniya abayizihlobo zami , ababe yiziboshwa kanye nami , abaqhamileyo kubaphostoli nababe kuKristu ngaphambi kwami .
45016008	Khonzani ku-Ampiliyatu , isithandwa sami eNkosini .
45016009	Khonzani ku-Urbanu , isisebenzi kanye nathi kuKristu nakuStaku , isithandwa sami .
45016010	Khonzani ku-Aphele , othembekileyo kuKristu . Khonzani kwabakwa-Arisitobulu .
45016011	Khonzani kuHerodiyone , isihlobo sami . Khonzani kwabakwaNarkisu abaseNkosini .
45016012	Khonzani koTrifina noTrifosa abakhandleka eNkosini . Khonzani kuPersisi othandekayo , owakhandleka kakhulu eNkosini .
45016013	Khonzani kuRufu okhethiweyo eNkosini nakunina ongumame .
45016014	Khonzani ko-Asinkiritu , noFilegu , noHerme , noPhatroba , noHerma nabazalwane abanabo .
45016015	Khonzani koFilologu noJuliya , kuNerewu nodadewabo , naku-Olimpa nakwabangcwele bonke abanabo .
45016016	Bingelelanani ngokwanga okungcwele . Ayakhonza kini onke amabandla kaKristu .
45016017	Ngiyanincenga , bazalwane , ukuba niqaphele ababanga ukwahlukana nokukhubekisa , bephambene nesifundiso enafundiswa sona nina , nahlukane nabo ;
45016018	ngokuba abanjalo abayikhonzi iNkosi yethu uKristu , bakhonza isisu sabo ; nangamazwi amahle namnandi bakhohlisa izinhliziyo zabangenacala .
45016019	Ngokuba ukulalela kwenu kuzwakele kubo bonke ; ngakho-ke ngiyathokoza ngani , kepha ngithanda ukuba nihlakaniphe kokuhle , nibe ngabangahlakaniphile kokubi .
45016020	Kepha uNkulunkulu wokuthula uzakumchoboza masinyane uSathane phansi kwezinyawo zenu . Umusa weNkosi yethu uKristu mawube nani .
45016021	Uyakhonza kini uThimothewu , isisebenzi kanye nami , noLukiyu , noJasoni , noSosiphatru , izihlobo zami .
45016022	Mina Tertiyu engilobe le ncwadi ngiyakhonza kini eNkosini .
45016023	Uyakhonza kini uGayu ongingenise kwakhe , mina nebandla lonke . Uyakhonza kini u-Erastu , umphathisikhwama womuzi , noKwartu umzalwane .
45016024	Umusa weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu mawube nani nonke . Amen .
45016025	Kuye onamandla okuniqinisa ngokwevangeli lami nentshumayelo kaJesu Kristu , ngokwambulwa kwemfihlakalo eyayifihliwe ngezikhathi zaphakade
45016026	kepha manje isibonakalisiwe ngemibhalo yabaprofethi , ngokomyalo kaNkulunkulu ongunaphakade , yazisiwe ezizweni zonke , kube ngukulalela kokukholwa ,
45016027	kuye uNkulunkulu onokwazi yedwa akube kuye inkazimulo ngoJesu Kristu kuze kube phakade . Amen .
46001001	UPawulu , obizelwe ngentando kaNkulunkulu ukuba abe ngumphostoli kaJesu Kristu , noSostene umzalwane ,
46001002	kulo ibandla likaNkulunkulu eliseKorinte , kubo abangcwelisiwe kuKristu Jesu , ababiziweyo abangcwele , kanye nabo bonke abakhuleka egameni leNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu ezindaweni zonke , eyabo neyethu :
46001003	Makube kini umusa nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba wethu naseNkosini uJesu Kristu .
46001004	Ngibonga uNkulunkulu wami ngesikhathi sonke ngani ngenxa yomusa kaNkulunkulu eniwuphiweyo kuKristu Jesu
46001005	ukuthi ezintweni zonke nicetshisiwe kuye , ekukhulumeni konke nasekwazini konke ,
46001006	njengalokho ubufakazi ngoKristu baqiniswa kini ,
46001007	ukuze ningasilalelwa nasinye isiphiwo somusa , nisahlalele ukwambulwa kweNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu ,
46001008	yena oyakuniqinisa nani kuze kube sekupheleni , ningabi nacala ngosuku lweNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu .
46001009	Uthembekile uNkulunkulu , okungaye nabizelwa ekuhlanganyeleni neNdodana yakhe uJesu Kristu iNkosi yethu .
46001010	Kepha ngiyanincenga , bazalwane , ngegama leNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu ukuba nikhulume zwilinye nonke , kungabikho ukwahlukana phakathi kwenu , kodwa nipheleliswe emqondweni munye nasekuboneni kunye .
46001011	Ngokuba ngitsheliwe ngani bazalwane bami ngabendlu kaKlowe ukuthi kukhona ukuphikisana phakathi kwenu .
46001012	Ngisho lokhu ukuthi yilowo nalowo kini uthi : " Mina ngingokaPawulu " ; " Mina ngingoka-Apholo " ; " Mina ngingokaKhefase " ; " Mina ngingokaKristu " .
46001013	UKristu wahlukanisiwe yini ? UPawulu wabethelwa esiphambanweni ngenxa yenu na ? Nabhapathizwa egameni likaPawulu na ?

46001016	Kodwa ngabhapathiza nabendlu kaStefana ; ngaphandle kwalokho angazi ukuba ngabhapathiza omunye .
46001017	Ngokuba uKristu kangithumanga ukuba ngibhapathize , kepha ukuba ngishumayele ivangeli , kungabi ngokuhlakanipha kwamazwi , funa isiphambano sikaKristu senziwe ize .
46001018	Ngokuba izwi lesiphambano kwababhubhayo lingubuwula , kepha kithina esisindiswayo lingamandla kaNkulunkulu .

46001020	Siphi isazi na ? Uphi umbhali na ? Uphi umphikisi walesi sikhathi na ? UNkulunkulu kakwenzanga kube yize ukuhlakanipha kwaleli zwe na ?
46001021	Ngokuba njengalokho ekuhlakanipheni kukaNkulunkulu izwe alimazanga uNkulunkulu ngokuhlakanipha kwalo , kwaba kuhle kuNkulunkulu ukusindisa abakholwayo ngobuwula bentshumayelo .
46001022	Ngokuba abaJuda babiza izibonakaliso , namaGreki afuna ukuhlakanipha ,

46001025	Ngokuba ubuwula bukaNkulunkulu buhlakaniphile kunabantu ; nobuthakathaka bukaNkulunkulu bunamandla kunabantu .
46001026	Ngokuba bhekani ukubizwa kwenu bazalwane : kababaningi abahlakaniphileyo ngokwenyama , kababaningi abanamandla , kababaningi abayizikhulu ,

46001028	nezinto eziphansi zezwe nezinto ezidelelwayo uNkulunkulu wazikhetha , nezinto ezingekho , ukuba achithe ezikhona ,
46001029	ukuze kungabikho nyama ezibongayo phambi kukaNkulunkulu .

46002001	Nami , bazalwane , ekufikeni kwami kini angifikanga ngobungcweti bokukhuluma nobokuhlakanipha , ngimemezele kini ubufakazi bukaNkulunkulu .
46002002	Ngokuba nganquma ukuthi angiyikwazi okunye phakathi kwenu , kuphela uJesu Kristu , lowo obethelwe esiphambanweni .
46002003	Mina ngangikini ngobuthakathaka , nangokwesaba , nangokuthuthumela okukhulu ;
46002004	nokukhuluma kwami nokushumayela kwami akubanga ngamazwi okuhlakanipha ahungayo , kepha kwaba ngesibonakaliso sikaMoya nesamandla ,
46002005	ukuze ukukholwa kwenu kungemi ngokuhlakanipha kwabantu , kume ngamandla kaNkulunkulu .
46002006	Kepha ukuhlakanipha sikukhuluma phakathi kwabapheleleyo , ukuhlakanipha kambe okungesikho okwalesi sikhathi nokwababusi balesi sikhathi , ababhubhayo .
46002007	Kodwa sikhuluma ukuhlakanipha kukaNkulunkulu emfihlakalweni efihliweyo uNkulunkulu akumisela ngaphambili kube yinkazimulo yethu , kusukela kwaphakade ,
46002008	okungaziwa namunye wababusi balesi sikhathi ; ngokuba uma bebekwazi , babengayikuyibethela esiphambanweni iNkosi yenkazimulo ;
46002009	kepha kunjengokuba kulotshiwe ukuthi : " Lokho iso elingakubonanga , nendlebe engakuzwanga , okungavelanga enhliziyweni yamuntu , uNkulunkulu akulungisela abamthandayo . "
46002010	Ngokuba kithina uNkulunkulu ukwambulile ngoMoya ; ngokuba uMoya uhlolisisa konke , yebo , nokujulileyo kukaNkulunkulu .
46002011	Ngokuba ngumuphi kubantu owazi okomuntu , uma kungesiye umoya womuntu okuye na ? Ngokunjalo nokukaNkulunkulu akwaziwa muntu , kuphela nguMoya kaNkulunkulu .
46002012	Kepha thina asamukelanga umoya wezwe kodwa umoya ovela kuNkulunkulu , ukuze sikwazi esikuphiwe nguNkulunkulu ngomusa ,
