48006004	Kepha makube yilowo nalowo ahlole owakhe umsebenzi , yikhona eyakuba nokubongwa ngokungokwakhe yedwa , kungengokomunye ,
48006005	ngokuba yilowo nalowo uyakuthwala owakhe umthwalo .
48006006	Kepha yena ofundiswa izwi makahlanganyele nalowo omfundisayo kuzo zonke izinto ezinhle .
48006007	Ningaduki ; uNkulunkulu akahlekwa . Ngokuba lokho akuhlwanyelayo umuntu , lokho wokuvuna .
48006008	Ngokuba ohlwanyelela inyama yakhe uyakuvuna ukubhubha kuyo inyama ; kepha ohlwanyelela uMoya uyakuvuna ukuphila okuphakade kuMoya .
48006009	Kepha masingakhathali ekwenzeni okuhle , ngokuba siyakuvuna ngesikhathi esifaneleyo , uma singadangali .
48006010	Ngakho-ke njengokuba sinethuba , asenze okuhle kubo bonke , kepha ikakhulu kwabendlu yokukholwa .
48006011	Ake nibone ukuloba okungaka enginilobele ngakho ngesami isandla .
48006012	Bonke abafuna ukubukeka enyameni , yibona abaniphoqela ukusoka , kuphela ukuba bangayikuzingelwa ngenxa yesiphambano sikaKristu .
48006013	Ngokuba ngisho bona abasokayo nabo kabawugcini umthetho , kodwa bathanda ukuba nisoke , ukuze bazibonge ngenyama yenu .
48006014	Kepha kimi makungabikho nakanye ukuzibonga , kuphela ngesiphambano seNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu , okubethelwe ngaye izwe kimi nami kulo izwe .
48006015	Ngokuba nakusoka nakungasoki akulutho , isidalwa esisha kuphela .
48006016	Bonke abahamba ngale ndlela makube kubo ukuthula nesihawu , yebo , ku-Israyeli kaNkulunkulu .
48006017	Mangingabe ngisakhathazwa muntu , ngokuba ngiphethe emzimbeni wami izimpawu zikaJesu .
48006018	Umusa weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu mawube nomoya wenu , bazalwane . Amen .
49001001	UPawulu , umphostoli kaKristu Jesu ngentando kaNkulunkulu , kubo abangcwele abase-Efesu nakubo abakholwa nguKristu Jesu :
49001002	Makube kini umusa nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba wethu naseNkosini uJesu Kristu .
49001003	Makabongwe uNkulunkulu , uYise weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu osibusisile ezulwini kuKristu ngesibusiso sonke sokomoya ,
49001004	njengalokho asikhethela kuye ngothando ngaphambi kokusekelwa kwezwe ukuba sibe ngcwele , singabi nakusolwa phambi kwakhe ;
49001005	wasimisela ngaphambili ukuba sibe ngabantwana kuye ngoJesu Kristu , njengalokho kwaba kuhle kuye ngentando yakhe ,
49001006	ukuze kutuswe inkazimulo yomusa wakhe asiphe wona ngesihle ngaye oThandiweyo ;
49001007	esinokuhlengwa kuye ngegazi lakhe , ukuthethelelwa kwezono ngokwengcebo yomusa wakhe
49001008	awuvamisa kithi ngakho konke ukuhlakanipha nokuqonda ,
49001009	esazisa imfihlakalo yentando yakhe njengokuzibonela kwakhe azimisela khona ngaphambili ,
49001010	kuze kube yihlelo lokuphelela kwezikhathi lokuba kuhlanganiselwe ndawonye kuKristu konke okusezulwini nokusemhlabeni ;
49001011	kuyena esabelwa futhi ifa kuye , esakumiselwa ngaphambili ngokwesimiso salowo osebenza izinto zonke ngokunquma kwentando yakhe ,
49001012	ukuze sibe ludumo lwenkazimulo yakhe , thina esethemba ngaphambili kuKristu ;
49001013	kuye nani esenizwile izwi leqiniso , ivangeli lokusindiswa kwenu , enakholwa nguye futhi , nani nabekwa uphawu olunguMoya oNgcwele wesithembiso
49001014	oyisibambiso sefa lethu , kube ngukuhlengwa kokungokwakhe , ukuze kutuswe inkazimulo yakhe .
49001015	Ngalokho nami , sengizwile ngokukholwa okukini eNkosini uJesu nothando kubo bonke abangcwele ,
49001016	angiyeki ukubonga ngenxa yenu , nginikhumbula emikhulekweni yami ,
49001017	ukuze uNkulunkulu weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu , uYise wenkazimulo , aniphe umoya wokuhlakanipha nokwambulelwa ekumazini yena ;
49001018	ekhanyisiwe amehlo enhliziyo yenu , nize nazi okuyithemba lobizo lwakhe nokuyingcebo yenkazimulo yefa lakhe kubo abangcwele ,
49001019	nokungubukhulu obumangalisayo bamandla akhe kithina esikholwayo , ngokokusebenza kwamandla akhe amakhulu
49001020	asebenze ngawo kuKristu emvusa kwabafileyo , wamhlalisa ngakwesokunene sakhe ezulwini ,
49001021	ngaphezu kwakho konke ukubusa , negunya , namandla , nobukhosi , namagama onke aphathwayo , kungekuleli zwe lodwa kepha nakulo elizayo ;
49001022	wakubeka konke phansi kwezinyawo zakhe , wammisa abe yinhloko phezu kwakho konke kulo ibandla ,
49001023	elona lingumzimba wakhe , ukugcwala kwakhe ogcwalisa konke kubo bonke .
49002001	Uniphilisile nani enanifile ngeziphambeko nangezono zenu ,
49002002	enanikade nihamba kuzo ngokwendlela yaleli zwe , ngokombusi wamandla omkhathi , ongumoya osasebenza kubantwana bokungalaleli ,
49002003	esasikade sihamba phakathi kwabo sonke ezinkanukweni zenyama yethu , senza intando yenyama neyengqondo ; ngemvelo sasingabantwana bolaka njengabo abanye .
49002004	Kepha uNkulunkulu ecebile ngesihawu , ngenxa yothando lwakhe olukhulu asithanda ngalo ,
49002005	sesifile ngeziphambeko , wenza siphile kanye noKristu — kungomusa nisindisiwe —
49002006	wasivusa kanye naye , wasihlalisa kanye naye embusweni wezulu kuKristu Jesu ,
49002007	kuze kuthi ezikhathini ezizayo abonakalise ingcebo enkulu yomusa wakhe ngobubele kithina kuKristu Jesu .
49002008	Ngokuba ngomusa nisindisiwe ngokukholwa ; nalokhu akuveli kini , kuyisipho sikaNkulunkulu ;
49002009	akuveli ngemisebenzi , ukuze kungabikho ozibongayo .
49002010	Ngokuba singumsebenzi wakhe kuKristu Jesu , sidalelwe imisebenzi emihle ayilungisela ngaphambili uNkulunkulu ukuba sihambe kuyo .
49002011	Ngakho khumbulani ukuthi nina enanikade ningabezizwe ngokwenyama , ababizwa ngokuthi abangasoki yilabo ababizwa ngokuthi abokusoka , okwenziwa ngezandla enyameni ,
49002012	ukuthi ngaleso sikhathi naningenaye uKristu , naningaphandle kombuso ka-Israyeli , naningabafokazi ezivumelwaneni zesithembiso , ningenathemba , ningenaNkulunkulu ezweni .
49002013	Kepha manje kuKristu Jesu nina enanikade nikude senenziwe abaseduze ngegazi likaKristu .
49002014	Ngokuba yena ungukuthula kwethu , owenza kokubili kwaba kunye , nowabhidliza udonga olwahlukanisayo olungubutha ,
49002015	ngenyama yakhe ewenzile ize umthetho wemiyalo esezimisweni ukuba adale kuyena labo ababili babe muntu munye omusha , enze ukuthula ,
49002016	enze futhi ukuba bobabili babuyisane noNkulunkulu emzimbeni munye ngesiphambano , esebulele ubutha ngakho .
49002017	Weza washumayela ivangeli lokuthula kinina enanikude , yebo , ukuthula nakubo abaseduze .
49002018	Ngokuba ngaye sinokungena sobabili ngoMoya munye kuYise .
49002019	Ngakho aniseyibo abafokazi nezihambi , kodwa senimbuso munye nabangcwele , ningabendlu kaNkulunkulu ,
49002020	nakhiwe phezu kwesisekelo sabaphostoli nabaprofethi , uKristu Jesu uqobo lwakhe eyitshe legumbi ,
49002021	okuhlanganiselwe kuye isakhiwo sonke , sikhule sibe yithempeli elingcwele eNkosini ,
49002022	okukuyo nani , nakhiwe kanye nabanye , ukuba nibe yindlu kaNkulunkulu ngoMoya .
49003001	Ngenxa yalokho mina Pawulu ngiyisiboshwa sikaKristu Jesu ngenxa yenu nina bezizwe —
49003002	uma ngabe senizwile ngohlelo lomusa kaNkulunkulu engiwuphiweyo ngenxa yenu
49003003	ukuthi ngaziswa imfihlakalo ngesambulo , njengalokho sengaloba ngokufushane —
49003004	okungakho , nxa nikufunda , ningaqonda ukwazi kwami ngemfihlakalo kaKristu ,
49003005	bengayaziswanga abantwana babantu ezizukulwaneni ezinye , njengalokhu isiyambuliwe manje kubaphostoli bakhe abangcwele nabaprofethi ngoMoya
49003006	ukuthi abezizwe bayizindlalifa kanye nathi , nokuthi bamzimba munye nathi , nokuthi bangabahlanganyeli besithembiso kanye nathi kuKristu Jesu ngevangeli ;
49003007	engenziwa isikhonzi salo ngokwesipho somusa kaNkulunkulu engiwuphiwe ngokokusebenza kwamandla akhe .
49003008	Mina engimncinyane kunabo bonke abangcwele ngaphiwa lowo musa wokushumayeza abezizwe ivangeli lengcebo kaKristu engaphenyekiyo
49003009	nokubakhanyisela ukuthi luyini uhlelo lwemfihlakalo ebifihliwe kwaphakade kuNkulunkulu owadala izinto zonke ,
49003010	ukuze imibuso nabanamandla emazulwini baziswe manje ngebandla ukuhlakanipha okuninginingi kukaNkulunkulu ,
49003011	ngokwecebo laphakade alenza ngoKristu Jesu iNkosi yethu ;
49003012	okungaye sinesibindi ukungena ngokwethemba , ngokukholwa nguye .
49003013	Ngalokho ngiyacela ukuba ningadangali ngezinhlupheko zami ngenxa yenu , okuludumo lwenu .
49003014	Ngenxa yalokho ngiguqa ngamadolo ami kuYise ,
49003015	eyethiwa ngaye imindeni yonke ezulwini nasemhlabeni ,
49003016	ukuba ngokwengcebo yenkazimulo yakhe aninike ukuqiniseka emandleni ngoMoya wakhe kumuntu ongaphakathi ;
49003017	uKristu ahlale ezinhliziyweni zenu ngokukholwa , ukuze nigxile , nisekelwe othandweni ,
49003018	nibe namandla okuqonda kanye nabangcwele bonke okungububanzi , nobude , nokuphakama , nokujula ,
49003019	nokulwazi uthando lukaKristu oludlula ukwazi konke , ukuze nigcwaliswe kube ngukugcwala konke kukaNkulunkulu .
49003020	Kepha yena onamandla okwenza okukhulu kakhulu kunakho konke esikucelayo nesikuqondayo ngokwamandla asebenza kithi ,
49003021	makube kuye udumo ebandleni nakuKristu Jesu ezizukulwaneni zonke zaphakade naphakade . Amen .
49004001	Ngakho mina siboshwa eNkosini ngiyanincenga ukuba nihambe ngokufanele ukubizwa enabizwa ngakho ,
49004002	ngokuthobeka konke nobumnene , ngokubheka kade nokubekezelelana ngothando ,
49004003	nikhuthalele ukugcina ubunye bukaMoya ngesibopho sokuthula ;
49004004	munye umzimba , munye uMoya , njengalokho nabizelwa ethembeni linye lokubizwa kwenu ;
49004005	yinye iNkosi , yinye inkolo , munye umbhapathizo ;
49004006	munye uNkulunkulu , uYise wabo bonke , ophezu kwabo bonke , okubo bonke , ophakathi kwabo bonke .
49004007	Kepha yilowo nalowo kithina uphiwe umusa ngokwesilinganiso sesipho sikaKristu .
49004008	Ngalokho uthi : " Esenyukele phezulu wathumba abathunjiweyo , wapha abantu izipho . "
49004009	Kepha lokhu ukuthi wenyuka , kuthini , uma kungesikho ukuthi wake wehlela ezindaweni zomhlaba eziphansi na ?
49004010	Owehlayo nguyena owenyukela futhi ngaphezu kwamazulu onke , ukuze agcwalise konke .
49004011	Nguyena futhi owanika abanye ukuba babe ngabaphostoli , abanye abaprofethi , abanye abavangeli , abanye abelusi nabafundisi ,
49004012	ukuze abangcwele bapheleliselwe umsebenzi wokukhonza , kwakhiwe umzimba kaKristu ,
49004013	size sifinyelele sonke ebunyeni bokukholwa nasekwazini iNdodana kaNkulunkulu , ebudodeni obupheleleyo , esilinganisweni sobukhulu sokugcwala kukaKristu ,
49004014	ukuze singabe sisaba yizingane , sishukunyiswa okwamaza , sipheshulwa yimimoya yonke yezifundiso ngenkohliso yabantu , ngobuqili obunamacebo okudukisayo ;
49004015	kodwa sithi sikhuluma iqiniso ngothando , sikhulele ngakho konke kuye oyinhloko , uKristu ,
49004016	okungaye umzimba wonke uhlanganisiwe , ubambene ngokwelekelelana kwamalungu onke awo njengokusebenza okulinganiselwe yilelo nalelo lungu , kukhuliswe umzimba , ube yisakhiwo othandweni .
49004017	Ngakho ngisho , ngifakaza eNkosini , ngithi ningabe nisahamba njengalokhu kuhamba abezizwe ebuzeni bengqondo yabo ,
49004018	behlwelwe emqondweni , behlukanisiwe nokuphila kukaNkulunkulu ngokungazi okukubo ngenxa yobulukhuni benhliziyo yabo ,
49004019	abathi bebuthuntu , bazinikela emanyaleni , ukuze basebenze ukungcola konke ngokuhuheka .
49004020	Kepha nina animfundanga uKristu kanjalo ,
49004021	uma-ke nimzwile nafundiswa kuye , njengokuba iqiniso likuJesu ,
49004022	ukuba nikhumule umuntu omdala ongowenkambo yokuqala , owonakala ngezinkanuko zenkohliso ,
49004023	nenziwe basha emoyeni wengqondo yenu ,
49004024	nembathe umuntu omusha owadalwa ngokukaNkulunkulu ekulungeni nasebungcweleni beqiniso .
49004025	Ngakho lahlani amanga , nikhulume iqiniso , yilowo nalowo nomakhelwane wakhe , lokhu singamalungu omunye komunye .
49004026	Thukuthelani ningoni ; ilanga malingashoni nisathukuthele .
49004027	Ningamniki uSathane indawo .
49004028	Owebayo angabe eseba , kepha kunalokho akhuthale asebenze okuhle ngezandla zakhe , ukuze abe nokokwabela osweleyo .
49004029	Makungaphumi emlonyeni wenu nalinye izwi elibolileyo , kodwa kube ngelilungele ukwakha njengokuswelekileyo , ukuze libavezele umusa abezwayo .
49004030	Ningamdabukisi uMoya oNgcwele kaNkulunkulu enabekwa uphawu ngaye kuze kube lusuku lokuhlengwa .
49004031	Konke okubabayo , nentukuthelo , nolaka , nomsindo , nokuhlambalaza makususwe kini kanye nakho konke okubi .
49004032	Maniphathane ngobumnene , nihawukelane , nithethelelane , njengalokho noNkulunkulu wanithethelela ngoKristu .
49005001	Ngakho yibani ngabalingisa uNkulunkulu njengabantwana abathandekayo ,
49005002	nihambe othandweni , njengalokho uKristu wanithanda , wazinikela ngenxa yethu , abe ngumnikelo nomhlatshelo , abe yiphunga elimnandi kuNkulunkulu .
49005003	Kepha ubufebe , nakho konke ukungcola , noma isangabe , makungaphathwa nangegama phakathi kwenu , njengokuba kufanele abangcwele ,
49005004	nehlazo , nokubheda , nokulawula , okuyizinto ezingafanele , kepha kunalokho makube ngukubonga .
49005005	Ngokuba yazini lokhu , nikuqonde ukuthi akukho sifebe , noma ongcolileyo , noma onesangabe ongokhonza izithombe , onefa embusweni kaKristu noNkulunkulu .
49005006	Masingakhohliswa muntu ngamazwi ayize , ngokuba ngenxa yalezo zinto ulaka lukaNkulunkulu lwehlela phezu kwabantwana bokungalaleli .
49005007	Ngakho-ke ningabi ngabahlanganyela nabo .
49005008	Ngokuba kade naningubumnyama , kepha manje ningukukhanya eNkosini ; hambani njengabantwana bokukhanya ,
49005009	ngokuba izithelo zokukhanya zisebuhleni bonke nasekulungeni naseqinisweni ,
49005010	nihlole ukuthi kuyini okuthandeka eNkosini ,
49005011	ningahlanganyeli imisebenzi yobumnyama engenazithelo , kepha kunalokho niyidalule ;
49005012	ngokuba okwenziwa yibo ngasese kuyihlazo nokukhuluma ngakho .
49005013	Kepha konke okudalulwayo kubonakaliswa ngukukhanya , ngokuba konke okubonakaliswayo kungukukhanya .
49005014	Ngalokho uthi : " Phaphama wena oleleyo , uvuke kwabafileyo , uKristu uzakukukhanyisa . "
49005015	Ngakho-ke bhekisisani ukuthi nihamba kanjani , kungabi njengabangahlakaniphile kepha njengabahlakaniphileyo ,
49005016	nithengisise isikhathi , ngokuba izinsuku zimbi .
49005017	Ngakho-ke ningabi yiziwula , kodwa qondani okuyintando yeNkosi .
49005018	Ningadakwa yiwayini , kuvela kulo umhumheko , kodwa nigcwaliswe ngoMoya ,
49005019	niphendulane ngamahubo nangezihlabelelo nangamaculo okomoya , nihlabelele , nihubele iNkosi enhliziyweni yenu ,
49005020	nimbonge njalo uNkulunkulu uYise ngakho konke egameni leNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu ,
49005021	nithobelane ngokumesaba uKristu .
49005022	Abafazi mabathobele amadoda abo kungathi kukuyo iNkosi ,
49005023	ngokuba indoda iyinhloko yomfazi , njengokuba noKristu uyinhloko yebandla , yena engumsindisi womzimba .
49005024	Kepha njengokuba ibandla lithobela uKristu , kanjalo nabafazi mabathobele amadoda ezintweni zonke .
49005025	Madoda , thandani omkenu , njengalokho noKristu ulithandile ibandla , wazinikela ngenxa yalo
49005026	ukuba alingcwelise , alihlambulule ngesigezo samanzi ngezwi ,
49005027	ukuze azimisele ibandla elinenkazimulo , lingenasisihla , nambimbi , nanto enjalo , kodwa libe ngcwele lingenacala .
49005028	Kanjalo amadoda afanele ukuthanda omkawo njengemizimba yawo . Othanda umkakhe uzithanda yena .
49005029	Ngokuba akakho owake wazonda eyakhe inyama , kepha uyayondla , ayiphathe kahle , njengalokhu noKristu enza kulo ibandla ;
49005030	ngokuba singamalungu omzimba wakhe .
49005031	Ngenxa yalokho umuntu uyakushiya uyise nonina , anamathele kumkakhe ; labo ababili bayakuba nyamanye .
49005032	Le mfihlakalo inkulu , kepha ngikhuluma ngoKristu nebandla .
49005033	Nani-ke , yilowo nalowo makathande umkakhe njengokuba ezithanda yena , kepha umfazi makahloniphe indoda yakhe .
49006001	Bantwana , lalelani abazali benu eNkosini , ngokuba lokho kulungile .
49006002	Yazisa uyihlo nonyoko , okungumyalelo wokuqala onesithembiso :
49006003	ukuze kube kuhle kuwe , uhlale kade emhlabeni .
49006004	Nani boyise , ningabathukuthelisi abantwana benu , kodwa nibondle ngokuyala nangokuqondisa kweNkosi .
49006005	Zinceku , abangamakhosi enu ngokwenyama , balaleleni ngokwesaba nokuthuthumela ngobuqotho benhliziyo yenu kungathi kukuKristu ,
49006006	ningathengi amehlo njengabathokozisa abantu , kodwa njengezinceku zikaKristu nenze intando kaNkulunkulu ngenhliziyo ,
49006007	nikhonze ngothando kungathi kuseNkosini kungekubantu ,
49006008	nazi ukuthi konke okuhle yilowo nalowo akwenzayo , uzakukwamukela okunjalo eNkosini , noma eyinceku noma engokhululekileyo .
49006009	Nani makhosi , yenzani okunjalo kuzo , niyeke ukusongela , nazi ukuthi neyazo neyenu iNkosi isezulwini nokuthi ukukhetha umuntu akukho kuye .
49006010	Elokugcina , qinani eNkosini nasemandleni ayo amakhulu .
49006011	Hlomani izikhali zonke zikaNkulunkulu , ukuze nibe namandla okumelana namaqhinga kaSathane ;
49006012	ngokuba asibambene negazi nenyama , kodwa sibambene nemibuso , namandla , nababusi bezwe balobu bumnyama , nabawomoya bobubi emkhathini .
49006013	Ngakho hlomani izikhali zonke zikaNkulunkulu ukuba nibe namandla okuzabalaza ngosuku olubi , nalapho senifeze konke , nime .
49006014	Ngakho yimani izinkalo zenu ziboshiwe ngeqiniso , nifakile isivikelo sesifuba sokulunga ,
49006015	izinyawo zigqokisiwe ukulungela kukho ukushumayela ivangeli lokuthula ;
49006016	kukho konke nithathe isihlangu sokukholwa eniyakuba namandla okucima ngaso yonke imicibisholo evuthayo yomubi ,
49006017	namukele futhi isigqoko sensindiso , nenkemba kaMoya eyizwi likaNkulunkulu ,
49006018	ngokukhuleka konke nokunxusa , nikhuleka ngezikhathi zonke ngoMoya ; kulokho nilinde ngesineke sonke nangokunxusela abangcwele bonke ,
49006019	ninginxusele nami ukuba ngiphiwe izwi , nxa ngivula umlomo wami , ngize ngiyishumayele ngesibindi imfihlakalo yevangeli ;
49006020	engiyisithunywa ngalo esiboshiwe ngamaketanga , ukuze ngikhulume ngesibindi ngalo , njengokuba kufanele ukuba ngikhulume .
49006021	Kepha ukuba nani nazi okuqondene nami nalokhu engikwenzayo , uyakunazisa konke uThikhiku , umzalwane othandekayo nesikhonzi esikholekileyo eNkosini ,
49006022	engamthumela kini ngakho lokho ukuba nazi izindaba zethu , nokuba aduduze izinhliziyo zenu .
49006023	Ukuthula makube kubazalwane , nothando kanye nokukholwa okuvela kuNkulunkulu uYise naseNkosini uJesu Kristu .
49006024	Umusa mawube nabo bonke abathanda iNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu ngokunganqamukiyo .
50001001	OPawulu noThimothewu , izinceku zikaKristu Jesu , kubo bonke abangcwele kuKristu Jesu abaseFilipi , kanye nababonisi namadiyakoni :
50001002	Makube kini umusa nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba wethu naseNkosini uJesu Kristu .
50001003	Ngiyambonga uNkulunkulu wami ekunikhumbuleni kwami konke
50001004	ngezikhathi zonke ekunxuseni kwami konke ngani nonke , nginxusa ngokuthokoza ,
50001005	ngenxa yokuhlanganyela kwenu evangelini , kusukela osukwini lokuqala kuze kube manje ;
50001006	ngethembile ngempela yona le nto ukuthi owaqala umsebenzi omuhle kinina uyakuwufeza kuze kube lusuku lukaKristu Jesu ,
50001007	njengalokhu kufanele ukuba ngibe nomqondo onjalo ngani nonke , njengokuba nginithwele enhliziyweni yami , lokhu ekuboshweni kwami nasekulivikeleni nasekuliqiniseni ivangeli nina nonke nihlanganyele nami emseni .
50001008	Ngokuba uNkulunkulu ungufakazi wami wokuthi nginilangazelela kangakanani nonke ngesihe sikaJesu Kristu .
50001009	Ngikhulekela lokhu ukuba uthando lwenu luvame kakhulu njalo ekwazini nasekuqondeni konke ,
50001010	ukuze nikwazi ukwahlukanisa , nize nibe mhlophe nabangakhubekisiyo kuze kube lusuku lukaKristu ,
50001011	nigcwaliswe ngezithelo zokulunga ezingaye uJesu Kristu , kube yinkazimulo nodumo kuNkulunkulu .
50001012	Kepha ngithanda ukuba nazi , bazalwane , ukuthi lokho okwangehlelayo kugcine kwaveza ukuqhubeka kwevangeli ,
50001013	kwaze kwathi izibopho zami zabonakala enqabeni yonke nakubo bonke abanye ukuthi zingenxa kaKristu
50001014	nokuthi iningi labazalwane eNkosini betholile ithemba ngezibopho zami bazuzile kakhulu isibindi sokukhuluma izwi likaNkulunkulu ngokungesabi .
50001015	Abanye kambe bashumayela uKristu ngomhawu nangombango kepha abanye ngenhliziyo enhle ;
50001016	laba bashumayela ngothando , bazi ukuthi ngimiselwe ukuvikela ivangeli ,
50001017	kepha labo bamemezela uKristu ngombango kungenganhliziyo emhlophe , bethi bazakungivusela ukukhathazeka ekuboshweni kwami .
50001018	Kunani pho ? Nokho uKristu uyamenyezelwa ngezindlela zonke , noma ngokuzenzisa noma ngesiminya ; kulokho-ke ngiyathokoza , yebo , ngiyakuthokoza ,
50001019	ngokuba ngiyazi ukuthi lokhu kuyakungenzela ukusindiswa ngokunxusa kwenu nangokusiza kukaMoya kaJesu Kristu ,
50001020	njengokulangazela nokwethemba kwami ukuthi ayikho into engizakujabhiswa kuyo , kepha ngesibindi sonke , njengasezikhathini zonke namanje , uKristu uyakwenziwa mkhulu emzimbeni wami , nokuba kungokuphila nokuba kungokufa .
50001021	Ngokuba kimina ukuphila kunguKristu , ukufa kuyinzuzo .
50001022	Kepha uma ukuphila enyameni kuyisithelo somsebenzi kimi , angisakwazi engizakukukhetha .
50001023	Kepha ngiphakathi kokubili ; nginesifiso sokumuka ngibe noKristu , ngokuba yikhona okuhle kakhulu ;
50001024	kanti-ke ukuhlala enyameni kuswelekile kakhulu ngenxa yenu .
50001025	Lokhu nginalo leli themba , ngiyazi ukuthi ngiyakuhlala , yebo , ngihlale nani nonke , kube ngukuqhubeka nokuthokoza kwenu ekukholweni ,
50001026	ukuze ukuzibonga kwenu ngami kuvame kuKristu Jesu ngokufika kwami futhi kini .
50001027	Kuphela hambani ngokufanele ivangeli likaKristu , kuze kuthi , noma ngiza nginibona noma ngingekho , ngizwe izindaba zenu zokuthi nimi niqinile emoyeni munye , nangomphefumulo munye nilwela inkolo yevangeli ,
50001028	ningethuswa ngalutho ngabamelene nani , okuyisiboniso sokubhubha kubona kepha ngesokusindiswa kwenu ; lokhu-ke kuvela kuNkulunkulu .
50001029	Ngokuba ngenxa kaKristu nina nabelwa ngomusa , angisho ukukholwa kuye kuphela kepha nokuhlupheka ngenxa yakhe ,
50001030	nikukho khona lokho kulwa enakubona kimina , nakalokhu nizwa ukuthi kukimina .
50002001	Ngakho-ke uma kukhona induduzo kuKristu , uma kukhona ukududuzeka kothando , uma kukhona inhlangano kaMoya , uma kukhona isisa nesihawu ,
50002002	gcwalisani ukuthokoza kwami ukuba nibe nomqondo munye , ninothando lunye , nibe nhliziyonye , niqonde into inye ;
50002003	ningenzi lutho ngombango nangodumo lwezwe ; kepha ngokuthobeka nishaye sengathi abanye bakhulu kunani ,
50002004	yilowo nalowo angabheki okwakhe , kepha yilowo abheke nokwabanye .
50002005	Mawube kini lowo mqondo owawukhona nakuKristu Jesu
50002006	owathi enesimo sikaNkulunkulu , akaze asho ukuthi kuyinto yokuphangwa ukulingana noNkulunkulu ,
50002007	kepha wazidela ethabatha isimo senceku , enziwe ngomfanekiso wabantu ;
50002008	wathi efunyenwe enjengomuntu ngesimilo , wazithobisa , elalela kwaze kwaba sekufeni , yebo , ekufeni kwesiphambano .
50002009	Ngalokho-ke uNkulunkulu wamphakamisa kakhulu , wamnika igama eliphezu kwamagama onke ,
50002010	ukuze kuthi ngegama likaJesu amadolo onke aguqe , awabasezulwini , nawabasemhlabeni , nawabangaphansi komhlaba ,
50002011	nezilimi zonke zivume ngokuthi UJESU KRISTU UYINKOSI , kube yinkazimulo kuNkulunkulu uYise .
50002012	Ngakho-ke , bathandiweyo bami , njengalokho nilalele ngezikhathi zonke , kungesikho nxa ngikhona kuphela , kodwa ikakhulu manje nxa ngingekho , fezani ukusindiswa kwenu ngokwesaba nangokuthuthumela ,
50002013	ngokuba nguNkulunkulu osebenza kini nokuthanda nokwenza njengentando yakhe .
50002014	Yenzani konke ngokungakhononi nokungangabazi ,
50002015	ukuze nibe ngabangasolekiyo nabangenacala , abantwana bakaNkulunkulu abangenasici phakathi kwesizukulwane esiyisigwegwe nesiphambeneyo , enikhanya phakathi kwaso njengezinkanyiso ezweni ,
50002016	nibambelele ezwini lokuphila , ngize ngibe nokuzibonga ngosuku lukaKristu ngokuthi angigijimelanga ize , angisebenzelanga ize .
50002017	Yebo , nokuba nginikelwa emhlatshelweni nasenkonzweni yokukholwa kwenu , ngiyathokoza , ngithokoza kanye nani nonke ;
50002018	ngokunjalo-ke thokozani nani , nithokoze kanye nami .
50002019	Kepha ngiyethemba eNkosini uJesu ukuthuma uThimothewu kini masinyane , ukuze nami ngename nxa sengazi izindaba zenu .
50002020	Ngokuba anginamuntu onenhliziyo enjengeyakhe , onganakekela izindaba zenu ngobuqotho ;
50002021	ngokuba bonke bafuna okwabo , abafuni okukaJesu Kristu .
50002022	Kepha niyakwazi ukuthembeka kwakhe ukuthi ukhonzile kanye nami ngenxa yevangeli njengomntwana kuyise .
50002023	Yena-ke ngiyethemba ukumthuma masinyane , uma sengibonile ukuthi okuqondene nami kophelelaphi ;
50002024	kepha ngiyethemba eNkosini ukuthi nami ngizakuza eduzane .
50002025	Kodwa ngibone ukuthi kudingekile ukuba ngithume kinina u-Ephafrodithu , umzalwane nesisebenzi nebutho kanye nami , nesithunywa senu , isikhonzi ekusweleni kwami ,
50002026	lokhu wayenilangazelela nonke , eyaluza ngokuba nizwile ukuthi wayegula .
50002027	Ngokuba nempela wayegula ephansi kokufa ; kepha uNkulunkulu wamhawukela , kungeyena yedwa , wangihawukela nami , ukuze ngingabi nalusizi phezu kosizi .
50002028	Ngalokho ngakhuthalela kakhulu ukumthuma , ukuze kuthi nxa senimbona futhi nithokoze , kimi kunciphe usizi .
50002029	Ngakho-ke mamukeleni eNkosini ngokuthokoza konke , abanjalo-ke nibaphathe ngokubatusa ,
50002030	ngokuba ngenxa yomsebenzi kaKristu wacishe wafa ezidela amathambo , ukuze agcwalise okusileleyo ekungikhonzeni kwenu .
50003001	Elokugcina , bazalwane bami , thokozani eNkosini . Ukunilobela khona lokho angikwenqeni , kepha nina kuyanigcina .
50003002	Xwayani izinja , nixwaye izisebenzi ezimbi , nixwaye abokusika .
50003003	Ngokuba singukusoka thina esikhonza ngoMoya kaNkulunkulu , sizibonga kuKristu Jesu , singethembi enyameni ,
50003004	nakuba nami bengingaba nokwethemba enyameni . Uma omunye umuntu ecabanga ukuthi unokwethemba enyameni , mina kakhulu ;
50003005	ngasokwa ngosuku lwesishiyagalombili ngingowohlanga luka-Israyeli , owesizwe sakwaBenjamini , umHeberu wamaHeberu , ngokomthetho umFarisi ;
50003006	ngokokushisekela ngingowazingela ibandla , ngokokulunga okusemthethweni ngingongasolekiyo .
50003007	Kanti-ke lokho okwakuyinzuzo kimi ngakushaya indiva ngenxa kaKristu .
50003008	Yebo impela , konke ngikushaya indiva ngobukhulu bokumazi uKristu Jesu iNkosi yami , engilahlekelwe yikho konke ngenxa yakhe , ngikushaya izibi , ukuze ngizuze uKristu ,
50003009	ngifunyanwe kuyena , ngingenakho ukulunga okungokwami okuya ngomthetho kodwa lokho okuya ngokukholwa nguKristu , ngisho ukulunga okuvela kuNkulunkulu ngokukholwa ,
50003010	ukuze ngimazi yena , namandla okuvuka kwakhe , nokuhlanganyela ezinhluphekweni zakhe , ngimfuze ngokufa kwakhe ,
50003011	uma mhlawumbe ngingaze ngifinyelele ekuvukeni kwabafileyo ,
50003012	kungesikho ukuthi sengibambile nokuthi sengiphelelisiwe , kepha ngijonga ukuba kumbe ngingakubamba yini lokho nami engabanjelwa khona nguKristu Jesu .
50003013	Bazalwane , angisho ukuthi mina uqobo sengikubambile ; kepha kunye engikwenzayo : ngikhohlwa okungasemuva , ngizelulela kokungaphambili ,
50003014	ngijonge emgomeni , emklomelweni wokubizwa okukhulu kwaphezulu nguNkulunkulu kuJesu Kristu .
50003015	Ngakho-ke thina sonke esiphelele masibe nokuqonda okunjalo ; kepha uma kokuthile niqonda ngokunye , nalokho uNkulunkulu uyakunambulela khona ,
50003016	kuphela ukuthi kwesesifinyelele kukho , sihambe ngawo lowo mkhondo .
50003017	Ngilingiseni , bazalwane , nibabhekisise abahamba njengathi esiyisibonelo kini .
50003018	Ngokuba abaningi , enganitshela kaningi ngabo namanje nginitshela nangezinyembezi , bahamba beyizitha zesiphambano sikaKristu ,
50003019	abakuphela kwabo ngukubhujiswa , abankulunkulu wabo yisisu , nodumo lwabo lusehlazweni labo , abangabanaka okomhlaba .
50003020	Kepha thina singabombuso wasezulwini , lapho futhi silindela khona ukuba kuvele uMsindisi , iNkosi uJesu Kristu ,
50003021	oyakuguqula isimo somzimba wethu wokuthotshiswa , ufane nomzimba wakhe wenkazimulo , ngamandla angazihlelela ngawo konke phansi kwakhe .
50004001	Ngalokho , bazalwane bami abathandekayo nabalangazelelwayo , ntokozo yami nomqhele wami , yimani niqinile kanjalo eNkosini , bathandwa .
50004002	Ngiyamyala u-Evodiya , ngiyamyala noSintike ukuba babe nokuqonda kunye eNkosini .
50004003	Yebo , ngiyakunxusa nawe mana wami oqotho , yelekelela labo besifazane , lokhu babambisana nami evangelini , kanye noKlemente nezinye izisebenzi zami abamagama abo asencwadini yokuphila .
50004004	Thokozani eNkosini njalonjalo ; ngiyaphinda ngithi : Thokozani !
50004005	Ukubekezela kwenu akwaziwe ngabantu bonke ; iNkosi iseduze .
50004006	Ningakhathazeki ngalutho , kepha kukho konke izicelo zenu mazaziwe nguNkulunkulu ngokukhuleka nokunxusa kanye nokubonga .
50004007	Ukuthula kukaNkulunkulu okudlula ukuqonda konke kuyakulondoloza izinhliziyo zenu nemicabango yenu kuKristu Jesu .
50004008	Elokugcina , bazalwane , konke okuyiqiniso , konke okuhloniphekayo , konke okulungileyo , konke okumhlophe , konke okuthandekayo , konke okutusekayo , noma kukhona okuhle , noma kukhona okubongekayo , zindlani ngalokho ;
50004009	enakufunda , nakwamukela , nakuzwa , nakubona kimi , kwenzeni lokho ; khona uNkulunkulu wokuthula uyakuba nani .
50004010	Kepha-ke ngathokoza kakhulu eNkosini , ngokuba manje senize navuselela ukunginakekela kwenu ; beninginakekela kambe , kepha anibanga nathuba .
50004011	Akusikho ukuthi ngisho maqondana nokuswela , ngokuba mina ngifundile ukuba nganeliswe noma ngihlezi kanjani .
50004012	Ngiyakwazi ukuba phansi , ngiyakwazi nokubusa ; kukho konke nasezintweni zonke ngifundisiwe : ukusutha , nokulamba , nokubusa , nokuswela .
50004013	Nginamandla ukwenza konke ngaye ongiqinisayo .
50004014	Nokho nenze kahle ngokuhlanganyela nami ekuhluphekeni kwami .
50004015	Niyazi nani nina baseFilipi ukuthi ekuqaleni kwevangeli ekuphumeni kwami eMakedoniya kwakungekho bandla nelilodwa elahlanganyela nami endabeni yokupha nokwamukela , kuphela nina nodwa ,
50004016	ngokuba naseThesalonika nathumela kanye nakabili ngokuswela kwami .
50004017	Akusikho ukuthi ngifuna isipho , kodwa ngifuna isithelo esiyakwandisa okubalelwa nina .
50004018	Kepha nginakho konke ngokweqileyo ; nganelisiwe sengamukelisiwe ngu-Ephafrodithu okuvela kinina , iphunga elimnandi , umhlatshelo omuhle nothokozisayo kuNkulunkulu .
50004019	UNkulunkulu wami uzakugcwalisa ukuswela konke kwenu njengokwengcebo yakhe ekukhazimuleni kuKristu Jesu .
50004020	KuNkulunkulu noBaba wethu makube ludumo kuze kube phakade naphakade . Amen .
50004021	Ngikhonzeleni kwabangcwele bonke abakuKristu Jesu . Abazalwane abanami bakhonza kinina .
50004022	Abangcwele bonke bayakhonza kini , ikakhulu abendlu kaKesari .
50004023	Umusa weNkosi uJesu Kristu mawube nomoya wenu .
51001001	UPawulu , umphostoli kaKristu Jesu ngentando kaNkulunkulu , noThimothewu umzalwane
51001002	kubo abaseKolose , abangcwele nabazalwane abakholwayo kuKristu ; makube kini umusa nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba wethu .
51001003	Simbonga njalonjalo uNkulunkulu uYise weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu , nxa sinikhulekela ,
51001004	lokhu sizwile ngokukholwa kwenu kuKristu Jesu nangothando eninalo kubo bonke abangcwele ,
51001005	ngenxa yethemba enibekelwe lona ezulwini , enezwa ngalo ngaphambili ngezwi leqiniso levangeli
51001006	elifikile kini , njengalokhu likhona ezweni lonke lithela izithelo , landa , njengokuba kunjalo naphakathi kwenu , kusukela osukwini enezwa ngalo , nazi umusa kaNkulunkulu ngeqiniso ,
51001007	njengalokho nafunda ku-Ephafra othandekayo oyinceku kanye nathi , oyisikhonzi esithembekayo sikaKristu ngenxa yenu ;
51001008	okunguyena futhi wasitshela ngothando lwenu ngoMoya .
51001009	Ngalokho nathi , kusukela osukwini esezwa ngalo , asiyeki ukunikhulekela nokuninxusela ukuba nigcwaliswe ngokwazi intando yakhe ngokuhlakanipha konke nokuqonda okungomoya ,
51001010	nihambe ngokufanele iNkosi , niyithokozise ngakho konke , nithela izithelo emisebenzini yonke elungileyo , nikhula ekumazini uNkulunkulu ,
51001011	niqiniswe nokuqiniswa konke ngokwamandla enkazimulo yakhe , kuze kube ngukubekezela konke nokubheka kade ngokujabula ;
51001012	nibonga uYise owanenza nifanele isabelo sefa labangcwele ekukhanyeni ,
51001013	owasikhulula emandleni obumnyama nowasibeka embusweni weNdodana yothando lwakhe ;
51001014	okukuyo sinokuhlengwa , ukuthethelelwa kwezono ,
51001015	yona ingumfanekiso kaNkulunkulu ongenakubonwa , izibulo lezidalwa zonke ,
51001016	ngokuba kwadalelwa kuyo konke okusezulwini nasemhlabeni , okubonwayo nokungenakubonwa , nokuba kuyizihlalo zobukhosi , nokuba kuyimibuso , nokuba kuyizikhulu , nokuba kuyiziphathimandla ; konke kwadalwa ngayo , kwadalelwa yona ;
51001017	yona ingaphambi kwakho konke , nezinto zonke zimi ngayo ;
51001018	yona iyinhloko yomzimba , ngisho ibandla , engukuqala , izibulo kwabafileyo , ukuze yona ibe ngowokuqala ezintweni zonke ,
51001019	ngokuba kwaba kuhle kuye ukuba ukugcwala konke kuhlale kuyo
51001020	nokuba ngayo abuyisane nakho konke esenzile ukuthula ngegazi lesiphambano sayo , yebo ngayo , nokuba kuyizinto ezisemhlabeni nokuba ngezisezulwini .
51001021	Nani ekade ningabafokazi nezitha engqondweni ngemisebenzi emibi ,
51001022	nokho manje usebuyisene nani emzimbeni wenyama yayo ngokufa ukuba animise ningcwele , ningenasisihla nacala phambi kwakhe ,
51001023	uma kambe nihlala ekukholweni , nisekeliwe nigxilile , ningagudluzwa ethembeni levangeli enalizwayo , elashunyayelwa kukho konke okudaliweyo okuphansi kwezulu , engenziwa isikhonzi salo mina Pawulu .
51001024	Kalokhu ngiyathokoza ezinhluphekweni zami ngenxa yenu ngokugcwalisa okusileleyo osizini lukaKristu enyameni yami ngenxa yomzimba wakhe , oyibandla ;
51001025	engenziwa isikhonzi salo ngokwesimiso sikaNkulunkulu enganikwa sona maqondana nani ukuba ligcwaliswe izwi likaNkulunkulu ,
51001026	ngisho imfihlakalo ebifihlakele selokhu kwaqala izikhathi nezizukulwane , kepha kalokhu yambuliwe kwabangcwele bakhe ;
51001027	okubona uNkulunkulu athanda ukubazisa ukuthi iyini ingcebo yenkazimulo yaleyo mfihlakalo phakathi kwabezizwe , enguKristu phakathi kwenu , ithemba lenkazimulo ;
51001028	okunguye esimshumayelayo , siluleka wonke umuntu , sifundisa wonke umuntu ngokuhlakanipha konke , ukuze simise wonke umuntu ephelele kuKristu ,
51001029	engikusebenzelayo futhi , ngilwa ngokusebenza kwakhe okusebenza kimi ngamandla .
51002001	Ngokuba ngiyathanda ukuba nazi ukuthi kukhulu kangakanani ukulwa enginakho ngenxa yenu nabaseLawodikeya nabo bonke abangabonanga ubuso bami ngamehlo ,
51002002	ukuze izinhliziyo zabo ziduduzwe , behlanganisiwe othandweni babe nengcebo yonke yokwazi okuphelele , bazisise imfihlakalo kaNkulunkulu enguKristu ,
51002003	okufihlwe kuye amagugu onke okuhlakanipha nowokwazi .
51002004	Ngikusho lokhu , ukuze kungabikho muntu onikhohlisa ngamazwi okuyenga .
51002005	Ngokuba noma ngingekho ngomzimba , nokho ngikhona kini ngomoya ngithokoza , ngibona inhlelo yenu nokuqina kokukholwa kwenu kuKristu .
51002006	Ngakho-ke njengalokho nimamukele uKristu Jesu iNkosi , hambani nikuye ,
51002007	nigxilile , nakhiwe kuye , niqinisiwe ekukholweni , njengalokho nifundisiwe , nivame ukubonga .
51002008	Xwayani funa kube khona onithumbayo ngokuhlakanipha nangenkohliso eyize njengokwemvelo yabantu , njengezifundiso zokucathula kwezwe , kungenjengokukaKristu .
51002009	Ngokuba kuhlala kuye ngokomzimba ukugcwala konke kobuNkulunkulu ;
51002010	nigcwalisiwe kuye , yena oyinhloko yemibuso yonke namandla ,
51002011	enasokela kuye futhi ngokusoka okungenziwanga ngezandla ngokukhumula umzimba wenyama , ngokusoka kukaKristu ;
51002012	nimbelwe kanye naye ngombhapathizo , okungawo futhi navuswa kanye naye ngokukholwa ngamandla kaNkulunkulu owamvusa kwabafileyo .
51002013	Nani-ke ebenifile ngeziphambeko nangokungasoki kwenyama yenu wanenza nibe ngabaphilayo kanye naye esithethelela zonke izono zethu ;
51002014	esehlangule incwadi yecala lethu , emelana nathi ngemiyalo yayo , wayeyisusa ngokuyibethela esiphambanweni ;
51002015	ebaphucile ababusi nabanamandla izikhali wabathela ngehlazo obala , ebanqoba ngaso .
51002016	Ngakho makungabikho muntu onilahla ngokudla nesiphuzo , noma ngemikhosi , noma ukwethwasa kwenyanga , noma amasabatha ,
51002017	okuyisithunzi nje salokhu obekuzakuza ; kepha umzimba ngokaKristu .
51002018	Makungabikho muntu onamuka umvuzo wenu , othanda ukuzenza othobile ekhonza izingelosi , ephike ngemibono yakhe , ezikhukhumeza ngeze ngengqondo yakhe yenyama ,
51002019	engabambeleli kuye oyinhloko , okungaye umzimba wonke usizwa , uhlanganiswa ngamalungu nemisipha , ukhula ngokukhula kukaNkulunkulu .
51002020	Uma nifile kanye noKristu nakhululwa ezifundisweni zokucathula kwezwe , yini ukuba okungathi nisaphila ngokwezwe nithobele izifundiso zokuthi :
51002021	" Ungaphathi , ungezwa ngolimi , ungathinti , "
51002022	okuphela konke ngokudliwa ngokweziyalezo nezifundiso zabantu
51002023	ezinegama lokuhlakanipha kambe ngokuzikhethela inkonzo , nangokuzithoba , nangokuhlupha umzimba ; akusizi lutho maqondana nokuzithiba kwenyama .
51003001	Ngakho uma navuswa kanye noKristu , funani okwaphezulu , lapho ekhona uKristu , ehlezi ngakwesokunene sikaNkulunkulu ;
51003002	nakani okwaphezulu , ninganaki okusemhlabeni .
51003003	Ngokuba nafa , ukuphila kwenu kufihliwe noKristu kuNkulunkulu ;
51003004	nxa ebonakaliswa uKristu ongukuphila kwethu , khona-ke nani niyakubonakaliswa kanye naye ekukhazimuleni .
51003005	Ngakho-ke bulalani amalungu enu asemhlabeni , ubufebe , nokungcola , nokuhuheka , nokukhanuka , nesangabe , okungukukhonza izithombe ,
51003006	okuza ngakho ulaka lukaNkulunkulu ,
51003007	ekade nihamba kukho nani , lapho nisahlezi kukho ;
51003008	kepha kalokhu nani manilahle konke lokho , ulaka , nokuthukuthela , nobubi , nokuhlambalaza , nokukhuluma amahlazo aphuma emlonyeni wenu ;
51003009	ningaqambelani amanga , lokhu nikhumule umuntu omdala kanye nezenzo zakhe ,
51003010	nembethe omusha , owenziwa musha abe nokwazi ngokomfanekiso walowo owamdalayo ,
51003011	lapho kungekho mGreki namJuda , ukusoka nokungasoki , owezizwe noma umSkithe , isigqila noma okhululekileyo , kepha uKristu uyikho konke , ukubo bonke .
51003012	Ngakho-ke njengabakhethiweyo bakaNkulunkulu , abangcwele nabathandekayo , yembathani ububele benhliziyo , nesisa , nokuzithoba , nobumnene , nokubheka kade ,
51003013	nibekezelelane , nithethelelane , uma umuntu enensolo komunye ; njengokuba neNkosi yanithethelela , yenzani njalo nani .
51003014	Kepha phezu kwakho konke lokho yembathani uthando oluyisibopho sokuphelela .
51003015	Ukuthula kukaKristu makubuse ezinhliziyweni zenu , enabizelwa futhi kukho emzimbeni munye ; futhi yibani ngababongayo .
51003016	Izwi likaKristu alihlale phakathi kwenu , livame , nifundisane ngokuhlakanipha konke , niyalane ngamahubo , nangezihlabelelo , nangamaculo okomoya , nimhubele uNkulunkulu ezinhliziyweni zenu ngokubonga .
51003017	Konke enikwenzayo , noma kungezwi noma kungomsebenzi , kwenzeni konke egameni leNkosi uJesu , nimbonge uNkulunkulu uYise ngaye .
51003018	Bafazi , thobelani amadoda enu njengokufanele eNkosini .
51003019	Madoda , thandani omkenu , ningabacasukeli .
51003020	Bantwana , lalelani abazali benu ezintweni zonke , ngokuba lokho kuyathandeka eNkosini .
51003021	Boyise , ningabathukuthelisi abantwana benu ukuba bangadangali .
51003022	Zinceku , lalelani ezintweni zonke labo abangamakhosi enu ngokwenyama , kungengokuthenga amehlo njengabathokozisa abantu kodwa ngobuqotho benhliziyo , niyesabe iNkosi .
51003023	Konke enikwenzayo kwenzeni ngenhliziyo , kungathi kwenzelwa iNkosi , qha abantu ,
51003024	nazi ukuthi niyakwamukela umvuzo wefa eNkosini . Khonzani iNkosi uKristu .
51003025	Ngokuba lowo owenza ukungalungi uyakwamukeliswa ukungalungi akwenzileyo ; akukho ukukhetha umuntu .
51004001	Makhosi , zenzeleni izinceku zenu okulungileyo nokufaneleyo ; nazi ukuthi nani nineNkosi ezulwini .
51004002	Qiniselani ekukhulekeni , nilinde kukho ninokubonga .
51004003	Nathi nisikhulekele , ukuze uNkulunkulu asivulele umnyango wezwi ukuba sikhulume imfihlakalo kaKristu engiboshwe ngenxa yayo ,
51004004	ukuze ngiyibonakalise njengalokhu ngifanele ukukhuluma .
51004005	Hambani ngokuhlakanipha kubo abangaphandle , nithengisise isikhathi .
51004006	Ukukhuluma kwenu makube nomusa njalo , kuyolisiwe ngosawoti , ukuze nazi enifanele ukubaphendula ngakho bonke abantu .
51004007	Konke okuqondene nami uyakunazisa khona uThikhiku , umzalwane othandekayo nesikhonzi esikholekileyo oyinceku kanye nami eNkosini ,
51004008	engimthumile kini ngakho lokhu ukuba nazi ukuthi sihlezi kanjani , aduduze izinhliziyo zenu ,
51004009	kanye no-Onesimu , umzalwane okholekileyo nothandekayo , ongomunye wakini ; bazakunazisa konke okwalapha .
51004010	Uyakhonza kini u-Aristarku oyisiboshwa kanye nami , noMarku umzala kaBarnaba , enayalezwa ngaye — uma efika kini mamukeleni —
51004011	noJesu othiwa uJustu ; yibo bodwa abangabokusoka abasebenzela umbuso kaNkulunkulu kanye nami , abakade beyinduduzo kimi .
51004012	Uyakhonza kini u-Ephafra ongomunye wakini , inceku kaKristu Jesu , enilwela njalo emikhulekweni , ukuze nime niphelele niqinisekile entandweni yonke kaNkulunkulu .
51004013	Ngokuba ngingufakazi wakhe wokuthi uyanisebenzela kakhulu nina , nabaseLawodikeya , nabaseHiyerapholi .
51004014	Uyakhonza kini uLuka inyanga ethandekayo , noDema .
51004015	Khonzani kubazalwane abaseLawodikeya , nakuNimfa , nasebandleni lakwakhe .
51004016	Nxa le ncwadi isifundiwe kini , bhekani ukuba ifundwe nasebandleni labaseLawodikeya ; nani niyifunde leyo evela eLawodikeya .
51004017	Nimtshele u-Arkiphu , nithi : " Qaphela inkonzo oyitholile eNkosini , ukuze uyifeze . "
51004018	Yilokhu ukukhonza kwami ngesandla sami , mina Pawulu . Khumbulani izibopho zami . Umusa mawube nani .
52001001	OPawulu , noSilvanu , noThimothewu kulo ibandla labaseTheselonika elikuNkulunkulu uBaba , naseNkosini uJesu Kristu : Makube kini umusa nokuthula . gevangeli eliqinisileyo abalamukele
52001002	Sibonga uNkulunkulu njalo ngani nonke , siniphatha emikhulekweni yethu ,
52001003	sikhumbula ngokungayeki isenzo senu sokukholwa , nomsebenzi wothando , nokukhuthazela kwethemba lenu eliseNkosini yethu uJesu Kristu phambi kukaNkulunkulu noBaba wethu ,
52001004	sikwazi , bazalwane abathandiwe nguNkulunkulu , ukukhethwa kwenu
52001005	ukuthi ivangeli lethu alizanga kini ngezwi kuphela kodwa nangamandla , nangoMoya oNgcwele , nangokwethemba okukhulu , njengokuba nazi ukuthi saba ngabantu abanjani phakathi kwenu ngenxa yenu .
52001006	Nani naba ngabalingisi bethu , nabeNkosi senilamukele izwi ekukhathazekeni okukhulu ngokuthokoza kukaMoya oNgcwele ,
52001007	naze naba yisibonelo kubo bonke abakholwayo eMakedoniya nase-Akhaya .
52001008	Ngokuba udumo lwezwi leNkosi lwaphuma kinina , lwafika , angisho eMakedoniya nase-Akhaya kuphela , kepha ezindaweni zonke lapho ukukholwa kwenu nguNkulunkulu kuphumele khona ; ngakho asisadingi ukukhuluma lutho .
52001009	Ngokuba bona uqobo balanda ngathi ukuthi kwaba njani ukungena kwethu kinina nokuthi naphendukela kanjani kuNkulunkulu , nishiya izithombe , ukuba nikhonze uNkulunkulu ophilayo oweqiniso ,
52001010	nilindele iNdodana yakhe ivela ezulwini , ayivusa kwabafileyo , uJesu osihlangulisa olakeni oluzayo .
52002001	Ngokuba niyazi nina bazalwane ukuthi ukungena kwethu kinina akubanga yize .
52002002	Kepha noma sasihlushiwe kuqala saphathwa kabi eFilipi , njengokuba nazi , saba nesibindi kuNkulunkulu wethu sokunishumayeza ivangeli likaNkulunkulu ngokulwa okukhulu .
52002003	Ngokuba ukuyala kwethu akusikho okokuduka nokokungcola nangenkohliso ,
52002004	kepha njengokuba sivunyiwe nguNkulunkulu ukuba siphathiswe ivangeli , siyakhuluma ngokunjalo , singenzeli ukuthokozisa abantu kepha uNkulunkulu ovivinya izinhliziyo zethu .
52002005	Ngokuba asizange sibe namazwi okuthopha , njengokuba nazi ; asizange futhi sibe nobuqili bokufisa , uNkulunkulu ungufakazi ,
52002006	singafunanga nokutuswa ngabantu , nakinina nakwabanye ,
52002007	ingani sasingaba namandla okunisinda njengabaphostoli bakaKristu , nokho saba mnene phakathi kwenu njengokuba umdlezane ondla abantwana bakhe .
52002008	Ngokunjalo lokhu besinilangazelele , sasifuna ukuninika kungesilo ivangeli likaNkulunkulu kuphela , kepha nokuphila kwethu uqobo , ngokuba nase ningabathandekayo kithina .
52002009	Ngokuba niyakhumbula , bazalwane , ukukhandleka nokushikashikeka kwethu ; sisebenza ubusuku nemini , ukuze singasindi noyedwa kinina , sanishumayeza ivangeli likaNkulunkulu .
52002010	Nina ningofakazi , naye uNkulunkulu , bokuthi sahlala kanjani phakathi kwenu nina enikholwayo ngobungcwele , nangokulunga , nangokungasoleki ,
52002011	njengokuba nazi ukuthi saniphatha abanye ngabanye njengoyise ephatha abantwana bakhe ,
52002012	siniyala , sinimisa isibindi , sifakazela ukuba nihambe ngokufaneleyo phambi kukaNkulunkulu onibizela embusweni nasebukhosini bakhe .
52002013	Ngalokho nathi sibonga uNkulunkulu singaphezi , ngokuba , kuthe lapho namukela izwi likaNkulunkulu enalizwa ngathi , anilamukelanga njengezwi labantu kepha njengezwi likaNkulunkulu , njengokuba liyilo isibili , elona lisebenza futhi phakathi kwenu nina enikholwayo .
52002014	Ngokuba nina bazalwane naba ngabalingisi bamabandla kaNkulunkulu aseJudiya akuKristu Jesu , ngokuba nani nahlushwa ngabesizwe sakini , njengalokho nawo ahlushwa ngabaJuda
52002015	ababulala neNkosi uJesu nabaprofethi , basixosha nathi , bengamthokozisi uNkulunkulu , bemelana nabantu bonke ,
52002016	besivimbela ukukhuluma nabezizwe ukuba basindiswe , ukuze bagcwalise njalo izono zabo ; kepha ulaka selufinyelele phezu kwabo ngokupheleleyo .
52002017	Kepha thina , bazalwane , lokhu besahlukanisiwe nani isikhashana ngobuso kungenganhliziyo , kwaba yikhona sikhuthalela kakhulu ukubona ubuso benu ngokunxanela okukhulu .
52002018	Ngakho besithanda ukuza kinina , mina Pawulu ngokwami kanye nakabili , kepha uSathane wasivimbela .
52002019	Ngokuba liyini ithemba lethu , nokuthokoza , nomqhele wokuzibonga phambi kweNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu ekufikeni kwakhe , kungeyinina na ?
52002020	Ngokuba nina niludumo lwethu nokuthokoza kwethu .
52003001	Ngalokho kwathi singasenakubekezela , sathi kuhle ukuba sisale sodwa e-Athene ,
52003002	sathuma uThimothewu umzalwane wethu , isikhonzi sikaNkulunkulu evangelini likaKristu , ukuba aniqinise , anivuse maqondana nokukholwa kwenu
52003003	ukuba kunganyakaziswa muntu ngalezo zinhlupheko ; ngokuba niyazi nina ukuthi simiselwe lokho .
52003004	Ngokuba kuthe sisekhona kini , sanitshela ngaphambili ukuthi siyakuhlushwa , njengokuba kwaba njalo , nani nikwazi .
52003005	Ngalokho nami , lapho ngingasenakubekezela , ngathumela ukuba ngiqonde ukukholwa kwenu , ingabe mhlawumbe umlingi unilingile yini , ukukhandleka kwethu kube yize .
52003006	Kepha kalokhu uThimothewu esefikile kithi evela kini , esibikela izindaba ezinhle zokukholwa nothando lwenu , nokuthi nisikhumbula kahle njalo , nokuthi nilangazelela ukusibona , njengokuba nathi silangazelela ukubona nina ,
52003007	ngalokho , bazalwane , saduduzeka ngani ngokukholwa kwenu ekusweleni nasosizini lwethu lonke ,
52003008	ngokuba kalokhu siyaphila , uma nina nimi niqinile eNkosini .
52003009	Ngokuba ngukubonga okunjani esingakubuyisela kuNkulunkulu ngani ngokuthokoza konke esithokoza ngakho ngenxa yenu phambi kukaNkulunkulu wethu na ?
52003010	Ubusuku nemini sinxusa nokunxusa ukuba sibone ubuso benu , siphelelise okusileleyo ekukholweni kwenu .
52003011	Sengathi uNkulunkulu noBaba wethu uqobo neNkosi yethu uJesu angayiqondisa indlela yethu yokuza kini ,
52003012	iNkosi ininike ukwanda nokuchichima othandweni , omumye komunye nakubo bonke , njengokuba sinjalo kinina ,
52003013	ukuze iqinise izinhliziyo zenu , zingabi nakusoleka ebungcweleni phambi kukaNkulunkulu noBaba wethu ekufikeni kweNkosi yethu uJesu kanye nabangcwele bakhe bonke .
52004001	Elokugcina-ke , bazalwane , siyaninxusa , siyaniyala ngeNkosi uJesu ukuba njengalokho nakwamukela kithi ukuthi nifanele ukuhamba nokumthokozisa kanjani uNkulunkulu , njengalokho nihamba kanjalo , manivame kakhulu kulokho .
52004002	Ngokuba niyayazi imiyalo esaninika yona ngayo iNkosi uJesu .
52004003	Ngokuba lokhu kuyintando kaNkulunkulu , ukungcweliswa kwenu , ukuba nidede ebufebeni
52004004	ukuba yilowo nalowo kini akwazi ukuhlala nomkakhe ngobungcwele nangokuhlonipha ,
52004005	kungabi ngokushisa kwenkanuko njengabezizwe abangamazi uNkulunkulu
52004006	ukuba kungabikho noyedwa omonayo , aphambe umfowabo ngento , ngokuba iNkosi ingumphindiseli kukho konke lokho , njengokuba sanitshela phambili , saqinisa .
52004007	Ngokuba uNkulunkulu kasibizelanga amanyala , kepha wasibizela ebungcweleni .
52004008	Ngakho-ke owalayo akali umuntu , kepha wala uNkulunkulu , yena oninika uMoya wakhe oNgcwele .
52004009	Kepha maqondana nothando lobuzalwane anisweli ukuba umuntu anilobele , ngokuba nina uqobo ningabafundisiwe nguNkulunkulu ukuba nithandane ;
52004010	nempela niyakwenza lokho kubo bonke abazalwane abaseMakedoniya lonke . Kepha siyaniyala , bazalwane , ukuba nivame nokuvama kulokho ,
52004011	nikhuthalele ukuhlala ngokuthula , nokwenza okwenu , nokusebenza ngezandla zenu , njengokuba saniyala ,
52004012	ukuze nihambe ngokufaneleyo kwabangaphandle , ningasweli lutho .
52004013	Kepha asithandi , bazalwane , ukuba ningabi nakwazi ngabalalayo , ukuze ningadabuki njengabanye abangenalo ithemba .
52004014	Ngokuba uma sikholwa ukuthi uJesu wafa , wavuka , ngokunjalo-ke uNkulunkulu uyakubaletha nabaleleyo kuJesu kanye naye .
52004015	Ngokuba lokho sikusho kini ngezwi leNkosi ukuthi thina , esisekhona sisasele kuze kube sekufikeni kweNkosi , asiyikubandulela nempela abaleleyo ,
52004016	ngokuba iNkosi uqobo iyakwehla ezulwini ngezwi lenhlokomo , ngephimbo lengelosi enkulu nangecilongo likaNkulunkulu , nabafileyo kuKristu bayakuvuka kuqala ,
52004017	khona thina , esisekhona sisasele siyakuhlwithwa kanye nabo emafwini , sihlangabeze iNkosi emoyeni ; kanjalo-ke siyakuba nayo iNkosi njalo .
52004018	Ngakho-ke duduzanani ngalawo mazwi .
52005001	Kepha ngezikhathi nangemizuzu , bazalwane , anisweli ukulotshelwa ,
52005002	ngokuba nina uqobo niyazi kahle ukuthi usuku lweNkosi luza njengesela ebusuku .
52005003	Nxa bethi : " Ngukuthula nokuhlala kahle , " khona ukubhujiswa kuyabazuma njengemihelo ifikela okhulelweyo , abasoze baphunyuka .
52005004	Kepha nina bazalwane anikho ebumnyameni , ukuze lolo suku lunifice njengesela ,
52005005	ngokuba nina nonke ningabantwana bokukhanya , ningabantwana bemini . Asisibo abobusuku noma abobumnyama ;
52005006	ngalokho-ke masingalali njengabanye , kodwa masiqwashe , siqonde .
52005007	Ngokuba abalalayo balala ebusuku , nabadakwayo badakwa ebusuku ;
52005008	kepha thina esingabemini masiqonde , sifake isivikelo sesifuba sokukholwa nesothando , isigqoko sibe yithemba lokusindiswa ;
52005009	ngokuba uNkulunkulu kasimiselanga ulaka kepha ukuba sizuze ukusindiswa ngeNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu
52005010	owasifelayo ukuba , noma siqwashile noma silele , siphile kanye naye .
52005011	Ngalokho-ke vuselelanani , nakhane njengokuba futhi nikwenza .
52005012	Kepha siyanincenga , bazalwane , ukuba nibazi abakhandlekayo phakathi kwenu , nabaniphetheyo eNkosini , nabanilulekayo ,
52005013	nibazisise kakhulu othandweni ngenxa yomsebenzi wabo . Hlalisanani ngokuthula .
52005014	Kepha siyaniyala , bazalwane , ukuba niluleke abangahambi ngomthetho , nithokozise abadanileyo , nisekele ababuthakathaka , nibabekezelele bonke .
52005015	Qaphelani ukuba kungabikho ophindisela omunye okubi ngokubi ; kepha jongani njalo ukwenza okuhle , omunye komunye nakubo bonke .
52005016	Thokozani njalo ;
52005017	khulekani ningaphezi ;
52005018	kukho konke bongani ; ngokuba lokhu kuyintando kaNkulunkulu kuKristu Jesu ngani .
52005019	Ningamcimi uMoya ;
52005020	ningakudeleli ukuprofetha ;
52005021	vivinyani konke , nibambisise okuhle ;
52005022	dedani kukho konke okubonakala kukubi .
52005023	Kepha uNkulunkulu wokuthula , yena uqobo , makaningcwelise ngokupheleleyo , kulondolozwe umoya wenu wonke nomphefumulo nomzimba , kungabi nacala ekufikeni kweNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu .
52005024	Uthembekile yena onibizayo , oyakukwenza futhi .
52005025	Bazalwane , sikhulekeleni .
52005026	Khonzani kubazalwane bonke ngokwanga okungcwele .
52005027	Ngiyanifungisa iNkosi ukuba le ncwadi ifundwe kubo bonke abazalwane .
52005028	Umusa weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu mawube nani .
53001001	OPawulu , noSilvanu , noThimothewu kulo ibandla labaseThesalonika elikuNkulunkulu , uBaba wethu , naseNkosini uJesu Kristu :
53001002	Makube kini umusa nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba naseNkosini uJesu Kristu .
53001003	Simelwe ukumbonga njalo uNkulunkulu ngani bazalwane , njengokuba kufanele , ngokuba inkolo yenu iyanda kakhulu , nothando lwenu nonke omunye komunye luyakhula ,
53001004	kuze kuthi thina ngokwethu sizincome ngani emabandleni kaNkulunkulu ngenxa yokukhuthazela kwenu nokukholwa ekuzingelweni kwenu konke nasezinhluphekweni enibekezela kuzo ,
53001005	okuyisiboniso sokwahlulela okulungileyo kukaNkulunkulu , ukuze kuthiwe ningabalungele umbuso kaNkulunkulu enihlupheka ngenxa yawo ,
53001006	uma kambe kuyinto elungile kuNkulunkulu ukuba abuyisele ukuhlupheka kubo abanihluphayo ,
53001007	aniphe nina enihluphekayo ukuphumula kanye nathi ekwambulweni kweNkosi uJesu , evela ezulwini , enezingelosi zamandla akhe ,
53001008	elangabini lomlilo , ephindisela kwabangamazi uNkulunkulu nakwabangalaleli ivangeli leNkosi yethu uJesu ,
53001009	abazakunikwa isijeziso esingukubhujiswa okuphakade , basuke phambi kobuso beNkosi naphambi kwenkazimulo yamandla akhe ,
53001010	nxa efika ukuba akhazimuliswe kubo abangcwele bakhe , abe ngomangalisayo kubo bonke abakholwa ngalowo muhla , ngokuba nakholwa ngukufakaza kwethu .
53001011	Ngenxa yalokho siyanikhulekela njalo , ukuze uNkulunkulu wethu anenze nibe ngabafanele ukubizwa kwenu , agcwalise ngamandla konke okuhle enikuthandayo nomsebenzi wokukholwa ,
53001012	ukuze igama leNkosi yethu uJesu likhazimuliswe kini , nani kuye , ngokomusa kaNkulunkulu wethu noweNkosi uJesu Kristu .
53002001	Kepha siyanxusa , bazalwane , mayelana nokufika kweNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu nokubuthanela kwethu kuyo ,
53002002	ukuba ningasheshi ninyakaziswe engqondweni yenu , ningethuswa noma ngomoya , noma ngezwi , noma ngencwadi ngokungathi ivela kithi , sengathi usuku lukaKristu selufikile .
53002003	Makungabikho muntu onikhohlisayo nangayiphi indlela ; ngokuba aluyikufika , kungaveli kuqala ukuhlubuka , kwambulwe umuntu ongenamthetho , indodana yokulahlwa ,
53002004	omelana nakho konke , nozikhukhumeza phezu kwakho konke okuthiwa uNkulunkulu noma into ekhonzwayo , aze azihlalise ethempelini likaNkulunkulu ezishaya uNkulunkulu .
53002005	Anikhumbuli yini ukuthi ngisekhona kini nganitshela lokho na ?
53002006	Senikwazi okumbambezelayo , ukuze ambulwe ngesikhathi sakhe .
53002007	Ngokuba imfihlakalo yokungabi namthetho isiyasebenza , kuphela ukuze kudediswe yena obambezelayo manje .
53002008	Lapho-ke uzakwambulwa lowo ongenamthetho , eyakumqeda iNkosi uJesu Kristu ngomoya womlomo wayo , imchithe ngokubonakala kokufika kwayo ,
53002009	lowo okufika kwakhe kungokokusebenza kukaSathane ngawo onke amandla , nezibonakaliso , nezimangaliso zamanga ,
53002010	nangayo yonke inkohliso yokungalungi kwababhubhayo , ngenxa yokuba bengavumanga ukuthanda iqiniso , ukuze basindiswe .
53002011	Ngalokho-ke uNkulunkulu ubathumela amandla okuduka , baze bakholwe ngamanga ,
53002012	ukuba bonke abangakholwanga yiqiniso benamela ukungalungi balahlwe .
53002013	Kepha thina simelwe ukubonga uNkulunkulu njalo ngani bazalwane abathandwa yiNkosi , ngokuba kwasekuqaleni uNkulunkulu wanikhethela ukusindiswa ngokungcwelisa kukaMoya nangokukholwa yiqiniso
53002014	anibizela kukho ngevangeli lethu , nize nizuze inkazimulo yeNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu .
53002015	Ngalokho-ke , bazalwane , yimani niqinile , nibambelele kuwo amasiko enawafundiswa noma ngezwi noma ngencwadi yethu .
53002016	Kepha iNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu uqobo , noNkulunkulu uBaba wethu owasithanda nowasipha ngomusa induduzo yaphakade nethemba elihle ,
53002017	makaduduze izinhliziyo zenu , aniqinise emisebenzini yonke nasemazwini onke amahle .
53003001	Elokugcina , bazalwane , sikhulekeleni ukuba izwi leNkosi likhawuleze , lidunyiswe , njengalokhu kunjalo nakini ,
53003002	nokuba sikhululwe kubantu abadukileyo nababi ; ngokuba ukukholwa akusikho okwabo bonke .
53003003	Kepha iNkosi ithembekile , eyakuniqinisa , inilondoloze komubi .
53003004	Siyethemba eNkosini ngani ukuthi lokhu esiniyala ngakho niyakwenza nokuthi nizakukwenza .
53003005	Kepha iNkosi mayiqondise izinhliziyo zenu othandweni lukaNkulunkulu nasekubekezeleni kukaKristu .
53003006	Kodwa siyaniyala , bazalwane , egameni leNkosi uJesu Kristu ukuba nizahlukanise nabazalwane bonke abahamba ngokungafanele , bengahambi ngomyalo eniwamukele kithina .
53003007	Ngokuba nani niyazi ngokwenu ukuthi kufanele ukuba nisilingise kanjani , ngokuba asihambanga ngokungafanele phakathi kwenu ,
53003008	asidlanga sinkwa samuntu ngesihle , kodwa sadla ngokukhandleka nangokukhathazeka , sisebenza ubusuku nemini ukuba singasindi muntu kini ,
53003009	kungengokuba singenalo ilungelo , kodwa ukuze sizinikele sibe yisibonelo kini sokuba nisilingise .
53003010	Ngokuba nalapho sisekini , saniyala ngalokhu ukuthi : " Uma umuntu engathandi ukusebenza , makangadli . "
53003011	Ngokuba sizwa ukuthi abanye phakathi kwenu bahamba ngokungafanele , bengasebenzi lutho , kepha benza okuyize nje ;
53003012	abanjalo siyabayala sibaluleka eNkosini uJesu Kristu ukuba basebenze ngokuthula , badle esabo isinkwa .
53003013	Kepha nina bazalwane , ningadinwa ngukwenza okuhle .
53003014	Uma ekhona ongalaleli izwi lethu kule ncwadi , mphawuleni lowo , ningahlanganyeli naye , ukuze abe namahloni ;
53003015	kepha ningamphathisi okwesitha , kodwa mlulekeni njengomzalwane .
53003016	Kepha iNkosi yokuthula uqobo mayiniphe ukuthula ngezikhathi zonke nangezindlela zonke . INkosi mayibe nani nonke .
53003017	Ngiyakhonza ngesandla sami mina Pawulu , okuluphawu ezincwadini zonke ; ngiloba kanjalo .
53003018	Umusa weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu mawube nani nonke .
54001001	UPawulu , umphostoli kaKristu Jesu ngomyalo kaNkulunkulu uMsindisi wethu noKristu Jesu ithemba lethu ,
54001002	kuThimothewu , umntanami ngesiminya ekukholweni : Makube kuwe umusa , nesihawu , nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba nakuKristu Jesu iNkosi yethu .
54001003	Njengokuba ngakutshela mhla ngiya eMakedoniya ukuthi wohlala e-Efesu , ukuze uyale abathile ngokuthi bangafundisi okwahlukileyo ,
54001004	futhi banganaki izinganekwane nezindaba zolibo olokuzalana ezingapheliyo , ezibanga ukuphikisana kunokuba ziqhube isimiso sikaNkulunkulu esisekukholweni , ngenza njalo namanje ;
54001005	kepha umgomo womyalo uluthando oluvela enhliziyweni emhlophe , nakunembeza omuhle , nasekukholweni okungazenzisiyo ,
54001006	abathe abanye bephaphalazile kulokho , baphambukela ekukhulumeni okuyize ,
54001007	befuna ukuba babe ngabafundisi bomthetho , ingani kabaqondi abakushoyo nabaqinisa ngakho begomela .
54001008	Siyazi kambe ukuthi umthetho muhle , nxa umuntu ewusebenzisa ngokomthetho ,
54001009	ekwazi lokhu ukuthi umthetho awumiselwe olungileyo , umiselwe abangenamthetho namahlongandlebe , abangamesabi uNkulunkulu nabayizoni abahlazisayo nabadumazayo , nababulali bawonina , nababulala abantu ,
54001010	nezifebe , nabesilisa abalalanayo , nabathumbabantu , nabaqambimanga , nabafungela amanga , noma kungakhona okunye okuphambene nesifundiso esiphilileyo ,
54001011	ngokwevangeli lenkazimulo kaNkulunkulu obongekayo , engaphathiswa lona mina .
54001012	Ngiyambonga owangenzela amandla , uKristu Jesu iNkosi yethu , ngokuba wathi ngikholekile , engimisa enkonzweni ,
54001013	noma kade ngingohlambalazayo , nozingelayo , nohluphayo ; kodwa ngahawukelwa ngokuba ngakwenza ngokungazi , ngokungakholwa .
54001014	Kepha umusa weNkosi yethu wavama kakhulu kanye nokukholwa nothando olukuKristu Jesu .
54001015	Likholekile leli zwi , lifanele impela ukwamukelwa ukuthi uKristu Jesu weza ezweni ukusindisa izoni , engingesikhulu kuzo ;
54001016	kepha ngahawukelwa ngalokhu ukuze uJesu Kristu abonakalise kimi engingesikhulu konke ukubekezela kwakhe , ngibe yisibonelo kwabazakukholwa nguye , baze babe nokuphila okuphakade .
54001017	Kuyo iNkosi yaphakade engabhubhiyo , engenakubonwa , uNkulunkulu yedwa , makube ludumo nenkazimulo kuze kube phakade naphakade . Amen .
54001018	Lo myalo ngiwuthwesa wena mntanami Thimothewu njengeziprofetho ezandulelayo ngawe , ukuze ulwe ukulwa okuhle ngazo ,
54001019	unokukholwa nonembeza omuhle , okuthe abanye bekulahlile , bafelwa umkhumbi wokukholwa ,
54001020	abakubona oHimenewu no-Aleksandru engibanikele kuSathane , ukuze balaywe ukuba bangahlambalazi .
54002001	Ngakho-ke kuqala kukho konke ngiyala ukuba ukunxusa , nokukhuleka , nokucela , nokubonga kwenzelwe abantu bonke ,
54002002	amakhosi nabo bonke abakhulu , ukuze sihlale kahle nangokuthula , ngokumesaba uNkulunkulu nangesizotha esipheleleyo .
54002003	Lokhu kuhle , kuyabongeka emehlweni kaNkulunkulu uMsindisi wethu
54002004	othanda ukuba abantu bonke basindiswe , bafinyelele ekulazini iqiniso .
54002005	Ngokuba munye uNkulunkulu , munye nomlamuleli phakathi kukaNkulunkulu nabantu , umuntu uKristu Jesu ,
54002006	owazinikela abe yinhlawulo yabo bonke , kube ngubufakazi besikhathi esiyiso ,
54002007	engamiselwa khona mina ukuba ngibe ngummemezeli nomphostoli — ngikhuluma iqiniso , angiqambi amanga — yebo , umfundisi wabezizwe ekukholweni naseqinisweni .
54002008	Ngalokho ngithanda ukuba amadoda akhuleke ezindaweni zonke , ephakamisa izandla ezingcwele , engenalulaka nokuphikisana .
54002009	Ngokunjalo nabesifazane mabagqoke izingubo ezifaneleyo , bazihlobise ngokuhlonipha nokuqonda , kungabi ngezinwele ezalukiweyo , nangegolide , nangamaparele , nangezambatho ezinemali eningi ,
54002010	kepha njengokufanele abesifazane abashoyo ukuthi besaba uNkulunkulu bahlobe ngemisebenzi emihle .
54002011	Owesifazane makafunde ukuthula nokuthobeka konke .
54002012	Kepha angimvumeli owesifazane ukuba afundise , nokuba abuse phezu kwendoda ; kodwa makazithulele .
54002013	Ngokuba u-Adamu wabunjwa kuqala , emva kwalokho u-Eva .
54002014	Futhi u-Adamu kakhohliswanga , kepha owesifazane wathi ekhohlisiwe , waphambuka ;
54002015	kepha uyakusindiswa ngokuzala abantwana , uma behlala ekukholweni nasothandweni nasebungcweleni kanye nokuqonda .
54003001	Likholekile leli zwi elithi : Uma umuntu efisa isikhundla sombonisi , unxanela umsebenzi omuhle .
54003002	Ngakho umbonisi umelwe abe ngongasolekiyo , indoda emfazi munye , abe ngozikhuzayo , oqondileyo , oziphatha ngokufaneleyo , ongenisa izihambi , onesu lokufundisa ,
54003003	ongesilo ixhwele lewayini , ongesiso isilwi , kepha omnene , ongaxabaniyo , onganxaneli imali ,
54003004	ophatha kahle indlu yakhe , abantwana bakhe bemthobela ngenhlonipho yonke —
54003005	kepha uma umuntu engakwazi ukuphatha owakhe umuzi , angaliphatha kanjani ibandla likaNkulunkulu na ? —
54003006	angabi ngosanda kukholwa , funa ngokukhukhumala ayele ekulahlweni kukaSathane .
54003007	Kumelwe futhi ukuba abe nobufakazi obuhle kwabangaphandle , funa ayele esihlambeni nasesihibeni sikaSathane .
54003008	Ngokunjalo namadiyakoni kufanele abe nesizotha , angabi ndimimbili , angabi ngabanaka kakhulu iwayini , angahaheli inzuzo embi ,
54003009	ephethe imfihlakalo yokukholwa kunembeza omhlophe .
54003010	Nalabo mabaqale bahlolwe , andukuba babe ngamadiyakoni , uma bengasoleki .
54003011	Ngokunjalo nabesifazane mababe nesizotha , abangahlebi , abazithibayo , abathembekayo ezintweni zonke .
54003012	Amadiyakoni mawabe ngamadoda amfazi munye , abusa kahle abantwana bawo nemizi yawo .
54003013	Ngokuba amadiyakoni akhonze kahle azizuzela ukuma kahle nesibindi esikhulu ekukholweni okukuKristu Jesu .
54003014	Lokhu ngikulobela khona ngithemba ukuza kuwe masinyane ;
54003015	kepha uma ngilibala , khona uyakwazi ukuthi kumelwe ukuba abantu bahambe kanjani endlini kaNkulunkulu eyibandla likaNkulunkulu ophilayo , insika nesisekelo seqiniso .
54003016	Kuvunyiwe ukuthi inkulu imfihlakalo yokukhonza uNkulunkulu yokuthi : Owabonakaliswa enyameni , walungisiswa emoyeni , wabonwa yizingelosi , washunyayelwa ezizweni , wakholeka ezweni , waphakanyiselwa enkazimulweni .
54004001	Kepha uMoya usho ngokuchachileyo ukuthi ngezikhathi zokugcina abanye bayakuhlubuka ekukholweni , benaka omoya abadukisayo nezifundiso zamademoni ,
54004002	ngokuzenzisa kwabaqamba amanga abashiswe uphawu kunembeza wabo ,
54004003	benqabela ukuganana , bethi akuzilwe ukudla akudalayo uNkulunkulu ukuba kwamukelwe ngokubonga yibo abakholwayo nabalaziyo iqiniso .
54004004	Ngokuba konke okudalwe nguNkulunkulu kuhle ; akulahlwa lutho , uma kwamukelwa ngokubonga ,
54004005	ngokuba kungcweliswa ngezwi likaNkulunkulu nomkhuleko .
54004006	Nxa ubeka lezo zinto kubazalwane , uyakuba yisikhonzi esihle sikaKristu Jesu , wondliwa ngamazwi okukholwa nesifundiso esihle osilandeleyo ;
54004007	kepha wale izinganekwane ezingcolileyo nezezalukazi . Kepha zijwayeze ekumesabeni uNkulunkulu .
54004008	Ngokuba ukujwayeza umzimba kusiza ingcosana , kepha ukumesaba uNkulunkulu kusiza ezintweni zonke , kunesithembiso salokhu kuphila nalokho okuzayo .
54004009	Likholekile leli zwi , lifanele impela ukwamukelwa ,
54004010	ngokuba sikhandlekela lokho , siyashikashikeka , ngokuba sithembele kuNkulunkulu ophilayo onguMsindisi wabantu bonke , ikakhulu wabakholwayo .
54004011	Woyala ngalezo zinto , ufundise ngazo .
54004012	Makungabikho muntu odelela ubusha bakho , kepha yiba yisibonelo kwabakholwayo ngezwi , nangenkambo , nangothando , nangokukholwa , nangokuhlanzeka .
54004013	Nakekela ukufunda , nokuyala , nokufundisa , ngize ngifike .
54004014	Ungasidebeseli isiphiwo esikuwe , owasiphiwa ngezwi lokuprofetha nangokubekwa izandla ngamalunga .
54004015	Nakekela lezo zinto , ume kuzo , ukuze ukuqhubeka kwakho kuqhame kubo bonke .
54004016	Ziqaphele wena kanye nesifundiso , ume kulezo zinto ; ngokuba ngokwenza lokho uyakuzisindisa wena nabakuzwayo .
54005001	Ungayikhaci indoda endala , kodwa yiyale njengoyihlo , namadoda amasha njengabafowenu ,
54005002	abesifazane abadala njengawonyoko , nabesifazane abasha njengawodadewenu ngenhlanzeko epheleleyo .
54005003	Yazisa abafelokazi abangabafelokazi ngoqobo .
54005004	Kepha uma umfelokazi enabantwana noma enabazukulwane , labo-ke mabafunde kuqala ukuhlonipha indlu yakwabo , babuyisele okufaneleyo kubazali babo , ngokuba kuyabongeka lokho phambi kukaNkulunkulu .
54005005	Lowo ongumfelokazi ngoqobo osele eyedwa uthembele kuNkulunkulu , uhlala ekunxuseni nasekukhulekeni ubusuku nemini ,
54005006	kepha lowo ozinikela ekutamaseni ufile esekhona .
54005007	Yala ngalezo zinto , ukuze bangabi nokusoleka .
54005008	Kepha-ke uma umuntu engabondli abakubo , kakhulu abakwakhe , ukulahlile ukukholwa , mubi kunongakholwayo .
54005009	Makangafakwa esibalweni umfelokazi , uma engaphansi kweminyaka engamashumi ayisithupha , owabe ngumfazi wendoda inye ,
54005010	ebongwa ngemisebenzi emihle , uma ondlile abantwana , uma engenisile izihambi , uma egezile izinyawo zabangcwele , uma esizile abahluphekayo , uma ekhuthalele umsebenzi wonke omuhle .
54005011	Kepha abafelokazi abasha ubenqabe ; ngokuba uma sebetamasile bedela uKristu , bafuna ukugana ;
54005012	banokulahlwa , ngokuba bechithile ukukholwa kwabo kokuqala .
54005013	Futhi-ke bafunda nokuvilapha , bezula izindlu ngezindlu , bengavilaphi kuphela , kepha behleba , bezigaxa ngokungekwabo , bekhuluma okungafanele .
54005014	Ngakho-ke ngithanda ukuba abafelokazi abasha bagane , bazale abantwana , baphathe indlu yabo , bangasiniki isitha ithuba lokuthuka .
54005015	Ngokuba nakalokhu abanye sebechezukele kuSathane .
54005016	Uma owesifazane okholwayo enabafelokazi , makabasize , ibandla lingasindwa , ukuze lisize abafelokazi boqobo .
54005017	Amalunga aphatha kahle akuthiwe afanele ukutuswa ngokuphindiweyo , ikakhulu lawo akhuthalela izwi nokufundisa .
54005018	Ngokuba umbhalo uthi : " Ungayifaki isifonyo inkabi ebhulayo , " futhi : " Isisebenzi siyifanele inkokhelo yaso . "
54005019	Icala eliqondene nelunga ungalemukeli , kungekho ofakazi ababili noma abathathu .
54005020	Abonayo ubasole phambi kwabo bonke , ukuze nabanye besabe .
54005021	Ngiyaqinisa phambi kukaNkulunkulu noKristu Jesu nezingelosi ezikhethiweyo ukuba ulonde lezo zinto ngokungazinqumeli , ungenzi lutho ngokukhetha .
54005022	Ungasheshi ubeke izandla noma kubani , futhi ungahlanganyeli izono zabanye , uzigcine ube mhlophe .
54005023	Ungabe usaphuza amanzi odwa , kepha phuza iwayini eliyingcosana ngenxa yesisu sakho nobuthakathaka bakho obuvamileyo .
54005024	Izono zabanye abantu zisobala , zibandulela ekwahlulelweni ; kepha abanye ziyabalandela .
54005025	Ngokunjalo nemisebenzi emihle isobala ; naleyo engenjalo ingesitheke .
54006001	Bonke abayizigqila phansi kwejoka mabathi abanumzane babo bafanele ukutuswa impela , ukuze igama likaNkulunkulu nesifundiso kungahlanjalazwa .
54006002	Abanabanumzane abakholwayo bangabadeleli , ngokuba bengabazalwane , kodwa kube yikhona bebakhonza kakhulu , ngokuba bengabakholwayo nabathandekayo labo abasizakala ngomsebenzi wabo . Wofundisa lezo zinto , uyale ngazo .
54006003	Uma kukhona umuntu ofundisa okwahlukileyo , engawalandeli amazwi aphilileyo eNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu nesifundiso esiya ngokumesaba uNkulunkulu ,
54006004	ukhukhumele lowo engaqondi lutho , kumphethe ukubuzana nokuphikisana ngamazwi okuvela kukho umhawu , nombango , nokuhlambalaza , nokuzindla okubi ,
54006005	nokuxabana kwabantu abangqondo yabo yonakele , abamukwe iqiniso , bethi ukumesaba uNkulunkulu kuyindlela yenzuzo .
54006006	Yebo , ukumesaba uNkulunkulu kanye nokwaneliswa kuyinzuzo enkulu ,
54006007	ngokuba asilethanga lutho ezweni ; kusobala ukuthi singemuke nalutho futhi ;
54006008	kepha uma sinokudla nezambatho , asaneliswe yikho .
54006009	Kepha abafuna ukuceba bayela ekulingweni , nasesihibeni , nasezinkanukweni eziningi zobuwula ezilimazayo , ezishonisa abantu ekufeni nasekubhujisweni .
54006010	Ngokuba ukuthanda imali kuyimpande yakho konke okubi ; abanye ngokuyifisa badukelwa ukukholwa , bazigwaza ngeminjunju eminingi .
54006011	Kepha wena muntu kaNkulunkulu , balekela lezo zinto ; jonga ukulunga , nokumesaba uNkulunkulu , nokukholwa , nothando , nokubekezela , nobumnene .
54006012	Yilwa ukulwa okuhle kokukholwa , ubambelele ekuphileni okuphakade owabizelwa kukho , wavuma ukuvuma okuhle phambi kofakazi abaningi .
54006013	Ngiyakuyala phambi kukaNkulunkulu ophilisa konke , naphambi kukaKristu Jesu owavuma ukuvuma okuhle phambi kukaPontiyu Pilatu ,
54006014	ukuba ugcine umyalo ungenabala , ungenakusoleka , kuze kube sekubonakaleni kweNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu
54006015	ayakukubonakalisa ngezikhathi zakhe uSomandla obongekayo , oyedwa , iNkosi yamakhosi , uMbusi wababusi ,
54006016	yena yedwa onokungafi , ehlala ekukhanyeni okungenakusondelwa kukho , ongazange abonwe muntu , nongebonwe ; makube kuye udumo namandla aphakade . Amen .
54006017	Yala abacebileyo kuleli zwe lamanje ngokuthi bangakhukhumali , bangathembeli engcebeni engemiyo , kepha mabathembele kuNkulunkulu osicebisa ngakho konke , sithokoze ngakho ,
54006018	benze okuhle , bacebe ngemisebenzi emihle , baphane , babelane ,
54006019	bezibekelela isisekelo esihle sesikhathi esizayo , ukuze babambe ukuphila okuyikho .
54006020	Thimothewu , londa kahle okubekiweyo kuwe , ugweme ukukhuluma okuyize nokuphikisana kwalokho okuthiwa ukwazi kungesikho ,
54006021	okuthi abanye bekuvuma , baduka ekukholweni . Umusa mawube nani .
55001001	UPawulu , umphostoli kaKristu Jesu ngentando kaNkulunkulu ngokwesithembiso sokuphila okukuKristu Jesu ,
55001002	kuThimothewu , umntwana othandekayo : Makube kuwe umusa , nobubele , nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba nakuKristu Jesu iNkosi yethu .
55001003	Ngiyambonga uNkulunkulu engimkhonzayo kusukela kokhokho ngonembeza omhlophe , njengalokhu ngikukhumbula ngokungaphezi emikhulekweni yami ubusuku nemini ,
55001004	ngilangazelela ukukubona , ngikhumbula izinyembezi zakho , ukuze ngigcwaliswe ngentokozo ,
55001005	ngikhunjuzwe ukukholwa okungenakuzenzisa okukuwe , okwahlala kuqala kunyokokhulu uLowisi nakunyoko uYunisi , yebo , ngiyethemba , nakuwena .
55001006	Ngaleso sizathu ngiyakukhumbuza ukuba uvuse isipho somusa sikaNkulunkulu esikhona kuwe ngokubeka izandla zami .
55001007	Ngokuba uNkulunkulu akasiphanga umoya wobugwala , kepha owamandla , nowothando , nowokuzikhuza .
55001008	Ngalokho ungabi namahloni ngobufakazi ngeNkosi yethu nangami , isiboshwa sayo , kodwa hlanganyela ukuhluphekela ivangeli ngamandla kaNkulunkulu
55001009	owasisindisa , wasibiza ngobizo olungcwele , kungengokwemisebenzi yethu kepha ngokwelakhe icebo nomusa , esawuphiwa kuKristu Jesu zingakabikho izikhathi ,
55001010	kepha osubonakalisiwe manje ngokubonakala koMsindisi wethu uKristu Jesu , owachitha ukufa , walethela ekukhanyeni ukuphila nokungabhubhi ngevangeli ,
55001011	engamiselwa lona ukuba ngibe ngummemezeli , nomphostoli , nomfundisi ;
55001012	ngaleso sizathu ngiyahlupheka nangalokhu , kepha anginamahloni , ngokuba ngiyamazi engikholwa nguye , ngiyethemba ukuthi unamandla okulonda lokho engikubekile kuye , kuze kube yilolo suku .
55001013	Isibonelo samazwi aphilayo masibe yilawo owawezwa kimi ngokukholwa nangothando olukuKristu Jesu ;
55001014	okuhle okubekiwe kuwe ukulonde ngoMoya oNgcwele ohlala kithi .
55001015	Uyazi lokhu ukuthi bonke abase-Asiya bangifulathele , abaphakathi kwabo ngoFigelu noHermogene .
55001016	INkosi mayinike indlu ka-Onesiforu umusa , ngokuba wangihlumelela kaningi , wayengenamahloni ngeketanga lami ,
55001017	kepha esefikile eRoma wangifunisisa , wangifumana —
55001018	iNkosi mayimnike ukuba athole ububele eNkosini ngalolo suku — konke akhonza ngakho e-Efesu uyakwazi wena kakhulu .
55002001	Ngakho wena mntanami , yiba namandla emseni okuKristu Jesu ;
55002002	lokho okuzwileyo kimi phambi kofakazi abaningi , lokho-ke kubeke kubantu abathembekileyo abazakuba namandla okufundisa nabanye .
55002003	Hlanganyela nami ukuhlupheka njengebutho elihle likaKristu .
55002004	Akakho osempini olibala izidingo zalokhu kuphila , aze akholeke kulowo abuthwe nguye .
55002005	Futhi nxa umuntu encintisana , kaqheliswa engancintisananga ngokomthetho .
55002006	Umlimi osebenzayo kufanele ukuba kwamukele yena izithelo kuqala .
55002007	Qonda engikushoyo ; ngokuba iNkosi iyakukunika ukuqonda ngezinto zonke .
55002008	Khumbula uJesu Kristu ovukile kwabafileyo , wenzalo kaDavide ngokwevangeli lami ,
55002009	engihlupheka ngalo kuze kube sekuboshweni njengeselelesi ; kepha izwi likaNkulunkulu aliboshiwe .
55002010	Ngalokho ngiyakhuthazela kukho konke ngenxa yabakhethiweyo , ukuze nabo bazuze insindiso ekuKristu Jesu , kanye nenkazimulo yaphakade .
55002011	Likholekile leli zwi lokuthi : Ngokuba uma safa naye , siyakuphila naye futhi ;
55002012	uma sikhuthazela , siyakubusa naye futhi ; uma simphika , naye uyakusiphika ;
55002013	uma singathembeki , yena uhlala ethembekile , ngokuba akanakuziphika .
55002014	Bakhumbuze ngalokho , ufakaze phambi kukaNkulunkulu ukuba bangalwi ngamazwi , okungasizi lutho , okuyincithakalo kwabezwayo .
55002015	Khuthalela ukuba uziveze uthembekile kuNkulunkulu , isisebenzi esingenamahloni , esiqondisa kahle izwi leqiniso .
55002016	Kepha ukukhuluma kwezwe okuyize ukugweme ; ngokuba bayakuqhubekela phambili ekungamesabini uNkulunkulu ,
55002017	nezwi labo liyakubhibha njengesilonda esibhucukayo , abaphakathi kwabo ngoHimenewu noFiletu
55002018	abadukileyo mayelana neqiniso , bethi ukuvuka kwabafileyo sekudlulile , bechitha ukukholwa kwabanye .
55002019	Nokho isisekelo esiqinileyo sikaNkulunkulu simi , sinalolu phawu lokuthi : " INkosi iyabazi abangabayo , " nokuthi : " Yilowo nalowo ophatha igama likaKristu makadede kukho ukungalungi . "
55002020	Kepha endlini enkulu akukho izitsha zegolide nezesiliva kuphela kodwa nezemithi nezebumba , ezinye ezihloniphekayo , ezinye ezingahloniphekiyo ;
55002021	ngalokho uma umuntu ezihlanza kulezo zinto , uyakuba yisitsha esihloniphekayo , esingcwelisiwe , esinosizo kumninindlu , esilungiselwe umsebenzi wonke omuhle .
55002022	Kepha balekela izinkanuko zobusha , ujonge ukulunga , nokukholwa , nothando , nokuthula kanye nabakhuleka eNkosini ngenhliziyo ehlambulukileyo .
55002023	Kepha ukuphikisana kobuwula nokokungazi ukunqabe , wazi ukuthi kuzala ukulwa ;
55002024	inceku kaKristu ayifanele ukulwa , kodwa mayibe mnene kubo bonke , inesu lokufundisa , ibekezela ,
55002025	ibalaya ngomoya omnene abamelene nayo , kumbe uNkulunkulu angabanika ukuphenduka , baze balazisise iqiniso ,
55002026	basanguluke , baphume ogibeni lukaSathane ababanjwe nguye ukuba benze intando yakhe .
55003001	Kepha yazi lokhu ukuthi ezinsukwini zokugcina kuzakuvela izikhathi ezinzima ;
55003002	ngokuba abantu bazakuba ngabazithandayo , nabathandimali , nabazigabisayo , nabazidlayo , nabahlambalazayo , nabangalaleli abazali , nabangabongiyo , nabahlazisayo ,
55003003	nabangenaluthando , nabahlebi , nabangazithibi , nabangenabumnene , nabangathandi okuhle ,
55003004	nabakhapheli , nabanamawala , nabakhukhumele , nabathanda injabulo kunokuthanda uNkulunkulu ,
55003005	nabanesimo sokumesaba uNkulunkulu , kepha amandla akho bewaphika ; labo-ke wobagwema .
55003006	Ngokuba kulabo kuvela abanyonyobela ezindlini bethumba abesifazane abasindwa yizono , beqhutshwa yizinkanuko eziyizinhlobonhlobo ,
55003007	befunda njalo , kepha bengeke bakwazi ukufika ekulazini iqiniso .
55003008	NjengoJane noJambre bamelana noMose , kanjalo laba bamelana neqiniso , abantu abonakele ingqondo , abehluleka enkolweni .
55003009	Kepha abasayikuqhubekela phambili ; ngokuba ubuwula babo buyakuba sobala kubo bonke , njengokuba kwaba njalo nobabo .
55003010	Kepha wena walandela isifundiso sami nokuziphatha , nomgomo , nenkolo , nokubheka kade , nothando , nokubekezela ,
55003011	nokuzingelwa , nezinhlupheko ezangehlela e-Antiyokiya nase-Ikoniyu naseListra ; ukuzingelwa okunje ngakhuthazela kukho , kepha iNkosi yangikhulula kukho konke .
55003012	Yebo , bonke abathanda ukuhamba ngokumesaba uNkulunkulu kuKristu Jesu bayakuzingelwa .
55003013	Kepha abantu ababi nabakhohlisi bazakuqhubekela phambili ebubini , bedukisa , bedukiswa .
55003014	Kepha wena yima kulokho okufundile nowaqiniseka kukho , wazi ukuthi ukufunde kobani ,
55003015	nokuthi kusukela ebuntwaneni wazi imibhalo engcwele enamandla okukuhlakaniphisa , kube yinsindiso ngokukholwa kuKristu Jesu .
55003016	Yonke imibhalo iphefumulelwe nguNkulunkulu ilungele ukufundisa , nokusola , nokuqondisa , nokuyala ekulungeni ,
55003017	ukuze umuntu kaNkulunkulu aphelele , apheleliselwe yonke imisebenzi emihle .
55004001	Ngiyaqinisa phambi kukaNkulunkulu noKristu Jesu oyakwahlulela abaphilayo nabafileyo nangokubonakala kwakhe nombuso wakhe , ngithi :
55004002	Shumayela izwi , uqinise , noma kuyisikhathi noma kungesiso ; sola , ukhuze , uyale ngakho konke ukubekezela nokufundisa .
55004003	Ngokuba kuyakuba khona isikhathi abangayikuvuma ngaso isifundiso esiphilayo , kepha ngokwezinkanuko zabo bayakuzibuthela abafundisi njengokubatshwa kwezindlebe zabo ,
55004004	bafulathelise izindlebe zabo eqinisweni , baphambukele ezinganekwaneni .
55004005	Kepha wena , qonda ezintweni zonke , ubekezele ekuhluphekeni , wenze umsebenzi womvangeli , ufeze ukukhonza kwakho .
55004006	Ngokuba mina sengiyanikelwa , nesikhathi sokumuka kwami sesifikile .
55004007	Ngikulwile ukulwa okuhle , ngiqedile ibanga , ngigcinile ukukholwa ;
55004008	sengibekelwe umqhele wokulunga eyakungipha wona ngalolo suku iNkosi , umahluleli olungileyo , kungeyimi ngedwa , kepha bonke abathandile ukubonakala kwayo .
55004009	Shesha uze kimi masinyane .
55004010	Ngokuba uDema wangishiya ethanda leli zwe lamanje , waya eThesalonika ; uKreske waya eGalathiya , uThithu eDalmathiya ;

55004012	UThikhiku sengamthuma e-Efesu .

55004014	U-Aleksandru , umkhandi wethusi wenza okubi okuningi kimi ; iNkosi iyakumbuyisela ngokwemisebenzi yakhe ;
55004015	umxwaye nawe , ngokuba wamelana kakhulu namazwi ethu .
55004016	Ekuziphenduleleni kwami kokuqala kwakungekho muntu ongimelayo , kepha bonke bangishiya ; makungabalelwa kubo lokho ;
55004017	kodwa iNkosi yangimela , yangipha amandla ukuba intshumayelo ipheleliswe ngami , nabezizwe bonke bezwe ; ngase ngikhululwa emlonyeni wengonyama .

55004019	Khonza koPriska no-Akwila nendlu ka-Onesiforu .
