56001001	UPawulu , inceku kaNkulunkulu nomphostoli kaJesu Kristu ngokokukholwa kwabakhethiweyo bakaNkulunkulu nangokokwazi iqiniso elingokokukhonza uNkulunkulu ,
56001002	ethembeni lokuphila okuphakade uNkulunkulu ongaqambi amanga akwethembisa phambi kwezikhathi zaphakade ,
56001003	kepha ngesikhathi esifaneleyo ubonakalisile izwi lakhe entshumayelweni engayiphathiswayo ngokomyalo kaNkulunkulu uMsindisi wethu ,
56001004	kuThithu , umntanami ngempela ngokokukholwa esikuhlanganyele sonke : Makube kuwe umusa nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba nakuKristu Jesu uMsindisi wethu . abafundisi bamanga
56001005	Ngakushiya eKrethe ngenxa yalokhu ukuba uhlele okusaseleyo , umise amalunga emizini yonke , njengokuba ngakuyala ,
56001006	uma kukhona ongasolekiyo , indoda emfazi munye , enabantwana abakholwayo abangenakusolwa ngokushinga nabangalaleliyo .
56001007	Ngokuba umbonisi umelwe ukuba abe ngongasolekiyo njengomphathimuzi kaNkulunkulu , ongaziqhenyi , ongesiso isififane , ongesiso isiphuzi , ongesiso isilwi , ongesiye ohahela inzuzo embi ,
56001008	kepha ophatha kahle izihambi , othanda okuhle , oqondileyo , olungileyo , ongcwele , ozithibayo ,
56001009	obambelele ezwini elithembekileyo ngokwesifundiso , aze abe nakho nokuyala ngesifundiso esiphilileyo nokwahlula abaphikayo .
56001010	Ngokuba baningi abangalaleliyo abakhuluma ize , nabakhohlisayo , ikakhulu abokusoka ,
56001011	abamelwe ukuthuliswa , abachitha indlu iphela , befundisa okungafanele ngenxa yenzuzo embi .
56001012	Omunye kubona , umprofethi wakubo , washo wathi : " AbaseKrethe bangabaqambimanga njalo , izilwane ezimbi , iziminzi ezivilaphayo . "
56001013	Lobo bufakazi buqinisile . Ngalokho-ke ubayalisise , ukuze baphile ekukholweni ,
56001014	benganaki izinganekwane zabaJuda nemiyalo yabantu abafulathela iqiniso .
56001015	Kwabahlanzekileyo konke kuhlanzekile ; kepha kwabangcolileyo nabangakholwayo akukho lutho oluhlanzekileyo , kodwa kungcole ingqondo yabo nonembeza wabo .
56001016	Bavuma ukuthi bayamazi uNkulunkulu , kepha bayamphika ngemisebenzi yabo bengabenyanyekayo , nabangalaleliyo , nasemisebenzini yonke emihle kabasizi lutho .
56002001	Kepha wena khuluma lokhu okufanele isifundiso esiphilileyo
56002002	sokuthi : Amadoda amadala mawabe ngazithibayo , azothileyo , aqondileyo , aphilile ekukholweni , nasothandweni , nasekubekezeleni ;
56002003	kanjalo nabesifazane abadala baziphathe ngokufanele abangcwele , bangabi ngabahlebi , bangabi yizigqila zewayini eliningi , babe ngabafundisi bokuhle ,
56002004	ukuze bafundise abesifazane abasha ukuthanda amadoda abo , bathande nabantwana babo ;
56002005	babe ngabaqondileyo , abamhlophe , abaphatha kahle amakhaya , abamnene , abathobela amadoda abo ukuba izwi likaNkulunkulu lingahlanjalazwa .
56002006	Ngokunjalo ubayale abesilisa abasha ukuba babe ngabaqondileyo ,
56002007	uzibonakalise kukho konke ube yisibonelo semisebenzi emihle , nasekufundiseni kwakho ubonakalise ukungonakali , ube nesizotha ,
56002008	ukhulume okuqondileyo okungasolekiyo , ukuze omelana nathi abe namahloni , engenalutho olubi angalukhuluma ngathi .
56002009	Yala izinceku ukuba zithobele amakhosi azo , zikholeke ezintweni zonke , zingaphiki nkani ,
56002010	zingantshontshi , zibonakalise konke ukwethemba okuhle , ukuze zihlobise isifundiso sikaNkulunkulu uMsindisi wethu ezintweni zonke .
56002011	Ngokuba umusa kaNkulunkulu wokusindisa ubonakalisiwe kubantu bonke ;
56002012	uyasifundisa ukuba sidele ukungakholwa nezinkanuko zezwe , sihambe ngokuqonda , nangokulunga , nangokumesaba uNkulunkulu kulesi sikhathi samanje ,
56002013	sibheke ithemba elibusisiweyo nokuvela kwenkazimulo kaNkulunkulu omkhulu noMsindisi wethu uJesu Kristu
56002014	owazinikela ngenxa yethu , ukuze asihlenge ebubini bonke , asihlambulule isizwe esingesakhe , sishisekele imisebenzi emihle .
56002015	Khuluma lokho , uyale , ukhuze ngamandla onke . Ungadelelwa muntu .
56003001	Bakhumbuze ukuba bathobele ababusi neziphathimandla , balalele , balungele imisebenzi yonke emihle ,
56003002	bangahlambalazi muntu , bangabi yizilwi , babe ngabavileyo , bebonakalisa ubumnene obukhulu kubantu bonke .
56003003	Ngokuba nathi kade sasiyiziwula , abangalaleliyo , abadukiswayo , sikhonza izinkanuko nokutamasa okuyizinhlobonhlobo , sihlezi ebubini nangomhawu , sizondekile sizondana .
56003004	Kepha lapho sekubonakalisiwe ububele bukaNkulunkulu uMsindisi wethu nothando lwakhe kubantu ,
56003005	wasisindisa kungengamisebenzi yokulunga esayenzayo thina kepha ngokwesihawu sakhe ngesigezo sokuphindukuzalwa nokwenziwa sibe basha ngoMoya oNgcwele ,
56003006	amthelayo kakhulu phezu kwethu ngaye uJesu Kristu uMsindisi wethu ,
56003007	ukuze silungisiswe ngomusa wakhe , sibe yizindlalifa zokuphila okuphakade ngokwethemba .
56003008	Lithembekile leli zwi . Ngithanda ukuba uqinise impela ngalezo zinto , ukuze abakholwa nguNkulunkulu bakhuthalele ukwenza imisebenzi emihle . Lezo zinto zinhle , zinosizo kubantu ;
56003009	kepha gwema imibuzo yobuwula , nezindaba zolibo lokuzalana , nokubanga nokuphikisana ngomthetho ; ngokuba lokho akusizi , kuyize .
56003010	Umuntu onezifundiso ezidukisayo , eselulekwe kanye nakabili male ,
56003011	wazi ukuthi onjalo uphambukile , uyona , ezahlulela yena .
56003012	Nxa sengithuma u-Arethema noma uThikhiku kuwe , woshesha ukuza kimi eNikopholi ; ngokuba nginqumile ukuthi ngizakuhlala lapho ubusika .
56003013	UZena , ummeli , no-Apholo wobahambisa ngokunakekela , bangasweli lutho .

56003015	Bonke abanami bayakhonza kuwe . Khonza kwabasithandayo ekukholweni . Umusa mawube nani nonke .
57001001	UPawulu , isiboshwa sikaKristu Jesu , noThimothewu umzalwane kuFilemoni , isithandwa sethu nesisebenzi kanye nathi ,
57001002	naku-Apifiya udadewethu , naku-Arkiphu , ibutho kanye nathi , nakulo ibandla elisendlini yakho :
57001003	Makube kini umusa nokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba wethu naseNkosini uJesu Kristu .
57001004	Ngibonga uNkulunkulu wami njalo ngikukhumbula emikhulekweni yami ,
57001005	uma ngizwa ngothando lwakho nokukholwa onakho eNkosini uJesu nakubo bonke abangcwele ,
57001006	ukuze ukuhlanganyela kokukholwa kwakho kube nomsebenzi ekwazini konke okuhle okukithi kuKristu ,
57001007	ngokuba nginokuthokoza okukhulu nenduduzo ngothando lwakho , ngokuba izinhliziyo zabangcwele zihlunyelelwe ngawe mzalwane .
57001008	Ngalokho noma nginesibindi esikhulu kuKristu sokuba ngikuyale ngakho okufaneleyo ,
57001009	nokho ngenxa yothando okungcono ngiyancenga , njengokuba nginje mina Pawulu osemdala , manje futhi ngiyisiboshwa sikaKristu Jesu ,
57001010	ngikuncenga ngomntanami engimzeleyo ekuboshweni kwami , u-Onesimu ;
57001011	okade engenalusizo kuwe , kepha kalokhu unosizo nakuwe nakimi ,
57001012	engimbuyisele kuwe , yena oyinhliziyo yami ,
57001013	ebengifuna ukumbamba ahlale kimi , ukuze angikhonze esikhundleni sakho ngisekuboshweni ngenxa yevangeli ;
57001014	kepha ngaphandle kokubona kwakho ngangingathandi ukwenza lutho , ukuze umusa wakho ungabi ngokucindezelwa , kodwa ube ngesihle .
57001015	Ngokuba mhlawumbe kungenxa yalokho ukuba ahlukaniswe nawe isikhashana , ukuze abe ngowakho kuze kube phakade ,
57001016	angabi esaba njengesigqila , kodwa abe ngaphezu kwesigqila , engumzalwane othandekayo , kakhulu kimi kepha kakhulu kangakanani kuwe , nasenyameni naseNkosini .
57001017	Ngakho uma uthi ngingumhlanganyeli nawe , mamukele ngokungathi yimi .

57001019	mina Pawulu ngikuloba ngesandla sami , ngiyakukukhokha ukuba ngingaze ngisho kuwe ukuthi nawe unecala kimi elinguwe uqobo .

57001021	Ngikulobele ngokwethemba ukulalela kwakho , ngazi ukuthi uzakwenza nokungaphezu kwengikushoyo .

57001024	noMarku , no-Aristarku , noDema , noLuka , izisebenzi kanye nami .

58001001	UNkulunkulu esekhulumile endulo kokhokho ngabaprofethi ngamathuba amaningi nangezindlela eziningi ,

58001003	Yona ethi ingukumenyezela kwenkazimulo yakhe , ifuze yena uqobo , iphasa konke ngezwi lamandla ayo , isiyenzile ukuhlanzwa kwezono , yahlala ngakwesokunene soMkhulu kweliphezulu ,

58001005	Ngokuba yiyiphi yezingelosi ake asho kuyo ukuthi : " UyiNdodana yami wena , namuhla ngikuzele , " na ? nokuthi : " Ngiyakuba nguYise kuyona , yona ibe yiNdodana kimina , " na ?

58001014	Azisibo yini zonke omoya bokukhonza abathunyelwe ukukhonza ngenxa yabayakudla ifa lokusindiswa na ?
58002001	Ngalokho kakhulu siqaphelisisa esikuzwileyo , funa mhlawumbe sikhukhulwe .
58002002	Ngokuba uma izwi elakhulunywa ngezingelosi laqiniseka , nakho konke ukuphambuka nokungalaleli kwaphindiselwa ngokufaneleyo ,
58002003	thina siyakuphunyuka kanjani , uma sidebesela ukusindiswa okungaka na ? — okwakhulunywa kuqala ngeNkosi , kwaqiniswa kithina yilabo abamuzwayo ,
58002004	uNkulunkulu futhi efakaza kanye nabo ngezibonakaliso , nangezimangaliso , nangemisebenzi yamandla eyizinhlobo nhlobo , nangokwabelwa kukaMoya oNgcwele ngokwentando yakhe .
58002005	Ngokuba kwakungesizo izingelosi athobisela phansi kwazo izwe elizayo esikhuluma ngalo .
58002006	Kepha omunye ufakazile endaweni ethile ngokuthi : " Umuntu uyini ukuba umkhumbule , noma indodana yomuntu ukuba uyinake , na ?
58002007	Isikhashana wamenza waba mncinyane kunezingelosi ; wambeka umqhele wenkazimulo nodumo , wammisa phezu kwemisebenzi yezandla zakho , izinto zonke wazibeka phansi kwezinyawo zakhe . "
58002008	Ngokuba ekubekeni izinto zonke phansi kwakhe kashiyanga lutho olungabekwanga phansi kwakhe . Kepha kalokhu asikaziboni izinto zonke zibekiwe phansi kwakhe ;
58002009	kodwa siyambona owenziwe waba mncinyane isikhashana kunezingelosi , uJesu , ebekiwe umqhele wenkazimulo nodumo ngenxa yokuhlupheka kokufa , ukuze ngomusa kaNkulunkulu ezwe ukufa ngenxa yabo bonke .
58002010	Ngokuba kwakumfanele yena , okukhona konke ngenxa yakhe nokukhona konke ngaye , ukuba , lapho eyisa amadodana amaningi enkazimulweni , amphelelise ngezinhlupheko yena oyinkosi yokusindiswa kwabo .
58002011	Ngokuba ongcwelisayo nabangcweliswayo bonke baphuma kumunye ; ngakho-ke akananhloni ukubabiza ngokuthi : Ngabafowethu ,
58002012	ethi : " Ngizakushumayeza abafowethu igama lakho , ngihlabelele ngawe phakathi kwebandla ; "
58002013	futhi : " Ngiyakubeka ithemba lami kuye , " futhi : " Bheka mina nabantwana uNkulunkulu anginike bona . "
58002014	Ngakho-ke njengokuba abantwana bahlanganyela igazi nenyama , naye uqobo wahlanganyela khona lokho , ukuze ngokufa amchithe obe nawo amandla okufa onguSathane ,
58002015	abakhulule bonke labo abathi ngokwesaba ukufa ekuhambeni kwabo konke babeboshelwe ebugqileni .
58002016	Ngokuba akahlangulisi izingelosi , kodwa uhlangulisa inzalo ka-Abrahama .
58002017	Ngakho-ke kwamfanela ukuba abe njengabafowabo kukho konke , ukuze abe ngumpristi omkhulu ohawukelayo nothembekayo kokukaNkulunkulu , kube yinhlawulo yezono zabantu .
58002018	Ngokuba lokhu wahlupheka yena uqobo elingwa , unamandla okusiza abalingwayo .
58003001	Ngakho-ke , bazalwane abangcwele , enihlanganyela ukubiza kwasezulwini , qaphelani umPhostoli nomPristi omkhulu wesivumo sethu uJesu ,
58003002	owayethembeka kuyena owammisayo , njengoMose naye wayenjalo endlini yakhe yonke .
58003003	Ngokuba lowo kwathiwa ufanele inkazimulo enkulu kunoMose , njengalokhu oyakhileyo indlu unodumo olukhulu kunendlu .
58003004	Ngokuba yileyo ndlu yakhiwa ngothile ; kepha owakha konke nguNkulunkulu .
58003005	UMose kambe wayethembekile endlini yakhe yonke njengenceku , kuze kube ngubufakazi balokho obekuzakukhulunywa ,
58003006	kepha uKristu uthembekile njengendodana phezu kwendlu yakhe , esiyindlu yakhe thina , uma sibambisisa isibindi nentokozo yethemba liqine kuze kube sekupheleni .
58003007	Ngalokho njengokusho kukaMoya oNgcwele ukuthi : " Namuhla , uma nilizwa izwi lakhe ,
58003008	ningazenzi lukhuni izinhliziyo zenu njengasekucunuleni ngosuku lokulingwa ehlane ,
58003009	lapho oyihlo bangilinga bengihlola , noma bebona imisebenzi yami iminyaka engamashumi amane ;
58003010	ngalokho nganengwa yileso sizukulwane , ngathi : ‘ Bayaduka njalonjalo enhliziyweni yabo , abazazanga izindlela zami , ’
58003011	ngaze ngafunga ekuthukutheleni kwami , ngathi : ‘ Abayikungena ekuphumuleni kwami . ’ "
58003012	Xwayani , bazalwane , ukuba nakoyedwa kini kungabikho nhliziyo embi , engakholwayo , emhlubukisa kuNkulunkulu ophilayo ;
58003013	kepha yalanani imihla ngemihla kusathiwa namuhla , ukuze kungabikho kini owenziwa lukhuni ngokukhohlisa kwesono ,
58003014	ngokuba sesingabahlanganyela kuKristu , uma sibambisisa ithemba lethu lokuqala kuze kube sekupheleni .
58003015	Uma kuthiwa : " Namuhla , uma nilizwa izwi lakhe , ningazenzi lukhuni izinhliziyo zenu njengasekucunuleni , "
58003016	pho-ke , yibaphi abezwayo bacunula na ? Akusibo bonke abaphuma eGibithe ngoMose na ?
58003017	Yibaphi-ke anengwa yibo iminyaka engamashumi amane na ? Kwakungesibo abonayo , abazidumbu zabo zawa ehlane na ?
58003018	Yibaphi afunga kubo ngokuthi abayikungena ekuphumuleni kwakhe , uma kungesibo abangalalelanga na ?
58003019	Siyabona-ke ukuthi babengenakungena ngenxa yokungakholwa kwabo .
58004001	Ngakho-ke masesabe ukuba , kuthi kusekhona isithembiso sokungena ekuphumuleni kwakhe , kungabikho noyedwa kini obonakala esele emuva .
58004002	Ngokuba phela nathi sashunyayezwa ivangeli njengabo ; kepha izwi abalizwayo alibasizanga bona , lokhu lingahlangananga nabezwayo ngokukholwa .
58004003	Ngokuba siyangena ekuphumuleni thina esikholwayo njengokusho kwakhe ukuthi : " Kanjalo ngafunga ekuthukutheleni kwami , ngathi : ‘ Abayikungena ekuphumuleni kwami , ’ " nakuba imisebenzi yayenziwa kwasekusekelweni kwezwe .
58004004	Ngokuba ushilo endaweni ethile ngosuku lwesikhombisa ukuthi : " UNkulunkulu waphumula ngosuku lwesikhombisa emisebenzini yakhe yonke ; "
58004005	nakule ndawo uthi futhi : " Abayikungena ekuphumuleni kwami . "
58004006	Ngakho-ke lokhu kusasele ukuba abanye bangene kukho , nalabo abashunyayezwa kuqala ivangeli bengangenanga ngokungalaleli ,
58004007	uyanquma futhi usuku oluthile oluthiwa Namuhla , esho ngoDavide emva kwesikhathi esingaka njengokushiwo kuqala ukuthi : " Namuhla , uma nilizwa izwi lakhe , ningazenzi lukhuni izinhliziyo zenu . "
58004008	Ngokuba uma uJoshuwa wayebaphumuzile , wayengayikukhuluma emva kwalokhu ngolunye usuku .
58004009	Ngakho-ke kubasalele abantu bakaNkulunkulu ukuphumula kwesabatha .
58004010	Ngokuba ongenile ekuphumuleni kwakhe yena uphumula emisebenzini yakhe njengoNkulunkulu kweyakhe .
58004011	Ngakho-ke masikhuthalele ukungena kulokho kuphumula , ukuze kungawi muntu ngaleso siboniso sokungalaleli .
58004012	Ngokuba izwi likaNkulunkulu liphilile , linamandla , libukhali kunezinkemba zonke ezisika nhlangothi zombili , lihlaba kuze kwahlukaniswe umphefumulo nomoya , amalungu nomnkantsha , lahlulela imicabango nezizindlo zenhliziyo ;
58004013	futhi akukho nto edaliweyo engabonakali phambi kwakhe , kepha konke kwambuliwe kusobala emehlweni akhe esiyakuzilanda kuye .
58004014	Ngakho-ke lokhu sinomPristi omkhulu kakhulu odabulile amazulu , uJesu iNdodana kaNkulunkulu , masibambelele kuso isivumo sethu .
58004015	Ngokuba asinaye umPristi omkhulu ongenakuzwelana nobuthakathaka bethu , kepha olingiwe kukho konke njengathi , engenasono .
58004016	Ngakho-ke masisondele ngesibindi esihlalweni somusa ukuba samukeliswe isihawu , sifumane umusa wokusiza ngesikhathi esifaneleyo .
58005001	Ngokuba yilowo nalowo mpristi omkhulu okhethwa kubantu umiselwa abantu kokukaNkulunkulu , ukuze anikele izipho nemihlatshelo ngenxa yezono ;
58005002	angabekezelela abangazi lutho nabadukayo , lokhu naye uzungeziwe ngubuthakathaka ;
58005003	ngenxa yabo kufanele ukuba , njengalokhu enikela ngezono zabantu , anikele kanjalo nangezakhe .
58005004	Akukho muntu ozithathela leso sikhundla , kuphela obizelwa kuso nguNkulunkulu njengo-Aroni .
58005005	Kanjalo noKristu akazidumisanga yena aze abe ngumpristi omkhulu , kepha wadunyiswa nguye owakhuluma kuye , wathi : " UyiNdodana yami wena , namuhla ngikuzele , "
58005006	njengokuba esho nakwenye indawo ngokuthi : " Wena ungumpristi kuze kube phakade ngokokuma kukaMelkisedeki , "
58005007	owathi esenikele emihleni yenyama yakhe ngemikhuleko , nokunxusa , nokudazuluka okukhulu , nezinyembezi kuyena onamandla okumsindisa ekufeni , wezwiwa ngenxa yokumesaba uNkulunkulu .
58005008	Noma eyiNdodana , wafunda ukulalela ngalokho ahlupheka ngakho ;
58005009	esephelelisiwe waba yisisusa sokusindiswa okuphakade kubo bonke abamlalelayo ,
58005010	ebizwa nguNkulunkulu ukuthi umpristi omkhulu ngokokuma kukaMelkisedeki .
58005011	Sinokuningi esingakusho ngalokho , okulukhuni ukuchasisela , lokhu senaba buthuntu ekuzweni .
58005012	Ngokuba noma benifanele ukuba nibe ngabafundisi , uma kuya ngesikhathi , nisadinga futhi ukuba kube khona onifundisa iziqalo zezifundiso zamazwi kaNkulunkulu ; senaba ngabadinga ubisi , kungesikho ukudla okuqinileyo .
58005013	Ngokuba lowo odla ubisi akakaqondi lutho lwezwi lokulunga , ngokuba uyingane .
58005014	Kepha ukudla okuqinileyo kungokwabakhulileyo , abathi ngokujwayela ukuwusebenzisa umqondo , sebenawo osulungele ukwahlukanisa okuhle nokubi .
58006001	Ngakho-ke masidlule esifundisweni sokuqala ngoKristu , siqhubekele kokupheleleyo , singabuyi sibeke isisekelo sokuphenduka emisebenzini efileyo , nokukholwa nguNkulunkulu ,
58006002	nesifundiso sombhapathizo nokubeka izandla , nokuvuka kwabafileyo nokwahlulelwa okuphakade .
58006003	Siyakukwenza lokho , uma uNkulunkulu evuma .
58006004	Ngokuba akunakwenzeka ukuba labo asebake bakhanyiswa banambitha isiphiwo sasezulwini , benziwa abahlanganyeli kuMoya oNgcwele ,
58006005	banambitha izwi elihle likaNkulunkulu namandla ezwe elizayo ,
58006006	babuye bahlubuka — akunakwenzeka ukuba babuye bavuswe , baphenduke , lokhu sebezibethelela iNdodana kaNkulunkulu , bayithela ngehlazo obala .
58006007	Ngokuba umhlabathi , ophuze imvula efika kaningi phezu kwawo , umilisa imifino ebasizayo abawulinyelwayo , uyabusiswa nguNkulunkulu ;
58006008	kepha uma uveza ameva nekhakhasi , uyaleka , useduze nokuqalekiswa , ukuphela kwawo ngukushiswa .
58006009	Kepha siyethemba ngani bathandekayo okuhle kunalokho , ngisho okuqondene nokusindiswa , noma sikhuluma kanje .
58006010	Ngokuba uNkulunkulu kasiye ongalungile ukuba akhohlwe umsebenzi wenu nothando enalubonakalisa ngakulo igama lakhe , lokhu nibakhonzile abangcwele , nisabakhonza .
58006011	Kepha sinxanela ukuba yilowo nalowo kini abonakalise lokho kukhuthalela , lize liphelele ithemba kuze kube sekupheleni ,
58006012	ukuba ningabi buthuntu , kodwa nibalingise labo abadla ifa lesithembiso ngokukholwa nangokubekezela .
58006013	Ngokuba lapho uNkulunkulu wamthembisa u-Abrahama , wazifunga yena , lokhu kungekho omkhulu kunaye angamfunga ,
58006014	wathi : " Impela ngiyakukubusisa nokukubusisa , ngiyakukwandisa nokukwandisa ; "
58006015	kanjalo kwathi esebekezele , wakuzuza okwathenjiswayo .
58006016	Ngokuba abantu bafunga omkhulu kunabo ; kubona isifungo siyaqeda ukuphikisana konke , siqinise .
58006017	Kulokhu-ke uNkulunkulu , ethanda kakhulu impela ukubonisa izindlalifa zesithembiso ukungaguquleki kwecebo lakhe , walamula ngesifungo ,
58006018	ukuze ngezinto ezimbili ezingeguquleke , uNkulunkulu angeqambe amanga ngazo , sibe nenduduzo enamandla thina esibalekele ekulibambeni ithemba esilimiselweyo ,
58006019	esinalo njengehange lomphefumulo , liqinile , ligxilile , lingena kokungaphakathi kwesihenqo ,
58006020	lapho uJesu eyisigijimi sokusandulela wangena khona , esewaba ngumpristi omkhulu kuze kube phakade ngokokuma kukaMelkisedeki .
58007001	Ngokuba uMelkisedeki lo , inkosi yaseSalema , umpristi kaNkulunkulu oPhezukonke , owahlangabeza u-Abrahama mhla ebuya ekubulaleni amakhosi , wambusisa ;
58007002	u-Abrahama wamabela okweshumi kukho konke yena ogama lakhe lithi kuqala ukuhunyushwa kwalo inkosi yokulunga , bese kuba yinkosi yaseSalema , okungukuthi inkosi yokuthula ,
58007003	engenayise , engenanina , engenaluzalo , engenakuqala kwezinsuku nakuphela kokuphila , kepha efaniswe neNdodana kaNkulunkulu , uhlala engumpristi njalonjalo .
58007004	Qondani-ke ukuthi ungakanani yena owanikwa okweshumi kwempango ngu-Abrahama ukhokho .
58007005	Nalabo bamadodana kaLevi abamukeliswa ubupristi banomyalo wokuthatha okweshumi kubantu ngokomthetho , okungukuthi kubafowabo , ingani baphume okhalweni luka-Abrahama ;
58007006	kepha yena ongabalwa ozalweni lwabo uthathile okweshumi ku-Abrahama , wambusisa lowo onezithembiso .
58007007	Kepha akunakuphikwa ukuthi omncinyane ubusiswa ngomkhulu .
58007008	Lapha-ke abantu abafayo bamukeliswa okweshumi , kepha lapho ngofakazelwa ukuthi uyaphila .
58007009	Futhi kungathiwa noLevi owamukela okweshumi watheliswa okweshumi ngaye u-Abrahama ,
58007010	ngokuba wayesesokhalweni lukayise mzukwana uMelkisedeki emhlangabeza .
58007011	Uma-ke kwakukhona ukuphelela ngobupristi bukaLevi ngokuba isizwe samiselwa bona ngomthetho — kwakusaswelekelani ukuba kuvele omunye umpristi ngokukaMelkisedeki engabizwa ngokokuma kuka-Aroni na ?
58007012	Ngokuba uma ubupristi buguquliwe , kuyadingeka ukuba kuguqulwe nomthetho .
58007013	Kepha lowo okushiwo lokho ngaye ungowesinye isizwe okungabanga bikho kuso umuntu owake wakhonza e-altare .
58007014	Ngokuba kusobala ukuthi iNkosi yethu ivele kuJuda , isizwe uMose angakhulumanga lutho ngaso ngobupristi .
58007015	Ikakhulu kusobala lokho , uma kumiswa omunye umpristi ofana noMelkisedeki ,
58007016	ongamiswanga ngomthetho womyalo wenyama kodwa ngamandla okuphila okungabhubhiyo .
58007017	Ngokuba kufakazwa ngaye ukuthi : " Wena ungumpristi kuze kube phakade ngokokuma kukaMelkisedeki . "
58007018	Ngokuba umthetho wokuqala uyachithwa ngenxa yobuthakathaka bawo nokungasizi kwawo ,
58007019	lokhu umthetho awuphelelisanga lutho , kepha sekungeniswa ithemba elingcono , esisondela ngalo kuNkulunkulu .
58007020	Futhi ngalokho ukuthi akubanga ngaphandle kokufunga — ngokuba labo kambe babekwa babe ngabapristi ngaphandle kokufunga ,
58007021	kepha yena wabekwa ngokufunga nguye owasho kuye ukuthi : " INkosi yafunga , ayiyikuzisola , yathi : ‘ Wena ungumpristi kuze kube phakade . ’ "
58007022	Ngokungakho-ke uJesu waba yisiboniso sesivumelwano esingcono .
58007023	Kulabo-ke baba baningi ababekwa babe ngabapristi , ngokuba bathiyeka ngenxa yokufa ukuba baqhube njalo ;
58007024	kepha yena , ngenxa yokuba ehlala phakade , unobupristi obungenakuguquka ;
58007025	ngakho-ke unamandla okusindisa ngokupheleleyo abeza kuNkulunkulu ngaye , lokhu ephilela njalo ukubamela .
58007026	Ngokuba umpristi omkhulu onjalo usifanele thina , ongcwele , ongenacala , ongenabala , owahlukanisiwe nezoni , owenziwa aphakame phezu kwamazulu ,
58007027	ongadingi imihla ngemihla njengalabo bapristi abakhulu ukunikela ngemihlatshelo ngenxa yezakhe izono kuqala nangasemuva ngenxa yezabantu ; ngokuba wenza lokho kanye mhla ezinikela yena .
58007028	Ngokuba umthetho umisa abantu babe ngabapristi abakhulu abanobuthakathaka , kepha izwi lesifungo elalandela umthetho limisa iNdodana epheleliswe kuze kube phakade .
58008001	Kepha okuyindikimba kwesikushoyo yilokhu : sinompristi omkhulu onjalo osewahlala ngakwesokunene sesihlalo sobukhosi soMkhulu emazulwini ,
58008002	isikhonzi sokungcwele nesetabernakele lempela elamiswa yiNkosi kungemuntu .
58008003	Ngokuba yilowo nalowo mpristi omkhulu umiselwa ukunikela ngeminikelo nemihlatshelo ; ngakho-ke kuyadingeka ukuba naye lo abe nakho okuthile kokunikela .
58008004	Ngokuba uma ebesemhlabeni , ubengayikuba ngumpristi nakanye , ngokuba bakhona abapristi abanikela ngeminikelo ngomthetho ,
58008005	bekhonza okungumfanekiso nesithunzi sokwasezulwini , njengokuba uMose wayalwa esezakwenza itabernakele ngokuthi : " Bheka , wokwenza konke ngesifanekiso owaboniswa sona entabeni ; "
58008006	kepha kalokhu unikiwe inkonzo enhle kakhulu , njengalokhu engumlamuleli wesivumelwano esihle kakhulu , esimisiwe ngokwezithembiso ezinhle kakhulu .
58008007	Ngokuba uma leso sivumelwano sokuqala besingasoleki , bekungayikufunwa indawo yesibili .
58008008	Ngokuba lapho ebasolayo , uthi kubo : " Bhekani , izinsuku ziyeza , isho iNkosi , lapho ngiyakwenza isivumelwano esisha nendlu ka-Israyeli , nendlu kaJuda ,
58008009	kungenjengesivumelwano engasenzayo nawoyise mhla ngibabamba ngesandla ukubakhipha ezweni laseGibithe , ngokuba abahlalanga esivumelwaneni sami , nami angibanakanga , isho iNkosi .
58008010	Ngokuba yilesi esiyisivumelwano engiyakusenza nendlu ka-Israyeli emva kwalezo zinsuku , isho iNkosi : ngiyakufaka imithetho yami engqondweni yabo , ngiyilobe ezinhliziyweni zabo , ngibe nguNkulunkulu wabo , bona babe ngabantu bami .
58008011	Abasayikufundisa kube yilowo nalowo owakubo , nalowo umfowabo , ngokuthi : ‘ Yazi INkosi ; ’ ngokuba bonke bayakungazi , kusukela komncane kuze kufike komkhulu wabo .
58008012	Ngokuba ngiyakuba nesihawu ngokungalungi kwabo , nezono zabo angisayikuzikhumbula . "
58008013	Ngokusho lokho ukuthi : " Esisha , " uthe esokuqala sigugile ; kepha okugugayo osekukudala kuseduze nokunyamalala .
58009001	Kepha nesivumelwano sokuqala kambe sasinezimiso zenkonzo nendlu engcwele yasezweni .
58009002	Ngokuba kwakhiwa itabernakele lokuqala okwakukhona kulo uthi lwezibani , netafula , nezinkwa zokubukwa , okuthiwa elingcwele ;
58009003	ngasemva kwesihenqo sesibili kwakukhona itabernakele elithiwa elingcwelengcwele ,
58009004	eline-altare legolide lokuthunqisa nomphongolo wesivumelwano umboziwe ngegolide nxazonke , okwakukhona kuwo isitsha segolide esiphethe imana , nenduku ka-Aroni eyahlumayo , nezibhebhe zesivumelwano ;
58009005	phezu kwawo kwakukhona amakherubi enkazimulo engamele isihlalo somusa , okungenakukhulunywa ngakho ngakunye manje .
58009006	Kepha lezo zinto zilungisiwe ngokunjalo , abapristi bangena njalo etabernakele lokuqala befeza izinkonzo ,
58009007	kodwa kwelesibili kungena umpristi omkhulu yedwa kanye ngomnyaka , kungengaphandle kwegazi anikela ngalo ngenxa yakhe uqobo nangenxa yezono zabantu ,
58009008	uMoya oNgcwele etshengisa lokhu ukuthi ayikabonakaliswa indlela eya endaweni engcwele , lisemi itabernakele lokuqala ,
58009009	elona lingumfanekiso kulesi sikhathi samanje , okulethwa ngawo iminikelo nemihlatshelo engenakumenza okhonzayo aphelele maqondana nonembeza ,
58009010	kodwa yona kanye nokudla nokuphuza nokugeza okuyizinhlobonhlobo iyizimiso zenyama kuphela ezibekiweyo , kuze kufike isikhathi sokupheleliswa kwezinto .
58009011	Kepha lokhu uKristu esefikile , engumpristi omkhulu wezinto ezinhle ezizayo , wadabula itabernakele elikhulu neliphelele kunalelo , elingenziwanga ngezandla , okungukuthi elingesilo lalokhu kudalwa ,
58009012	wangena kanye kuphela endaweni engcwele , kungengegazi lezimbuzi nelamathole kepha ngegazi lakhe , ezuzile ukukhululwa okuphakade .
58009013	Ngokuba uma igazi lezimbuzi nelezinkunzi nomlotha wesithole kufafaza abangcolileyo , kuhlambulula kube ngukuhlanzeka kwenyama ,
58009014	kakhulu kangakanani igazi likaKristu owazinikela kuNkulunkulu ngoMoya ophakade engenacala lizakuhlanza unembeza wethu emisebenzini efileyo , ukuze sikhonze uNkulunkulu ophilayo .
58009015	Ngalokho-ke ungumlamuleli wesivumelwano esisha , kuze kuthi ngokufa okungenxa yokukhululwa eziphambekweni zesivumelwano sokuqala ababiziweyo bazuze ifa eliphakade elathenjiswayo .
58009016	Ngokuba lapho kukhona itestamente , kufuneka ukuba kubikwe ukufa kowalenzayo ;
58009017	ngokuba itestamente lisebenza sekufiwe , ngokuba alize lingaba namandla esekhona owalenzayo .
58009018	Ngalokho-ke isivumelwano sokuqala asimiswanga ngaphandle kwegazi .
58009019	Ngokuba isikhulunyiwe imiyalelo yonke ngokomthetho nguMose kubantu bonke , wayesethatha igazi lamathole nelezimbuzi kanye namanzi noboya obubomvu nehisopi , wafafaza incwadi nabantu bonke ,
58009020	ethi : " Lokhu kuyigazi lesivumelwano aniyale ngaso uNkulunkulu . "
58009021	Netabernakele futhi , nezitsha zonke zenkonzo wakufafaza kanjalo ngegazi .
58009022	Yebo , cishe zonke izinto zihlanjululwa ngegazi ngokomthetho ; ngaphandle kokuchitha igazi akukho ukuthethelelwa .
58009023	Njalo-ke kwakudingekile ukuba imifanekiso yokusezulwini ihlanzwe ngalokho , kepha okusezulwini uqobo lwakho kuhlanzwe ngeminikelo emihle kunalena .
58009024	Ngokuba uKristu kangenanga endaweni engcwele eyenziwe ngezandla , engumfanekiso waleyo okuyiyo ngempela , kepha wangena ezulwini uqobo ukuba manje abonakale ebusweni bukaNkulunkulu ngenxa yethu ,
58009025	kungesikho futhi ukuba azinikele kaningi , njengalokhu umpristi omkhulu engena endaweni engcwele iminyaka ngeminyaka , ephethe igazi elingesilo elakhe ;
58009026	uma kwakunjalo wayemelwe ukuhlupheka kaningi selokhu kwasekelwa izwe ; kodwa kalokhu ubonakalisiwe kanye ekupheleni kwezikhathi ukuba asuse izono ngokuzinikela kwakhe .
58009027	Futhi njengalokhu kumiselwe abantu ukuba bafe kanye , emva kwalokhu ukwahlulelwa ,
58009028	kunjalo noKristu , esenikelwe kanye ukuba athwale izono zabaningi , uyakubonakala ngokwesibili ngaphandle kwesono kulabo abamlindeleyo , kube ngukusindiswa .
58010001	Ngokuba lokhu umthetho unesithunzi sezinto ezinhle ezizayo , ungesiwo umfanekiso wazo uqobo , ungeze waba namandla ngemihlatshelo enikelwa njalonjalo iminyaka ngeminyaka ukubenza baphelele labo abasondelayo ;
58010002	uma kwakungenjalo , nga ingayekwanga ukunikelwa na ? lokhu phela abakhonzayo sebehlanjululwe kanye babengasayikuba novalo ngezono .
58010003	Kodwa kuleyo mihlatshelo kukhona ukukhunjulwa kwezono iminyaka ngeminyaka ;
58010004	ngokuba akunakwenzeka ukuba igazi lezinkunzi nelezimbuzi lisuse izono .
58010005	Ngalokho-ke esefika ezweni uthi : " Umhlatshelo nomnikelo awuwuthandanga , kodwa ungilungisele umzimba .
58010006	Iminikelo yokushiswa nemihlatshelo ngenxa yesono awuyithokozelanga .
58010007	Ngase ngithi : ‘ Bheka , ngiyeza — emqulwini wencwadi kulotshiwe ngami — ukuba ngiyenze , Nkulunkulu , intando yakho . ’ "
58010008	Eseshilo ngasenhla ukuthi : " Imihlatshelo , neminikelo , neminikelo yokushiswa , nemihlatshelo ngenxa yezono awuyithandanga , awuyithokozelanga , " eyona ilethwa ngokomthetho ,
58010009	ubuye wathi : " Bheka , ngiyeza ukwenza intando yakho . " Ususa okokuqala , ukuze amise okwesibili .
58010010	Ngaleyo ntando singcwelisiwe ngokunikelwa komzimba kaJesu Kristu kanye kuphela .
58010011	Abapristi bonke kambe bemi bekhonza imihla ngemihla , benikela kaningi ngayona leyo mihlatshelo engasoze yaba namandla okususa izono ;
58010012	kepha yena , esenikele ngomhlatshelo waba munye ngenxa yezono , wahlala phakade ngakwesokunene sikaNkulunkulu ,
58010013	usalindele izitha zakhe zize zenziwe isenabelo sezinyawo zakhe .
58010014	Ngokuba ngomnikelo munye uphelelise njalonjalo labo abangcwelisiweyo .
58010015	Kepha noMoya oNgcwele uyafakaza kithina , ngokuba emva kokusho kwakhe ukuthi :
58010016	" Yilesi sivumelwano engizakusenza nabo , emva kwalezo zinsuku , isho iNkosi : Ngiyakufaka imithetho yami ezinhliziyweni zabo , ngiyilobe engqondweni yabo ,
58010017	nezono zabo nobubi babo angisoze ngakukhumbula futhi . "
58010018	Kepha lapho kukhona ukuthethelelwa kwalokho , akusadingeki ukunikela ngenxa yesono .
58010019	Ngakho-ke , bazalwane , njengokuba sinesibindi sokungena endaweni engcwele ngegazi likaJesu
58010020	ngendlela asivulela yona , indlela entsha ephilayo , edabula isihenqo , okungukuthi inyama yakhe ,
58010021	sinompristi omkhulu wendlu kaNkulunkulu ,
58010022	masisondele ngenhliziyo eqinisileyo ngokwethemba okupheleleyo kokukholwa , zifafaziwe izinhliziyo zethu kungasekho valo lokubi , umzimba wethu ugeziwe ngamanzi acwebileyo ;
58010023	masibambisise isivumo sethemba lethu singaxegi , ngokuba ukholekile lowo owethembisayo ;
58010024	masiqaphelane , ukuze kuvuswe uthando nemisebenzi emihle ,
58010025	singakuyeki ukuhlangana kwethu njengomkhuba wabanye , kepha masivuselelane , ikakhulu njengokuba nibona usuku lusondela .
58010026	Ngokuba uma sona ngamabomu emva kokuba sesamukele ukwazi kweqiniso , akusekho umnikelo ngezono ,
58010027	kepha kuphela ukulindela okwesabekayo ukwahlulelwa nomlilo oshisayo ozakuqeda amaphikankani .
58010028	Odelele umthetho kaMose uyakufa engahawukelwa ngezwi lawofakazi ababili noma bebathathu ;
58010029	pho , nithi ufanele ukushaywa kangakanani kunalokho lowo onyathele phansi iNdodana kaNkulunkulu , wadelela igazi lesivumelwano angcweliswa ngalo , wahlambalaza uMoya womusa , na ?
58010030	Ngokuba siyamazi owathi : " Ngeyami impindiselo , yimina engiyakubuyisela , " futhi-ke : " INkosi iyakubahlulela abantu bayo . "
58010031	Kuyesabeka ukuwela ezandleni zikaNkulunkulu ophilayo .
58010032	Kepha khumbulani izinsuku zakuqala okwathi ngazo senikhanyisiwe nakhuthazela empini enkulu yezinhlupheko ,
58010033	kokunye ngokuba ngumbukwane ngezinhlamba nangezimbandezeko , kokunye ngokuba ngabahlanganyeli nababephathwa kanjalo .
58010034	Ngokuba nazwelana nababoshiweyo , navuma ngokuthokoza ukuphangwa kwempahla yenu , nazi ukuthi nina ninempahla enhle kunaleyo , nemiyo njalo .
58010035	Ngakho-ke maningalahli isibindi senu esinomvuzo omkhulu .
58010036	Ngokuba nidinga ukubekezela , ukuze seniyenzile intando kaNkulunkulu namukele isithembiso .
58010037	Ngokuba kuse yisikhashana nje , ozayo uyeza , akayikulibala ;
58010038	kepha olungileyo wami uyakuphila ngokukholwa ; kepha uma ehlehla nyovane , umphefumulo wami awunakuthokoza ngaye .
58010039	Kepha thina asisibo abokuhlehlela ekubhujisweni , kodwa singabokukholwa , kuze kube ngukusindiswa komphefumulo .
58011001	Kepha ukukholwa kungukuqiniseka ngezinto ezithenjwayo , kuyiqiniso ngezinto ezingabonwayo .
58011002	Ngokuba okhokho bafakazelwa ngakho .
58011003	Ngokukholwa siqonda ukuthi izwe lonke ladatshulwa ngezwi likaNkulunkulu , kuze kuthi okubonwayo akuvelanga kokubonwayo .
58011004	Ngokukholwa u-Abela wanikela kuNkulunkulu ngomhlatshelo omuhle kunoKayini , athola ngakho ubufakazi bokuthi ulungile , uNkulunkulu uqobo efakaza ngezipho zakhe ; nangakho usakhuluma , noma efile .
58011005	Ngokukholwa u-Enoke wathathwa , ukuze angaboni ukufa , akabe esafunyanwa , ngokuba uNkulunkulu wayemthabathile . Ngokuba engakathathwa ufakazelwe ukuthi wayethokozisa uNkulunkulu ;
58011006	kepha-ke ngaphandle kokukholwa akwenzeki ukumthokozisa ; ngokuba ozayo kuNkulunkulu umelwe ukukholwa ukuthi ukhona nokuthi ungumvuzi walabo abamfunayo .
58011007	Ngokukholwa uNowa exwayisiwe ngezinto ebezingakabonwa , esaba uNkulunkulu , wakha umkhumbi wokusindisa indlu yakhe , okungakho walahla izwe , waba yindlalifa yokulunga okuvela ngokukholwa .
58011008	Ngokukholwa u-Abrahama walalela ebizwa ukuba aphume aye endaweni abezakuyamukeliswa ibe yifa lakhe ; waphuma engazi lapho eya khona .
58011009	Ngokukholwa waba ngumfokazi ezweni lesithembiso kwangathi ngelezizwe , ehlala ematendeni , beno-Isaka noJakobe , beyizindlalifa kanye naye zaleso sithembiso ,
58011010	ngokuba wayebheke umuzi onezisekelo , omakhi nomenzi wawo nguNkulunkulu .
58011011	Ngokukholwa naye uSara uqobo wathola amandla okukhulelwa esedlulelwe yisikhathi , ngokuba wathi ukholekile owethembisayo .
58011012	Ngakho-ke kwavela koyedwa , yena enjengosewafa , abangangezinkanyezi zezulu ngobuningi , bengangesihlabathi esisogwini lolwandle esingenakubalwa .
58011013	Bonke laba bafa bekholiwe , bengazamukeliswanga izithembiso , kepha bezibonile , bezithakazele zikude , bevumile ukuthi bangabafokazi nezihambi emhlabeni .
58011014	Ngokuba abasho kanjalo babonakalisa ukuthi bafuna izwe lakubo .
58011015	Uma kambe bebecabanga ngalelo ababephuma kulo , bebeyakuba nethuba lokubuyela kulo ;
58011016	kepha manje balangazelela elihle kunalelo , okungukuthi elasezulwini . Ngalokho uNkulunkulu akanamahloni ngabo ukuba abizwe ngokuthi uNkulunkulu wabo , ngokuba ubalungisele umuzi .
58011017	Ngokukholwa u-Abrahama evivinywa wanikela ngo-Isaka , yebo , yena owayamukele izithembiso , wanikela ngozelwe yedwa wakhe ,
58011018	okwathiwa kuye : " Inzalo yakho iyakubizwa ngo-Isaka , "
58011019	ethi uNkulunkulu unamandla okuvusa nakwabafileyo ; ngokulinganisa wabuye wamthola futhi evela khona .
58011020	Ngokukholwa u-Isaka wabusisa oJakobe no-Esawu ngezinto ebezizakuza .
58011021	Ngokukholwa uJakobe esezakufa wabusisa leyo naleyo yamadodana kaJosefa , wakhuleka encikile esihlokweni sodondolo lwakhe .
58011022	Ngokukholwa uJosefa esezakufa wakhuluma ngokuphuma kwabantwana bakwa-Israyeli , wayaleza ngamathambo akhe .
58011023	Ngokukholwa uMose esezelwe wafihlwa ngabazali bakhe izinyanga ezintathu , ngokuba bembona engumntwana omuhle ; abawesabanga umyalo wenkosi .
58011024	Ngokukholwa uMose esekhulile wala ukubizwa ngokuthi indodana yendodakazi kaFaro ;
58011025	kunalokho wakhetha ukuphathwa kabi kanye nabantu bakaNkulunkulu kunokuba athokoze isikhashana esonweni ,
58011026	ethi ukuthukwa ngenxa kaKristu kuyimfuyo enkulu kunengcebo yaseGibithe , ngokuba wayebheke umvuzo .
58011027	Ngokukholwa washiya iGibithe engesabi ulaka lwenkosi ; ngokuba wakhuthazela sengathi uyambona ongabonwayo .
58011028	Ngokukholwa wamisa iPhasika nokufafaza ngegazi , ukuze umbhubhisi angathinti amazibulo abo .
58011029	Ngokukholwa badabula uLwandle Olubomvu kungathi kusemhlabathini owomileyo , okwathi abaseGibithe bekulinga lokho , baminza .
58011030	Ngokukholwa izingange zaseJeriko zawa , sezizungeziwe izinsuku eziyisikhombisa .
58011031	Ngokukholwa , uRahabi isifebe , akabhubhanga kanye nabangalalelanga , esezamukele izinhloli ngokuthula .
58011032	Ngisezakuthini futhi na ? Isikhathi kambe sizakungishiya , uma ngibalisa ngoGideyoni , noBaraki , noSamsoni , noJefta , noDavide , noSamuweli nabaprofethi ,
58011033	abathi ngokukholwa banqoba imibuso , basebenza ukulunga , bazuza izithembiso , bavimba imilomo yezingonyama ,
58011034	bacima amandla omlilo , baphepha osikweni lwenkemba , baphiwa amandla ebuthakathakeni , baba yiziqhwaga empini , baxosha izimpi zabezizwe .
58011035	Abesifazane bamukeliswa abafileyo babo bevusiwe ; abanye bahlushwa , kabavuma ukukhululwa , ukuze bathole ukuvuka okuhle ;
58011036	abanye balingwa ngokujivazwa nokushaywa , yebo , nokuboshwa nokufakwa etilongweni ;
58011037	bakhandwa ngamatshe , banqunywa ngesaha , balingwa , babulawa ngenkemba , bazulazula bembethe izikhumba zezimvu nezezimbuzi , beswela , behlushwa , bephathwa kabi ,
58011038	izwe elingabafanele bona , behamba emahlane , nasezintabeni , nasemihumeni , nasemigedeni yomhlaba .
58011039	Labo bonke , befakazelwe ngokukholwa , abazuzanga isithembiso ,
58011040	ngokuba uNkulunkulu wayesibonele okuhle kunalokho , ukuze bangapheleliswa ngaphandle kwethu .
58012001	Ngalokho-ke nathi , lokhu sinefu elingaka lawofakazi elisihaqileyo , masilahle konke okusindayo nesono esithandela kangaka kithi , sigijime ngokubekezela kulokhu kuncintisana esikumiselweyo ,
58012002	sibhekile kuJesu , umqalisi nomphelelisi wokukholwa kwethu , owathi esikhundleni sentokozo ayibekelweyo wathwala isiphambano engalinaki ihlazo , wahlala ngakwesokunene sesihlalo sobukhosi sikaNkulunkulu .
58012003	Yebo , mqondeni yena owakhuthazela ephikwa kangaka yizoni , ukuze ningakhathali , niphele amandla emiphefumulweni yenu .
58012004	Anikamelani nezono nilwa kuze kube segazini ;
58012005	senikhohliwe umyalo okhuluma kinina njengakubantwana wokuthi : " Ndodana yami , ungadeleli ukulaya kweNkosi , uphele amandla , nxa usolwa yiyo ,
58012006	ngokuba iNkosi iyamlaya emthandayo ishaye yileyo naleyo ndodana eyamukelayo . "
58012007	Bekezelani ekulayweni ; uNkulunkulu uyaniphathisa okwabantwana , ngokuba yiyiphi indodana engalaywa nguyise na ?
58012008	Kepha uma ningalaywa , abathe bonke benziwa abahlanganyeli kukho , khona-ke ningabesihlahla , anisiwo amadodana .
58012009	Futhi-ke sasinawobaba bethu benyama abasilayayo , sabazisa ; pho , asiyikuthobela uYise wawomoya kakhulu kunalokho , siphile , na ?
58012010	Ngokuba bona kambe basilaya izinsukwana njengokubona kwabo , kepha yena kube yinsizakalo , size sithole ukuhlanganyela ubungcwele bakhe .
58012011	Ukulaya konke okwamanje kungathi akusikho okwentokozo , kepha kungokosizi , kodwa ngasemuva kuyabathelela isithelo esihle sokulunga labo abahlakahliswe yikho .
58012012	Ngakho-ke qinisani izandla ezibuthakathaka namadolo axegayo ,
58012013	nenzele izinyawo zenu izindlela eziqondileyo ukuba okuqhugayo kungaphinyizeki , kepha kunalokho kuphulukiswe .
58012014	Zamelani ukuthula nabo bonke kanye nokungcweliswa , ongenakho angeyibone iNkosi ;
58012015	niqaphelisise kungabikho osilelayo emseni kaNkulunkulu , funa kumile impande imbe ebabayo , inixobise , kungcoliswe abaningi yiyo ,
58012016	kungabikho oyisifebe noma odumazayo njengo-Esawu owathengisa ubuzibulo bakhe ngesidlo sinye nje .
58012017	Ngokuba niyazi ukuthi , nokuba ngasemuva ethanda ukudla ifa lesibusiso , waliwa , ngokuba akalitholanga ithuba lokuphenduka , noma ekufunisisa ngezinyembezi .
58012018	Ngokuba anizanga entabeni ephathekayo nesha umlilo , nasekufiphaleni , nasebumnyameni , nasesivunguvungwini ,
58012019	nasekukhaleni kwecilongo , nasekuzwakaleni kwamazwi , abathe ukukuzwa , bancenga ukuba kungabe kusakhulunywa izwi kubo ,
58012020	ngokuba babengenakukuthwala lokho abayalwa ngakho kokuthi : " Ngisho nesilwane , uma sithinta intaba , siyakukhandwa ngamatshe ; "
58012021	yebo , umbono wesabeka kangaka , waze wathi uMose : " Nginovalo olukhulu , ngiyathuthumela ; "
58012022	kodwa nize entabeni yaseSiyoni nasemzini kaNkulunkulu ophilayo , iJerusalema lasezulwini , nasezigidigidini zezingelosi ,
58012023	nasebandleni lamazibulo abhaliwe ezulwini , nakuNkulunkulu , uMahluleli wabo bonke , nakuyo imimoya yabalungileyo abaphelelisiweyo ,
58012024	nakuJesu , umlamuleli wesivumelwano esisha , nasegazini lokufafaza elikhuluma okukhulu kunelika-Abela .
58012025	Bhekani , ningamali okhulumayo ; ngokuba uma bengaphunyukanga labo ababemala lowo owabaxwayisa emhlabeni , kakhulu asiyikuphunyuka thina esimfulathelayo oxwayisa esezulwini ,
58012026	ozwi lakhe lanyakazisa umhlaba ngaleso sikhathi , kepha manje uthembisile wathi : " Kusezakuba kanye ngizamazamise kungabi ngumhlaba wodwa , kepha nezulu futhi . "
58012027	Lokho kokuthi : " Kusezakuba kanye " kutshengisa ukuguqulwa kwezinto ezinyakaziswayo , njengokuba zenziwe , ukuze lezo ezinganyakaziswayo zime .
58012028	Ngakho-ke lokhu samukeliswa umbuso ongenakunyakaziswa , masibonge ngesingamkhonza ngakho uNkulunkulu ngokumthokozisa , nangokumhlonipha , nangokuthuthumela ,
58012029	ngokuba uNkulunkulu wethu ungumlilo oqothulayo .
58013001	Malume njalo uthando lobuzalwane .
58013002	Ningakhohlwa ukungenisa izihambi ngokuba ngalokho abanye bangenisa izingelosi bengazi .
58013003	Bakhumbuleni ababoshiweyo kungathi niboshiwe kanye nabo , nabaphethwe kabi , njengalokhu nani nisemzimbeni .
58013004	Ukuganana makuhlonishwe yibo bonke , umbhede ungabi nasisihla , ngokuba izifebe neziphingi uNkulunkulu uyakuzahlulela .
58013005	Ukwenza kwenu makungabi ngokokufisa imali ; yaneliswani ngeninakho ; ngokuba yena ushilo wathi : " Angisoze ngakuyeka , angisoze ngakushiya , "
58013006	ukuze sisho ngesibindi , sithi : " INkosi ingumsizi wami , angiyikwesaba ; umuntu angangenzani na ? "
58013007	Bakhumbuleni ababenihola bekhuluma izwi likaNkulunkulu kini , niqonda ukuphela kokuhamba kwabo , nilingise ukukholwa kwabo .
58013008	UJesu Kristu nguyena izolo nanamuhla , yebo , naphakade .
58013009	Ningadukiswa yizifundiso eziyizinhlobonhlobo nezingaziwayo ; ngokuba kuhle ukuba inhliziyo iqiniswe ngomusa , kungabi ngokudla , abangasizakalanga ngakho abahamba ngakho .
58013010	Sine-altare thina , abangenalungelo lokudla kulo abakhonza etabernakele .
58013011	Ngokuba izidumbu zalezo zilwane ezigazi lazo lingeniswa ngumpristi omkhulu endaweni engcwele ngenxa yezono zishiswa ngaphandle kwekamu .
58013012	Ngakho-ke naye uJesu , ukuze angcwelise abantu ngegazi lakhe , wahlupheka ngaphandle kwesango .
58013013	Masiphumele kuye ngaphandle kwekamu , sithwale ihlazo lakhe .
58013014	Ngokuba lapha asinamuzi omiyo , kepha siyawufuna ozayo .
58013015	Masinikele njalonjalo kuNkulunkulu ngaye umhlatshelo wokubonga , okungukuthi isithelo sezindebe ezivuma igama lakhe .
58013016	Kepha maningakhohlwa ukwenza okuhle nokuphana , ngokuba iminikelo enjalo uNkulunkulu uthokoziswa yiyo .
58013017	Lalelani abaniholayo , nibathobele , ngokuba balinda imiphefumulo yenu njengabazakulandiswa ngayo , ukuze bakwenze lokhu ngokujabula , bangabubuli , ngokuba lokhu akunakunisiza .
58013018	Sikhulekeleni , ngokuba siyethemba ukuthi sinonembeza omuhle , sithanda ukuhamba kahle ezintweni zonke .
58013019	Ngiyaniyala kakhulu ukuba nenze lokho , ukuze ngibuyiselwe kini masinyane .
58013020	Kepha uNkulunkulu wokuthula owakhuphula kwabafileyo umalusi omkhulu wezimvu ngegazi lesivumelwano esimiyo njalo , iNkosi yethu uJesu ,
58013021	makaniphelelise kukho konke okuhle , ukuze nenze intando yakhe , esebenza phakathi kwethu khona lokho okuthokozisayo emehlweni akhe ngoJesu Kristu ; makube kuye inkazimulo kuze kube phakade naphakade . Amen .
58013022	Ngiyaniyala , bazalwane , lamukeleni kahle izwi lokuyala , ngokuba nginilobele ngokufushane .
58013023	Yazini ukuthi umfowethu uThimothewu ukhululiwe ; uma efika masinyane , ngiyakunibona sinaye .
58013024	Khonzani kubo bonke abaniholayo nakubo bonke abangcwele . Abase-Italiya bayakhonza kini .
58013025	Umusa mawube nani nonke . Amen .
59001001	UJakobe , inceku kaNkulunkulu neyeNkosi uJesu Kristu , uyakhonza kuzo izizwe eziyishumi nambili ezihlakazekileyo .
59001002	Bazalwane bami , nxa nehlelwa yizilingo ngezilingo , anothi kungukuthokoza kodwa ,
59001003	nazi ukuthi ukuvivinywa kokukholwa kwenu kuveza ukukhuthazela .
59001004	Kepha ukukhuthazela makube nomsebenzi opheleleyo , ukuze nibe ngabapheleleyo nabangenacala abangasweli lutho .
59001005	Uma-ke kukhona kini oswela ukuhlakanipha , makacele kuNkulunkulu obapha bonke ngobuhle engajakadi , khona uyakuphiwa .
59001006	Kepha makacele ngokukholwa engangabazi ngalutho ; ngokuba ongabazayo unjengedlambi lolwandle eliqhutshwa , ligujiswa ngumoya .
59001007	Ngakho makangasho lowo muntu ukuthi uyakwamukeliswa utho yiNkosi ,
59001008	umuntu onhliziyombili oguquguqukayo ezindleleni zakhe zonke .

60002024	yena owathwala izono zethu emzimbeni wakhe emthini , ukuze kuthi sesifile ezonweni siphile ekulungeni , oyena imivimbo yakhe naphulukiswa ngayo ;
60002025	ngokuba beninjengezimvu ezidukileyo , kodwa manje seniphendukele kuMalusi noMbonisi wemiphefumulo yenu .
60003001	Kanjalo , bafazi , thobelani amadoda enu , ukuze kuthi , uma ekhona ongakholwa yizwi , azuzwe ngaphandle kwezwi ngenkambo yabafazi bawo ,
60003002	ebona inkambo yenu emhlophe esekwesabeni .
60003003	Ukuhloba kwenu makungabi ngokungaphandle , okokwaluka izinwele , nokokufaka igolide , noma okokugqoka izingubo ,
60003004	kepha makube ngumuntu osithekileyo wenhliziyo ohloba ngokungabhubhiyo komoya omnene onokuthula , okuyigugu phambi kukaNkulunkulu .
60003005	Ngokuba kade babezihlobisa kanjalo abesifazane abangcwele abamethembayo uNkulunkulu , bethobela amadoda abo ,
60003006	njengalokho uSara wamlalela u-Abrahama embiza ngokuthi inkosi , eningabantwana bakhe , uma nenza okuhle , ningesatshiswa nokukodwa okwesabisayo .
60003007	Kanjalo , madoda , hlalani nabo ngokokwazi , njengalokhu owesifazane eyisitsha esibuthakathaka , nibanike udumo , lokhu beyizindlalifa zomusa wokuphila kanye nani , ukuze imikhuleko yenu ingathiywa .
60003008	Okokugcina , manibe nhliziyonye nonke , nihawukelane , nithandane ngokwabazalwane , nibe nobubele nokuthobeka ,
60003009	ningaphindisi okubi ngokubi nokuthuka ngokuthuka , kepha kakhulu manibusise , ngokuba nabizelwa lokho ukuba nidle ifa lokubusiswa .
60003010	" Ngokuba osuka ethanda ukuphila nokubona izinsuku ezinhle , makanqande ulimi lwakhe kokubi , nezindebe zakhe zingakhulumi inkohliso ,
60003011	adede ebubini , enze okuhle , afune ukuthula , akujonge ,
60003012	ngokuba amehlo eNkosi aphezu kwabalungileyo , izindlebe zayo zisekunxuseni kwabo , kepha ubuso beNkosi buphezu kwabenza okubi . "
60003013	Pho , ubani onganilimaza , uma nishisekela okuhle na ?
60003014	Kepha noma nihlupheka ngenxa yokulunga , nibusisiwe . Ningesabi ukwesabisa kwabo , ningakhathazeki ,
60003015	kepha mngcweliseni uKristu abe yiNkosi ezinhliziyweni zenu , nihlale ningabalungele ukubaphendula bonke abanibuza isizathu sethemba elikini ,
60003016	kodwa kube ngobumnene nangokwesaba , nibe nonembeza omuhle , ukuze kuthi kulokho abanihleba ngakho bajabhiswe labo abathuka ukuhamba kwenu okuhle kuKristu .
60003017	Ngokuba kuhle ukuhlupheka ngokwenza okuhle , uma kuyintando kaNkulunkulu , kunokwenza okubi .
60003018	Ngokuba naye uKristu wahlupheka kwaba kanye ngezono , olungileyo ngenxa yabangalungile , ukuba asiyise kuNkulunkulu , ebulawa enyameni kepha ephiliswa emoyeni ,
60003019	ehamba ngawo ukushumayeza omoya abasekuboshweni
60003020	abakade bengalaleli , lapho ukubekezela kukaNkulunkulu kubalindele ezinsukwini zikaNowa umkhumbi usakhiwa , abasindiswa ngawo abayingcosana , okungukuthi abayisishiyagalombili ngawo amanzi ;
60003021	enisindiswa ngawo manje nani ngokomfanekiso , okungukuthi ngombhapathizo , kungesikho ukususa insila yenyama kepha ukucela kuNkulunkulu unembeza omuhle , ngokuvuka kukaJesu Kristu
60003022	okhona ngakwesokunene sikaNkulunkulu esenyukele ezulwini , sekubekwe phansi kwakhe izingelosi , negunya , namandla .
60004001	Njengokuba uKristu wahlupheka enyameni , hlomani nani ukuqonda okunjalo , ngokuba ohluphekile enyameni uyekile ukona ,
60004002	ukuze ngesikhathi esiseleyo nisesenyameni ningabe nisahlala ngezinkanuko zabantu kodwa ngentando kaNkulunkulu .
60004003	Ngokuba isikhathi esidlulileyo sasanele ukwenza okuthandwa ngabezizwe ngokuhamba ngamanyala , nangezinkanuko , nangokudakwa , nangokuminza , nangokuxokozela , nangokukhonza izithombe okuyichilo .
60004004	Bayamangala ngokungagijimeli kwenu kulowo msindo wokushinga kwabo , behlambalaza ;
60004005	bayakuziphendulela kulowo olungele ukwahlulela abahambayo nabafileyo .
60004006	Ngokuba ngalokho ivangeli lashunyayelwa nakwabafileyo , ukuze bahlulelwe ngokwabantu enyameni kepha baphile ngokukaNkulunkulu emoyeni .
60004007	Kepha ukuphela kwezinto zonke sekusondele . Ngakho zikhuzeni , nizithibe , ukuze nikhuleke ;
60004008	kunakho konke yibani nokuthandana okunganqamukiyo , ngokuba uthando lusibekela inqwaba yezono ;
60004009	anongenisana ngenjabulo , ningakhononi ,
60004010	nikhonzane , kube yilowo nalowo ngesipho asiphiweyo njengabaphathi abahle bomusa omninginingi kaNkulunkulu ;
60004011	uma umuntu ekhuluma , makakhulume njengokwamazwi kaNkulunkulu ; uma umuntu ekhonza , makakhonze ngamandla awanikwa nguNkulunkulu , ukuze uNkulunkulu adunyiswe kukho konke ngoJesu Kristu okukuye inkazimulo namandla kuze kube phakade naphakade . Amen .
60004012	Bathandekayo , ningamangali ngomlilo ophakathi kwenu enifikelwa yiwo ukuba nilingwe ngokungathi nehlelwe yinto engaziwayo ,
60004013	kodwa njengalokhu ningabahlanganyeli bezinhlupheko zikaKristu , thokozani , ukuze kuthi nasekwambulweni kwenkazimulo yakhe nithokoze , nethabe nokwethaba .
60004014	Uma nithukwa ngenxa yegama likaKristu , nibusisiwe , ngokuba uMoya wenkazimulo nokaNkulunkulu uhlezi phezu kwenu .
60004015	Ngokuba makungabikho kini ohlupheka ngokuba engumbulali , noma eyisela , noma engowenza okubi , noma engozigaxa ezindabeni zabanye ;
60004016	kepha uma ehlupheka ngokuba engumKristu , makangabi namahloni , kepha makadumise uNkulunkulu ngenxa yalelo gama .
60004017	Ngokuba sekuyisikhathi sokuba ukwahlulela kuqale endlini kaNkulunkulu ; kepha uma kuthathela kithina , kuyakuba yini ukuphela kwabangalaleli ivangeli likaNkulunkulu na ?
60004018	Uma olungileyo esindiswa kalukhuni , uyakubonakalaphi ongamesabi uNkulunkulu noyisoni na ?
60004019	Ngakho abahluphekayo ngokwentando kaNkulunkulu mababeke imiphefumulo yabo kuMdali othembekayo ngokwenza okuhle .
60005001	Ngakho ngiyawancenga amalunga aphakathi kwenu mina engiyilunga kanye nawo , nofakazi wezinhlupheko zikaKristu , nomhlanganyeli wenkazimulo ezakwambulwa , ngithi :
60005002	Yalusani umhlambi kaNkulunkulu ophakathi kwenu , kungabi ngokucindezelwa kodwa ngokwentando kaNkulunkulu , kungabi ngenxa yenzuzo eyihlazo kodwa ngenhliziyo evumayo ,
60005003	kungabi njengabazenza amakhosi phezu kwamabandla enabelwa wona , kodwa nibe yizibonelo zomhlambi ;
60005004	kuyakuthi , nxa esebonakaliswa uMalusi omkhulu , niyakuzuza umqhele wenkazimulo ongabuniyo .
60005005	Ngokunjalo , nina basha , thobelani amalunga ; kepha nonke yembathani ukuthobeka , nithobelane , ngokuba uNkulunkulu umelana nabazidlayo , kepha abathobekileyo ubapha umusa .
60005006	Ngalokho zithobeni phansi kwesandla sikaNkulunkulu esinamandla , ukuze aniphakamise ngesikhathi esifaneleyo ,
60005007	niphonse izinkathazo zenu zonke phezu kwakhe , ngokuba uyanikhathalela .
60005008	Qondani , nilinde . Isitha senu , uSathane , siyahamba njengebhubesi elibhodlayo sifuna esingamgwinya ;
60005009	melanani naye niqinile ekukholweni , nazi ukuthi zona lezo zinhlupheko zehlela abazalwane benu abasezweni .
60005010	Kepha uNkulunkulu womusa wonke owanibizela enkazimulweni yakhe yaphakade ngoKristu , senihluphekile isikhashana , yena uqobo uyakuniphelelisa , aniqinise , aninike amandla , asisekele .
60005011	Makube kuye amandla kuze kube phakade naphakade . Amen .
60005012	NgoSilvanu umfowethu othembekayo ngokubona kwami nginilobele ngokufushane , ngincenga , ngifakaza ukuthi lo yiwo umusa oqinisekileyo kaNkulunkulu ; yimani kuwo .
60005013	Liyakhonza kini ibandla elikhethiweyo , kanye nani eliseBabiloni , noMarku indodana yami .
60005014	Bingelelanani ngokwanga kothando . Ukuthula makube kini nonke enikuKristu .
61001001	USimeyoni Petru , inceku nomphostoli kaJesu Kristu , kubo abazuzile ukukholwa okuyigugu ngokufana nokwethu ngokulunga kukaNkulunkulu wethu noMsindisi uJesu Kristu :
61001002	Makwandiswe kini umusa nokuthula ngokumazi uNkulunkulu noJesu iNkosi yethu .
61001003	Njengokuba amandla akhe obuNkulunkulu esinikile konke okuqondene nokuphila nokumesaba uNkulunkulu ngokumazi yena owasibiza ngenkazimulo nobuhle bakhe ,
61001004	esiphiwe ngakho izithembiso eziyigugu nezikhulukazi , ukuze ngazo nibe ngabahlanganyeli nesimo sobuNkulunkulu , nibalekele ukubhubha okusezweni ngezinkanuko ,
61001005	ngalokho nengezela inkuthalo yonke nelekele ubuhle ekukholweni , nasebuhleni ukwazi ,
61001006	nasekwazini ukuzithiba , nasekuzithibeni ukukhuthazela , nasekukhuthazeleni ukumesaba uNkulunkulu ,
61001007	nasekumesabeni uNkulunkulu ukuthanda abazalwane , nasekuthandeni abazalwane uthando .
61001008	Ngokuba uma lezo zinto zikhona kini zivama , ziyanenza ningabi ngabavilaphayo nabangenazithelo ekwazini iNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu ,
61001009	ngokuba okungekho kuye lezo zinto uyimpumputhe , ebona kalufifi , ekhohliwe ukuhlanjululwa ezonweni zakhe zokuqala .
61001010	Ngakho-ke , bazalwane , khuthalelani kakhulu ukwenza kuqiniseke ukubizwa nokukhethwa kwenu ; ngokuba uma nenza lokho , anisoze nakhubeka .
61001011	Ngokuba ngokwenze njalo niyakuphiwa ngokwengcebo ukungena embusweni waphakade weNkosi yethu noMsindisi uJesu Kristu .
61001012	Ngakho-ke ngiyakuba yilokhu nginikhumbuza njalo ngalezo zinto , nakuba nizazi , nime niqinile eqinisweni elikhona .
61001013	Ngithi kufanele , nxa ngisekhona kuleli dokodo , nginivuse ngokunikhumbuza ,
61001014	ngazi ukuthi kuseduze ukususwa kwedokodo lami , njengalokho neNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu yangitshengisa ;
61001015	kepha ngizakukhuthalela ukuba ngezikhathi zonke emva kokumuka kwami nisale nizikhumbule lezo zinto .
61001016	Ngokuba sasingalandeli izinganekwane zobuqili , lapho sanazisa amandla nokufika kweNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu , kodwa sasingababonayo amandla obukhosi bakhe .
61001017	Ngokuba wamukela kuNkulunkulu uYise udumo nenkazimulo , lapho kwafika kuye izwi elinje , livela enkazimulweni yobukhosi , lithi : " Lo uyiNdodana yami ethandekayo engithokozile ngayo " —
61001018	lelo zwi salizwa thina livela ezulwini , sikanye naye entabeni engcwele .
61001019	Sesinalo izwi lesiprofetho eliqinisekile kakhulu , enenza kahle ukuliqaphela kungathi liyisibani esikhanyayo endaweni emnyama kuze kuse , ikhwezi liphumele ezinhliziyweni zenu ,
61001020	nazi lokhu kuqala ukuthi kasikho isiprofetho sombhalo esingachasiselwa ngumuntu ngokwakhe ;
61001021	ngokuba akuzange kuvezwe isiprofetho ngentando yomuntu , kepha abantu beqhutshwa nguMoya oNgcwele bakhuluma okukaNkulunkulu .
61002001	Kepha kwavela nabaprofethi bamanga phakathi kwesizwe , njengokuba nakinina kuzakuba khona abafundisi bamanga abazakungenisa ngasese izifundiso zamanga ezibhubhisayo , bephika noMbusi owabathengayo , bezilethela ukubhujiswa okusheshayo ;
61002002	nabaningi bayakulandela amanyala abo ; ngenxa yabo indlela yeqiniso iyakuhlanjalazwa ;
61002003	nangokufisa bayakuthengiselana ngani ngamazwi obuqili , abakulahlwa kwabo kwamandulo akulibali nokubhujiswa kwabo akozeli .
61002004	Ngokuba uma uNkulunkulu engayekanga izingelosi ezonileyo , kodwa wazinikela ukuba ziphonswe esihogweni , emigodini yobumnyama , ukuba zigcinelwe ukwahlulelwa ,
61002005	nezwe lamandulo engaliyekanga , kodwa wamlondoloza uNowa , umshumayeli wokulunga , engowesishiyagalombili , mhla eletha uzamcolo ezweni elingamesabi uNkulunkulu ;
61002006	nemizi yaseSodoma neGomora wayahlulela wayichitha ngokuyiphendula umlotha , eyenza ibe yisiboniso kubo abangayikumesaba uNkulunkulu ;
61002007	noLoti olungileyo , ehlushwa ngukuhamba ngamanyala kwabangenamthetho , wamhlangulisa —
61002008	ngokuba ngokubona nangokuzwa lona olungileyo , ehlala phakathi kwabo , wezwisa ubuhlungu umphefumulo wakhe olungileyo imihla ngemihla ngenxa yezenzo ezingenamthetho —
61002009	iNkosi iyakwazi ukuhlangulisa ekulingweni abamesabayo uNkulunkulu , kepha abangalungile iyabagcinela usuku lokwahlulelwa , bajeziswe ,
61002010	ikakhulu labo abahamba ngokwenyama enkanukweni yokuzingcolisa , bedelela ubukhosi ; bengamaphikankani nabaziqhenyayo abesabi nokuhlambalaza abenkazimulo ,
61002011	kanti izingelosi , nokuba zizinkulu ngobuqhwaga namandla , azibamangaleli ngenhlamba phambi kweNkosi .
61002012	Kepha laba behlambalaza , benjengezidalwa ezingenangqondo , ngemvelo zizalelwe ukubanjwa nokubhujiswa , nabo bazakubhujiswa ekubhujisweni kwazo , behlambalaza abangakwaziyo ,
61002013	bamukele umvuzo wokungalungi . Labo bathi ukutamasa emini kungukujabula ; bayizisihla nezinsolo , bezitika ekukhohliseni kwabo bedla nani ;
61002014	benamehlo agcwele ukuphinga nangayeki izono , bayenga imiphefumulo engaqinile , benenhliziyo ejwayele ukufisa , abantwana bokuqalekiswa ,
61002015	beshiya indlela eqondileyo beduka , belandela indlela kaBalami kaBeyori owathanda umvuzo wokungalungi ,
61002016	kepha waba nokusolwa ngenxa yokweqa kwakhe umthetho : imbongolo eyisimungulu yakhuluma ngezwi lomuntu , yanqabela ukuhlanya komprofethi .
61002017	Labo bayimithombo engenamanzi nezinkungu eziqhutshwa yisiphepho , abagcinelwe ubumnyama bobumnyama .
61002018	Ngokuba bekhuluma udwadwa , amazwi ayize , babayenga ngezinkanuko zenyama nangamanyala labo abasaphephayo abahamba ngokuduka ;
61002019	bebathembisa inkululeko , kanti bona uqobo lwabo bayizigqila zokubhubha ; ngokuba lokho umuntu ahlulwa yikho uyisigqila sakho .
61002020	Ngokuba uma bebuye bahilelwe , bahlulwe yikho , sebebalekele ukungcola kwezwe ngokuyazi iNkosi noMsindisi uJesu Kristu , khona ukugcina kwabo kubi kunokuqala .
61002021	Ngokuba ngabe kwaba ngcono kubo ukuba babengayazanga indlela yokulunga kunokuba kuthi sebayazile bafulathele umyalo ongcwele ababewunikeziwe .
61002022	Kubehlele njengokwesaga esiqinisileyo esithi : " Inja yabuyela ebuhlanzweni bayo , " nokuthi : " Ingulube igezwe qede yaphindela ukuzibhixa odakeni . "
61003001	Le ncwadi , bathandekayo , isingeyesibili enginilobele yona , engivusa ngazo ingqondo yenu emhlophe ngokunikhumbuza ,
61003002	ukuze nikhumbule amazwi ashunyayelwa phambili yibo abaprofethi abangcwele nomyalo weNkosi noMsindisi owashunyayelwa ngabaphostoli benu ,
61003003	nazi kuqala lokhu ukuthi ngezinsuku zokugcina kuyakufika abahleki abahleka usulu , behamba ngezinkanuko zabo ,
61003004	bethi : " Siphi isithembiso sokufika kwakhe na ? Ngokuba kuselokhu obaba balala , konke kumi kunjalo njengakwasekuqaleni kokudalwa . "
61003005	Ngokuba bathanda ukukhohlwa lokhu ukuthi kwaphakade izulu lalikhona kanye nomhlaba owavela emanzini nangawo amanzi , umi ngezwi likaNkulunkulu ,
61003006	okwathi ngawo izwe elalikhona labhubha ngokukhukhula kwamanzi ;
61003007	kepha izulu nomhlaba okukhona manje kubekelelwe umlilo ngalo lona leli zwi , kulindele usuku lokwahlulela nolokubhubha kwabantu abangamesabi uNkulunkulu .
61003008	Kodwa , bathandekayo , maningakhohlwa lento inye yokuthi kuyo iNkosi usuku lunye lunjengeminyaka eyinkulungwane nokuthi iminyaka eyinkulungwane injengosuku lunye .
61003009	INkosi ayilibali ngesithembiso sayo , njengalokhu abanye bathi kungukulibala , kepha iyanibekezelela , ingathandi ukuba kubhubhe namunye , kodwa ukuba bonke beze ekuphendukeni .
61003010	Kepha usuku lweNkosi luyakufika njengesela mhla amazulu eyakudlula ngokuhlokoma ; kuyakusha konke , kubhidlike ; nomhlaba nemisebenzi yawo kuyakusha .
61003011	Njengokuba konke kuyakubhidlika kanjalo , kumelwe ukuba nibe ngabantu abanjani ekuhambeni okungcwele nase kumesabeni uNkulunkulu ,
61003012	nibheka nilangazelela ukufika kosuku lukaNkulunkulu ayakubhidlika ngalo amazulu , ashe , konke kushe , kuncibilike , na ?
61003013	Kepha siyalindela ngesithembiso sakhe amazulu amasha nomhlaba omusha okukhona kuwo ukulunga .
61003014	Ngakho , bathandekayo , lokhu nibheka lezo zinto , khuthalelani ukuba nifunyanwe ninokuthula , ningenabala , ningenacala kuye ,
61003015	nithi ukubekezela kweNkosi yethu kungukusindiswa , njengalokho nomzalwane wethu othandekayo uPawulu wanilobela njengokuhlakanipha ayekuphiweyo ,
61003016	njengalokhu nasezincwadini zonke ekhuluma kuzo ngalezo zinto , okukhona kuzo okunye okulukhuni ukuzwisiswa , okuthi abangafundile nabangaqinile bakuhlanekezela , njengalokhu benze njalo nangezinye izincwadi , kube ngukubhujiswa kwabo .
61003017	Ngakho , bathandekayo , njengokuba nazi lokhu ngaphambili , xwayani , ukuze ningadukiswa ngokukhohlisa kwabangenamthetho , niwe ekuqineni kwenu ,
61003018	kepha khulani emseni nasekwazini iNkosi noMsindisi wethu uJesu Kristu . Inkazimulo mayibe kuye namanje nakuze kube lusuku lwaphakade .
62001001	Lokho okwakukhona kwasekuqaleni , esakuzwa , sakubona ngamehlo ethu , sakubheka , nezandla zethu zakuphatha , okwezwi lokuphila —
62001002	lokho kuphila kwabonakaliswa , sakubona , siyaqinisa sinishumayeza lokho kuphila okuphakade okwakukhona kuYise , kwabonakaliswa kithina —
62001003	lokho esikubonileyo , sakuzwa , sinishumayeza khona nani , ukuze nani nibe nenhlanganyelo nathi . Kepha thina sinenhlanganyelo noYise naneNdodana yakhe uJesu Kristu .
62001004	Sesiyanilobela lokhu , ukuze intokozo yenu iphelele .
62001005	Nanti izwi esalizwa kuye , sinishumayeza lona lokuthi uNkulunkulu ungukukhanya , ubumnyama abukho kuye nakanye .
62001006	Uma sithi sinenhlanganyelo naye sibe sisahamba ebumnyameni , sinamanga , asenzi iqiniso ;
62001007	kepha uma sihamba ekukhanyeni , njengalokhu yena uqobo esekukhanyeni , khona sinenhlanganyelo omunye nomunye , negazi likaJesu iNdodana yakhe liyasihlambulula ezonweni zonke .
62001008	Uma sithi asinasono , siyazikhohlisa , neqiniso alikho kithi .
62001009	Uma sizivuma izono zethu , uthembekile , ulungile ukuba asithethelele izono , asihlambulule kukho konke ukungalungi .
62001010	Uma sithi asonanga , simenza umqambimanga , nezwi lakhe alikho kithi .
62002001	Bantwana bami , nginilobela lokhu ukuba ningoni . Kepha uma umuntu ona , sinoMmeli kuYise , uJesu Kristu olungileyo ;
62002002	yena uyinhlawulo ngezono zethu , kungengezethu zodwa kodwa nangezezwe lonke .
62002003	Ngalokho siyazi ukuthi siyamazi yena , uma sigcina imiyalo yakhe .
62002004	Lowo othi : " Ngiyamazi , " engagcini imiyalo yakhe , ungumqambimanga , iqiniso alikho kuye ;
62002005	kepha ogcina izwi lakhe , uthando lukaNkulunkulu luphelelisiwe kuye impela . Ngalokho siyazi ukuthi sikuye ;
62002006	lowo othi uhlala kuye , yena umelwe ukuhamba njengalokho ahamba yena .
62002007	Bathandekayo , anginilobeli umyalo omusha , kodwa umyalo omdala enaninawo kwasekuqaleni ; umyalo omdala uyizwi enalizwayo .
62002008	Futhi nginilobela umyalo omusha owona uyiqiniso kuye nakini , ngokuba ubumnyama buyadlula nokukhanya kweqiniso sekuyakhanya .
62002009	Lowo othi usekukhanyeni , abe ezonda umzalwane wakhe , usesebumnyameni kuze kube kalokhu .
62002010	Othanda umzalwane wakhe uhlala ekukhanyeni , akukho sikhubekiso kuye ;
62002011	kepha ozonda umzalwane wakhe usebumnyameni , uhamba ebumnyameni , akazi lapho eya khona , ngokuba ubumnyama buwaphuphuthekisile amehlo akhe .
62002012	Ngilobela nina bantwanyana , ngokuba nithethelelwe izono ngenxa yegama lakhe .
62002013	Ngilobela nina boyise , ngokuba niyamazi yena okhona kwasekuqaleni . Ngilobela nina zinsizwa , ngokuba nimnqobile omubi .
62002014	Nginilobele , bantwanyana , ngokuba niyamazi uYise . Nginilobele , boyise , ngokuba niyamazi yena okhona kwasekuqaleni . Nginilobele , zinsizwa , ngokuba ninamandla , izwi likaNkulunkulu lihlala kini , nimnqobile omubi .

62002016	ngokuba konke okusezweni , inkanuko yenyama , nenkanuko yamehlo , nokuzigabisa ngalokhu kuphila , akuveli kuYise , kodwa kuvela ezweni .
62002017	Izwe liyadlula kanye nenkanuko yalo ; kepha owenza intando kaNkulunkulu uhlala kuze kube phakade .
62002018	Bantwanyana , sekuyisikhathi sokugcina , njengalokho nezwa ukuthi umphikukristu uyeza , nakalokhu sekukhona abaphikukristu abaningi ; ngalokho siyazi ukuthi sekuyisikhathi sokugcina .
62002019	Baphuma kithi , kodwa babengesibo abakithi ; ngokuba uma bebengabakithi , babeyakuhlala nathi ; kodwa baphuma , ukuze babonakaliswe ukuthi bonke abasibo abakithi .
62002020	Nina ninokugcotshwa okuvela koNgcwele , niyazi nonke .
62002021	Anginilobelanga ngokuba ningalazi iqiniso , kodwa ngokuba niyalazi nangokuba akukho manga avela eqinisweni .
62002022	Ngubani ongumqambimanga , uma kungesiye ophika ukuthi uJesu unguKristu na ? Nguye ongumphikukristu ophika uYise neNdodana .
62002023	Yilowo nalowo ophika iNdodana akanaye uYise ; ovuma iNdodana unaye noYise .
62002024	Lokho enakuzwayo kwasekuqaleni , makuhlale kinina . Uma kuhlala kini enakuzwayo kwasekuqaleni , nani niyakuhlala kuyo iNdodana nakuye uYise .
62002025	Yilesi isithembiso yena asethembisa sona : ukuphila okuphakade .
62002026	Nganilobela lokho ngabo abanidukisayo .

62002029	Uma nazi ukuthi ulungile , yazini ukuthi yilowo nalowo owenza ukulunga uzelwe nguye .
62003001	Bhekani uthando olungaka asinike lona uBaba lokuba sithiwe singabantwana bakaNkulunkulu ; futhi siyibo . Ngalokho izwe alisazi , ngokuba alimazanga yena .
62003002	Bathandekayo , manje singabantwana bakaNkulunkulu , kepha akukabonakali esiyakuba yikho . Siyazi ukuthi , nxa ebonakaliswa , siyakuba njengaye , ngokuba siyakumbona njengokuba enjalo .
62003003	Bonke abanalo lelo themba kuye bayazihlambulula , njengokuba yena ehlambulukile .
62003004	Bonke abenza isono bayeqa nomthetho , ngokuba isono singukweqa umthetho .
62003005	Senazi ukuthi yena wabonakaliswa , ukuze asuse izono ; akukho sono kuye .
62003006	Lowo ohlala kuye akoni ; lowo owonayo akambonanga , futhi akamazi .
62003007	Bantwanyana , maningadukiswa muntu ; owenza ukulunga ulungile , njengokuba yena elungile ;
62003008	owenza isono ungokaSathane , ngokuba uSathane uyona kwasekuqaleni . INdodana kaNkulunkulu yabonakaliswa ngalokhu , ukuze ichithe imisebenzi kaSathane .

62003010	Ngalokho kubonakala abantwana bakaNkulunkulu nabantwana bakaSathane ; lowo ongenzi ukulunga akasiye okaNkulunkulu , naye ongamthandi umzalwane wakhe .
62003011	Nanti izwi enalizwayo kwasekuqaleni lokuba sithandane ,
62003012	kungabi njengoKayini owaba ngowomubi , wabulala umfowabo ; wambulalelani na ? Ngokuba imisebenzi yakhe yayimibi , kepha eyomfowabo yayilungile .
62003013	Ningamangali , bazalwane , uma izwe linizonda .
62003014	Siyazi ukuthi sidlulile ekufeni , sangena ekuphileni , ngokuba sithanda abazalwane ; ongathandiyo uhlezi ekufeni .
62003015	Lowo ozonda umzalwane wakhe ungumbulali ; niyazi ukuthi akukho mbulali onokuphila okuphakade okuhlezi kuye .
62003016	Uthando silwazi ngalokho ukuthi yena wabeka ukuphila kwakhe ngenxa yethu ; nathi sifanele ukubeka ukuphila ngenxa yabazalwane .
62003017	Kepha yena onemfuyo yezwe , ebona umzalwane wakhe eswele , amvalele isihawu sakhe , uthando lukaNkulunkulu lungahlala kanjani kuye na ?
62003018	Bantwanyana , masingathandi ngezwi nangolimi , kodwa ngezenzo nangeqiniso .

62003020	ngokuthi uma inhliziyo yethu isilahla , uNkulunkulu mkhulu kunenhliziyo yethu , futhi uyazi konke .
62003021	Bathandekayo , uma inhliziyo ingasilahli , sinesibindi kuNkulunkulu ,
62003022	nesikucelayo siyakukwamukeliswa nguye , ngokuba sigcina imiyalo yakhe , senza okuthandekayo ebusweni bakhe .

62004001	Bathandekayo , maningakholwa yibo bonke omoya , kepha hlolani omoya ukuthi bangabakaNkulunkulu yini ; ngokuba baningi abaprofethi bamanga abaphumele ezweni .

62004019	Thina siyathanda , ngokuba yena wasithanda kuqala .

62005005	Ngubani onqoba izwe , uma kungesiye okholwa ukuthi uJesu uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu na ?

62005010	Okholwa yiNdodana kaNkulunkulu unobufakazi phakathi kwakhe . Ongakholwa nguNkulunkulu umenze umqambimanga , ngokuba engakholwanga ngubufakazi uNkulunkulu abufakazile ngeNdodana yakhe .

62005014	Yilesi sibindi esinaso kuye sokuthi , uma sicela utho ngokwentando yakhe , uyasizwa .

62005016	Uma umuntu ebona umzalwane wakhe ona ngesono esingesiso esokufa , makacele , uyakumnika ukuphila , ekunika labo abenza isono esingesiso esokufa . Sikhona isono sokufa ; angisho ukuba kucelwe ngaleso .
62005017	Konke ukungalungi kuyisono ; kukhona isono esingesiso esokufa .

62005021	Bantwanyana , zilindeni ezithombeni .

65001001	UJuda inceku kaJesu Kristu , umfowabo kaJakobe , kubo ababiziweyo abathandwa kuNkulunkulu uYise nabagcinelwe uJesu Kristu :
65001002	Makwandiswe kini umusa nokuthula nothando .
65001003	Bathandekayo , njengokuba ngenza inkuthalo yonke ukunilobela ngensindiso esiyihlanganyele sonke , ngacindezeleka ukunilobela ukuba nginivuselele ukulwela inkolo abayinikelwayo abangcwele kwaba kanye .
65001004	Ngokuba sebengenile ngokunyenya abantu abathile okwalotshwa ngabo phambili endulo ukuthi bayakwehlelwa yilokhu kulahlwa , abangamesabi uNkulunkulu , bephendukezela umusa kaNkulunkulu wethu ube ngamanyala , bephika uMbusi oyedwa neNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu .

65001007	njengokuba iSodoma neGomora nemizi yangakhona yenza ubufebe ngendlela efana neyayo , yalandela inyama imbe imisiwe ibe yisiboniso , izwa isijeziso somlilo omiyo njalo .
65001008	Nokho ngokunjalo-ke nalabo abaphuphayo bangcolisa inyama , bayeyisa imibuso , bahlambalaza ubukhosi .
65001009	Kepha uMikayeli , ingelosi enkulu , lapho ephikisana noSathane , ekhulumisana naye ngesidumbu sikaMose , akabanga nasibindi sokuletha ukwahlulela kokuhlambalaza , kodwa wathi : " INkosi mayikujezise . "
65001010	Kepha laba bayahlambalaza konke abangakwaziyo , nalokho abakwaziyo ngemvelo njengezidalwa ezingenangqondo babhubha ngakho .
65001011	Maye kubo , ngokuba bahamba endleleni kaKayini , bagijimela ekudukeni kukaBalami ngenxa yomvuzo , babhubha ekuphikeni kukaKora !
65001012	Yilabo abayizisihla emadilini enu othando bedla nani , bengesabi , baziklabisa ; bangamafu angenamanzi , aqhutshwa yimimoya ; bayimithi yasebusika engenazithelo , efe kabili , isishuliwe ;
65001013	bangamaza adlangalalayo olwandle , ekhephuza amahlazo awo , izinkanyezi ezidukayo ezigcinelwe ubumnyama bobumnyama baphakade .
65001014	U-Enoke ongowesikhombisa kusukela kuAdamu waprofetha ngabo , wathi : " Bheka , iNkosi iyakufika nabangcwele bayo abayizigidigidi ,
65001015	ukuze yahlulele bonke , ijezise bonke abangamesabi uNkulunkulu ngenxa yemisebenzi yonke yabo yokungahloniphi uNkulunkulu abadelela ngayo , nangawo onke amazwi alukhuni izoni ezingamesabi uNkulunkulu eziwakhulumile ngaye . "
65001016	Yilabo abakhononayo nabasolayo , behamba ngezinkanuko zabo , umlomo wabo ukhuluma uwangala , betusa ubuso ngenxa yenzuzo .
65001017	Kepha nina bathandekayo , khumbulani amazwi akhulunywe phambili ngabaphostoli beNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu
65001018	abasho ukuthi ngesikhathi sokugcina kuyakuba khona abahleka usulu , behamba ngezinkanuko zabo zokungamesabi uNkulunkulu .
65001019	Yilabo abaveza ukwahlukana , bengabenyama bengenaMoya .
65001020	Kepha nina bathandekayo , yakhelanani ekukholweni kwenu okungcwele kakhulu , nikhuleke ngoMoya oNgcwele ,
65001021	nizigcine othandweni lukaNkulunkulu , nibheke umusa weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu , kube ngukuphila okuphakade .
65001022	Abanye , abangabazayo , nibahawukele ,
65001023	nibasindise ngokubahlwitha emlilweni , kepha abanye nibahawukele ngokwesaba , nizonde nengubo enindwe yinyama .
65001024	Kepha kuyena onamandla okunilinda ukuba ningakhubeki , nimiswe phambi kwenkazimulo yakhe ningenasici , ninokuthokoza okukhulu ,

66001004	UJohane kuwo amabandla ayisikhombisa ase-Asiya : Makube kini umusa nokuthula okuvela kuye okhona nowayekhona nozayo , nakoMoya abayisikhombisa abaphambi kwesihlalo sakhe sobukhosi ,
66001005	nakuJesu Kristu ufakazi othembekayo , izibulo labafileyo nombusi wamakhosi omhlaba . Kuye osithandayo nowasikhululayo ezonweni zethu ngegazi lakhe

66004004	Nesihlalo sobukhosi sasihaqiwe yizihlalo zobukhosi ezingamashumi amabili nane , naphezu kwezihlalo zobukhosi kwakuhlezi amalunga angamashumi amabili nane , embethe izingubo ezimhlophe , enemiqhele yegolide emakhanda awo .

66005001	Ngase ngibona esandleni sokunene sakhe owayehlezi esihlalweni sobukhosi incwadi ilotshiwe ngaphakathi nangaphandle , inamathelisiwe ngezimpawu eziyisikhombisa .

66005004	Ngakhala kakhulu ngokuba kungafunyanwanga namunye ofanele ukuyivula leyo ncwadi , abuke kuyo .
66005005	Omunye wamalunga wayesethi kimi : " Ungakhali ; bheka , inqobile iNgonyama yesizwe sakwaJuda , iMpande kaDavide , ukuba ivule incwadi nezimpawu zayo eziyisikhombisa . "
66005006	Ngase ngibona ngaphakathi kwesihlalo sobukhosi nezidalwa ezine nangaphakathi kwamalunga kumi iWundlu kungathi lihlatshiwe , linezimpondo eziyisikhombisa namehlo ayisikhombisa angoMoya abayisikhombisa bakaNkulunkulu abathunyelwe emhlabeni wonke .
