66007009	Emva kwalokho ngabona , bheka-ke , isixuku esikhulu ebesingenakubalwa muntu , sivela kuzo zonke izizwe , nemindeni , nabantu , nezilimi , simi phambi kwesihlalo sobukhosi naphambi kweWundlu , sembethe izingubo ezinde ezimhlophe , siphethe amahlamvu esundu ngezandla zaso ,
66007010	samemeza ngezwi elikhulu , sithi : " Insindiso ngekaNkulunkulu wethu ohlezi esihlalweni sobukhosi neyeWundlu ! "
66007011	Nezingelosi zonke ezazimi zihaqe isihlalo sobukhosi namalunga nezidalwa ezine zawa phansi ngobuso phambi kwesihlalo sobukhosi , zakhuleka kuNkulunkulu , zathi :
66007012	" Amen ! Isibusiso , nenkazimulo , nokuhlakanipha , nokubongwa , nodumo , namandla , nokunqoba makube kuNkulunkulu wethu kuze kube phakade naphakade . Amen ! "
66007013	Elinye lamalunga lase liphendula , lithi kimi : " Laba abembethe izingubo ezimhlophe bangobani , bavelaphi , na ? "
66007014	Ngase ngithi kulo : " Nkosi yami , nguwe owaziyo . " Lase lithi kimi : " Laba yibo abaphuma osizini olukhulu , bahlanza izingubo zabo , bazenza zaba mhlophe egazini leWundlu .
66007015	Ngalokho-ke baphambi kwesihlalo sobukhosi sikaNkulunkulu bemkhonza imini nobusuku ethempelini lakhe , nohlezi esihlalweni sobukhosi uyakumisa itabernakele phezu kwabo .
66007016	Kabasayikulamba , kabasayikoma kabasoze bahlatshwa yilanga nakushisa kuni ,
66007017	ngokuba iWundlu elingaphakathi nesihlalo sobukhosi liyakubelusa , libaholele emithonjeni yamanzi okuphila ; noNkulunkulu uyakwesula izinyembezi zonke emehlweni abo . "
66008001	Kuthe ukuba liluvule uphawu lwesikhombisa , kwathi du ezulwini kungathi inxenye yehora .
66008002	Ngase ngibona izingelosi eziyisikhombisa zimi phambi kukaNkulunkulu , zanikwa amacilongo ayisikhombisa .
66008003	Kwase kufika enye ingelosi , yema ngase-altare inesitsha segolide sempepho , yanikwa impepho eningi ukuba iyelekele emikhulekweni yabangcwele bonke phezu kwe-altare legolide eliphambi kwesihlalo sobukhosi .
66008004	Kwase kwenyuka esandleni sengelosi umusi wempepho nemikhuleko yabangcwele phambi kukaNkulunkulu .
66008005	Ingelosi yayisithabatha isitsha sempepho , yasigcwalisa ngomlilo wase-altare , yasiphonsa emhlabeni ; kwase kuba khona ukuduma , namazwi , nemibani , nokuzamazama komhlaba . okuqala ziyabetha amacilongo
66008006	Izingelosi eziyisikhombisa ezazinamacilongo ayisikhombisa zazilungiselela ukubetha .
66008007	Eyokuqala yayisibetha ; kwase kuba khona isichotho nomlilo kuxutshaniswe negazi , kwaphonswa emhlabeni ; okwesithathu komhlaba kwasha kwaqothuka , nokwesithathu kwemithi kwasha kwaqothuka , nabo bonke utshani obuluhlaza basha baqothuka .
66008008	Ingelosi yesibili yayisibetha ; kwangathi intaba enkulu ivutha umlilo , yaphonswa elwandle ; okwesithathu kolwandle kwaba yigazi ,
66008009	kwafa okwesithathu kokudaliweyo okwakuselwandle okuphilayo , nokwesithathu kwemikhumbi kwabhujiswa .
66008010	Ingelosi yesithathu yayisibetha ; kwase kuwa ezulwini inkanyezi enkulu ivuthisa okwesibani , yawela phezu kokwesithathu kwemifula naphezu kwemithombo yamanzi .
66008011	Igama lenkanyezi lithiwa uMhlonyane . Okwesithathu kwamanzi kwaba ngumhlonyane , nabaningi kubantu bafa ngamanzi , ngokuba enziwa ababa .
66008012	Ingelosi yesine yayisibetha ; kwashaywa okwesithathu kwelanga , nokwesithathu kwenyanga , nokwesithathu kwezinkanyezi , ukuze okwesithathu kwakho kufiphazwe , nemini ingakhanyi okwesithathu kwayo , nobusuku ngokunjalo .
66008013	Ngase ngibona , ngezwa ukhozi lundiza emkhathini wezulu , lumemeza ngezwi elikhulu , luthi : " Maye , maye , maye kwabakhileyo emhlabeni ngokunye ukukhala kwecilongo lezingelosi ezintathu ezisezakubetha ! "
66009001	Ingelosi yesihlanu yayisibetha ; ngase ngibona inkanyezi ivela ezulwini , iwela emhlabeni , yanikwa isihluthulelo somgodi wakwalasha .
66009002	Yayisivula umgodi wakwalasha ; kwenyuka umusi emgodini njengomusi weziko elikhulu , kwafiphazwa ilanga nomkhathi ngomusi womgodi .
66009003	Kwaphuma isikhonyane emsini , seza emhlabeni , sanikwa amandla njengamandla abanawo ofezela bomhlaba .
66009004	Kwathiwa kuso masingoni utshani bomhlaba , nanye into eluhlaza , nowodwa umuthi , kuphela labo bantu abangenalo uphawu lukaNkulunkulu emabunzini abo .
66009005	Sanikwa ukuba singababulali kepha sibahluphe izinyanga eziyisihlanu ; nokuhlushwa kwabo kwaba njengobuhlungu bukafezela , nxa emqosela umuntu .
66009006	Ngaleyo mihla abantu bayakufuna ukufa , bangaze bakufumana ; futhi bayakufisa ukufa , kepha ukufa kubabalekele .
66009007	Nesimo sesikhonyane sasifana namahhashi alungiselwe ukulwa , nasemakhanda aso kukhona okunjengemiqhele efana negolide , nobuso bunjengobuso babantu ;
66009008	futhi sasinezinwele ezinjengezinwele zabesifazane , namazinyo aso ayenjengawezingonyama ,
66009009	sinezivikelo zezifuba njengezivikelo zensimbi , nomdumo wamaphiko aso wawunjengomdumo wezinqola zamahhashi amaningi egijimela ekulweni .
66009010	Sasinemisila efana neyawofezela inezindosi , nasemisileni yaso kukhona amandla aso okona abantu izinyanga eziyisihlanu .
66009011	Sinenkosi phezu kwaso , ingelosi yakwalasha , igama layo ngesiHeberu lingu-Abadoni , kepha ngesiGreki inegama lokuthi u-Apholiyoni .
66009012	UMaye wokuqala udlulile ; bheka , kuseza oMaye ababili ngasemva kwalokho .
66009013	Ingelosi yesithupha yayisibetha ; ngezwa izwi livela ezimpondweni ezine ze-altare legolide eliphambi kukaNkulunkulu ,
66009014	lithi kuyo ingelosi yesithupha enecilongo : " Thukulula izingelosi ezine eziboshwe ngasemfuleni omkhulu u-Ewufrathe . "
66009015	Zase zithukululwa izingelosi ezine ezilungiselwe ihora , nosuku , nenyanga , nomnyaka , ukuba zibulale okwesithathu kwabantu .
66009016	Umumo wezimpi zabakhwele amahhashi wawungukuphindwa kabili kwezinkulungwane eziyishumi ziphindwe kazinkulungwane eziyishumi .
66009017	Nakanjalo ngabona ngombono amahhashi nabakhwele kuwo benezivikelo zezifuba , zibomvu njengomlilo nezehiyakinte nezesibabule ; namakhanda amahhashi ayenjengamakhanda ezingonyama , nasemilonyeni yawo kuphuma umlilo , nomusi , nesibabule .
66009018	Ngalezo zinhlupho ezintathu kwabulawa okwesithathu kwabantu ngomlilo , nangomusi , nangesibabule , okwaphuma emilonyeni yawo .
66009019	Ngokuba amandla amahhashi asemilonyeni yawo nasemisileni yawo ; ngokuba imisila yawo ifana nezinyoka , inamakhanda ona ngawo .
66009020	Kepha abaseleyo babantu abangabulawanga ngalezo zinhlupho abaphendukanga emisebenzini yezandla zabo ukuba bangakhuleki kuwo amademoni , nezithombe zegolide , nezesiliva , nezethusi , nezamatshe , nezemithi , ezingenakho ukubona , nakuzwa , nakuhamba ,
66009021	futhi abaphendukanga ekubulaleni kwabo , nasekuthakatheni kwabo , nasebufebeni babo , nasekwebeni kwabo .
66010001	Ngase ngibona enye ingelosi enamandla yehla ezulwini yembethe ifu , nothingo lwenkosikazi lwaluphezu kwekhanda layo , nobuso bayo babunjengelanga , nezinyawo zayo zinjengezinsika zomlilo ,
66010002	iphethe esandleni sayo incwadi encane evulekileyo . Yayisimisa unyawo lwayo lokunene phezu kolwandle nolokhohlo phezu komhlabathi ,
66010003	yamemeza ngezwi elikhulu njengokubhonga kwengonyama , nalapho isimemezile , imidumo eyisikhombisa yezwakalisa amazwi ayo .
66010004	Nalapho imidumo eyisikhombisa isikhulumile , ngase ngizakuloba ; kepha ngezwa izwi livela ezulwini , lithi : " Namathisela ngophawu okukhulunywe yimidumo eyisikhombisa , kodwa ungakulobi . "
66010005	Ingelosi engayibona imi phezu kolwandle naphezu komhlabathi yayisiphakamisela ezulwini isandla sayo sokunene ,
66010006	yafunga yena ophilayo kuze kube phakade naphakade , owadala izulu nokukulo , nomhlaba nokukuwo , nolwandle nokukulo , yathi : " Akusayikubakho isikhathi ,
66010007	kepha ngezinsuku zezwi lengelosi yesikhombisa , lapho isizakubetha icilongo , imfihlakalo kaNkulunkulu isiyakube ifeziwe , njengalokho azazisa izinceku zakhe abaprofethi ngezindaba ezijabulisayo . "
66010008	Izwi engalizwa livela ezulwini lase liphinda likhuluma nami , lithi : " Hamba uye uthabathe incwadi evulekileyo esesandleni sengelosi emi phezu kolwandle naphezu komhlabathi . "
66010009	Ngaya kuyo ingelosi ; ngase ngithi kuyo mayinginike incwadi encane . Yayisithi kimi : " Yithabathe , uyidle uyiqede ; izakubaba esiswini sakho , kepha emlonyeni wakho iyakuba mnandi njengezinyosi . "
66010010	Ngase ngiyithatha incwadi encane esandleni sengelosi , ngayidla ngayiqeda ; yayisiba mnandi njengezinyosi emlonyeni wami ; nalapho sengiyidlile , yababa esiswini sami .
66010011	Zase zithi kimi : " Kumelwe ukuba uphinde uprofethe ngabantu abaningi , nezizwe , nezilimi , namakhosi . "
66011001	Nganikwa uhlanga lufana nenduku , kwathiwa : " Sukuma , ulinganise ithempeli likaNkulunkulu , ne-altare , nabakhulekayo kulo .
66011002	Kepha igceke elingaphandle kwethempeli ulishiye ngaphandle , ungalilinganisi , ngokuba linikwe izizwe , nomuzi ongcwele ziyakuwunyathela phansi izinyanga ezingamashumi amane nambili .
66011003	Ngiyakubanika ofakazi bami ababili ukuba baprofethe izinsuku eziyinkulungwane namakhulu amabili namashumi ayisithupha bembethe indwangu yamasaka . "
66011004	Labo bayiminqumo emibili nezinti zezibani ezimbili ezimi phambi kweNkosi yomhlaba .
66011005	Uma kukhona ofuna ukona laba , kuphuma umlilo emlonyeni wabo , udle izitha zabo , uziqede ; yebo , uma kukhona ofuna ukona laba , kumelwe ukuba abulawe kanjalo .
66011006	Banamandla laba okuvala izulu ukuba lingani ngezinsuku zokuprofetha kwabo , futhi banamandla phezu kwamanzi okuwaphendula igazi nawokushaya umhlaba ngezinhlupho zonke , noma kungaba kangaki ngokuthanda kwabo .
66011007	Kuyakuthi sebebuqedile ubufakazi babo , isilo esiphuma kwalasha siyakulwa nabo , sibanqobe , sibabulale .
66011008	Nezidumbu zabo ziyakusala ezitaladini zomuzi omkhulu othiwa ngokomoya iSodoma neGibithe , lapho neNkosi yabo yabethelwa khona .
66011009	Abanye kubantu nabemindeni nabezilimi nabezizwe bayakuzibona izidumbu zabo izinsuku ezintathu nenxenye , bengavumi ukuba izidumbu zabo zifakwe ethuneni .
66011010	Nabakhileyo emhlabeni bayakujabula ngabo , bethabe , bathumelane izipho , ngokuba laba baprofethi ababili babebahluphile abakhileyo emhlabeni .
66011011	Kwathi emva kwalezo zinsuku ezintathu nenxenye umoya wokuphila ovela kuNkulunkulu wangena kubo ; base bema ngezinyawo zabo , nabababonayo behlelwa ngukwesaba okukhulu .
66011012	Bezwa izwi elikhulu livela ezulwini , lithi kubo : " Yenyukelani lapha . " Base benyukela ezulwini ngefu , nezitha zabo zababona .
66011013	Ngalelo hora kwaba khona ukuzamazama okukhulu komhlaba , kwawa okweshumi komuzi , nangokuzamazama komhlaba kwabulawa abantu abayizinkulungwane eziyisikhombisa , nabaseleyo bashaywa luvalo , bamdumisa uNkulunkulu wezulu .
66011014	Kwadlula uMaye wesibili ; bheka , uMaye wesithathu uyeza masinyane .
66011015	Ingelosi yesikhombisa yayisibetha ; kwase kuba khona amazwi amakhulu ezulwini athi : " Umbuso wezwe usungoweNkosi yethu nokaKristu wayo ; iyakubusa kuze kube phakade naphakade . "
66011016	Namalunga angamashumi amabili nane ahlezi phambi kukaNkulunkulu ezihlalweni zawo zobukhosi akhothama ngobuso bawo , akhuleka kuNkulunkulu ,
66011017	ethi : " Siyakubonga , Nkosi Nkulunkulu , Mninimandla onke , okhona nowawukhona , ngokuba uthabathe amandla akho amakhulu , wabusa ;
66011018	nezizwe zazinolaka , kepha kwafika ulaka lwakho , nesikhathi sokwahlulelwa kwabafileyo , nokunika umvuzo izinceku zakho , abaprofethi nabangcwele nabesabayo igama lakho , abancane nabakhulu , nokubhubhisa ababhubhisa umhlaba . "
66011019	Kwase kuvulwa ithempeli likaNkulunkulu elisezulwini , kwabonakala umphongolo wesivumelwano sakhe ethempelini lakhe ; kwase kuba khona imibani , namazwi , nokuduma , nokuzamazama komhlaba , nesichotho esikhulu .
66012001	Kwaba khona ezulwini isibonakaliso esikhulu : owesifazane embethe ilanga , nenyanga iphansi kwezinyawo zakhe , nasekhanda lakhe kukhona umqhele wezinkanyezi eziyishumi nambili ,
66012002	ekhulelwe wakhala , enemihelo esikwa ngubuhlungu bokubeletha .
66012003	Kwabonakala esinye isibonakaliso ezulwini ; bheka , nango udrako omkhulu obomvu , enamakhanda ayisikhombisa nezimpondo eziyishumi , nasemakhanda akhe enemiqhele eyisikhombisa ;
66012004	umsila wakhe wadonsa okwesithathu kwezinkanyezi zezulu , waziphonsa emhlabeni . Nodrako wema phambi kowesifazane obezakubeletha , ukuze kuthi nxa esebelethile , ashwabadele umntwana wakhe .
66012005	Wabeletha umntwana wesilisa ozakubusa izizwe zonke ngentonga yensimbi , nomntanakhe wahlwithelwa kuNkulunkulu nasesihlalweni sakhe sobukhosi .
66012006	Owesifazane wayesebalekela ehlane , lapho enendawo ayilungiselwe nguNkulunkulu , ukuba bamondle izinsuku eziyinkulumgwane namakhulu amabili namashumi ayisithupha .
66012007	Kwase kuba khona ukulwa ezulwini ; uMikayeli nezingelosi zakhe balwa nodrako . Nodrako walwa enezingelosi zakhe ,
66012008	kepha kabaze banqoba , nendawo yabo kayabe isafunyanwa ezulwini .
66012009	Wayesephonswa phansi udrako omkhulu , inyoka endala ethiwa uMhlebi noSathane , odukisa izwe lonke , waphonswa phansi emhlabeni , nezingelosi zakhe zaphonswa kanye naye .
66012010	Ngase ngizwa izwi elikhulu ezulwini , lithi : " Kalokhu insindiso namandla nobukhosi ngokukaNkulunkulu wethu , nombuso ngokaKristu wakhe , ngokuba uphonswe phansi ummangaleli wabazalwane bethu obamangalelayo phambi kukaNkulunkulu wethu imini nobusuku .
66012011	Nabo uqobo lwabo bamnqoba ngegazi leWundlu nangezwi lobufakazi babo , futhi abakuthandanga ukuphila kwabo kwaze kwaba sekufeni .
66012012	Ngalokho thokozani nina mazulu nabahlala kuwo ; maye kuwe mhlaba nakuwe lulwandle , ngokuba uSathane wehlele kini enolaka olukhulu , azi ukuthi unesikhathi esifushane ! "
66012013	Kuthe udrako esebona ukuthi usephonswe phansi emhlabeni , wazingela owesifazane owayezale umntwana wesilisa .
66012014	Owesifazane wayesenikwa amaphiko amabili okhozi olukhulu ukuba andizele ehlane endaweni yakhe lapho ondliwa khona isikhathi , nezikhathi , nenxenye yesikhathi , engekho ebusweni benyoka .
66012015	Nenyoka yakhwifa , kwaphuma emlonyeni wayo emva kowesifazane amanzi kungathi umfula ukuba immukise nomfula .
66012016	Umhlaba wamsiza owesifazane , umhlaba wakhamisa umlomo wawo , wawuminza umfula owawukhwifa udrako ngomlomo wakhe .
66012017	Udrako wamthukuthelela owesifazane , wamuka , wayokulwa nabaseleyo benzalo yakhe , labo abagcina imiyalo kaNkulunkulu nabanobufakazi bukaJesu .
66013001	Ngema esihlabathini solwandle . Ngase ngibona isilo sikhuphuka elwandle , sinezimpondo eziyishumi namakhanda ayisikhombisa , nasezimpondweni zaso kukhona imiqhele eyishumi nasemakhanda aso kukhona amagama enhlamba .
66013002	Isilo engasibonayo sasifana nengwe , nezinyawo zaso zazinjengezebhere , nomlomo waso wawunjengomlomo wengonyama . Udrako wasinika amandla akhe , nesihlalo sakhe sobukhosi , nokubusa okukhulu .
66013003	Elinye lamakhanda aso kungathi lalidebezwe okokufa , kepha ingozi yaso yokufa yelashwa , umhlaba wonke walandela isilo , umangala ;
66013004	bakhuleka kudrako , ngokuba wanika isilo amandla akhe , bakhuleka nakuso isilo , bethi : " Ngubani ofana nesilo , ngubani ongalwa naso na ? "
66013005	Sase sinikwa umlomo wokukhuluma izinto ezinkulu nenhlamba , sanikwa amandla okwenza lokho izinyanga ezingamashumi amane nambili .
66013006	Savula umlomo waso ukuhlambalaza uNkulunkulu , ukuhlambalaza igama lakhe netabernakele lakhe , nabo abahlezi ezulwini .
66013007	Sanikwa ukuba silwe nabangcvele , sibanqobe ; sanikwa futhi amandla phezu kwemindeni yonke , nabantu , nezilimi , nezizwe .
66013008	Bayakhuleka kuso bonke abakhileyo emhlabeni , wonke ogama lakhe lingalotshwanga encwadini yokuphila yeWundlu elihlatshiweyo , selokhu kwasekelwa umhlaba .
66013009	Uma ekhona onendlebe , makezwe .
66013010	Uma ekhona oyisa ekuthunjweni , uya naye ekuthunjweni ; uma ekhona obulala ngenkemba , umelwe naye ukubulawa ngenkemba . Nakhu ukubekezela nokukholwa kwabangcwele .
66013011	Ngase ngibona esinye isilo siphuma emhlabeni , sinezimpondo ezimbili ezifana nezewundlu , kepha sikhuluma njengodrako .
66013012	Amandla onke esilo sokuqala siyawenza phambi kwaso . Siyenza ukuba umhlaba nabo bonke abakhileyo kuwo bakhuleke kuso isilo sokuqala esingozi yaso yelashwa .
66013013	Senza nezibonakaliso ezinkulu , size senze nomlilo uphume ezulwini , wehlele emhlabeni phambi kwabantu .
66013014	Futhi sibadukisa abakhileyo emhlabeni ngezibonakaliso esazinikwayo ukuba sizenze phambi kwesilo , sithi kwabakhileyo emhlabeni mabasenzele umfanekiso isilo , ebesinenxeba lenkemba kepha sasinda .
66013015	Sanikwa futhi ukuba siwuphe umfanekiso wesilo umoya , ukuze umfanekiso wesilo ukhulume , senze futhi ukuba bonke abangakhuleki kumfanekiso wesilo babulawe .
66013016	Senza futhi ukuba bonke , abancane nabakhulu , nabacebileyo nabampofu , nabakhululekileyo nabayizigqila , bazibeke uphawu esandleni sabo sokunene noma ebunzini labo
66013017	ukuba angabikho ongathenga nokuba athengise , uma engenalo uphawu , igama lesilo noma isibalo segama laso .
66013018	Nakhu ukuhlakanipha . Onengqondo makabale isibalo sesilo , ngokuba siyisibalo somuntu . Nesibalo sakhe singamakhulu ayisithupha namashumi ayisithupha nesithupha .
66014001	Ngase ngibona ; bheka , iWundlu limi entabeni yaseSiyoni , kumi kanye nalo abayizinkulungwane eziyikhulu namashumi amane nane , benegama lalo negama likaYise lilotshwe emabunzini abo .
66014002	Ngase ngizwa izwi livela ezulwini , linjengezwi lamanzi amaningi nanjengezwi lokuduma okukhulu ; nezwi engalizwayo lalinjengelababetha amahabhu , bebetha amahabhu abo .
66014003	Bahlabelela igama elisha phambi kwesihlalo sobukhosi , naphambi kwezidalwa ezine , namalunga ; kepha akubangakho onamandla okufunda lelo gama , kuphela abayizinkulungwane eziyikhulu namashumi amane nane abathengiweyo emhlabeni .
66014004	Labo yibo abangangcoliswanga yisifazane , ngokuba bayizintombi . Labo yibo abalandela iWundlu noma liyaphi . Labo bathengwa ebantwini , babe lulibo kuNkulunkulu nakulo iWundlu ,
66014005	nasemlonyeni wabo akufunyaniswanga amanga ; kabanasici .
66014006	Ngase ngibona enye ingelosi indiza emkhathini wezulu , inevangeli eliphakade ilishumayela kwabahlezi emhlabeni , nakuzo zonke izizwe , nemindeni , nezilimi , nabantu ,
66014007	isho ngezwi elikhulu , ithi : " Mesabeni uNkulunkulu , nimnike inkazimulo , ngokuba ihora lokwahlulela kwakhe selifikile ; nikhuleke kuye owenza izulu nomhlaba nolwandle nemithombo yamanzi . "
66014008	Yayisilandela enye ingelosi , ithi : " Liwile , liwile iBabiloni elikhulu , eliphuzise izizwe zonke iwayini lolaka lobufebe balo . "
66014009	Yalandela enye ingelosi yesithathu , ithi ngezwi elikhulu : " Uma kukhona okhuleka kuso isilo nomfanekiso waso , elwamukela futhi uphawu ebunzini lakhe noma esandleni sakhe ,
66014010	naye uyakuliphuza iwayini lolaka lukaNkulunkulu elilungisiwe esitsheni solaka lwakhe , lingaxutshiwe , ahlushwe ngomlilo nesibabule phambi kwezingelosi ezingcwele naphambi kweWundlu .
66014011	Nomusi wokuhlushwa kwabo uyenyuka kuze kube phakade naphakade ; abasenakuphumula imini nobusuku abakhuleka kuso isilo nomfanekiso waso nalowo owamukela uphawu lwegama laso . "
66014012	Nakhu ukubekezela kwabangcwele abagcina imiyalo kaNkulunkulu nokukholwa nguJesu .
66014013	Ngase ngizwa izwi livela ezulwini , lithi : " Loba ukuthi : Babusisiwe abafileyo abafele eNkosini kusukela kulesi sikhathi . " " Yebo , " usho uMoya , " ukuze baphumule ekukhandlekeni kwabo ; ngokuba imisebenzi yabo iyabalandela . "
66014014	Ngase ngibona ; bheka , nanto ifu elimhlophe , naphezu kwefu kuhlezi ofana nendodana yomuntu enomqhele wegolide ekhanda lakhe nasesandleni sakhe enesikela elibukhali .
66014015	Enye ingelosi yayisiphuma ethempelini , imemeza ngezwi elikhulu , ithi kohlezi phezu kwefu : " Faka isikela lakho , uvune , ngokuba kufikile isikhathi sokuvuna , ngokuba sekomile okuvunwayo komhlaba . "
66014016	Ohlezi phezu kwefu wayeseliphonsa isikela emhlabeni ; wawusuvunwa umhlaba .
66014017	Enye ingelosi yayisiphuma ethempelini elisezulwini , nayo inesikela elibukhali .
66014018	Nenye ingelosi futhi yaphuma e-altare , inamandla phezu komlilo , yamemeza ngezwi elikhulu kuyo ebinesikela elibukhali , ithi : " Faka isikela lakho elibukhali , ubuthe amahlukuzo omvini womhlaba , ngokuba izithelo zomvini zivuthiwe . "
66014019	Ingelosi yayisiliphonsa isikela layo emhlabeni , yawuvuna umvini womhlaba , yawuphonsa esikhamweni sewayini esikhulu solaka lukaNkulunkulu .
66014020	Isikhamo sanyathelwa ngaphandle komuzi , kwaphuma igazi esikhamweni , laze lafika ematomini amahhashi , liqeda amastadiyu ayinkulungwane namakhulu ayisithupha .
66015001	Ngase ngibona esinye isibonakaliso ezulwini esikhulu nesimangalisayo : izingelosi eziyisikhombisa zinezinhlupho eziyisikhombisa zokugcina , ngokuba kwapheleliswa ngazo ulaka lukaNkulunkulu .
66015002	Ngabona kungathi ulwandle lwengilazi luxubene nomlilo , nabavela ekunqobeni isilo nomfanekiso waso nesibalo segama laso bemi ngaselwandle lwengilazi , benamahabhu kaNkulunkulu .
66015003	Bahlabelela igama likaMose inceku kaNkulunkulu negama leWundlu , bathi : " Mikhulu , iyamangalisa imisebenzi yakho , Nkosi Nkulunkulu , Mninimandla onke ; zilungile , ziqinisile izindlela zakho wena Nkosi yezizwe ;
66015004	ngubani ongayikwesaba , Nkosi , adumise igama lakho , na ? Ngokuba wena wedwa ungcwele , nezizwe zonke ziyakuza zikhuleke phambi kwakho , ngokuba izenzo zakho zokulunga zibonakalisiwe . "
66015005	Emva kwalokho ngabona , kwase kuvulwa ithempeli letabernakele lobufakazi ezulwini ,
66015006	kwaphuma ethempelini izingelosi eziyisikhombisa ezinezinhlupho eziyisikhombisa , zembethe ingubo yelineni ehlanzekileyo nekhazimulayo , zizibophe ezifubeni ngamabhande egolide .
66015007	Esinye sezidalwa ezine sanika izingelosi eziyisikhombisa izitsha zegolide , zigcwele ulaka lukaNkulunkulu ophilayo kuze kube phakade naphakade .
66015008	Ithempeli lagcwala umusi ovela ekukhazimuleni kukaNkulunkulu nasemandleni akhe ; akakho owayengangena ethempelini , zingakapheleli izinhlupho eziyisikhombisa zezingelosi eziyisikhombisa .
66016001	Ngase ngizwa izwi elikhulu livela ethempelini , lithi kuzo izingelosi eziyisikhombisa : " Hambani nithululele emhlabeni izitsha eziyisikhombisa zolaka lukaNkulunkulu . "
66016002	Eyokuqala yaya-ke , yathululela isitsha sayo emhlabeni ; kwase kuvela isilonda esibi esinobuhlungu kubantu abanophawu lwesilo nabakhuleka kumfanekiso waso .
66016003	Neyesibili yathululela isitsha sayo elwandle ; lwase luba yigazi elinjengelofileyo , nakho konke okuzwayo okuphila elwandle kwafa .
66016004	Neyesithathu yathululela isitsha sayo emifuleni nasemithonjeni yamanzi , kwase kuba yigazi .
66016005	Ngezwa ingelosi yamanzi ithi : " Ulungile wena okhona nowawukhona , oNgcwele , ngokuba wakunquma lokho ,
66016006	ngokuba bachitha igazi labangcwele nelabaprofethi , wabanika ukuba baliphuze igazi ; bakufanele . "
66016007	Ngase ngizwa i-altare lithi : " Yebo , Nkosi Nkulunkulu , Mninimandla onke , ziqinisile , zilungile izahlulelo zakho . "
66016008	Eyesine yayisithululela isitsha sayo elangeni ; lase linikwa ukubashisa abantu ngomlilo .
66016009	Abantu bashiswa ngokushiswa okukhulu , kepha bahlambalaza igama likaNkulunkulu onamandla phezu kwalezi zinhlupho , kodwa abaphendukanga ukuba bamdumise .
66016010	Eyesihlanu yathululela isitsha sayo esihlalweni sobukhosi sesilo ; nombuso waso wenziwa mnyama , baluma izilimi zabo ngenxa yobuhlungu ,
66016011	futhi bahlambalaza uNkulunkulu wezulu ngenxa yobuhlungu babo nangenxa yezilonda zabo ; kepha abaphendukanga emisebenzini yabo .
66016012	Eyesithupha yathululela isitsha sayo emfuleni omkhulu u-Ewufrathe ; kwase kusha amanzi awo , ukuze indlela ilungiselwe amakhosi avela empumalanga .
66016013	Ngabona kuphuma emlonyeni kadrako , nasemlonyeni wesilo , nasemlonyeni womprofethi wamanga omoya abathathu abangcolileyo , befana nezingxangxa ;
66016014	ngokuba bangomoya bamademoni , benza izibonakaliso , abaphuma beya emakhosini ezwe lonke ukubahlanganisela ekulweni kosuku olukhulu lukaNkulunkulu uMninimandla onke .
66016015	Bheka , ngiyeza njengesela ; ubusisiwe olindayo , alonde izingubo zakhe ukuba angabi ngohamba ze , baze balibone ihlazo lakhe .
66016016	Wayesebahlanganisela endaweni ethiwa ngesiHeberu iHarmagedoni .
66016017	Eyesikhombisa yayisithululela isitsha sayo emoyeni ; kwase kuphuma izwi elikhulu ethempelini esihlalweni sobukhosi , lithi : " Sekwenzekile . "
66016018	Kwase kuba khona imibani , namazwi , nokuduma , kwaba khona nokuzamazama okukhulu komhlaba okungazange kube khona okunjalo , selokhu kwaba khona abantu emhlabeni , ukuzamazama komhlaba okukhulu kangaka .
66016019	Umuzi omkhulu waba yizinqamu ezintathu , nemizi yabezizwe yawa . NeBabiloni elikhulu lakhunjulwa phambi kukaNkulunkulu ukuba alinike isitsha sewayini lolaka lwakhe oluvuthayo .
66016020	Iziqhingi zonke zabaleka , nezintaba azifunyaniswanga .
66016021	Isichotho esikhulu esisinda njengetalenta sivela ezulwini sehlela phezu kwabantu ; abantu bamhlambalaza uNkulunkulu ngenxa yohlupho lwesichotho , ngokuba uhlupho lwaso lulukhulu kakhulu .
66017001	Kwase kuza enye yezingelosi eziyisikhombisa ezazinezitsha eziyisikhombisa , yakhuluma nami , yathi : " Woza lapha , ngikutshengise ukwahlulelwa kwesifebe esikhulu esihlezi phezu kwamanzi amaningi ,
66017002	afeba naso amakhosi omhlaba , nabakhileyo emhlabeni badakiswa yiwayini lobufebe baso . "
66017003	Yayisingiyisa ehlane ngikuMoya . Ngabona owesifazane ekhwele isilo esibomvu , sigcwele amagama enhlamba , sinamakhanda ayisikhombisa nezimpondo eziyishumi .
66017004	Nowesifazane wayembethe okububende nokubomvu , evunule ngegolide nangamatshe anenani nangamaparele , ephethe isitsha segolide ngesandla sakhe , sigcwele amanyala nokungcolileyo kobufebe bakhe ,
66017005	nasebusweni bakhe kulotshiwe igama eliyimfihlakalo lokuthi : IBABILONI ELIKHULU , UNINA WEZIFEBE NOWAMANYALA OMHLABA
66017006	Ngase ngibona owesifazane edakiwe yigazi labangcwele negazi lawofakazi bakaJesu . Kuthe lapho ngimbona , ngamangala ngokumangala okukhulu .
66017007	Yayisithi kimi ingelosi : " Umangalelani na ? Ngizakukutshela imfihlakalo yowesifazane neyesilo esimthweleyo , esinamakhanda ayisikhombisa nezimpondo eziyishumi .
66017008	Isilo owasibonayo sasikhona , asisekho ; kepha sesizakwenyuka , siphuma kwalasha , siye ekubhujisweni ; nabakhileyo emhlabeni bayakumangala , labo abamagama abo angalotshwanga encwadini yokuphila , selokhu kwasekelwa izwe , nxa bebona isilo ukuthi sasikhona , kepha asisekho , kanti sizakuba khona .
66017009	" Nansi ingqondo enokuhlakanipha . Amakhanda ayisikhombisa ayizintaba eziyisikhombisa , lapho owesifazane ehlezi phezu kwazo . Futhi zingamakhosi ayisikhombisa ;
66017010	ayisihlanu asewile , enye ikhona , enye ayikafiki ; nanxa isifikile , kumelwe ukuba ihlale isikhashana .
66017011	Nesilo esasikhona , kepha esingasekho , singesesishiyagalombili , sikuwo ayisikhombisa , siya ekubhujisweni .
66017012	" Izimpondo eziyishumi owazibonayo zingamakhosi ayishumi angakamukeli umbuso , kepha amukeliswa amandla njengamakhosi ihora linye kanye nesilo .
66017013	Lawo anomqondo munye , anika isilo amandla nokubusa kwawo .
66017014	Ayakulwa neWundlu , neWundlu liyakuwanqoba , ngokuba liyiNkosi yamakhosi noMbusi wababusi , nabakanye nalo , ababiziweyo , nabakhethiweyo , nabathembekileyo . "
66017015	Yayisithi kimi : " Amanzi owabonayo , lapho sihlezi khona isifebe , angabantu , nezixuku , nezizwe , nezilimi .
66017016	Izimpondo eziyishumi owazibonayo , nesilo , lezi ziyakusizonda isifebe , zisenze incithakalo , sibe yize , zidle inyama yaso , zisishise ngomlilo , zisiqede ;
66017017	ngokuba uNkulunkulu ukufakile ezinhliziyweni zazo ukuba zenze umqondo wakhe , ziwenze umqondo munye , zinike isilo umbuso wazo , aze agcwaliseke amazwi kaNkulunkulu .
66017018	Owesifazane owambonayo ungumuzi omkhulu onombuso phezu kwamakhosi omhlaba . "
66018001	Emva kwalokho ngabona enye ingelosi yehla ezulwini , inamandla amakhulu , nomhlaba wakhanyiswa ngokukhazimula kwayo .
66018002	Yamemeza ngezwi elinamandla , yathi : " Liwile , liwile iBabiloni elikhulu , selibe yindawo yokuhlala amademoni , nendawo yokubopha bonke omoya abangcolileyo , nendawo yokubopha zonke izinyoni ezingcolileyo nezizondekayo ,
66018003	ngokuba izizwe zonke ziphuzile iwayini lobufebe balo , namakhosi omhlaba afebile nalo , nabathengisi bomhlaba bacebile ngamandla okutamasa kwalo . "
66018004	Ngase ngizwa elinye izwi livela ezulwini , lithi : " Phumani kulo , bantu bami , ukuze ningahlanganyeli nalo izono zalo , nokuba ningamukeli okwezinhlupho zalo ,
66018005	ngokuba izono zalo zifinyelele ezulwini , noNkulunkulu wakhumbula ukungalungi kwalo .
66018006	Buyiselani kulo njengalokho lona likwenzile , niphinde kabili okwemisebenzi yalo ; esitsheni elalixuba kuso , xubani kabili kuso ;
66018007	ngokungangalokho elizidumise latamasa ngakho , linikeni ukuhlupheka nokulila okungako . Ngokuba enhliziyweni yalo lithi : ‘ Ngihlezi ngiyinkosikazi , angisiye umfelokazi , futhi angisoze ngabona ukulila . ’
66018008	Ngakho kuyakufika ngalusuku lunye izinhlupheko zalo , ukufa , nokulila , nendlala , futhi liyakushiswa liqedwe ngomlilo ; ngokuba iNkosi uNkulunkulu elahlulelayo inamandla .
66018009	" Amakhosi omhlaba ayefeba nalo ehlala ngokutamasa ayakukhala ambongoze ngalo , nxa ebona umusi wokusha kwalo ,
66018010	emi kude ngokwesaba ukuhlupheka kwalo ethi : ‘ Maye , maye kuwe muzi omkhulu waseBabiloni , muzi onamandla , ngokuba ngehora linye nje , kufikile ukwahlulelwa kwakho ! ’
66018011	" Nabathengisi bomhlaba bayalikhalela , balililele , ngokuba impahla yabo ayisathengwa muntu ,
66018012	impahla yegolide neyesiliva , namatshe anenani , namaparele , nelineni elicolekileyo , nokububende , nosilika , nokubomvu , kanye nemithi yonke enamakha , nezitsha zonke zamazinyo endlovu , nezitsha zonke zomuthi onenani elikhulu , nezethusi , nezensimbi , nezetshe elimhlophe ,
66018013	nokinamona , nokunephunga elimnandi , nempepho , namafutha okuqhola , nenhlaka , newayini , namafutha eminqumo , nempuphu ecolekileyo , nokolweni , nezinkomo , nezimvu , namahhashi , nezinqola , nezigqila , nemiphefumulo yabantu .
66018014	" Nezithelo ezazifiswa ngumphefumulo wakho zimukile kuwe , nakho konke okunonileyo nokucwebezelayo konakele kuwe , akusoze kwabuye kufunyanwe .
66018015	Abathengisi balezo zinto abacetshisiwe yilo bayakumela kude ngokwesaba ukuhlupheka kwalo , bekhala belila ,
66018016	bethi : ‘ Maye , maye kuwe muzi omkhulu owawembethe ilineni elicolekileyo , nokububende , nokubomvu , uvunule ngegolide nangamatshe anenani nangamaparele !
66018017	Ngokuba ngehora linye nje ingcebo engaka ichithekile . ’ " Nabashayeli bonke bemikhumbi , nabo bonke abaya nomaphi ngomkhumbi , namatilosi , nabo bonke abasebenza elwandle bemela kude ,
66018018	badazuluka bebona umusi wokusha kwalo , bethi : ‘ Ngumuphi umuzi ofana nalowo muzi omkhulu na ? ’
66018019	Base bethela uthuli emakhanda abo , badazuluka bekhala , belila bethi : ‘ Maye , maye kuwe muzi omkhulu , abacebile kuwe bonke abanemikhumbi elwandle ngenxa yengcebo enqabileyo yakho , ngokuba ngehora linye nje uchithekile !
66018020	Thokoza ngawo wena zulu , nani bangcwele , nani baphostoli , nani baprofethi ; ngokuba uNkulunkulu uwahlulele , waniphindiselela kuwo . ’ "
66018021	Ingelosi enamandla yafukula itshe linjengelokusila elikhulu , yaliphonsa elwandle , yathi : " Ngokunjalo iBabiloni umuzi omkhulu liyakuphonswa phansi ngamandla , lingabe lisafunyanwa .
66018022	Izwi lababetha ihabhu nelabahlabeleli nelababetha imitshingo namacilongo alisoze laphinda lizwakale kuwe , namuphi umlumbi noma owaluphi uhlobo akasoze wafunyaniswa kuwe , nomsindo wetshe lokusila awusoze wabuye uzwakale kuwe ,
66018023	nokukhanya kwesibani akusoze kwaphinda kukhanye phakathi kwakho , nezwi lomyeni nelomlobokazi alisoze labuye lizwakale phakathi kwakho , ngokuba izizwe zonke zidukisiwe ngokuthakatha kwakho ,
66018024	futhi kwafunyaniswa kuwe igazi labaprofethi nelabangcwele nelabo bonke ababebulewe emhlabeni . "
66019001	Emva kwalokho ngezwa kungathi izwi elikhulu lesixuku esikhulu ezulwini , lithi : " Haleluya ! Insindiso , nenkazimulo , namandla ngokukaNkulunkulu wethu ,
66019002	ngokuba ziqinisile , zilungile izahlulelo zakhe ; ngokuba isifebe esikhulu esonakalisa umhlaba ngobufebe baso , uliphindisele igazi lezinceku zakhe esandleni saso . "
66019003	Bathi ngokwesibili : " Haleluya ! Nomusi waso wenyuka kuze kube phakade naphakade . "
66019004	Ayesewa phansi amalunga angamashumi amabili nane kanye nezidalwa ezine , akhuleka kuNkulunkulu ohlezi esihlalweni sobukhosi , athi : " Amen ! Haleluya ! "
66019005	Kwase kuphuma izwi esihlalweni sobukhosi , lithi : " Dumisani uNkulunkulu wethu nonke nina zinceku zakhe , nina enimesabayo , abancane nabakhulu . "
66019006	Ngase ngizwa kungathi izwi lesixuku esikhulu , linjengezwi lamanzi amaningi , nezwi lokuduma okunamandla , lithi : " Haleluya ! Ngokuba iNkosi uNkulunkulu wethu , uMninimandla onke , iyabusa .
66019007	Masithokoze , sethabe , futhi masimnike inkazimulo , ngokuba umshado weWundlu ufikile , nomkalo uzilungisele ;
66019008	wanikwa ukuba embathe ilineni elicolekileyo nelikhazimulayo nelihlanzekileyo ; " ngokuba ilineni elicolekileyo liyizenzo ezilungileyo zabangcwele .
66019009	Yayisithi kimi : " Loba ukuthi : ‘ Babusisiwe abamenyelwe esidlweni somshado weWundlu . ’ " Yayisithi kimi : " Lawo angamazwi aqinisileyo kaNkulunkulu . "
66019010	Ngase ngiwa phansi phambi kwezinyawo ukukhuleka kuyo . Yayisithi kimi : " Musa ; ngiyinceku kanye nawe nabazalwane bakho abaphethe ubufakazi bukaJesu ; khuleka kuNkulunkulu . Ngokuba ubufakazi bukaJesu bungumoya wokuprofetha . "
66019011	Ngase ngibona izulu livulekile ; bheka , nanto ihhashi elimhlophe nohlezi phezu kwalo obizwa ngokuthi oThembekileyo noQinisileyo ; uyahlulela , alwe ngokulunga .
66019012	Amehlo akhe angamalangabi omlilo , nasekhanda lakhe kukhona imiqhele eminingi ; unegama elilotshiweyo elingaziwa muntu , nguyena kuphela ;
66019013	wembethe ingubo efafazwe ngegazi ; igama lakhe nguLizwi kaNkulunkulu .
66019014	Izimpi zasezulwini zamlandela zikhwele amahhashi amhlophe , zembethe ilineni elicolekileyo , elimhlophe nelihlanzekileyo .
66019015	Emlonyeni wakhe kwaphuma inkemba ebukhali , ukuze ashaye izizwe ngayo ; yena uyakuzibusa ngentonga yensimbi ; yena uqobo uyanyathela isikhamo sewayini lentukuthelo yolaka lukaNkulunkulu uMninimandla onke .
66019016	Unegama lilotshiwe engutsheni yakhe nasethangeni lakhe elithi : INKOSI YAMAKHOSI NOMBUSI WABABUSI
66019017	Ngase ngibona ingelosi imi elangeni , yamemeza ngezwi elikhulu ezinyonini zonke ezindizayo emkhathini wezulu , ithi : " Wozani , nibuthane esidlweni esikhulu sikaNkulunkulu
66019018	ukuba nidle inyama yamakhosi , nenyama yezinduna , nenyama yamaqhawe , nenyama yamahhashi neyabakhwele kuwo , nenyama yabo bonke abakhululekileyo nabayizigqila , abancane nabakhulu . "
66019019	Ngabona isilo , namakhosi omhlaba , nezimpi zawo zibuthene ukulwa naye owayehlezi ehhashini nempi yakhe .
66019020	Isilo sase sibanjwa nomprofethi wamanga okanye naso owenza izibonakaliso phambi kwaso , abadukisa ngazo abamukela uphawu lwesilo nabakhuleka kumfanekiso waso ; labo bobabili baphonswa besezwa echibini lomlilo elivutha isibabule .
66019021	Nabaseleyo babulawa ngenkemba ephuma emlonyeni wakhe owayehlezi ehhashini , nezinyoni zonke zasutha inyama yabo .
66020001	Ngase ngibona ingelosi yehla ezulwini , iphethe isihluthulelo sakwalasha neketanga elikhulu ngesandla sayo .
66020002	Yambamba udrako , inyoka endala , onguMhlebi noSathane , yambopha iminyaka eyinkulungwane ,
66020003	yamphonsa-ke kwalasha , yamvalela phakathi , yamqinisa ngophawu ngaphezu kwakhe , ukuze angabe esadukisa izizwe , ize iphele iminyaka eyinkulungwane ; emva kwalokho kumelwe ukuba athukululwe isikhashana .
66020004	Ngase ngibona izihlalo zobukhosi ; bahlala kuzo , banikwa ukwahlulela ; ngabona nemiphefumulo yababenqunywe amakhanda ngenxa yokufakaza ngoJesu nangenxa yezwi likaNkulunkulu , nalabo abangakhulekanga kuso isilo nomfanekiso waso , nabangamukelanga uphawu lwesilo ebunzini labo nasesandleni sabo ; baphila , babusa kanye noKristu iminyaka eyinkulungwane .
66020005	Abafileyo ababesele kabaphila yaze yaphela iminyaka eyinkulungwane . Lokhu kungukuvuka kokuqala .
66020006	Ubusisiwe , ungcwele onesabelo ekuvukeni kokuqala ; kulabo ukufa kwesibili akunamandla , kepha bayakuba ngabapristi bakaNkulunkulu nabakaKristu , babuse kanye naye iminyaka eyinkulungwane .
66020007	Nanxa isiphelile iminyaka eyinkulungwane , uSathane uyakukhululwa etilongweni lakhe ,
66020008	aphumele ukudukisa izizwe ezisemagumbini omane omhlaba , oGogi noMagogi , azibuthele ekulweni ezimumo wazo ungangesihlabathi solwandle .
66020009	Zase zikhuphukela ngaphezu kobubanzi bomhlaba , zakaka ikamu labangcwele nomuzi othandiweyo ; kwehla umlilo uvela ezulwini , wazidla waziqeda ;
66020010	noSathane owazidukisayo waphonswa echibini lomlilo nesibabule , lapho kukhona isilo nomprofethi wamanga ; ziyakuhlushwa imini nobusuku kuze kube phakade naphakade .
66020011	Ngase ngibona isihlalo sobukhosi esikhulu esimhlophe nohlezi kuso , obuso bakhe babalekelwa yizulu nomhlaba , akutholelwanga indawo .
66020012	Ngabona abafileyo , abakhulu nabancane , bemi phambi kwesihlalo sobukhosi ; izincwadi zavulwa ; nenye incwadi yavulwa , ngeyokuphila ; nabafileyo bahlulelwa ngalokho okulotshiwe ezincwadini njengokwemisebenzi yabo .
66020013	Nolwandle lwakhipha abafileyo ababekulo , nokufa neHayidese kwakhipha abafileyo ababekukho , bahlulelwa yilowo nalowo njengokwemisebenzi yakhe .
66020014	Ukufa neHayidese kwaphonswa echibini lomlilo . Lokhu kungukufa kwesibili , ichibi lomlilo .
66020015	Uma ekhona ongafunyaniswanga elotshiwe encwadini yokuphila , waphonswa echibini lomlilo .
66021001	Ngase ngibona izulu elisha nomhlaba omusha ; ngokuba izulu lokuqala nomhlaba wokuqala kudlulile , nolwandle alusekho .
66021002	Ngabona umuzi ongcwele , iJerusalema elisha , wehla uvela ezulwini kuNkulunkulu , ulungisiwe njengomlobokazi ohlotshiselwe umyeni wakhe .
66021003	Ngase ngizwa izwi elikhulu livela esihlalweni sobukhosi , lithi : " Bheka , itabernakele likaNkulunkulu likubantu ; uyakuhlala nabo , babe ngabantu bakhe , yena uNkulunkulu abe nabo ,
66021004	azesule izinyembezi zonke emehlweni abo ; ukufa akusayikuba khona ; nokudabuka , nokukhala , nobuhlungu akusayikuba khona ; ngokuba okokuqala kudlulile . "
66021005	Wayesethi ohlezi esihlalweni sobukhosi : " Bheka , ngenza konke kube kusha . " Wathi : " Loba , ngokuba lawa mazwi athembekile , aqinisile . "
66021006	Wayesethi kimi : " Sekwenzekile . Ngingu-Alfa no-Omega , ukuqala nokugcina . Owomileyo ngiyakumphuzisa ngesihle emthonjeni wamanzi okuphila .
66021007	Onqobayo uyakulidla ifa lalezo zinto , futhi ngiyakuba nguNkulunkulu kuye , yena abe yindodana kimi .
66021008	Kepha amagwala , nabangakholwayo , nabanengekayo , nababulali , nezifebe , nabathakathi , nabakhonza izithombe , nabo bonke abaqamba amanga , isabelo sabo siyakuba sechibini elivutha umlilo nesibabule , okungukufa kwesibili . "
66021009	Kwase kufika enye yezingelosi eziyisikhombisa ezazinezitsha eziyisikhombisa ezigcwele izinhlupho eziyisikhombisa zokugcina , yakhuluma nami , yathi : " Woza lapha , ngikukhombise umlobokazi , umkaWundlu . "
66021010	Yamuka nami ngikuMoya , yaya entabeni enkulu nephakemeyo , yangikhombisa umuzi ongcwele waseJerusalema wehla ezulwini kuNkulunkulu ,
66021011	unenkazimulo kaNkulunkulu ; ukukhanya kwawo kwakunjengetshe elinenani elikhulu sengathi yitshe lejaspi elicwebezelayo ,
66021012	unogange olukhulu noluphakemeyo , unamasango ayishumi nambili , nasemasangweni kukhona izingelosi eziyishumi nambili , kulotshwe kuwo amagama angawezizwe eziyishumi nambili zabantwana bakwa-Israyeli ;
66021013	ngasempumalanga kwakukhona amasango amathathu , nangasenyakatho amasango amathathu , nangaseningizimu amasango amathathu , nangasentshonalanga amasango amathathu .
66021014	Ugange lomuzi lwalunezisekelo eziyishumi nambili , naphezu kwazo amagama ayishumi nambili abaphostoli abayishumi nambili beWundlu .
66021015	Owayekhuluma nami wayenohlanga lwegolide ukuba alinganise umuzi , namasango awo , nogange lwawo .
66021016	Umuzi umi unezinhlangothi ezine , nobude bawo bungangobubanzi bawo . Walinganisa umuzi ngohlanga , amastadiyu ayizinkulungwane eziyishumi nambili , ubude nobubanzi nokuphakama kwawo kulingene .
66021017	Walinganisa ugange lwawo , izingalo eziyikhulu namashumi amane nane , yisilinganiso somuntu esingesengelosi .
66021018	Nogange lwawo lwakhiwe ngejaspi , nomuzi wawungowegolide elihle , linjengengilazi ecwebezelayo .
66021019	Izisekelo zogange lomuzi zivunulisiwe ngawo onke amatshe anenani elikhulu ; isisekelo sokuqala siyijaspi , esesibili yisafire , esesithathu yikhalkedoni , esesine yisimaragidu ,
66021020	esesihlanu yisaridonikisi , esesithupha yisardiyu , esesikhombisa yikrisolithe , esesishiyagalombili yibherile , esesishiyagalolunye yitopazi , eseshumi yikrisoprasi , eseshumi nanye yihiyakinte , eseshumi nambili yi-amethiste .
66021021	Amasango ayishumi nambili ayengamaparele ayishumi nambili ; yilelo nalelo sango ngalinye laliyiparele linye . Isitaladi somuzi sasiyigolide elicwengekileyo , linjengengilazi ekhanyayo .
66021022	Angibonanga ithempeli kuwo , ngokuba iNkosi uNkulunkulu , uMninimandla onke , iyithempeli lawo kanye neWundlu .
66021023	Umuzi awudingi ilanga nenyanga ukuba kukhanye kuwo , ngokuba inkazimulo kaNkulunkulu iyawukhanyisa , nesibani sawo siyiWundlu .
66021024	Izizwe ziyakuhamba ekukhanyeni kwawo , namakhosi omhlaba aletha kuwo ubukhosi bawo ;
66021025	namasango awo awasoze avalwa emini , ngokuba ubusuku abuyikuba khona lapho ;
66021026	bayakuletha ubukhosi nodumo lwezizwe .
66021027	Akusoze kwangena lutho olungcolileyo kuwo nowenza amanyala namanga , kuphela abalotshiwe encwadini yokuphila yeWundlu .
66022001	Wayesengikhombisa umfula wamanzi okuphila ucwebezela njengekristalu , uvela esihlalweni sobukhosi sikaNkulunkulu neseWundlu .
66022002	Phakathi kwesitaladi sawo nomfula emaceleni omabili kukhona umuthi wokuphila , uthela izithelo eziyishumi nambili , uthela izithelo zawo izinyanga ngezinyanga , namaqabunga omuthi angawokuphulukisa izizwe .
66022003	Akusayikuba khona nokukodwa ukuqalekisa . Isihlalo sobukhosi sikaNkulunkulu neseWundlu siyakuba kuwo , nezinceku zakhe ziyakumkhonza ,
66022004	zibone ubuso bakhe , negama lakhe liyakuba semabunzini azo .
66022005	Ubusuku abusayikuba khona ; abadingi ukukhanya kwesibani nokukhanya kwelanga , ngokuba iNkosi uNkulunkulu iyakubakhanyisela ; bayakubusa phakade naphakade .
66022006	Yayisithi kimi : " Lawo mazwi athembekile , aqinisile , neNkosi uNkulunkulu wemimoya yabaprofethi iyithumile ingelosi yayo ukuzikhombisa izinceku zayo okuzakwenzeka masinyane . "
66022007	" Bheka , ngiyeza masinyane . Ubusisiwe ogcina amazwi esiprofetho sale ncwadi . "
66022008	Mina Johane nginguye owezwa nowabona lezi zinto . Kuthe sengizwile , sengibonile , ngawa phansi ukuba ngikhuleke phambi kwezinyawo zengelosi engikhombisile lezo zinto .
66022009	Yayisithi kimi : " Musa ; ngiyinceku kanye nawe nabazalwane bakho abaprofethi nabagcina amazwi ale ncwadi ; khuleka kuNkulunkulu . "
66022010	Yathi kimi : " Ungavali ngophawu amazwi esiprofetho sale ncwadi , ngokuba isikhathi siseduze .
66022011	Ongalungile makenze njalo okungalungile , nongcolileyo makazingcolise njalo , kepha olungileyo makenze njalo ukulunga , nongcwele makazingcwelise njalo . "
66022012	" Bheka , ngiyeza masinyane , nomvuzo wami unami ukumnika yilowo nalowo njengokomsebenzi wakhe .
66022013	Ngingu-Alfa no-Omega , owokuqala nowokuphela , isiqalo nesigcino .
66022014	" Babusisiwe abahlanza izingubo zabo ukuba bathole ilungelo labo emthini wokuphila , bangene emzini ngamasango .
66022015	Ngaphandle kukhona izinja , nabathakathi , nezifebe , nababulali , nabakhonza izithombe , nabo bonke abathanda nabenza amanga .
66022016	" Mina Jesu ngithumile ingelosi yami ukufakaza kini lezi zinto emabandleni . Ngiyimpande nenzalo kaDavide , inkanyezi yokusa ecwebezelayo . "
66022017	UMoya nomlobokazi bathi : " Woza ! " Nozwayo makathi : " Woza ! " Nowomileyo makeze ; othandayo makathabathe amanzi okuphila ngesihle .
66022018	Ngiyafakaza mina kubo bonke abezwayo amazwi esiprofetho sale ncwadi ; uma ekhona owenezela kulokhu , uNkulunkulu uyakwenezela kuye izinhlupho ezilotshiwe kule ncwadi ;
66022019	futhi uma ekhona osusa utho kuwo amazwi encwadi yalesi siprofetho , uNkulunkulu uyakususa isabelo sakhe emthini wokuphila , nasemzini ongcwele , nakulokhu okulotshiwe kule ncwadi .
66022020	Ofakaza ngalezi zinto uthi : " Yebo , ngiyeza masinyane . " Amen . Woza , Nkosi Jesu !
66022021	Umusa weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu mawube nani nonke . Amen . ”
